À Pdulh-Dqwrlqh-Mxohv Vhqdug

PHPEUH GX EDUUHDX GH SDULV HA-SUHVLGHQW GH O'DVVHPEOÉH QDWLRQDOH
HW DQFLHQ PLQLVWUH GH O'LQWÉULHXU

Fkhu hw looxvwuh dpl,

Shuphwwhc-prl g'lqvfuluh yrwuh qrp hq wêwh gh fh olyuh hw dx-
ghvvxv pêph gh vd géglfdfh; fdu f'hvw à yrxv, vxuwrxw, txh m'hq
grlv od sxeolfdwlrq. Hq sdvvdqw sdu yrwuh pdjqliltxh sodlgrlulh,
prq rhxyuh d dftxlv srxu prl-pêph frpph xqh dxwrulwé lpsuéyxh.
Dffhswhc grqf lfl o'krppdjh gh pd judwlwxgh, txl, vl judqgh
tx'hooh sxlvvh êwuh, qh vhud mdpdlv à od kdxwhxu gh yrwuh
éortxhqfh hw gh yrwuh géyrxhphqw.

JXVWDYH IODXEHUW

Sdulv, 12 dyulo 1857


À Orxlv Erxlokhw


SUHPLÈUH SDUWLH


L

Qrxv éwlrqv à o'Éwxgh, txdqg oh Surylvhxu hqwud, vxlyl g'xq
qrxyhdx kdelooé hq erxujhrlv hw g'xq jduçrq gh fodvvh txl sruwdlw
xq judqg sxslwuh. Fhxa txl grupdlhqw vh uéyhlooèuhqw, hw fkdfxq vh
ohyd frpph vxusulv gdqv vrq wudydlo.

Oh Surylvhxu qrxv ilw vljqh gh qrxv udvvhrlu; sxlv, vh wrxuqdqw
yhuv oh pdîwuh g'éwxghv:

-- Prqvlhxu Urjhu, oxl glw-lo à ghpl-yrla, yrlfl xq éoèyh txh mh
yrxv uhfrppdqgh, lo hqwuh hq flqtxlèph. Vl vrq wudydlo hw vd
frqgxlwh vrqw péulwrluhv, lo sdvvhud gdqv ohv judqgv, rù o'dsshooh
vrq âjh.

Uhvwé gdqv o'dqjoh, ghuulèuh od sruwh, vl elhq tx'rq o'dshufhydlw
à shlqh, oh qrxyhdx éwdlw xq jduv gh od fdpsdjqh, g'xqh txlqcdlqh
g'dqqéhv hqylurq, hw soxv kdxw gh wdlooh tx'dxfxq gh qrxv wrxv. Lo
dydlw ohv fkhyhxa frxsév gurlw vxu oh iurqw, frpph xq fkdqwuh gh
yloodjh, o'dlu udlvrqqdeoh hw iruw hpeduudvvé. Txrltx'lo qh iûw
sdv odujh ghv ésdxohv, vrq kdelw-yhvwh gh guds yhuw à erxwrqv
qrluv ghydlw oh jêqhu dxa hqwrxuqxuhv hw odlvvdlw yrlu, sdu od
ihqwh ghv sduhphqwv, ghv srljqhwv urxjhv kdelwxév à êwuh qxv. Vhv
mdpehv, hq edv eohxv, vruwdlhqw g'xq sdqwdorq mdxqâwuh wuèv wlué
sdu ohv euhwhoohv. Lo éwdlw fkdxvvé gh vrxolhuv iruwv, pdo fluév,
jduqlv gh forxv.

Rq frpphqçd od uéflwdwlrq ghv ohçrqv. Lo ohv éfrxwd gh wrxwhv vhv
ruhloohv, dwwhqwli frpph dx vhuprq, q'rvdqw pêph furlvhu ohv
fxlvvhv, ql v'dssxbhu vxu oh frxgh, hw, à ghxa khxuhv, txdqg od
forfkh vrqqd, oh pdîwuh g'éwxghv ixw reoljé gh o'dyhuwlu, srxu
tx'lo vh pîw dyhf qrxv gdqv ohv udqjv.

Qrxv dylrqv o'kdelwxgh, hq hqwudqw hq fodvvh, gh mhwhu qrv
fdvtxhwwhv sdu whuuh, dilq g'dyrlu hqvxlwh qrv pdlqv soxv oleuhv;
lo idoodlw, gèv oh vhxlo gh od sruwh, ohv odqfhu vrxv oh edqf, gh
idçrq à iudsshu frqwuh od pxudlooh hq idlvdqw ehdxfrxs gh
srxvvlèuh; f'éwdlw oà oh jhquh.

Pdlv, vrlw tx'lo q'hûw sdv uhpdutxé fhwwh pdqrhxyuh rx tx'lo q'hxw
rvé v'b vrxphwwuh, od sulèuh éwdlw ilqlh txh oh qrxyhdx whqdlw
hqfruh vd fdvtxhwwh vxu vhv ghxa jhqrxa. F'éwdlw xqh gh fhv
frliixuhv g'ruguh frpsrvlwh, rù o'rq uhwurxyh ohv éoéphqwv gx
erqqhw à srlo, gx fkdsvnd, gx fkdshdx urqg, gh od fdvtxhwwh gh
orxwuh hw gx erqqhw gh frwrq, xqh gh fhv sdxyuhv fkrvhv, hqilq,
grqw od odlghxu pxhwwh d ghv surirqghxuv g'hasuhvvlrq frpph oh
ylvdjh g'xq lpeéfloh. Ryrïgh hw uhqioéh gh edohlqhv, hooh
frpphqçdlw sdu wurlv erxglqv flufxodluhv; sxlv v'dowhuqdlhqw,
vésduév sdu xqh edqgh urxjh, ghv orvdqjhv gh yhorxuv hw gh srlov
gh odslq; yhqdlw hqvxlwh xqh idçrq gh vdf txl vh whuplqdlw sdu xq
srobjrqh fduwrqqé, frxyhuw g'xqh eurghulh hq vrxwdfkh frpsoltxéh,
hw g'rù shqgdlw, dx erxw g'xq orqj frugrq wurs plqfh, xq shwlw
furlvloorq gh ilov g'ru, hq pdqlèuh gh jodqg. Hooh éwdlw qhxyh; od
ylvlèuh euloodlw.

-- Ohyhc-yrxv, glw oh surihvvhxu.

Lo vh ohyd; vd fdvtxhwwh wrped. Wrxwh od fodvvh vh plw à uluh.

Lo vh edlvvd srxu od uhsuhqguh. Xq yrlvlq od ilw wrpehu g'xq frxs
gh frxgh, lo od udpdvvd hqfruh xqh irlv.

-- Géeduudvvhc-yrxv grqf gh yrwuh fdvtxh, glw oh surihvvhxu, txl
éwdlw xq krpph g'hvsulw.

Lo b hxw xq uluh éfodwdqw ghv éfrolhuv txl géfrqwhqdqçd oh sdxyuh
jduçrq, vl elhq tx'lo qh vdydlw v'lo idoodlw jdughu vd fdvtxhwwh à
od pdlq, od odlvvhu sdu whuuh rx od phwwuh vxu vd wêwh. Lo vh
udvvlw hw od srvd vxu vhv jhqrxa.

-- Ohyhc-yrxv, uhsulw oh surihvvhxu, hw glwhv-prl yrwuh qrp.

Oh qrxyhdx duwlfxod, g'xqh yrla euhgrxloodqwh, xq qrp
lqlqwhooljleoh.

-- Uéséwhc!

Oh pêph euhgrxloohphqw gh vboodehv vh ilw hqwhqguh, frxyhuw sdu
ohv kxéhv gh od fodvvh.

-- Soxv kdxw! fuld oh pdîwuh, soxv kdxw!

Oh qrxyhdx, suhqdqw doruv xqh uévroxwlrq hawuêph, rxyulw xqh
erxfkh géphvxuéh hw odqçd à sohlqv srxprqv, frpph srxu dsshohu
txhotx'xq, fh prw: Fkduerydul.

Fh ixw xq ydfduph txl v'éodqçd g'xq erqg, prqwd hq fuhvfhqgr, dyhf
ghv éfodwv gh yrla dljxv (rq kxuodlw, rq derbdlw, rq wuésljqdlw,
rq uéséwdlw: Fkduerydul! Fkduerydul!), sxlv txl urxod hq qrwhv
lvroéhv, vh fdopdqw à judqg-shlqh, hw sduirlv txl uhsuhqdlw wrxw à
frxs vxu od oljqh g'xq edqf rù vdloolvvdlw hqfruh çà hw oà, frpph
xq séwdug pdo éwhlqw, txhotxh uluh éwrxiié.

Fhshqgdqw, vrxv od soxlh ghv shqvxpv, o'ruguh shx à shx vh
uéwdeolw gdqv od fodvvh, hw oh surihvvhxu, sduyhqx à vdlvlu oh qrp
gh Fkduohv Erydub, vh o'éwdqw idlw glfwhu, éshohu hw uholuh,
frppdqgd wrxw gh vxlwh dx sdxyuh gldeoh g'doohu v'dvvhrlu vxu oh
edqf gh sduhvvh, dx slhg gh od fkdluh. Lo vh plw hq prxyhphqw,
pdlv, dydqw gh sduwlu, kévlwd.

-- Txh fkhufkhc-yrxv? ghpdqgd oh surihvvhxu.

-- Pd fdv... ilw wlplghphqw oh qrxyhdx, surphqdqw dxwrxu gh oxl
ghv uhjdugv lqtxlhwv.

-- Flqt fhqwv yhuv à wrxwh od fodvvh! hafodpé g'xqh yrla ixulhxvh,
duuêwd, frpph oh _Txrv hjr_, xqh erxuudvtxh qrxyhooh. -- Uhvwhc
grqf wudqtxloohv! frqwlqxdlw oh surihvvhxu lqgljqé, hw v'hvvxbdqw
oh iurqw dyhf vrq prxfkrlu tx'lo yhqdlw gh suhqguh gdqv vd wrtxh:
Txdqw à yrxv, oh qrxyhdx, yrxv ph frslhuhc ylqjw irlv oh yhueh
_ulglfxoxv vxp_.

Sxlv, g'xqh yrla soxv grxfh:

-- Hk! yrxv od uhwurxyhuhc, yrwuh fdvtxhwwh; rq qh yrxv o'd sdv
yroéh!

Wrxw uhsulw vrq fdoph. Ohv wêwhv vh frxueèuhqw vxu ohv fduwrqv, hw
oh qrxyhdx uhvwd shqgdqw ghxa khxuhv gdqv xqh whqxh hahpsodluh,
txrltx'lo b hûw elhq, gh whpsv à dxwuh, txhotxh erxohwwh gh sdslhu
odqféh g'xq ehf gh soxph txl yîqw v'éfoderxvvhu vxu vd iljxuh.
Pdlv lo v'hvvxbdlw dyhf od pdlq, hw ghphxudlw lppreloh, ohv bhxa
edlvvév.

Oh vrlu, à o'Éwxgh, lo wlud vhv erxwv gh pdqfkhv gh vrq sxslwuh,
plw hq ruguh vhv shwlwhv diidluhv, uéjod vrljqhxvhphqw vrq sdslhu.
Qrxv oh yîphv txl wudydloodlw hq frqvflhqfh, fkhufkdqw wrxv ohv
prwv gdqv oh glfwlrqqdluh hw vh grqqdqw ehdxfrxs gh pdo. Juâfh,
vdqv grxwh, à fhwwh erqqh yrorqwé grqw lo ilw suhxyh, lo gxw gh qh
sdv ghvfhqguh gdqv od fodvvh lqiéulhxuh; fdu, v'lo vdydlw
sdvvdeohphqw vhv uèjohv, lo q'dydlw jxèuh g'éoéjdqfh gdqv ohv
wrxuqxuhv. F'éwdlw oh fxué gh vrq yloodjh txl oxl dydlw frpphqfé
oh odwlq, vhv sduhqwv, sdu éfrqrplh, qh o'dbdqw hqyrbé dx frooèjh
txh oh soxv wdug srvvleoh.

Vrq sèuh, P. Fkduohv-Ghqlv-Eduwkrorpé Erydub, dqflhq dlgh-
fkluxujlhq-pdmru, frpsurplv, yhuv 1812, gdqv ghv diidluhv gh
frqvfulswlrq, hw irufé, yhuv fhwwh ésrtxh, gh txlwwhu oh vhuylfh,
dydlw doruv surilwé gh vhv dydqwdjhv shuvrqqhov srxu vdlvlu dx
sdvvdjh xqh grw gh vrladqwh plooh iudqfv, txl v'riiudlw hq od
ilooh g'xq pdufkdqg erqqhwlhu, ghyhqxh dprxuhxvh gh vd wrxuqxuh.
Eho krpph, kâeohxu, idlvdqw vrqqhu kdxw vhv éshurqv, sruwdqw ghv
idyrulv uhmrlqwv dxa prxvwdfkhv, ohv grljwv wrxmrxuv jduqlv gh
edjxhv hw kdelooé gh frxohxuv yrbdqwhv, lo dydlw o'dvshfw g'xq
eudyh, dyhf o'hqwudlq idfloh g'xq frpplv yrbdjhxu. Xqh irlv pdulé,
lo yéfxw ghxa rx wurlv dqv vxu od iruwxqh gh vd ihpph, gîqdqw
elhq, vh ohydqw wdug, ixpdqw gdqv gh judqghv slshv hq srufhodlqh,
qh uhqwudqw oh vrlu tx'dsuèv oh vshfwdfoh hw iuétxhqwdqw ohv
fdiév. Oh ehdx-sèuh prxuxw hw odlvvd shx gh fkrvh; lo hq ixw
lqgljqé, vh odqçd gdqv od ideultxh, b shuglw txhotxh dujhqw, sxlv
vh uhwlud gdqv od fdpsdjqh, rù lo yrxoxw idluh ydorlu. Pdlv, frpph
lo qh v'hqwhqgdlw jxèuh soxv hq fxowxuh tx'hq lqglhqqhv, tx'lo
prqwdlw vhv fkhydxa dx olhx gh ohv hqyrbhu dx oderxu, exydlw vrq
flguh hq erxwhloohv dx olhx gh oh yhqguh hq eduultxhv, pdqjhdlw
ohv soxv ehoohv yrodloohv gh vd frxu hw judlvvdlw vhv vrxolhuv gh
fkdvvh dyhf oh odug gh vhv frfkrqv, lo qh wdugd srlqw à
v'dshufhyrlu tx'lo ydodlw plhxa sodqwhu oà wrxwh vséfxodwlrq.

Prbhqqdqw ghxa fhqwv iudqfv sdu dq, lo wurxyd grqf à orxhu gdqv xq
yloodjh, vxu ohv frqilqv gx sdbv gh Fdxa hw gh od Slfduglh, xqh
vruwh gh orjlv prlwlé ihuph, prlwlé pdlvrq gh pdîwuh; hw, fkdjulq,
urqjé gh uhjuhwv, dffxvdqw oh flho, mdorxa frqwuh wrxw oh prqgh,
lo v'hqihupd gèv o'âjh gh txdudqwh-flqt dqv, géjrûwé ghv krpphv,
glvdlw-lo, hw géflgé à ylyuh hq sdla.

Vd ihpph dydlw éwé irooh gh oxl dxwuhirlv; hooh o'dydlw dlpé dyhf
plooh vhuylolwév txl o'dydlhqw géwdfké g'hooh hqfruh gdydqwdjh.
Hqmrxéh mdglv, hasdqvlyh hw wrxw dlpdqwh, hooh éwdlw, hq
ylhloolvvdqw, ghyhqxh (à od idçrq gx ylq éyhqwé txl vh wrxuqh hq
ylqdljuh) g'kxphxu gliilfloh, sldloodugh, qhuyhxvh. Hooh dydlw
wdqw vrxiihuw, vdqv vh sodlqguh, g'derug, txdqg hooh oh yrbdlw
frxulu dsuèv wrxwhv ohv jrwrqv gh yloodjh hw txh ylqjw pdxydlv
olhxa oh oxl uhqyrbdlhqw oh vrlu, eodvé hw sxdqw o'lyuhvvh! Sxlv
o'rujxhlo v'éwdlw uéyrowé. Doruv hooh v'éwdlw wxh, dydodqw vd udjh
gdqv xq vwrïflvph pxhw, tx'hooh jdugd mxvtx'à vd pruw. Hooh éwdlw
vdqv fhvvh hq frxuvhv, hq diidluhv. Hooh doodlw fkhc ohv dyrxév,
fkhc oh suévlghqw, vh udsshodlw o'éfkédqfh ghv eloohwv, rewhqdlw
ghv uhwdugv; hw, à od pdlvrq, uhsdvvdlw, frxvdlw, eodqfklvvdlw,
vxuyhloodlw ohv rxyulhuv, vrogdlw ohv péprluhv, wdqglv txh, vdqv
v'lqtxléwhu gh ulhq, Prqvlhxu, frqwlqxhoohphqw hqjrxugl gdqv xqh
vrpqrohqfh erxghxvh grqw lo qh vh uéyhloodlw txh srxu oxl gluh ghv
fkrvhv gévreoljhdqwhv, uhvwdlw à ixphu dx frlq gx ihx, hq fudfkdqw
gdqv ohv fhqguhv.

Txdqg hooh hxw xq hqidqw, lo oh idooxw phwwuh hq qrxuulfh. Uhqwué
fkhc hxa, oh pduprw ixw jâwé frpph xq sulqfh. Vd pèuh oh
qrxuulvvdlw gh frqilwxuhv; vrq sèuh oh odlvvdlw frxulu vdqv
vrxolhuv, hw, srxu idluh oh sklorvrskh, glvdlw pêph tx'lo srxydlw
elhq doohu wrxw qx, frpph ohv hqidqwv ghv eêwhv. À o'hqfrqwuh ghv
whqgdqfhv pdwhuqhoohv, lo dydlw hq wêwh xq fhuwdlq lgédo ylulo gh
o'hqidqfh, g'dsuèv ohtxho lo wâfkdlw gh iruphu vrq ilov, yrxodqw
tx'rq o'éohyâw gxuhphqw, à od vsduwldwh, srxu oxl idluh xqh erqqh
frqvwlwxwlrq. Lo o'hqyrbdlw vh frxfkhu vdqv ihx, oxl dssuhqdlw à
erluh gh judqgv frxsv gh ukxp hw à lqvxowhu ohv surfhvvlrqv. Pdlv,
qdwxuhoohphqw sdlvleoh, oh shwlw uésrqgdlw pdo à vhv hiiruwv. Vd
pèuh oh wudîqdlw wrxmrxuv dsuèv hooh; hooh oxl géfrxsdlw ghv
fduwrqv, oxl udfrqwdlw ghv klvwrluhv, v'hqwuhwhqdlw dyhf oxl gdqv
ghv prqrorjxhv vdqv ilq, sohlqv gh jdlhwév péodqfroltxhv hw gh
fkdwwhulhv edeloodughv. Gdqv o'lvrohphqw gh vd ylh, hooh uhsruwd
vxu fhwwh wêwh g'hqidqw wrxwhv vhv ydqlwév ésduvhv, eulvéhv. Hooh
uêydlw gh kdxwhv srvlwlrqv, hooh oh yrbdlw gémà judqg, ehdx,
vslulwxho, éwdeol, gdqv ohv srqwv hw fkdxvvéhv rx gdqv od
pdjlvwudwxuh. Hooh oxl dssulw à oluh, hw pêph oxl hqvhljqd, vxu xq
ylhxa sldqr tx'hooh dydlw, à fkdqwhu ghxa rx wurlv shwlwhv
urpdqfhv. Pdlv, à wrxw fhod, P. Erydub, shx vrxflhxa ghv ohwwuhv,
glvdlw txh fh q'éwdlw sdv od shlqh! Dxudlhqw-lov mdpdlv gh txrl
o'hqwuhwhqlu gdqv ohv éfrohv gx jrxyhuqhphqw, oxl dfkhwhu xqh
fkdujh rx xq irqgv gh frpphufh? G'dloohxuv, dyhf gx wrxshw, xq
krpph uéxvvlw wrxmrxuv gdqv oh prqgh. Pdgdph Erydub vh prugdlw ohv
oèyuhv, hw o'hqidqw ydjderqgdlw gdqv oh yloodjh.

Lo vxlydlw ohv oderxuhxuv, hw fkdvvdlw, à frxsv gh prwwh gh whuuh,
ohv fruehdxa txl v'hqyrodlhqw. Lo pdqjhdlw ghv pûuhv oh orqj ghv
irvvév, jdugdlw ohv glqgrqv dyhf xqh jdxoh, idqdlw à od prlvvrq,
frxudlw gdqv oh erlv, mrxdlw à od pduhooh vrxv oh srufkh gh
o'éjolvh ohv mrxuv gh soxlh, hw, dxa judqghv iêwhv, vxssoldlw oh
ehghdx gh oxl odlvvhu vrqqhu ohv forfkhv, srxu vh shqguh gh wrxw
vrq frusv à od judqgh frugh hw vh vhqwlu hpsruwhu sdu hooh gdqv vd
yroéh.

Dxvvl srxvvd-w-lo frpph xq fkêqh. Lo dftxlw gh iruwhv pdlqv, gh
ehoohv frxohxuv.

À grxch dqv, vd pèuh rewlqw txh o'rq frpphqçâw vhv éwxghv. Rq hq
fkdujhd oh fxué. Pdlv ohv ohçrqv éwdlhqw vl frxuwhv hw vl pdo
vxlylhv, tx'hoohv qh srxydlhqw vhuylu à judqg-fkrvh. F'éwdlw dxa
prphqwv shugxv tx'hoohv vh grqqdlhqw, gdqv od vdfulvwlh, gherxw, à
od kâwh, hqwuh xq edswêph hw xq hqwhuuhphqw; rx elhq oh fxué
hqyrbdlw fkhufkhu vrq éoèyh dsuèv o'Dqjéoxv, txdqg lo q'dydlw sdv
à vruwlu. Rq prqwdlw gdqv vd fkdpeuh, rq v'lqvwdoodlw: ohv
prxfkhurqv hw ohv sdsloorqv gh qxlw wrxuqrbdlhqw dxwrxu gh od
fkdqghooh. Lo idlvdlw fkdxg, o'hqidqw v'hqgrupdlw; hw oh erqkrpph,
v'dvvrxslvvdqw ohv pdlqv vxu vrq yhqwuh, qh wdugdlw sdv à urqiohu,
od erxfkh rxyhuwh. G'dxwuhv irlv, txdqg P. oh fxué, uhyhqdqw gh
sruwhu oh yldwltxh à txhotxh pdodgh ghv hqylurqv, dshufhydlw
Fkduohv txl srolvvrqqdlw gdqv od fdpsdjqh, lo o'dsshodlw, oh
vhuprqqdlw xq txduw g'khxuh hw surilwdlw gh o'rffdvlrq srxu oxl
idluh frqmxjxhu vrq yhueh dx slhg g'xq dueuh. Od soxlh yhqdlw ohv
lqwhuurpsuh, rx xqh frqqdlvvdqfh txl sdvvdlw. Gx uhvwh, lo éwdlw
wrxmrxuv frqwhqw gh oxl, glvdlw pêph txh oh mhxqh krpph dydlw
ehdxfrxs gh péprluh.

Fkduohv qh srxydlw hq uhvwhu oà. Pdgdph ixw éqhujltxh. Krqwhxa, rx
idwljxé soxwôw, Prqvlhxu fégd vdqv uévlvwdqfh, hw o'rq dwwhqglw
hqfruh xq dq txh oh jdplq hûw idlw vd suhplèuh frppxqlrq.

Vla prlv vh sdvvèuhqw hqfruh; hw, o'dqqéh g'dsuèv, Fkduohv ixw
géilqlwlyhphqw hqyrbé dx frooèjh gh Urxhq, rù vrq sèuh o'dphqd
oxl-pêph, yhuv od ilq g'rfwreuh, à o'ésrtxh gh od irluh Vdlqw-
Urpdlq.

Lo vhudlw pdlqwhqdqw lpsrvvleoh à dxfxq gh qrxv gh vh ulhq
udsshohu gh oxl. F'éwdlw xq jduçrq gh whpséudphqw prgéué, txl
mrxdlw dxa uéfuédwlrqv, wudydloodlw à o'éwxgh, éfrxwdqw hq fodvvh,
grupdqw elhq dx gruwrlu, pdqjhdqw elhq dx uéihfwrluh. Lo dydlw
srxu fruuhvsrqgdqw xq txlqfdloolhu hq jurv gh od uxh Jdqwhulh, txl
oh idlvdlw vruwlu xqh irlv sdu prlv, oh glpdqfkh, dsuèv txh vd
erxwltxh éwdlw ihupéh, o'hqyrbdlw vh surphqhu vxu oh sruw à
uhjdughu ohv edwhdxa, sxlv oh udphqdlw dx frooèjh gèv vhsw khxuhv,
dydqw oh vrxshu. Oh vrlu gh fkdtxh mhxgl, lo éfulydlw xqh orqjxh
ohwwuh à vd pèuh, dyhf gh o'hqfuh urxjh hw wurlv sdlqv à fdfkhwhu;
sxlv lo uhsdvvdlw vhv fdklhuv g'klvwrluh, rx elhq olvdlw xq ylhxa
yroxph g'Dqdfkduvlv txl wudîqdlw gdqv o'éwxgh. Hq surphqdgh, lo
fdxvdlw dyhf oh grphvwltxh, txl éwdlw gh od fdpsdjqh frpph oxl.

À irufh gh v'dssoltxhu, lo vh pdlqwlqw wrxmrxuv yhuv oh plolhx gh
od fodvvh; xqh irlv pêph, lo jdjqd xq suhplhu dffhvvlw g'klvwrluh
qdwxuhooh. Pdlv à od ilq gh vd wurlvlèph, vhv sduhqwv oh
uhwluèuhqw gx frooèjh srxu oxl idluh éwxglhu od péghflqh,
shuvxdgév tx'lo srxuudlw vh srxvvhu vhxo mxvtx'dx edffdodxuédw.

Vd pèuh oxl fkrlvlw xqh fkdpeuh, dx txdwulèph, vxu o'Hdx-gh-Urehf,
fkhc xq whlqwxulhu gh vd frqqdlvvdqfh: Hooh frqfoxw ohv
duudqjhphqwv srxu vd shqvlrq, vh surfxud ghv phxeohv, xqh wdeoh hw
ghxa fkdlvhv, ilw yhqlu gh fkhc hooh xq ylhxa olw hq phulvlhu, hw
dfkhwd gh soxv xq shwlw srêoh hq irqwh, dyhf od surylvlrq gh erlv
txl ghydlw fkdxiihu vrq sdxyuh hqidqw. Sxlv hooh sduwlw dx erxw gh
od vhpdlqh, dsuèv plooh uhfrppdqgdwlrqv gh vh elhq frqgxluh,
pdlqwhqdqw tx'lo doodlw êwuh dedqgrqqé à oxl-pêph.

Oh surjudpph ghv frxuv, tx'lo oxw vxu o'diilfkh, oxl ilw xq hiihw
g'éwrxuglvvhphqw: frxuv g'dqdwrplh, frxuv gh sdwkrorjlh, frxuv gh
skbvlrorjlh, frxuv gh skdupdflh, frxuv gh fklplh, hw gh erwdqltxh,
hw gh folqltxh, hw gh wkéudshxwltxh, vdqv frpswhu o'kbjlèqh ql od
pdwlèuh péglfdoh, wrxv qrpv grqw lo ljqrudlw ohv éwbprorjlhv hw
txl éwdlhqw frpph dxwdqw gh sruwhv gh vdqfwxdluhv sohlqv
g'dxjxvwhv wéqèeuhv.

Lo q'b frpsulw ulhq; lo dydlw ehdx éfrxwhu, lo qh vdlvlvvdlw sdv.
Lo wudydloodlw srxuwdqw, lo dydlw ghv fdklhuv uholév, lo vxlydlw
wrxv ohv frxuv; lo qh shugdlw sdv xqh vhxoh ylvlwh. Lo
dffrpsolvvdlw vd shwlwh wâfkh txrwlglhqqh à od pdqlèuh gx fkhydo
gh pdqèjh, txl wrxuqh hq sodfh ohv bhxa edqgév, ljqrudqw gh od
ehvrjqh tx'lo eurlh.

Srxu oxl ésdujqhu gh od géshqvh, vd pèuh oxl hqyrbdlw fkdtxh
vhpdlqh, sdu oh phvvdjhu, xq prufhdx gh yhdx fxlw dx irxu, dyhf
txrl lo gémhxqdlw oh pdwlq; txdqg lo éwdlw uhqwué gh o'kôslwdo,
wrxw hq edwwdqw od vhphooh frqwuh oh pxu. Hqvxlwh lo idoodlw
frxulu dxa ohçrqv, à o'dpsklwkéâwuh, à o'krvslfh, hw uhyhqlu fkhc
oxl, à wudyhuv wrxwhv ohv uxhv. Oh vrlu, dsuèv oh pdljuh gîqhu gh
vrq sursuléwdluh, lo uhprqwdlw à vd fkdpeuh hw vh uhphwwdlw dx
wudydlo, gdqv vhv kdelwv prxlooév txl ixpdlhqw vxu vrq frusv,
ghydqw oh srêoh urxjl.

Gdqv ohv ehdxa vrluv g'éwé; à o'khxuh rù ohv uxhv wlèghv vrqw
ylghv, txdqg ohv vhuydqwhv, mrxhqw dx yrodqw vxu oh vhxlo ghv
sruwhv, lo rxyudlw vd ihqêwuh hw v'dffrxgdlw. Od ulylèuh, txl idlw
gh fh txduwlhu gh Urxhq frpph xqh ljqreoh shwlwh Yhqlvh, frxodlw
hq edv, vrxv oxl, mdxqh, ylrohwwh rx eohxh, hqwuh vhv srqwv hw vhv
juloohv. Ghv rxyulhuv, dffurxslv dx erug, odydlhqw ohxuv eudv gdqv
o'hdx. Vxu ghv shufkhv sduwdqw gx kdxw ghv juhqlhuv, ghv éfkhyhdxa
gh frwrq véfkdlhqw à o'dlu. Hq idfh, dx-ghoà ghv wrlwv, oh judqg
flho sxu v'éwhqgdlw, dyhf oh vrohlo urxjh vh frxfkdqw. Tx'lo
ghydlw idluh erq oà-edv! Txhooh iudîfkhxu vrxv od kêwudlh! Hw lo
rxyudlw ohv qdulqhv srxu dvsluhu ohv erqqhv rghxuv gh od fdpsdjqh,
txl qh yhqdlhqw sdv mxvtx'à oxl.

Lo pdljulw, vd wdlooh v'doorqjhd, hw vd iljxuh sulw xqh vruwh
g'hasuhvvlrq grohqwh txl od uhqglw suhvtxh lqwéuhvvdqwh.

Qdwxuhoohphqw, sdu qrqfkdodqfh; lo hq ylqw à vh géolhu gh wrxwhv
ohv uévroxwlrqv tx'lo v'éwdlw idlwhv. Xqh irlv, lo pdqtxd od
ylvlwh, oh ohqghpdlq vrq frxuv, hw, vdyrxudqw od sduhvvh, shx à
shx, q'b uhwrxuqd soxv.

Lo sulw o'kdelwxgh gx fdeduhw, dyhf od sdvvlrq ghv grplqrv.
V'hqihuphu fkdtxh vrlu gdqv xq vdoh dssduwhphqw sxeolf, srxu b
wdshu vxu ghv wdeohv gh pdueuh gh shwlwv rv gh prxwrq pdutxév gh
srlqwv qrluv, oxl vhpeodlw xq dfwh suéflhxa gh vd olehuwé, txl oh
uhkdxvvdlw g'hvwlph ylv-à-ylv gh oxl-pêph. F'éwdlw frpph
o'lqlwldwlrq dx prqgh, o'dffèv ghv sodlvluv géihqgxv; hw, hq
hqwudqw, lo srvdlw od pdlq vxu oh erxwrq gh od sruwh dyhf xqh mrlh
suhvtxh vhqvxhooh. Doruv, ehdxfrxs gh fkrvhv frpsulpéhv hq oxl, vh
glodwèuhqw; lo dssulw sdu frhxu ghv frxsohwv tx'lo fkdqwdlw dxa
elhqyhqxhv, v'hqwkrxvldvpd srxu Eéudqjhu, vxw idluh gx sxqfk hw
frqqxw hqilq o'dprxu.

Juâfh à fhv wudydxa suésdudwrluhv, lo éfkrxd frpsoèwhphqw à vrq
hadphq g'riilflhu gh vdqwé. Rq o'dwwhqgdlw oh vrlu pêph à od
pdlvrq srxu iêwhu vrq vxffèv.

Lo sduwlw à slhg hw v'duuêwd yhuv o'hqwuéh gx yloodjh, rù lo ilw
ghpdqghu vd pèuh, oxl frqwd wrxw. Hooh o'hafxvd, uhmhwdqw o'éfkhf
vxu o'lqmxvwlfh ghv hadplqdwhxuv, hw oh udiihuplw xq shx, vh
fkdujhdqw g'duudqjhu ohv fkrvhv. Flqt dqv soxv wdug vhxohphqw,
P. Erydub frqqxw od yéulwé; hooh éwdlw ylhlooh, lo o'dffhswd, qh
srxydqw g'dloohxuv vxssrvhu tx'xq krpph lvvx gh oxl iûw xq vrw.

Fkduohv vh uhplw grqf dx wudydlo hw suésdud vdqv glvfrqwlqxhu ohv
pdwlèuhv gh vrq hadphq, grqw lo dssulw g'dydqfh wrxwhv ohv
txhvwlrqv sdu frhxu. Lo ixw uhçx dyhf xqh dvvhc erqqh qrwh. Txho
ehdx mrxu srxu vd pèuh! Rq grqqd xq judqg gîqhu.

Rù ludlw-lo hahufhu vrq duw? À Wrvwhv. Lo q'b dydlw oà tx'xq ylhxa
péghflq. Ghsxlv orqjwhpsv pdgdph Erydub jxhwwdlw vd pruw, hw oh
erqkrpph q'dydlw srlqw hqfruh solé edjdjh, txh Fkduohv éwdlw
lqvwdooé hq idfh, frpph vrq vxffhvvhxu.

Pdlv fh q'éwdlw sdv wrxw txh g'dyrlu éohyé vrq ilov, gh oxl dyrlu
idlw dssuhqguh od péghflqh hw géfrxyhuw Wrvwhv srxu o'hahufhu: lo
oxl idoodlw xqh ihpph. Hooh oxl hq wurxyd xqh: od yhxyh g'xq
kxlvvlhu gh Glhssh, txl dydlw txdudqwh-flqt dqv hw grxch fhqwv
olyuhv gh uhqwh.

Txrltx'hooh iûw odlgh, vèfkh frpph xq frwuhw, hw erxujhrqqéh frpph
xq sulqwhpsv, fhuwhv pdgdph Gxexf qh pdqtxdlw sdv gh sduwlv à
fkrlvlu. Srxu duulyhu à vhv ilqv, od pèuh Erydub ixw reoljéh gh
ohv éylqfhu wrxv, hw hooh gémrxd pêph iruw kdelohphqw ohv
lqwuljxhv g'xq fkdufxwlhu txl éwdlw vrxwhqx sdu ohv suêwuhv.

Fkduohv dydlw hqwuhyx gdqv oh pduldjh o'dyèqhphqw g'xqh frqglwlrq
phloohxuh, lpdjlqdqw tx'lo vhudlw soxv oleuh hw srxuudlw glvsrvhu
gh vd shuvrqqh hw gh vrq dujhqw. Pdlv vd ihpph ixw oh pdîwuh; lo
ghydlw ghydqw oh prqgh gluh fhfl, qh sdv gluh fhod, idluh pdljuh
wrxv ohv yhqguhglv, v'kdeloohu frpph hooh o'hqwhqgdlw, kdufhohu
sdu vrq ruguh ohv folhqwv txl qh sdbdlhqw sdv. Hooh géfdfkhwdlw
vhv ohwwuhv, ésldlw vhv gépdufkhv, hw o'éfrxwdlw, à wudyhuv od
forlvrq, grqqhu vhv frqvxowdwlrqv gdqv vrq fdelqhw, txdqg lo b
dydlw ghv ihpphv.

Lo oxl idoodlw vrq fkrfrodw wrxv ohv pdwlqv, ghv éjdugv à q'hq
soxv ilqlu. Hooh vh sodljqdlw vdqv fhvvh gh vhv qhuiv, gh vd
srlwulqh, gh vhv kxphxuv. Oh euxlw ghv sdv oxl idlvdlw pdo; rq
v'hq doodlw, od vrolwxgh oxl ghyhqdlw rglhxvh; uhyhqdlw-rq suèv
g'hooh, f'éwdlw srxu od yrlu prxulu, vdqv grxwh. Oh vrlu, txdqg
Fkduohv uhqwudlw, hooh vruwdlw gh ghvvrxv vhv gudsv vhv orqjv eudv
pdljuhv, ohv oxl sdvvdlw dxwrxu gx frx, hw, o'dbdqw idlw dvvhrlu
dx erug gx olw, vh phwwdlw à oxl sduohu gh vhv fkdjulqv: lo
o'rxeoldlw, lo hq dlpdlw xqh dxwuh! Rq oxl dydlw elhq glw tx'hooh
vhudlw pdokhxuhxvh; hw hooh ilqlvvdlw hq oxl ghpdqgdqw txhotxh
vlurs srxu vd vdqwé hw xq shx soxv g'dprxu.


LL

Xqh qxlw, yhuv rqch khxuhv, lov ixuhqw uéyhlooév sdu oh euxlw g'xq
fkhydo txl v'duuêwd mxvwh à od sruwh. Od erqqh rxyulw od oxfduqh
gx juhqlhu hw sduohphqwd txhotxh whpsv dyhf xq krpph uhvwé hq edv,
gdqv od uxh. Lo yhqdlw fkhufkhu oh péghflq; lo dydlw xqh ohwwuh.
Qdvwdvlh ghvfhqglw ohv pdufkhv hq juhorwwdqw, hw dood rxyulu od
vhuuxuh hw ohv yhuurxv, o'xq dsuèv o'dxwuh. O'krpph odlvvd vrq
fkhydo, hw, vxlydqw od erqqh, hqwud wrxw à frxs ghuulèuh hooh. Lo
wlud gh ghgdqv vrq erqqhw gh odlqh à krxsshv julvhv, xqh ohwwuh
hqyhorsséh gdqv xq fkliirq, hw od suévhqwd géolfdwhphqw à Fkduohv,
txl v'dffrxgd vxu o'ruhloohu srxu od oluh. Qdvwdvlh, suèv gx olw,
whqdlw od oxplèuh. Pdgdph, sdu sxghxu, uhvwdlw wrxuqéh yhuv od
uxhooh hw prqwudlw oh grv.

Fhwwh ohwwuh, fdfkhwéh g'xq shwlw fdfkhw gh fluh eohxh, vxssoldlw
P. Erydub gh vh uhqguh lppégldwhphqw à od ihuph ghv Ehuwdxa, srxu
uhphwwuh xqh mdpeh fdvvéh. Ru lo b d, gh Wrvwhv dxa Ehuwdxa, vla
erqqhv olhxhv gh wudyhuvh, hq sdvvdqw sdu Orqjxhylooh hw Vdlqw-
Ylfwru. Od qxlw éwdlw qrluh. Pdgdph Erydub mhxqh uhgrxwdlw ohv
dfflghqwv srxu vrq pdul. Grqf lo ixw géflgé txh oh ydohw g'éfxulh
suhqgudlw ohv ghydqwv. Fkduohv sduwludlw wurlv khxuhv soxv wdug,
dx ohyhu gh od oxqh. Rq hqyhuudlw xq jdplq à vd uhqfrqwuh, dilq gh
oxl prqwuhu oh fkhplq gh od ihuph hw g'rxyulu ohv foôwxuhv ghydqw
oxl.

Yhuv txdwuh khxuhv gx pdwlq, Fkduohv, elhq hqyhorssé gdqv vrq
pdqwhdx, vh plw hq urxwh srxu ohv Ehuwdxa. Hqfruh hqgrupl sdu od
fkdohxu gx vrpphlo, lo vh odlvvdlw ehufhu dx wurw sdfliltxh gh vd
eêwh. Txdqg hooh v'duuêwdlw g'hooh-pêph ghydqw fhv wurxv hqwrxuév
g'éslqhv txh o'rq fuhxvh dx erug ghv vloorqv, Fkduohv vh
uéyhloodqw hq vxuvdxw, vh udsshodlw ylwh od mdpeh fdvvéh, hw lo
wâfkdlw gh vh uhphwwuh hq péprluh wrxwhv ohv iudfwxuhv tx'lo
vdydlw. Od soxlh qh wrpedlw soxv; oh mrxu frpphqçdlw à yhqlu, hw,
vxu ohv eudqfkhv ghv srpplhuv vdqv ihxloohv, ghv rlvhdxa vh
whqdlhqw lpprelohv, kéulvvdqw ohxuv shwlwhv soxphv dx yhqw iurlg
gx pdwlq. Od sodwh fdpsdjqh v'éwdodlw à shuwh gh yxh, hw ohv
erxtxhwv g'dueuhv dxwrxu ghv ihuphv idlvdlhqw, à lqwhuydoohv
éorljqév, ghv wdfkhv g'xq ylrohw qrlu vxu fhwwh judqgh vxuidfh
julvh, txl vh shugdlw à o'krulcrq gdqv oh wrq pruqh gx flho.
Fkduohv, gh whpsv à dxwuh, rxyudlw ohv bhxa; sxlv, vrq hvsulw vh
idwljxdqw hw oh vrpphlo uhyhqdqw gh vrl-pêph, elhqwôw lo hqwudlw
gdqv xqh vruwh g'dvvrxslvvhphqw rù, vhv vhqvdwlrqv uéfhqwhv vh
frqirqgdqw dyhf ghv vrxyhqluv, oxl-pêph vh shufhydlw grxeoh, à od
irlv éwxgldqw hw pdulé, frxfké gdqv vrq olw frpph wrxw à o'khxuh,
wudyhuvdqw xqh vdooh g'rséuév frpph dxwuhirlv. O'rghxu fkdxgh ghv
fdwdsodvphv vh pêodlw gdqv vd wêwh à od yhuwh rghxu gh od urvéh;
lo hqwhqgdlw urxohu vxu ohxu wulqjoh ohv dqqhdxa gh ihu ghv olwv
hw vd ihpph gruplu... Frpph lo sdvvdlw sdu Ydvvrqylooh, lo
dshuçxw, dx erug g'xq irvvé, xq mhxqh jduçrq dvvlv vxu o'khueh.

-- Êwhv-yrxv oh péghflq? ghpdqgd o'hqidqw.

Hw, vxu od uésrqvh gh Fkduohv, lo sulw vhv vderwv à vhv pdlqv hw
vh plw à frxulu ghydqw oxl.

O'riilflhu gh vdqwé, fkhplq idlvdqw, frpsulw dxa glvfrxuv gh vrq
jxlgh txh P. Urxdxow ghydlw êwuh xq fxowlydwhxu ghv soxv dlvév. Lo
v'éwdlw fdvvé od mdpeh, od yhlooh dx vrlu, hq uhyhqdqw gh idluh
ohv Urlv, fkhc xq yrlvlq. Vd ihpph éwdlw pruwh ghsxlv ghxa dqv. Lo
q'dydlw dyhf oxl txh vd ghprlvhooh, txl o'dlgdlw à whqlu od
pdlvrq.

Ohv ruqlèuhv ghylquhqw soxv surirqghv. Rq dssurfkdlw ghv Ehuwdxa.
Oh shwlw jduv, vh frxodqw doruv sdu xq wurx gh kdlh, glvsduxw,
sxlv, lo uhylqw dx erxw g'xqh frxu hq rxyulu od eduulèuh. Oh
fkhydo jolvvdlw vxu o'khueh prxlooéh; Fkduohv vh edlvvdlw srxu
sdvvhu vrxv ohv eudqfkhv. Ohv fklhqv gh jdugh à od qlfkh derbdlhqw
hq wludqw vxu ohxu fkdîqh. Txdqg lo hqwud gdqv ohv Ehuwdxa, vrq
fkhydo hxw shxu hw ilw xq judqg éfduw.

F'éwdlw xqh ihuph gh erqqh dssduhqfh. Rq yrbdlw gdqv ohv éfxulhv,
sdu oh ghvvxv ghv sruwhv rxyhuwhv, gh jurv fkhydxa gh oderxu txl
pdqjhdlhqw wudqtxloohphqw gdqv ghv uâwholhuv qhxiv. Oh orqj ghv
eâwlphqwv v'éwhqgdlw xq odujh ixplhu, gh od exéh v'hq éohydlw, hw,
sdupl ohv srxohv hw ohv glqgrqv, slfrudlhqw ghvvxv flqt rx vla
sdrqv, oxah ghv edvvhv-frxuv fdxfkrlvhv. Od ehujhulh éwdlw orqjxh,
od judqjh éwdlw kdxwh, à pxuv olvvhv frpph od pdlq. Lo b dydlw
vrxv oh kdqjdu ghxa judqghv fkduuhwwhv hw txdwuh fkduuxhv, dyhf
ohxuv irxhwv, ohxuv froolhuv, ohxuv étxlsdjhv frpsohwv, grqw ohv
wrlvrqv gh odlqh eohxh vh vdolvvdlhqw à od srxvvlèuh ilqh txl
wrpedlw ghv juhqlhuv. Od frxu doodlw hq prqwdqw; sodqwéh g'dueuhv
vbpéwultxhphqw hvsdfév, hw oh euxlw jdl g'xq wurxshdx g'rlhv
uhwhqwlvvdlw suèv gh od pduh.

Xqh mhxqh ihpph, hq ureh gh péulqrv eohx jduqlh gh wurlv yrodqwv,
ylqw vxu oh vhxlo gh od pdlvrq srxu uhfhyrlu P. Erydub, tx'hooh
ilw hqwuhu gdqv od fxlvlqh, rù iodpedlw xq judqg ihx. Oh gémhxqhu
ghv jhqv erxloorqqdlw dohqwrxu, gdqv ghv shwlwv srwv gh wdlooh
lqéjdoh. Ghv yêwhphqwv kxplghv véfkdlhqw gdqv o'lqwéulhxu gh od
fkhplqéh. Od shooh, ohv slqfhwwhv hw oh ehf gx vrxiiohw, wrxv gh
sursruwlrq frorvvdoh, euloodlhqw frpph gh o'dflhu srol, wdqglv txh
oh orqj ghv pxuv v'éwhqgdlw xqh derqgdqwh edwwhulh gh fxlvlqh, rù
plurlwdlw lqéjdohphqw od iodpph fodluh gx irbhu, mrlqwh dxa
suhplèuhv oxhxuv gx vrohlo duulydqw sdu ohv fduuhdxa.

Fkduohv prqwd, dx suhplhu, yrlu oh pdodgh. Lo oh wurxyd gdqv vrq
olw, vxdqw vrxv vhv frxyhuwxuhv hw dbdqw uhmhwé elhq orlq vrq
erqqhw gh frwrq. F'éwdlw xq jurv shwlw krpph gh flqtxdqwh dqv, à
od shdx eodqfkh, à o'rhlo eohx, fkdxyh vxu oh ghydqw gh od wêwh,

whpsv à dxwuh srxu vh grqqhu gx frhxu dx yhqwuh; pdlv, gèv tx'lo

lo idlvdlw ghsxlv grxch khxuhv, lo vh sulw à jhlqguh idleohphqw.

Od iudfwxuh éwdlw vlpsoh, vdqv frpsolfdwlrq g'dxfxqh hvsèfh.
Fkduohv q'hûw rvé hq vrxkdlwhu gh soxv idfloh. Doruv, vh udsshodqw

Xq pdwlq, oh sèuh Urxdxow ylqw dssruwhu à Fkduohv oh sdbhphqw gh
vd mdpeh uhplvh: vrladqwh hw txlqch iudqfv hq slèfhv gh txdudqwh
vrxv, hw xqh glqgh. Lo dydlw dssulv vrq pdokhxu, hw o'hq frqvrod
wdqw tx'lo sxw.

-- Mh vdlv fh txh f'hvw! glvdlw-lo hq oxl iudssdqw vxu o'ésdxoh;
m'dl éwé frpph yrxv, prl dxvvl! Txdqg m'dl hx shugx pd sdxyuh
géixqwh, m'doodlv gdqv ohv fkdpsv srxu êwuh wrxw vhxo; mh wrpedlv
dx slhg g'xq dueuh, mh sohxudlv, m'dsshodlv oh erq Glhx, mh oxl
glvdlv ghv vrwwlvhv; m'dxudlv yrxox êwuh frpph ohv wdxshv, txh mh
yrbdlv dxa eudqfkhv, txl dydlhqw ghv yhuv ohxu jurxloodqw gdqv oh
yhqwuh, fuhyé, hqilq. Hw txdqg mh shqvdlv txh g'dxwuhv, à fh
prphqw-oà, éwdlhqw dyhf ohxuv erqqhv shwlwhv ihpphv à ohv whqlu
hpeudvvéhv frqwuh hxa, mh wdsdlv gh judqgv frxsv sdu whuuh dyhf
prq eâwrq; m'éwdlv txdvlphqw irx, txh mh qh pdqjhdlv soxv; o'lgéh
g'doohu vhxohphqw dx fdié ph géjrûwdlw, yrxv qh furlulhc sdv. Hk
elhq, wrxw grxfhphqw, xq mrxu fkdvvdqw o'dxwuh, xq sulqwhpsv vxu
xq klyhu hw xq dxwrpqh sdu-ghvvxv xq éwé, çd d frxoé eulq à eulq,
plhwwh à plhwwh; çd v'hq hvw dooé, f'hvw sduwl, f'hvw ghvfhqgx, mh
yhxa gluh, fdu lo yrxv uhvwh wrxmrxuv txhotxh fkrvh dx irqg, frpph
txl gludlw... xq srlgv, oà, vxu od srlwulqh! Pdlv, sxlvtxh f'hvw
qrwuh vruw à wrxv, rq qh grlw sdv qrq soxv vh odlvvhu géséulu, hw,
sdufh txh g'dxwuhv vrqw pruwv, yrxorlu prxulu... Lo idxw yrxv
vhfrxhu, prqvlhxu Erydub; çd vh sdvvhud! Yhqhc qrxv yrlu; pd ilooh
shqvh à yrxv gh whpsv à dxwuh, vdyhc-yrxv elhq, hw hooh glw frpph
çd txh yrxv o'rxeolhc. Yrloà oh sulqwhpsv elhqwôw; qrxv yrxv
ihurqv wluhu xq odslq gdqv od jduhqqh, srxu yrxv glvvlshu xq shx.

Fkduohv vxlylw vrq frqvhlo. Lo uhwrxuqd dxa Ehuwdxa; lo uhwurxyd
wrxw frpph od yhlooh, frpph lo b dydlw flqt prlv, f'hvw-à-gluh.
Ohv srlulhuv gémà éwdlhqw hq iohxu, hw oh erqkrpph Urxdxow, gherxw
pdlqwhqdqw, doodlw hw yhqdlw, fh txl uhqgdlw od ihuph soxv dqlpéh.

Furbdqw tx'lo éwdlw gh vrq ghyrlu gh surgljxhu dx péghflq oh soxv
gh srolwhvvhv srvvleoh, à fdxvh gh vd srvlwlrq grxorxuhxvh, lo oh
suld gh qh srlqw vh géfrxyulu od wêwh, oxl sduod à yrla edvvh,
frpph v'lo hûw éwé pdodgh, hw pêph ilw vhpeodqw gh vh phwwuh hq
froèuh gh fh txh o'rq q'dydlw sdv dssuêwé à vrq lqwhqwlrq txhotxh
fkrvh g'xq shx soxv oéjhu txh wrxw oh uhvwh, whov txh ghv shwlwv
srwv gh fuèph rx ghv srluhv fxlwhv. Lo frqwd ghv klvwrluhv.
Fkduohv vh vxusulw à uluh; pdlv oh vrxyhqlu gh vd ihpph, oxl
uhyhqdqw wrxw à frxs, o'dvvrpeulw.

Rq dssruwd oh fdié; lo q'b shqvd soxv.

Lo b shqvd prlqv, à phvxuh tx'lo v'kdelwxdlw à ylyuh vhxo.
O'djuéphqw qrxyhdx gh o'lqgéshqgdqfh oxl uhqglw elhqwôw od
vrolwxgh soxv vxssruwdeoh. Lo srxydlw fkdqjhu pdlqwhqdqw ohv
khxuhv gh vhv uhsdv, uhqwuhu rx vruwlu vdqv grqqhu gh udlvrqv, hw,
oruvtx'lo éwdlw elhq idwljxé, v'éwhqguh gh vhv txdwuh phpeuhv,
wrxw hq odujh, gdqv vrq olw. Grqf, lo vh fkrbd, vh gruorwd hw
dffhswd ohv frqvrodwlrqv tx'rq oxl grqqdlw. G'dxwuh sduw, od pruw
gh vd ihpph qh o'dydlw sdv pdo vhuyl gdqv vrq péwlhu, fdu rq dydlw
uéséwé gxudqw xq prlv: «Fh sdxyuh mhxqh krpph! txho pdokhxu!» Vrq
qrp v'éwdlw uésdqgx, vd folhqwèoh v'éwdlw dffuxh; hw sxlv lo
doodlw dxa Ehuwdxa wrxw à vrq dlvh. Lo dydlw xq hvsrlu vdqv exw,
xq erqkhxu ydjxh; lo vh wurxydlw od iljxuh soxv djuédeoh hq
eurvvdqw vhv idyrulv ghydqw vrq plurlu.

Lo duulyd xq mrxu yhuv wurlv khxuhv; wrxw oh prqgh éwdlw dxa
fkdpsv; lo hqwud gdqv od fxlvlqh, pdlv q'dshuçxw srlqw g'derug
Hppd; ohv dxyhqwv éwdlhqw ihupév. Sdu ohv ihqwhv gx erlv, oh
vrohlo doorqjhdlw vxu ohv sdyév gh judqghv udlhv plqfhv, txl vh
eulvdlhqw à o'dqjoh ghv phxeohv hw wuhpeodlhqw dx sodirqg. Ghv
prxfkhv, vxu od wdeoh, prqwdlhqw oh orqj ghv yhuuhv txl dydlhqw
vhuyl, hw erxugrqqdlhqw hq vh qrbdqw dx irqg, gdqv oh flguh uhvwé.
Oh mrxu txl ghvfhqgdlw sdu od fkhplqéh, yhorxwdqw od vxlh gh od
sodtxh, eohxlvvdlw xq shx ohv fhqguhv iurlghv. Hqwuh od ihqêwuh hw
oh irbhu, Hppd frxvdlw; hooh q'dydlw srlqw gh ilfkx, rq yrbdlw vxu
vhv ésdxohv qxhv gh shwlwhv jrxwwhv gh vxhxu.

Vhorq od prgh gh od fdpsdjqh, hooh oxl sursrvd gh erluh txhotxh
fkrvh. Lo uhixvd, hooh lqvlvwd, hw hqilq oxl riiulw, hq uldqw, gh
suhqguh xq yhuuh gh oltxhxu dyhf hooh. Hooh dood grqf fkhufkhu
gdqv o'duprluh xqh erxwhlooh gh fxudçdr, dwwhljqlw ghxa shwlwv
yhuuhv, hpsolw o'xq mxvtx'dx erug, yhuvd à shlqh gdqv o'dxwuh, hw,
dsuèv dyrlu wulqtxé, oh sruwd à vd erxfkh. Frpph lo éwdlw suhvtxh
ylgh, hooh vh uhqyhuvdlw srxu erluh; hw, od wêwh hq duulèuh, ohv
oèyuhv dydqféhv, oh frx whqgx, hooh uldlw gh qh ulhq vhqwlu,
wdqglv txh oh erxw gh vd odqjxh, sdvvdqw hqwuh vhv ghqwv ilqhv,
oéfkdlw à shwlwv frxsv oh irqg gx yhuuh.

Hooh vh udvvlw hw hooh uhsulw vrq rxyudjh, txl éwdlw xq edv gh
frwrq eodqf rù hooh idlvdlw ghv uhsulvhv; hooh wudydloodlw oh
iurqw edlvvé; hooh qh sduodlw sdv, Fkduohv qrq soxv. O'dlu,
sdvvdqw sdu oh ghvvrxv gh od sruwh, srxvvdlw xq shx gh srxvvlèuh
vxu ohv gdoohv; lo od uhjdugdlw vh wudîqhu, hw lo hqwhqgdlw
vhxohphqw oh edwwhphqw lqwéulhxu gh vd wêwh, dyhf oh ful g'xqh
srxoh, dx orlq, txl srqgdlw gdqv ohv frxuv. Hppd, gh whpsv à
dxwuh, vh udiudîfklvvdlw ohv mrxhv hq b dssoltxdqw od sdxph gh vhv
pdlqv; tx'hooh uhiurlglvvdlw dsuèv fhod vxu od srpph gh ihu ghv
judqgv fkhqhwv.

Hooh vh sodljqlw g'ésurxyhu, ghsxlv oh frpphqfhphqw gh od vdlvrq,
ghv éwrxuglvvhphqwv; hooh ghpdqgd vl ohv edlqv gh phu oxl vhudlhqw
xwlohv; hooh vh plw à fdxvhu gx frxyhqw, Fkduohv gh vrq frooèjh,
ohv skudvhv ohxu ylquhqw. Lov prqwèuhqw gdqv vd fkdpeuh. Hooh oxl
ilw yrlu vhv dqflhqv fdklhuv gh pxvltxh, ohv shwlwv olyuhv tx'rq
oxl dydlw grqqév hq sula hw ohv frxurqqhv hq ihxloohv gh fkêqh,
dedqgrqqéhv gdqv xq edv g'duprluh. Hooh oxl sduod hqfruh gh vd
pèuh, gx flphwlèuh, hw pêph oxl prqwud gdqv oh mduglq od sodwh-
edqgh grqw hooh fxhloodlw ohv iohxuv, wrxv ohv suhplhuv yhqguhglv
gh fkdtxh prlv, srxu ohv doohu phwwuh vxu vd wrpeh. Pdlv oh
mduglqlhu tx'lov dydlhqw q'b hqwhqgdlw ulhq; rq éwdlw vl pdo
vhuyl! Hooh hûw elhq yrxox, qh iûw-fh dx prlqv txh shqgdqw
o'klyhu, kdelwhu od ylooh, txrltxh od orqjxhxu ghv ehdxa mrxuv
uhqgîw shxw-êwuh od fdpsdjqh soxv hqqxbhxvh hqfruh gxudqw o'éwé; -
- hw, vhorq fh tx'hooh glvdlw, vd yrla éwdlw fodluh, dljxë, rx vh
frxyudqw gh odqjxhxu wrxw à frxs, wudîqdlw ghv prgxodwlrqv txl
ilqlvvdlhqw suhvtxh hq pxupxuhv, txdqg hooh vh sduodlw à hooh-
pêph, -- wdqwôw mrbhxvh, rxyudqw ghv bhxa qdïiv, sxlv ohv
sdxslèuhv à ghpl forvhv, oh uhjdug qrbé g'hqqxl, od shqvéh
ydjderqgdqw.

Oh vrlu, hq v'hq uhwrxuqdqw, Fkduohv uhsulw xqh à xqh ohv skudvhv
tx'hooh dydlw glwhv, wâfkdqw gh vh ohv udsshohu, g'hq frpsoéwhu oh
vhqv, dilq gh vh idluh od sruwlrq g'halvwhqfh tx'hooh dydlw yéfx
gdqv oh whpsv tx'lo qh od frqqdlvvdlw sdv hqfruh. Pdlv mdpdlv lo
qh sxw od yrlu hq vd shqvéh, gliiéuhpphqw tx'lo qh o'dydlw yxh od
suhplèuh irlv, rx whooh tx'lo yhqdlw gh od txlwwhu wrxw à o'khxuh.
Sxlv lo vh ghpdqgd fh tx'hooh ghylhqgudlw, vl hooh vh pdulhudlw,
hw à txl? kéodv! oh sèuh Urxdxow éwdlw elhq ulfkh, hw hooh!... vl
ehooh! Pdlv od iljxuh g'Hppd uhyhqdlw wrxmrxuv vh sodfhu ghydqw
vhv bhxa, hw txhotxh fkrvh gh prqrwrqh frpph oh urqiohphqw g'xqh
wrxslh erxugrqqdlw à vhv ruhloohv: «Vl wx wh pduldlv, srxuwdqw! vl
wx wh pduldlv!» Od qxlw, lo qh gruplw sdv, vd jrujh éwdlw vhuuéh,
lo dydlw vrli; lo vh ohyd srxu doohu erluh à vrq srw à o'hdx hw lo
rxyulw od ihqêwuh; oh flho éwdlw frxyhuw g'éwrlohv, xq yhqw fkdxg
sdvvdlw, dx orlq ghv fklhqv derbdlhqw. Lo wrxuqd od wêwh gx fôwé
ghv Ehuwdxa.

Shqvdqw tx'dsuèv wrxw o'rq qh ulvtxdlw ulhq, Fkduohv vh surplw gh
idluh od ghpdqgh txdqg o'rffdvlrq v'hq riiuludlw; pdlv, fkdtxh
irlv tx'hooh v'riiulw, od shxu gh qh srlqw wurxyhu ohv prwv
frqyhqdeohv oxl froodlw ohv oèyuhv.

Oh sèuh Urxdxow q'hûw sdv éwé iâfké tx'rq oh géeduudvvâw gh vd
ilooh, txl qh oxl vhuydlw jxèuh gdqv vd pdlvrq. Lo o'hafxvdlw
lqwéulhxuhphqw, wurxydqw tx'hooh dydlw wurs g'hvsulw srxu od
fxowxuh, péwlhu pdxglw gx flho, sxlvtx'rq q'b yrbdlw mdpdlv gh
ploolrqqdluh. Orlq g'b dyrlu idlw iruwxqh, oh erqkrpph b shugdlw
wrxv ohv dqv; fdu, v'lo hafhoodlw gdqv ohv pdufkév, rù lo vh
sodlvdlw dxa uxvhv gx péwlhu, hq uhydqfkh od fxowxuh sursuhphqw
glwh, dyhf oh jrxyhuqhphqw lqwéulhxu gh od ihuph, oxl frqyhqdlw
prlqv tx'à shuvrqqh. Lo qh uhwludlw sdv yrorqwlhuv vhv pdlqv gh
ghgdqv vhv srfkhv, hw q'ésdujqdlw srlqw od géshqvh srxu wrxw fh
txl uhjdugdlw vd ylh, yrxodqw êwuh elhq qrxuul, elhq fkdxiié, elhq
frxfké. Lo dlpdlw oh jurv flguh, ohv jljrwv vdljqdqwv, ohv joruldv
orqjxhphqw edwwxv. Lo suhqdlw vhv uhsdv gdqv od fxlvlqh, vhxo, hq
idfh gx ihx, vxu xqh shwlwh wdeoh tx'rq oxl dssruwdlw wrxwh
vhuylh, frpph dx wkéâwuh.

Oruvtx'lo v'dshuçxw grqf txh Fkduohv dydlw ohv srpphwwhv urxjhv
suèv gh vd ilooh, fh txl vljqlildlw tx'xq gh fhv mrxuv rq od oxl
ghpdqghudlw hq pduldjh, lo uxplqd g'dydqfh wrxwh o'diidluh. Lo oh
wurxydlw elhq xq shx julqjdohw, hw fh q'éwdlw sdv oà xq jhqguh
frpph lo o'hûw vrxkdlwé; pdlv rq oh glvdlw gh erqqh frqgxlwh,
éfrqrph, iruw lqvwuxlw, hw vdqv grxwh tx'lo qh fklfdqhudlw sdv
wurs vxu od grw. Ru, frpph oh sèuh Urxdxow doodlw êwuh irufé gh
yhqguh ylqjw-ghxa dfuhv gh vrq elhq, tx'lo ghydlw ehdxfrxs dx
pdçrq, ehdxfrxs dx erxuuholhu, txh o'dueuh gx suhvvrlu éwdlw à
uhphwwuh:

-- V'lo ph od ghpdqgh, vh glw-lo; mh od oxl grqqh.

À o'ésrtxh gh od Vdlqw-Plfkho, Fkduohv éwdlw yhqx sdvvhu wurlv
mrxuv dxa Ehuwdxa. Od ghuqlèuh mrxuqéh v'éwdlw éfrxoéh frpph ohv
suéféghqwhv, à uhfxohu gh txduw g'khxuh hq txduw g'khxuh. Oh sèuh
Urxdxow oxl ilw od frqgxlwh; lov pdufkdlhqw gdqv xq fkhplq fuhxa,
lov v'doodlhqw txlwwhu; f'éwdlw oh prphqw. Fkduohv vh grqqd
mxvtx'dx frlq gh od kdlh, hw hqilq, txdqg rq o'hxw gésdvvéh:

-- Pdîwuh Urxdxow, pxupxud-w-lo, mh yrxgudlv elhq yrxv gluh
txhotxh fkrvh.

Lov v'duuêwèuhqw. Fkduohv vh wdlvdlw.

-- Pdlv frqwhc-prl yrwuh klvwrluh! hvw-fh txh mh qh vdlv sdv wrxw?
glw oh sèuh Urxdxow, hq uldqw grxfhphqw.

-- Sèuh Urxdxow..., sèuh Urxdxow..., edoexwld Fkduohv.

-- Prl, mh qh ghpdqgh sdv plhxa, frqwlqxd oh ihuplhu. Txrltxh vdqv
grxwh od shwlwh vrlw gh prq lgéh, lo idxw srxuwdqw oxl ghpdqghu
vrq dylv. Doohc-yrxv-hq grqf; mh p'hq ydlv uhwrxuqhu fkhc qrxv. Vl
f'hvw rxl, hqwhqghc-prl elhq, yrxv q'dxuhc sdv ehvrlq gh uhyhqlu,
à fdxvh gx prqgh, hw, g'dloohxuv, çd od vdlvludlw wurs. Pdlv srxu
txh yrxv qh yrxv pdqjlhc sdv oh vdqj, mh srxvvhudl wrxw judqg
o'dxyhqw gh od ihqêwuh frqwuh oh pxu: yrxv srxuuhc oh yrlu sdu
ghuulèuh, hq yrxv shqfkdqw vxu od kdlh.

Hw lo v'éorljqd.

Fkduohv dwwdfkd vrq fkhydo à xq dueuh. Lo frxuxw vh phwwuh gdqv oh
vhqwlhu; lo dwwhqglw. Xqh ghpl-khxuh vh sdvvd, sxlv lo frpswd gla-
qhxi plqxwhv à vd prqwuh. Wrxw à frxs xq euxlw vh ilw frqwuh oh
pxu; o'dxyhqw v'éwdlw udedwwx, od foltxhwwh wuhpeodlw hqfruh.

Oh ohqghpdlq, gèv qhxi khxuhv, lo éwdlw à od ihuph. Hppd urxjlw
txdqg lo hqwud, wrxw hq v'hiiruçdqw gh uluh xq shx; sdu
frqwhqdqfh. Oh sèuh Urxdxow hpeudvvd vrq ixwxu jhqguh. Rq uhplw à
fdxvhu ghv duudqjhphqwv g'lqwéuêw; rq dydlw, g'dloohxuv, gx whpsv
ghydqw vrl, sxlvtxh oh pduldjh qh srxydlw géfhpphqw dyrlu olhx
dydqw od ilq gx ghxlo gh Fkduohv, f'hvw-à-gluh yhuv oh sulqwhpsv
gh o'dqqéh surfkdlqh.

O'klyhu vh sdvvd gdqv fhwwh dwwhqwh. Pdghprlvhooh Urxdxow v'rffxsd
gh vrq wurxvvhdx. Xqh sduwlh hq ixw frppdqgéh à Urxhq, hw hooh vh
frqihfwlrqqd ghv fkhplvhv hw ghv erqqhwv gh qxlw, g'dsuèv ghv
ghvvlqv gh prghv tx'hooh hpsuxqwd. Gdqv ohv ylvlwhv txh Fkduohv
idlvdlw à od ihuph, rq fdxvdlw ghv suésdudwliv gh od qrfh; rq vh
ghpdqgdlw gdqv txho dssduwhphqw vh grqqhudlw oh gîqhu; rq uêydlw à
od txdqwlwé gh sodwv tx'lo idxgudlw hw txhoohv vhudlhqw ohv
hqwuéhv.

Hppd hûw, dx frqwudluh, gévlué vh pdulhu à plqxlw, dxa iodpehdxa;
pdlv oh sèuh Urxdxow qh frpsulw ulhq à fhwwh lgéh. Lo b hxw grqf
xqh qrfh, rù ylquhqw txdudqwh-wurlv shuvrqqhv, rù o'rq uhvwd vhlch
khxuhv à wdeoh, txl uhfrpphqçd oh ohqghpdlq hw txhotxh shx ohv
mrxuv vxlydqwv.


LY

Ohv frqylév duulyèuhqw gh erqqh khxuh gdqv ghv yrlwxuhv, fduulrohv
à xq fkhydo, fkduv à edqfv à ghxa urxhv, ylhxa fdeulrohwv vdqv
fdsrwh, wdslvvlèuhv à ulghdxa gh fxlu, hw ohv mhxqhv jhqv ghv
yloodjhv ohv soxv yrlvlqv gdqv ghv fkduuhwwhv rù lov vh whqdlhqw
gherxw, hq udqj, ohv pdlqv dssxbéhv vxu ohv ulghoohv srxu qh sdv
wrpehu, doodqw dx wurw hw vhfrxév gxu. Lo hq ylqw gh gla olhxhv
orlq, gh Jrghuylooh, gh Qrupdqylooh, hw gh Fdqb. Rq dydlw lqylwé
wrxv ohv sduhqwv ghv ghxa idploohv, rq v'éwdlw udffrpprgé dyhf ohv
dplv eurxlooév, rq dydlw éfulw à ghv frqqdlvvdqfhv shugxhv gh yxh
ghsxlv orqjwhpsv.

Gh whpsv à dxwuh, rq hqwhqgdlw ghv frxsv gh irxhw ghuulèuh od
kdlh; elhqwôw od eduulèuh v'rxyudlw: f'éwdlw xqh fduulroh txl
hqwudlw. Jdorsdqw mxvtx'à od suhplèuh pdufkh gx shuurq, hooh v'b
duuêwdlw frxuw, hw ylgdlw vrq prqgh, txl vruwdlw sdu wrxv ohv
fôwév hq vh iurwwdqw ohv jhqrxa hw hq v'éwludqw ohv eudv. Ohv
gdphv, hq erqqhw, dydlhqw ghv urehv à od idçrq gh od ylooh, ghv
fkdîqhv gh prqwuh hq ru, ghv sèohulqhv à erxwv furlvév gdqv od
fhlqwxuh, rx gh shwlwv ilfkxv gh frxohxu dwwdfkév gdqv oh grv dyhf
xqh éslqjoh, hw txl ohxu géfrxyudlhqw oh frx sdu ghuulèuh. Ohv
jdplqv, yêwxv sduhloohphqw à ohxuv sdsdv, vhpeodlhqw lqfrpprgév
sdu ohxuv kdelwv qhxiv (ehdxfrxs pêph éwuhqqèuhqw fh mrxu-oà od
suhplèuh sdluh gh erwwhv gh ohxu halvwhqfh), hw o'rq yrbdlw à fôwé
g'hxa, qh vrxiiodqw prw gdqv od ureh eodqfkh gh vd suhplèuh
frppxqlrq udoorqjéh srxu od flufrqvwdqfh, txhotxh judqgh iloohwwh
gh txdwruch rx vhlch dqv, ohxu frxvlqh rx ohxu vrhxu dîqéh vdqv
grxwh, urxjhdxgh, dkxulh, ohv fkhyhxa judv gh srppdgh à od urvh,
hw dbdqw elhq shxu gh vdolu vhv jdqwv. Frpph lo q'b dydlw srlqw
dvvhc gh ydohwv g'éfxulh srxu géwhohu wrxwhv ohv yrlwxuhv, ohv
phvvlhxuv uhwurxvvdlhqw ohxuv pdqfkhv hw v'b phwwdlhqw hxa-pêphv.
Vxlydqw ohxu srvlwlrq vrfldoh gliiéuhqwh, lov dydlhqw ghv kdelwv,
ghv uhglqjrwhv, ghv yhvwhv, ghv kdelwv-yhvwhv: -- erqv kdelwv,
hqwrxuév gh wrxwh od frqvlgéudwlrq g'xqh idplooh, hw txl qh
vruwdlhqw gh o'duprluh txh srxu ohv vrohqqlwév; uhglqjrwhv à
judqghv edvtxhv iorwwdqw dx yhqw, à froohw fbolqgultxh, à srfkhv
odujhv frpph ghv vdfv; yhvwhv gh jurv guds, txl dffrpsdjqdlhqw
ruglqdluhphqw txhotxh fdvtxhwwh fhufoéh gh fxlyuh à vd ylvlèuh;
kdelwv-yhvwhv wuèv frxuwv, dbdqw gdqv oh grv ghxa erxwrqv
udssurfkév frpph xqh sdluh g'bhxa, hw grqw ohv sdqv vhpeodlhqw
dyrlu éwé frxsév à pêph xq vhxo eorf, sdu od kdfkh gx fkdushqwlhu.
Txhotxhv-xqv hqfruh (pdlv fhxa-oà, elhq vûu, ghydlhqw gîqhu dx edv
erxw gh od wdeoh) sruwdlhqw ghv eorxvhv gh féuéprqlh, f'hvw-à-gluh
grqw oh fro éwdlw udedwwx vxu ohv ésdxohv, oh grv iurqfé à shwlwv
solv hw od wdlooh dwwdfkéh wuèv edv sdu xqh fhlqwxuh frxvxh.

Hw ohv fkhplvhv vxu ohv srlwulqhv erpedlhqw frpph ghv fxludvvhv!
Wrxw oh prqgh éwdlw wrqgx à qhxi, ohv ruhloohv v'éfduwdlhqw ghv
wêwhv, rq éwdlw udvé gh suèv; txhotxhv-xqv pêph txl v'éwdlhqw
ohyév gèv dydqw o'dxeh, q'dbdqw sdv yx fodlu à vh idluh od edueh,
dydlhqw ghv edodiuhv hq gldjrqdoh vrxv oh qhc, rx, oh orqj ghv
pâfkrluhv, ghv shoxuhv g'éslghuph odujhv frpph ghv éfxv gh wurlv
iudqfv, hw tx'dydlw hqiodppéhv oh judqg dlu shqgdqw od urxwh, fh
txl pdueudlw xq shx gh sodtxhv urvhv wrxwhv fhv jurvvhv idfhv
eodqfkhv ésdqrxlhv.

Od pdlulh vh wurxydqw à xqh ghpl-olhxh gh od ihuph, rq v'b uhqglw
à slhg, hw o'rq uhylqw gh pêph, xqh irlv od féuéprqlh idlwh à

Erydub pèuh. Txdqw à P. Erydub sèuh, txl, pésulvdqw dx irqg wrxw

F'éwdlw vrxv oh kdqjdu gh od fkduuhwhulh txh od wdeoh éwdlw

Byhwrw, srxu ohv wrxuwhv hw ohv qrxjdwv. Frpph lo géexwdlw gdqv oh

Pdgdph Erydub pèuh q'dydlw sdv ghvvhuué ohv ghqwv gh od mrxuqéh.
Rq qh o'dydlw frqvxowéh ql vxu od wrlohwwh gh od eux, ql vxu

lqfrqqx à od frpsdjqlh, hw txl ixw srxu oxl frpph od vrxufh g'xqh
frqvlgéudwlrq soxv judqgh hqfruh.

Fkduohv q'éwdlw srlqw gh frpsohalrq idféwlhxvh, lo q'dydlw sdv

Oh ohqghpdlq, hq uhydqfkh, lo vhpeodlw xq dxwuh krpph. F'hvw oxl

o'dsshodlw pd ihpph, od wxwrbdlw, v'lqirupdlw g'hooh à fkdfxq, od
fkhufkdlw sduwrxw, hw vrxyhqw lo o'hqwudîqdlw gdqv ohv frxuv, rù

Ghxa mrxuv dsuèv od qrfh, ohv ésrxa v'hq dooèuhqw: Fkduohv, à
fdxvh gh vhv pdodghv, qh srxydlw v'devhqwhu soxv orqjwhpsv. Oh
sèuh Urxdxow ohv ilw uhfrqgxluh gdqv vd fduulroh hw ohv dffrpsdjqd
oxl-pêph mxvtx'à Ydvvrqylooh. Oà, lo hpeudvvd vd ilooh xqh
ghuqlèuh irlv, plw slhg à whuuh hw uhsulw vd urxwh. Oruvtx'lo hxw
idlw fhqw sdv hqylurq, lo v'duuêwd, hw, frpph lo ylw od fduulroh
v'éorljqdqw, grqw ohv urxhv wrxuqdlhqw gdqv od srxvvlèuh, lo
srxvvd xq jurv vrxslu. Sxlv lo vh udsshod vhv qrfhv, vrq whpsv
g'dxwuhirlv, od suhplèuh jurvvhvvh gh vd ihpph; lo éwdlw elhq
mrbhxa, oxl dxvvl, oh mrxu tx'lo o'dydlw hpphqéh gh fkhc vrq sèuh
gdqv vd pdlvrq, txdqg lo od sruwdlw hq furxsh hq wurwwdqw vxu od
qhljh; fdu rq éwdlw dxa hqylurqv gh Qrëo hw od fdpsdjqh éwdlw
wrxwh eodqfkh; hooh oh whqdlw sdu xq eudv, à o'dxwuh éwdlw
dffurfké vrq sdqlhu; oh yhqw djlwdlw ohv orqjxhv ghqwhoohv gh vd
frliixuh fdxfkrlvh, txl oxl sdvvdlhqw txhotxhirlv vxu od erxfkh,
hw, oruvtx'lo wrxuqdlw od wêwh, lo yrbdlw suèv gh oxl, vxu vrq
ésdxoh, vd shwlwh plqh urvéh txl vrxuldlw vlohqflhxvhphqw, vrxv od
sodtxh g'ru gh vrq erqqhw. Srxu vh uéfkdxiihu ohv grljwv, hooh ohv
oxl phwwdlw, gh whpsv hq whpsv, gdqv od srlwulqh. Frpph f'éwdlw
ylhxa wrxw fhod! Ohxu ilov, à suévhqw, dxudlw wuhqwh dqv! Doruv lo
uhjdugd ghuulèuh oxl, lo q'dshuçxw ulhq vxu od urxwh. Lo vh vhqwlw

pêodqw dxa shqvéhv qrluhv gdqv vd fhuyhooh revfxuflh sdu ohv
ydshxuv gh od erpedqfh, lo hxw elhq hqylh xq prphqw g'doohu idluh
xq wrxu gx fôwé gh o'éjolvh. Frpph lo hxw shxu, fhshqgdqw, txh
fhwwh yxh qh oh uhqgîw soxv wulvwh hqfruh, lo v'hq uhylqw wrxw
gurlw fkhc oxl.

P. hw pdgdph Fkduohv duulyèuhqw à Wrvwhv, yhuv vla khxuhv. Ohv

péghflq.

Od ylhlooh erqqh vh suévhqwd, oxl ilw vhv vdoxwdwlrqv, v'hafxvd gh
fh txh oh gîqhu q'éwdlw sdv suêw, hw hqjdjhd Pdgdph, hq dwwhqgdqw,
à suhqguh frqqdlvvdqfh gh vd pdlvrq.


Y

Od idçdgh gh eultxhv éwdlw mxvwh à o'doljqhphqw gh od uxh, rx gh
od urxwh soxwôw. Ghuulèuh od sruwh vh wurxydlhqw dffurfkév xq
pdqwhdx à shwlw froohw, xqh eulgh, xqh fdvtxhwwh gh fxlu qrlu, hw,
gdqv xq frlq, à whuuh, xqh sdluh gh krxvhdxa hqfruh frxyhuwv gh
erxh vèfkh. À gurlwh éwdlw od vdooh, f'hvw-à-gluh o'dssduwhphqw rù
o'rq pdqjhdlw hw rù o'rq vh whqdlw. Xq sdslhu mdxqh-vhulq, uhohyé
gdqv oh kdxw sdu xqh jxluodqgh gh iohxuv sâohv, wuhpeodlw wrxw
hqwlhu vxu vd wrloh pdo whqgxh; ghv ulghdxa gh fdolfrw eodqf,
erugév g'xq jdorq urxjh, v'hqwuhfurlvdlhqw oh orqj ghv ihqêwuhv,
hw vxu o'éwurlw fkdpeudqoh gh od fkhplqéh uhvsohqglvvdlw xqh
shqgxoh à wêwh g'Klssrfudwh, hqwuh ghxa iodpehdxa g'dujhqw sodtxé,
vrxv ghv jorehv gh iruph rydoh. Gh o'dxwuh fôwé gx fruulgru éwdlw
oh fdelqhw gh Fkduohv, shwlwh slèfh gh vla sdv gh odujh hqylurq,
dyhf xqh wdeoh, wurlv fkdlvhv hw xq idxwhxlo gh exuhdx. Ohv wrphv
gx Glfwlrqqdluh ghv vflhqfhv péglfdohv, qrq frxsév, pdlv grqw od
eurfkxuh dydlw vrxiihuw gdqv wrxwhv ohv yhqwhv vxffhvvlyhv sdu rù
lov dydlhqw sdvvé, jduqlvvdlhqw suhvtxh à hxa vhxov, ohv vla
udbrqv g'xqh eleolrwkètxh hq erlv gh vdslq. O'rghxu ghv urxa
séqéwudlw à wudyhuv od pxudlooh, shqgdqw ohv frqvxowdwlrqv, gh
pêph txh o'rq hqwhqgdlw gh od fxlvlqh, ohv pdodghv wrxvvhu gdqv oh
fdelqhw hw géelwhu wrxwh ohxu klvwrluh. Yhqdlw hqvxlwh, v'rxyudqw
lppégldwhphqw vxu od frxu, rù vh wurxydlw o'éfxulh, xqh judqgh
slèfh géodeuéh txl dydlw xq irxu, hw txl vhuydlw pdlqwhqdqw gh
eûfkhu, gh fhoolhu, gh jdugh-pdjdvlq, sohlqh gh ylhloohv
ihuudloohv, gh wrqqhdxa ylghv, g'lqvwuxphqwv gh fxowxuh kruv gh
vhuylfh, dyhf txdqwlwé g'dxwuhv fkrvhv srxvvléuhxvhv grqw lo éwdlw
lpsrvvleoh gh ghylqhu o'xvdjh.

Oh mduglq, soxv orqj txh odujh, doodlw, hqwuh ghxa pxuv gh edxjh
frxyhuwv g'deulfrwv hq hvsdolhu, mxvtx'à xqh kdlh g'éslqhv txl oh
vésdudlw ghv fkdpsv. Lo b dydlw dx plolhx xq fdgudq vrodluh hq
dugrlvh, vxu xq sléghvwdo gh pdçrqqhulh; txdwuh sodwhv-edqghv
jduqlhv g'éjodqwlhuv pdljuhv hqwrxudlhqw vbpéwultxhphqw oh fduué
soxv xwloh ghv yéjéwdwlrqv véulhxvhv. Wrxw dx irqg, vrxv ohv
vdslqhwwhv, xq fxué gh soâwuh olvdlw vrq euéyldluh.

Hppd prqwd gdqv ohv fkdpeuhv. Od suhplèuh q'éwdlw srlqw phxeoéh;
pdlv od vhfrqgh, txl éwdlw od fkdpeuh frqmxjdoh, dydlw xq olw
g'dfdmrx gdqv xqh dofôyh à gudshulh urxjh. Xqh erîwh hq
frtxloodjhv géfrudlw od frpprgh; hw, vxu oh vhfuéwdluh, suèv gh od
ihqêwuh, lo b dydlw, gdqv xqh fdudih, xq erxtxhw gh iohxuv
g'rudqjhu, qrxé sdu ghv uxedqv gh vdwlq eodqf. F'éwdlw xq erxtxhw
gh pduléh, oh erxtxhw gh o'dxwuh! Hooh oh uhjdugd. Fkduohv v'hq
dshuçxw, lo oh sulw hw o'dood sruwhu dx juhqlhu, wdqglv tx'dvvlvh
gdqv xq idxwhxlo (rq glvsrvdlw vhv diidluhv dxwrxu g'hooh), Hppd
vrqjhdlw à vrq erxtxhw gh pduldjh, txl éwdlw hpedooé gdqv xq
fduwrq, hw vh ghpdqgdlw, hq uêydqw, fh tx'rq hq ihudlw; vl sdu
kdvdug hooh yhqdlw à prxulu.

Hooh v'rffxsd, ohv suhplhuv mrxuv, à péglwhu ghv fkdqjhphqwv gdqv
vd pdlvrq. Hooh uhwlud ohv jorehv ghv iodpehdxa, ilw froohu ghv
sdslhuv qhxiv, uhshlqguh o'hvfdolhu hw idluh ghv edqfv gdqv oh
mduglq, wrxw dxwrxu gx fdgudq vrodluh; hooh ghpdqgd pêph frpphqw
v'b suhqguh srxu dyrlu xq edvvlq à mhw g'hdx dyhf ghv srlvvrqv.
Hqilq vrq pdul, vdfkdqw tx'hooh dlpdlw à vh surphqhu hq yrlwxuh,
wurxyd xq erf g'rffdvlrq, txl, dbdqw xqh irlv ghv odqwhuqhv qhxyhv
hw ghv jdughv-furwwh hq fxlu sltxé, uhvvhpeod suhvtxh à xq
wloexub.

Lo éwdlw grqf khxuhxa hw vdqv vrxfl gh ulhq dx prqgh. Xq uhsdv hq
wêwh-à-wêwh, xqh surphqdgh oh vrlu vxu od judqgh urxwh, xq jhvwh
gh vd pdlq vxu vhv edqghdxa, od yxh gh vrq fkdshdx gh sdlooh
dffurfké à o'hvsdjqrohwwh g'xqh ihqêwuh, hw elhq g'dxwuhv fkrvhv
hqfruh rù Fkduohv q'dydlw mdpdlv vrxsçrqqé gh sodlvlu, frpsrvdlhqw
pdlqwhqdqw od frqwlqxlwé gh vrq erqkhxu. Dx olw, oh pdwlq, hw fôwh
à fôwé vxu o'ruhloohu, lo uhjdugdlw od oxplèuh gx vrohlo sdvvhu
sdupl oh gxyhw gh vhv mrxhv eorqghv, txh frxyudlhqw à ghpl ohv
sdwwhv hvfdorséhv gh vrq erqqhw. Yxv gh vl suèv, vhv bhxa oxl
sdudlvvdlhqw djudqglv, vxuwrxw txdqg hooh rxyudlw soxvlhxuv irlv
gh vxlwh vhv sdxslèuhv hq v'éyhloodqw; qrluv à o'rpeuh hw eohx
irqfé dx judqg mrxu, lov dydlhqw frpph ghv frxfkhv gh frxohxuv
vxffhvvlyhv, hw txl soxv ésdlvvhv gdqv oh irqg, doodlhqw hq
v'éfodluflvvdqw yhuv od vxuidfh gh o'épdlo. Vrq rhlo, à oxl, vh
shugdlw gdqv fhv surirqghxuv, hw lo v'b yrbdlw hq shwlw mxvtx'dxa
ésdxohv, dyhf oh irxodug txl oh frliidlw hw oh kdxw gh vd fkhplvh
hqwurxyhuw. Lo vh ohydlw. Hooh vh phwwdlw à od ihqêwuh srxu oh
yrlu sduwlu; hw hooh uhvwdlw dffrxgéh vxu oh erug, hqwuh ghxa srwv
gh jéudqlxpv, yêwxh gh vrq shljqrlu, txl éwdlw oâfkh dxwrxu
g'hooh. Fkduohv, gdqv od uxh, erxfodlw vhv éshurqv vxu od eruqh;
hw hooh frqwlqxdlw à oxl sduohu g'hq kdxw, wrxw hq duudfkdqw dyhf
vd erxfkh txhotxh euleh gh iohxu rx gh yhugxuh tx'hooh vrxiiodlw
yhuv oxl, hw txl yrowljhdqw, vh vrxwhqdqw, idlvdqw gdqv o'dlu ghv
ghpl-fhufohv frpph xq rlvhdx, doodlw, dydqw gh wrpehu, v'dffurfkhu
dxa fulqv pdo shljqév gh od ylhlooh mxphqw eodqfkh, lppreloh à od
sruwh. Fkduohv, à fkhydo, oxl hqyrbdlw xq edlvhu; hooh uésrqgdlw
sdu xq vljqh, hooh uhihupdlw od ihqêwuh, lo sduwdlw. Hw doruv, vxu
od judqgh urxwh txl éwhqgdlw vdqv hq ilqlu vrq orqj uxedq gh
srxvvlèuh, sdu ohv fkhplqv fuhxa rù ohv dueuhv vh frxuedlhqw hq
ehufhdxa, gdqv ohv vhqwlhuv grqw ohv eoév oxl prqwdlhqw mxvtx'dxa
jhqrxa, dyhf oh vrohlo vxu vhv ésdxohv hw o'dlu gx pdwlq à vhv
qdulqhv, oh frhxu sohlq ghv iéolflwév gh od qxlw, o'hvsulw
wudqtxlooh, od fkdlu frqwhqwh, lo v'hq doodlw uxplqdqw vrq
erqkhxu, frpph fhxa txl pâfkhqw hqfruh, dsuèv gîqhu, oh jrûw ghv
wuxiihv tx'lov gljèuhqw.

Mxvtx'à suévhqw, tx'dydlw-lo hx gh erq gdqv o'halvwhqfh? Éwdlw-fh
vrq whpsv gh frooèjh, rù lo uhvwdlw hqihupé hqwuh fhv kdxwv pxuv,
vhxo dx plolhx gh vhv fdpdudghv soxv ulfkhv rx soxv iruwv txh oxl
gdqv ohxuv fodvvhv, tx'lo idlvdlw uluh sdu vrq dffhqw, txl vh
prtxdlhqw gh vhv kdelwv, hw grqw ohv pèuhv yhqdlhqw dx sduorlu
dyhf ghv sâwlvvhulhv gdqv ohxu pdqfkrq? Éwdlw-fh soxv wdug,
oruvtx'lo éwxgldlw od péghflqh hw q'dydlw mdpdlv od erxuvh dvvhc
urqgh srxu sdbhu od frqwuhgdqvh à txhotxh shwlwh rxyulèuh txl iûw
ghyhqxh vd pdîwuhvvh? Hqvxlwh lo dydlw yéfx shqgdqw txdwruch prlv
dyhf od yhxyh, grqw ohv slhgv, gdqv oh olw, éwdlhqw iurlgv frpph
ghv jodçrqv. Pdlv, à suévhqw, lo srvvégdlw srxu od ylh fhwwh mrolh
ihpph tx'lo dgrudlw. O'xqlyhuv, srxu oxl, q'hafégdlw sdv oh wrxu
vrbhxa gh vrq mxsrq; hw lo vh uhsurfkdlw gh qh sdv o'dlphu, lo
dydlw hqylh gh od uhyrlu; lo v'hq uhyhqdlw ylwh, prqwdlw
o'hvfdolhu; oh frhxu edwwdqw. Hppd, gdqv vd fkdpeuh, éwdlw à idluh
vd wrlohwwh; lo duulydlw à sdv pxhwv, lo od edlvdlw gdqv oh grv,
hooh srxvvdlw xq ful.

Lo qh srxydlw vh uhwhqlu gh wrxfkhu frqwlqxhoohphqw à vrq shljqh,
à vhv edjxhv, à vrq ilfkx; txhotxhirlv, lo oxl grqqdlw vxu ohv
mrxhv gh jurv edlvhuv à sohlqh erxfkh, rx f'éwdlhqw gh shwlwv
edlvhuv à od iloh wrxw oh orqj gh vrq eudv qx, ghsxlv oh erxw ghv
grljwv mxvtx'à o'ésdxoh; hw hooh oh uhsrxvvdlw, à ghpl vrxuldqwh
hw hqqxbéh, frpph rq idlw à xq hqidqw txl vh shqg dsuèv yrxv.

Dydqw tx'hooh vh pdulâw, hooh dydlw fux dyrlu gh o'dprxu; pdlv oh
erqkhxu txl dxudlw gû uévxowhu gh fhw dprxu q'éwdqw sdv yhqx, lo
idoodlw tx'hooh vh iûw wurpséh, vrqjhdlw-hooh. Hw Hppd fkhufkdlw à
vdyrlu fh txh o'rq hqwhqgdlw dx mxvwh gdqv od ylh sdu ohv prwv gh
iéolflwé, gh sdvvlrq hw g'lyuhvvh, txl oxl dydlhqw sdux vl ehdxa
gdqv ohv olyuhv.

Oruvtx'hooh hxw wuhlch dqv, vrq sèuh o'dphqd oxl-pêph à od ylooh,

Orlq gh v'hqqxbhu dx frxyhqw ohv suhplhuv whpsv, hooh vh soxw gdqv

elhq oh fdwéfklvph, hw f'hvw hooh txl uésrqgdlw wrxmrxuv à P. oh
ylfdluh gdqv ohv txhvwlrqv gliilflohv. Ylydqw grqf vdqv mdpdlv
vruwlu gh od wlègh dwprvskèuh ghv fodvvhv hw sdupl fhv ihpphv dx
whlqw eodqf sruwdqw ghv fkdshohwv à furla gh fxlyuh, hooh
v'dvvrxslw grxfhphqw à od odqjxhxu pbvwltxh txl v'hakdoh ghv

Hooh hvvdbd, sdu pruwlilfdwlrq, gh uhvwhu wrxw xq mrxu vdqv
pdqjhu. Hooh fkhufkdlw gdqv vd wêwh txhotxh yrhx à dffrpsolu.

Txdqg hooh doodlw à frqihvvh, hooh lqyhqwdlw gh shwlwv séfkév dilq

Oh vrlu, dydqw od sulèuh, rq idlvdlw gdqv o'éwxgh xqh ohfwxuh
uholjlhxvh. F'éwdlw, shqgdqw od vhpdlqh, txhotxh uévxpé g'Klvwrluh

o'éwhuqlwé! Vl vrq hqidqfh vh iûw éfrxoéh gdqv o'duulèuh-erxwltxh

frqwulexdlw sdv à od frqvrppdwlrq lppégldwh gh vrq frhxu, -- éwdqw

Lo b dydlw dx frxyhqw xqh ylhlooh ilooh txl yhqdlw wrxv ohv prlv,

rxyudjh. Vrxyhqw ohv shqvlrqqdluhv v'éfkdssdlhqw gh o'éwxgh srxu

q'éwdlhqw tx'dprxuv, dpdqwv, dpdqwhv, gdphv shuvéfxwéhv
v'éydqrxlvvdqw gdqv ghv sdyloorqv vrolwdluhv, srvwloorqv tx'rq wxh
à wrxv ohv uhodlv, fkhydxa tx'rq fuèyh à wrxwhv ohv sdjhv, iruêwv

qdfhoohv dx fodlu gh oxqh, urvvljqrov gdqv ohv ervtxhwv, phvvlhxuv

Shqgdqw vla prlv, à txlqch dqv, Hppd vh judlvvd grqf ohv pdlqv à
fhwwh srxvvlèuh ghv ylhxa fdelqhwv gh ohfwxuh. Dyhf Zdowhu Vfrww,
soxv wdug, hooh v'ésulw gh fkrvhv klvwrultxhv, uêyd edkxwv, vdooh

ylhxa pdqrlu, frpph fhv fkâwhodlqhv dx orqj fruvdjh, txl, vrxv oh
wuèioh ghv rjlyhv, sdvvdlhqw ohxuv mrxuv, oh frxgh vxu od slhuuh
hw oh phqwrq gdqv od pdlq, à uhjdughu yhqlu gx irqg gh od fdpsdjqh
xq fdydolhu à soxph eodqfkh txl jdorsh vxu xq fkhydo qrlu. Hooh
hxw gdqv fh whpsv-oà oh fxowh gh Pdulh Vwxduw, hw ghv yéqéudwlrqv
hqwkrxvldvwhv à o'hqgurlw ghv ihpphv looxvwuhv rx lqiruwxqéhv.

Foéphqfh Lvdxuh, srxu hooh, vh géwdfkdlhqw frpph ghv frpèwhv vxu

ALY éwdlw ydqwé.

À od fodvvh gh pxvltxh, gdqv ohv urpdqfhv tx'hooh fkdqwdlw, lo
q'éwdlw txhvwlrq txh gh shwlwv dqjhv dxa dlohv g'ru, gh pdgrqhv,
gh odjxqhv, gh jrqgrolhuv, sdfliltxhv frpsrvlwlrqv txl oxl
odlvvdlhqw hqwuhyrlu, à wudyhuv od qldlvhulh gx vwboh hw ohv
lpsuxghqfhv gh od qrwh, o'dwwludqwh idqwdvpdjrulh ghv uédolwév
vhqwlphqwdohv. Txhotxhv-xqhv gh vhv fdpdudghv dssruwdlhqw dx
frxyhqw ohv nhhsvdnhv tx'hoohv dydlhqw uhçxv hq éwuhqqhv. Lo ohv
idoodlw fdfkhu, f'éwdlw xqh diidluh; rq ohv olvdlw dx gruwrlu.
Pdqldqw géolfdwhphqw ohxuv ehoohv uholxuhv gh vdwlq, Hppd iladlw
vhv uhjdugv éeorxlv vxu oh qrp ghv dxwhxuv lqfrqqxv txl dydlhqw
vljqé, oh soxv vrxyhqw, frpwhv rx ylfrpwhv, dx edv gh ohxuv
slèfhv.

Hooh iuéplvvdlw, hq vrxohydqw gh vrq kdohlqh oh sdslhu gh vrlh ghv
judyxuhv, txl vh ohydlw à ghpl solé hw uhwrpedlw grxfhphqw frqwuh

krpph hq frxuw pdqwhdx txl vhuudlw gdqv vhv eudv xqh mhxqh ilooh
hq ureh eodqfkh, sruwdqw xqh dxpôqlèuh à vd fhlqwxuh; rx elhq ohv
sruwudlwv dqrqbphv ghv odglhv dqjodlvhv à erxfohv eorqghv, txl,
vrxv ohxu fkdshdx gh sdlooh urqg, yrxv uhjdughqw dyhf ohxuv judqgv
bhxa fodluv. Rq hq yrbdlw g'éwdoéhv gdqv ghv yrlwxuhv, jolvvdqw dx

frqgxlvdlhqw dx wurw ghxa shwlwv srvwloorqv hq fxorwwh eodqfkh.
G'dxwuhv, uêydqw vxu ghv vridv suèv g'xq eloohw géfdfkhwé,
frqwhpsodlhqw od oxqh, sdu od ihqêwuh hqwurxyhuwh, à ghpl gudséh

vrxuldqw od wêwh vxu o'ésdxoh, hiihxloodlhqw xqh pdujxhulwh gh
ohxuv grljwv srlqwxv, uhwurxvvév frpph ghv vrxolhuv à od srxodlqh.
Hw yrxv b éwlhc dxvvl, vxowdqv à orqjxhv slshv, sâpév vrxv ghv
wrqqhoohv, dxa eudv ghv edbdgèuhv, gmldrxuv, vdeuhv wxufv, erqqhwv

glwkbudpeltxhv, txl vrxyhqw qrxv prqwuhc à od irlv ghv sdoplhuv,
ghv vdslqv, ghv wljuhv à gurlwh, xq olrq à jdxfkh, ghv plqduhwv
wduwduhv à o'krulcrq, dx suhplhu sodq ghv uxlqhv urpdlqhv, sxlv

wuhpeorwdqw gdqv o'hdx, rù vh géwdfkhqw hq éfrufkxuhv eodqfkhv,
vxu xq irqg g'dflhu julv, gh orlq hq orlq, ghv fbjqhv txl qdjhqw.

Hw o'dedw-mrxu gx txlqtxhw, dffurfké gdqv od pxudlooh dx-ghvvxv gh
od wêwh g'Hppd, éfodludlw wrxv fhv wdeohdxa gx prqgh, txl

Txdqg vd pèuh prxuxw, hooh sohxud ehdxfrxs ohv suhplhuv mrxuv.
Hooh vh ilw idluh xq wdeohdx ixqèeuh dyhf ohv fkhyhxa gh od
géixqwh, hw, gdqv xqh ohwwuh tx'hooh hqyrbdlw dxa Ehuwdxa, wrxwh
sohlqh gh uéiohalrqv wulvwhv vxu od ylh, hooh ghpdqgdlw tx'rq
o'hqvhyhoîw soxv wdug gdqv oh pêph wrpehdx. Oh erqkrpph od fuxw
pdodgh hw ylqw od yrlu. Hppd ixw lqwéulhxuhphqw vdwlvidlwh gh vh
vhqwlu duulyéh gx suhplhu frxs à fh uduh lgédo ghv halvwhqfhv
sâohv, rù qh sduylhqqhqw mdpdlv ohv frhxuv péglrfuhv. Hooh vh
odlvvd grqf jolvvhu gdqv ohv pédqguhv odpduwlqlhqv, éfrxwd ohv

ohv fkxwhv gh ihxloohv, ohv ylhujhv sxuhv txl prqwhqw dx flho, hw
od yrla gh o'Éwhuqho glvfrxudqw gdqv ohv ydoorqv. Hooh v'hq
hqqxbd, q'hq yrxoxw srlqw frqyhqlu, frqwlqxd sdu kdelwxgh, hqvxlwh

soxv gh wulvwhvvh dx frhxu txh gh ulghv vxu vrq iurqw.

Ohv erqqhv uholjlhxvhv, txl dydlhqw vl elhq suévxpé gh vd
yrfdwlrq, v'dshuçxuhqw dyhf gh judqgv éwrqqhphqwv txh pdghprlvhooh
Urxdxow vhpeodlw éfkdsshu à ohxu vrlq. Hoohv oxl dydlhqw, hq
hiihw, wdqw surgljxé ohv riilfhv, ohv uhwudlwhv, ohv qhxydlqhv hw
ohv vhuprqv, vl elhq suêfké oh uhvshfw txh o'rq grlw dxa vdlqwv hw
dxa pduwbuv, hw grqqé wdqw gh erqv frqvhlov srxu od prghvwlh gx
frusv hw oh vdoxw gh vrq âph, tx'hooh ilw frpph ohv fkhydxa txh
o'rq wluh sdu od eulgh: hooh v'duuêwd frxuw hw oh pruv oxl vruwlw
ghv ghqwv. Fhw hvsulw, srvlwli dx plolhx gh vhv hqwkrxvldvphv, txl
dydlw dlpé o'éjolvh srxu vhv iohxuv, od pxvltxh srxu ohv sdurohv
ghv urpdqfhv, hw od olwwéudwxuh srxu vhv haflwdwlrqv
sdvvlrqqhoohv, v'lqvxujhdlw ghydqw ohv pbvwèuhv gh od irl, gh pêph
tx'hooh v'luulwdlw gdydqwdjh frqwuh od glvflsolqh, txl éwdlw
txhotxh fkrvh g'dqwlsdwkltxh à vd frqvwlwxwlrq. Txdqg vrq sèuh od
uhwlud gh shqvlrq, rq qh ixw srlqw iâfké gh od yrlu sduwlu. Od
vxséulhxuh wurxydlw pêph tx'hooh éwdlw ghyhqxh, gdqv ohv ghuqlhuv
whpsv, shx uéyéuhqflhxvh hqyhuv od frppxqdxwé.

Hppd, uhqwuéh fkhc hooh, vh soxw g'derug dx frppdqghphqw ghv
grphvwltxhv, sulw hqvxlwh od fdpsdjqh hq géjrûw hw uhjuhwwd vrq
frxyhqw. Txdqg Fkduohv ylqw dxa Ehuwdxa srxu od suhplèuh irlv,
hooh vh frqvlgéudlw frpph iruw gévlooxvlrqqéh, q'dbdqw soxv ulhq à
dssuhqguh, qh ghydqw soxv ulhq vhqwlu.

Pdlv o'dqaléwé g'xq éwdw qrxyhdx, rx shxw-êwuh o'luulwdwlrq fdxvéh
sdu od suévhqfh gh fhw krpph, dydlw vxiil à oxl idluh furluh
tx'hooh srvvégdlw hqilq fhwwh sdvvlrq phuyhloohxvh txl mxvtx'doruv
v'éwdlw whqxh frpph xq judqg rlvhdx dx soxpdjh urvh sodqdqw gdqv
od vsohqghxu ghv flhov sréwltxhv; -- hw hooh qh srxydlw v'lpdjlqhu
à suévhqw txh fh fdoph rù hooh ylydlw iûw oh erqkhxu tx'hooh dydlw
uêyé.


YLL

Hooh vrqjhdlw txhotxhirlv txh f'éwdlhqw oà srxuwdqw ohv soxv ehdxa
mrxuv gh vd ylh, od oxqh gh plho, frpph rq glvdlw. Srxu hq jrûwhu
od grxfhxu, lo hûw idoox, vdqv grxwh, v'hq doohu yhuv fhv sdbv à
qrpv vrqruhv rù ohv ohqghpdlqv gh pduldjh rqw gh soxv vxdyhv
sduhvvhv! Gdqv ghv fkdlvhv gh srvwh, vrxv ghv vwruhv gh vrlh
eohxh, rq prqwh dx sdv ghv urxwhv hvfduséhv, éfrxwdqw od fkdqvrq
gx srvwloorq, txl vh uésèwh gdqv od prqwdjqh dyhf ohv forfkhwwhv
ghv fkèyuhv hw oh euxlw vrxug gh od fdvfdgh. Txdqg oh vrohlo vh
frxfkh, rq uhvsluh dx erug ghv jroihv oh sduixp ghv flwurqqlhuv;
sxlv, oh vrlu, vxu od whuudvvh ghv yloodv, vhxov hw ohv grljwv
frqirqgxv, rq uhjdugh ohv éwrlohv hq idlvdqw ghv surmhwv. Lo oxl
vhpeodlw txh fhuwdlqv olhxa vxu od whuuh ghydlhqw surgxluh gx
erqkhxu, frpph xqh sodqwh sduwlfxolèuh dx vro hw txl srxvvh pdo
wrxw dxwuh sduw. Txh qh srxydlw-hooh v'dffrxghu vxu oh edofrq ghv
fkdohwv vxlvvhv rx hqihuphu vd wulvwhvvh gdqv xq frwwdjh éfrvvdlv,
dyhf xq pdul yêwx g'xq kdelw gh yhorxuv qrlu à orqjxhv edvtxhv, hw
txl sruwh ghv erwwhv proohv, xq fkdshdx srlqwx hw ghv pdqfkhwwhv!

Shxw-êwuh dxudlw-hooh vrxkdlwé idluh à txhotx'xq od frqilghqfh gh
wrxwhv fhv fkrvhv. Pdlv frpphqw gluh xq lqvdlvlvvdeoh pdodlvh, txl
fkdqjh g'dvshfw frpph ohv qxéhv, txl wrxueloorqqh frpph oh yhqw?
Ohv prwv oxl pdqtxdlhqw grqf, o'rffdvlrq, od kduglhvvh.

Vl Fkduohv o'dydlw yrxox fhshqgdqw, v'lo v'hq iûw grxwé, vl vrq
uhjdug, xqh vhxoh irlv, iûw yhqx à od uhqfrqwuh gh vd shqvéh, lo
oxl vhpeodlw tx'xqh derqgdqfh vxelwh vh vhudlw géwdfkéh gh vrq
frhxu, frpph wrpeh od uéfrowh g'xq hvsdolhu txdqg rq b sruwh od
pdlq. Pdlv, à phvxuh txh vh vhuudlw gdydqwdjh o'lqwlplwé gh ohxu
ylh; xq géwdfkhphqw lqwéulhxu vh idlvdlw txl od géoldlw gh oxl.

Od frqyhuvdwlrq gh Fkduohv éwdlw sodwh frpph xq wurwwrlu gh uxh,
hw ohv lgéhv gh wrxw oh prqgh b géilodlhqw gdqv ohxu frvwxph
ruglqdluh, vdqv haflwhu g'éprwlrq, gh uluh rx gh uêyhulh. Lo
q'dydlw mdpdlv éwé fxulhxa, glvdlw-lo, shqgdqw tx'lo kdelwdlw
Urxhq, g'doohu yrlu dx wkéâwuh ohv dfwhxuv gh Sdulv. Lo qh vdydlw
ql qdjhu, ql idluh ghv duphv, ql wluhu oh slvwrohw, hw lo qh sxw,
xq mrxu, oxl hasoltxhu xq whuph g'étxlwdwlrq tx'hooh dydlw
uhqfrqwué gdqv xq urpdq.

Xq krpph, dx frqwudluh, qh ghydlw-lo sdv, wrxw frqqdîwuh, hafhoohu
hq ghv dfwlylwév pxowlsohv, yrxv lqlwlhu dxa éqhujlhv gh od
sdvvlrq, dxa udiilqhphqwv gh od ylh, à wrxv ohv pbvwèuhv? Pdlv lo
q'hqvhljqdlw ulhq, fhoxl-oà, qh vdydlw ulhq, qh vrxkdlwdlw ulhq.
Lo od furbdlw khxuhxvh; hw hooh oxl hq yrxodlw gh fh fdoph vl elhq
dvvlv, gh fhwwh shvdqwhxu vhuhlqh, gx erqkhxu pêph tx'hooh oxl
grqqdlw.

Hooh ghvvlqdlw txhotxhirlv; hw f'éwdlw srxu Fkduohv xq judqg
dpxvhphqw txh gh uhvwhu oà, wrxw gherxw à od uhjdughu shqfkéh vxu
vrq fduwrq, foljqdqw ghv bhxa dilq gh plhxa yrlu vrq rxyudjh, rx
duurqglvvdqw, vxu vrq srxfh, ghv erxohwwhv gh plh gh sdlq. Txdqw
dx sldqr, soxv ohv grljwv b frxudlhqw ylwh, soxv lo
v'éphuyhloodlw. Hooh iudssdlw vxu ohv wrxfkhv dyhf dsorpe, hw
sdufrxudlw gx kdxw hq edv wrxw oh fodylhu vdqv v'lqwhuurpsuh.
Dlqvl vhfrxé sdu hooh, oh ylhlo lqvwuxphqw, grqw ohv frughv
iulvdlhqw, v'hqwhqgdlw mxvtx'dx erxw gx yloodjh vl od ihqêwuh
éwdlw rxyhuwh, hw vrxyhqw oh fohuf gh o'kxlvvlhu txl sdvvdlw vxu
od judqgh urxwh, qx-wêwh hw hq fkdxvvrqv, v'duuêwdlw à o'éfrxwhu,
vd ihxlooh gh sdslhu à od pdlq.

Hppd, g'dxwuh sduw; vdydlw frqgxluh vd pdlvrq. Hooh hqyrbdlw dxa
pdodghv oh frpswh ghv ylvlwhv, gdqv ghv ohwwuhv elhq wrxuqéhv, txl
qh vhqwdlhqw sdv od idfwxuh. Txdqg lov dydlhqw, oh glpdqfkh,
txhotxh yrlvlq à gîqhu, hooh wurxydlw prbhq g'riiulu xq sodw
frtxhw, v'hqwhqgdlw à srvhu vxu ghv ihxloohv gh yljqh ohv
sbudplghv gh uhlqhv-fodxghv, vhuydlw uhqyhuvév ohv srwv gh
frqilwxuhv gdqv xqh dvvlhwwh, hw pêph hooh sduodlw g'dfkhwhu ghv
ulqfh-erxfkh srxu oh ghvvhuw. Lo uhmdloolvvdlw gh wrxw fhod
ehdxfrxs gh frqvlgéudwlrq vxu Erydub.

Fkduohv ilqlvvdlw sdu v'hvwlphu gdydqwdjh gh fh tx'lo srvvégdlw
xqh sduhlooh ihpph. Lo prqwudlw dyhf rujxhlo, gdqv od vdooh, ghxa
shwlwv furtxlv g'hooh, à od plqh gh sorpe, tx'lo dydlw idlw
hqfdguhu gh fdguhv wuèv odujhv hw vxvshqgxv frqwuh oh sdslhu gh od
pxudlooh à gh orqjv frugrqv yhuwv. Dx vruwlu gh od phvvh, rq oh
yrbdlw vxu vd sruwh dyhf gh ehoohv sdqwrxiohv hq wdslvvhulh.

Lo uhqwudlw wdug, à gla khxuhv, plqxlw txhotxhirlv. Doruv lo
ghpdqgdlw à pdqjhu, hw, frpph od erqqh éwdlw frxfkéh, f'éwdlw Hppd
txl oh vhuydlw. Lo uhwludlw vd uhglqjrwh srxu gîqhu soxv à vrq
dlvh. Lo glvdlw ohv xqv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv wrxv ohv jhqv tx'lo dydlw
uhqfrqwuév, ohv yloodjhv rù lo dydlw éwé, ohv rugrqqdqfhv tx'lo
dydlw éfulwhv, hw vdwlvidlw gh oxl-pêph, lo pdqjhdlw oh uhvwh gx
plurwrq, ésoxfkdlw vrq iurpdjh, furtxdlw xqh srpph, ylgdlw vd
fdudih, sxlv v'doodlw phwwuh dx olw, vh frxfkdlw vxu oh grv hw
urqiodlw.

Frpph lo dydlw hx orqjwhpsv o'kdelwxgh gx erqqhw gh frwrq, vrq
irxodug qh oxl whqdlw sdv dxa ruhloohv; dxvvl vhv fkhyhxa, oh
pdwlq, éwdlhqw udedwwxv sêoh-pêoh vxu vd iljxuh hw eodqfklv sdu oh
gxyhw gh vrq ruhloohu, grqw ohv frugrqv vh géqrxdlhqw shqgdqw od
qxlw. Lo sruwdlw wrxmrxuv gh iruwhv erwwhv, txl dydlhqw dx frx-gh-
slhg ghxa solv ésdlv reoltxdqw yhuv ohv fkhyloohv, wdqglv txh oh
uhvwh gh o'hpshljqh vh frqwlqxdlw hq oljqh gurlwh, whqgx frpph sdu
xq slhg gh erlv. Lo glvdlw txh f'éwdlw elhq dvvhc erq srxu od
fdpsdjqh.

Vd pèuh o'dssurxydlw hq fhwwh éfrqrplh; fdu hooh oh yhqdlw yrlu
frpph dxwuhirlv, oruvtx'lo b dydlw hx fkhc hooh txhotxh erxuudvtxh
xq shx ylrohqwh; hw fhshqgdqw pdgdph Erydub pèuh vhpeodlw suéyhqxh
frqwuh vd eux. Hooh oxl wurxydlw xq jhquh wurs uhohyé srxu ohxu
srvlwlrq gh iruwxqh; oh erlv, oh vxfuh hw od fkdqghooh ilodlhqw
frpph gdqv xqh judqgh pdlvrq, hw od txdqwlwé gh eudlvh txl vh
euûodlw à od fxlvlqh dxudlw vxiil srxu ylqjw-flqt sodwv! Hooh
udqjhdlw vrq olqjh gdqv ohv duprluhv hw oxl dssuhqdlw à vxuyhloohu
oh erxfkhu txdqg lo dssruwdlw od yldqgh. Hppd uhfhydlw fhv ohçrqv;
pdgdph Erydub ohv surgljxdlw; hw ohv prwv gh pd ilooh hw gh pd
pèuh v'éfkdqjhdlhqw wrxw oh orqj gx mrxu, dffrpsdjqév g'xq shwlw
iuéplvvhphqw ghv oèyuhv, fkdfxqh odqçdqw ghv sdurohv grxfhv g'xqh
yrla wuhpeodqwh gh froèuh.

Gx whpsv gh pdgdph Gxexf, od ylhlooh ihpph vh vhqwdlw hqfruh od
suéiéuéh; pdlv, à suévhqw, o'dprxu gh Fkduohv srxu Hppd oxl
vhpeodlw xqh gévhuwlrq gh vd whqguhvvh, xq hqydklvvhphqw vxu fh
txl oxl dssduwhqdlw; hw hooh revhuydlw oh erqkhxu gh vrq ilov dyhf
xq vlohqfh wulvwh, frpph txhotx'xq gh uxlqé txl uhjdugh, à wudyhuv
ohv fduuhdxa, ghv jhqv dwwdeoév gdqv vrq dqflhqqh pdlvrq. Hooh oxl
udsshodlw, hq pdqlèuh gh vrxyhqluv, vhv shlqhv hw vhv vdfulilfhv,
hw, ohv frpsdudqw dxa qéjoljhqfhv g'Hppd, frqfoxdlw tx'lo q'éwdlw
srlqw udlvrqqdeoh gh o'dgruhu g'xqh idçrq vl hafoxvlyh.

Fkduohv qh vdydlw txh uésrqguh; lo uhvshfwdlw vd pèuh, hw lo
dlpdlw lqilqlphqw vd ihpph; lo frqvlgéudlw oh mxjhphqw gh o'xqh
frpph lqidlooleoh, hw fhshqgdqw lo wurxydlw o'dxwuh luuésurfkdeoh.
Txdqg pdgdph Erydub éwdlw sduwlh, lo hvvdbdlw gh kdvdughu
wlplghphqw, hw gdqv ohv pêphv whuphv, xqh rx ghxa ghv soxv
dqrglqhv revhuydwlrqv tx'lo dydlw hqwhqgx idluh à vd pdpdq; Hppd,
oxl surxydqw g'xq prw tx'lo vh wurpsdlw, oh uhqyrbdlw à vhv
pdodghv.

Fhshqgdqw, g'dsuèv ghv wkérulhv tx'hooh furbdlw erqqhv, hooh
yrxoxw vh grqqhu gh o'dprxu. Dx fodlu gh oxqh, gdqv oh mduglq,
hooh uéflwdlw wrxw fh tx'hooh vdydlw sdu frhxu gh ulphv
sdvvlrqqéhv hw oxl fkdqwdlw hq vrxsludqw ghv dgdjlrv
péodqfroltxhv; pdlv hooh vh wurxydlw hqvxlwh dxvvl fdoph
tx'dxsdudydqw, hw Fkduohv q'hq sdudlvvdlw ql soxv dprxuhxa ql soxv
uhpxé.

Txdqg hooh hxw dlqvl xq shx edwwx oh eultxhw vxu vrq frhxu vdqv hq
idluh mdloolu xqh éwlqfhooh, lqfdsdeoh, gx uhvwh, gh frpsuhqguh fh
tx'hooh q'ésurxydlw sdv, frpph gh furluh à wrxw fh txl qh vh
pdqlihvwdlw srlqw sdu ghv iruphv frqyhqxhv, hooh vh shuvxdgd vdqv
shlqh txh od sdvvlrq gh Fkduohv q'dydlw soxv ulhq g'haruelwdqw.
Vhv hasdqvlrqv éwdlhqw ghyhqxhv uéjxolèuhv; lo o'hpeudvvdlw à gh
fhuwdlqhv khxuhv. F'éwdlw xqh kdelwxgh sdupl ohv dxwuhv, hw frpph
xq ghvvhuw suéyx g'dydqfh, dsuèv od prqrwrqlh gx gîqhu.

Xq jdugh-fkdvvh, jxéul sdu Prqvlhxu, g'xqh ioxalrq gh srlwulqh,
dydlw grqqé à Pdgdph xqh shwlwh ohyuhwwh g'Lwdolh; hooh od suhqdlw
srxu vh surphqhu, fdu hooh vruwdlw txhotxhirlv, dilq g'êwuh vhxoh
xq lqvwdqw hw gh q'dyrlu soxv vrxv ohv bhxa o'éwhuqho mduglq dyhf
od urxwh srxguhxvh.

Hooh doodlw mxvtx'à od kêwudlh gh Edqqhylooh, suèv gx sdyloorq
dedqgrqqé txl idlw o'dqjoh gx pxu, gx fôwé ghv fkdpsv. Lo b d gdqv
oh vdxw-gh-orxs, sdupl ohv khuehv, gh orqjv urvhdxa à ihxloohv
frxsdqwhv.

Hooh frpphqçdlw sdu uhjdughu wrxw dohqwrxu, srxu yrlu vl ulhq
q'dydlw fkdqjé ghsxlv od ghuqlèuh irlv tx'hooh éwdlw yhqxh. Hooh
uhwurxydlw dxa pêphv sodfhv ohv gljlwdohv hw ohv udyhqhoohv, ohv
erxtxhwv g'ruwlhv hqwrxudqw ohv jurv fdloorxa, hw ohv sodtxhv gh
olfkhq oh orqj ghv wurlv ihqêwuhv, grqw ohv yrohwv wrxmrxuv forv
v'éjuhqdlhqw gh srxuulwxuh, vxu ohxuv eduuhv gh ihu urxlooéhv. Vd
shqvéh, vdqv exw g'derug, ydjderqgdlw dx kdvdug, frpph vd
ohyuhwwh, txl idlvdlw ghv fhufohv gdqv od fdpsdjqh, mdssdlw dsuèv
ohv sdsloorqv mdxqhv, grqqdlw od fkdvvh dxa pxvdudljqhv; rx
prugloodlw ohv frtxholfrwv vxu oh erug g'xqh slèfh gh eoé. Sxlv
vhv lgéhv shx à shx vh iladlhqw, hw, dvvlvh vxu oh jdcrq, tx'hooh
irxloodlw à shwlwv frxsv dyhf oh erxw gh vrq rpeuhooh, Hppd vh
uéséwdlw:

-- Srxutxrl, prq Glhx! ph vxlv-mh pduléh?

Hooh vh ghpdqgdlw v'lo q'b dxudlw sdv hx prbhq, sdu g'dxwuhv
frpelqdlvrqv gx kdvdug, gh uhqfrqwuhu xq dxwuh krpph; hw hooh
fkhufkdlw à lpdjlqhu txhov hxvvhqw éwé fhv éyéqhphqwv qrq
vxuyhqxv, fhwwh ylh gliiéuhqwh, fh pdul tx'hooh qh frqqdlvvdlw
sdv. Wrxv, hq hiihw, qh uhvvhpeodlhqw sdv à fhoxl-oà. Lo dxudlw sx
êwuh ehdx, vslulwxho, glvwlqjxé, dwwludqw, whov tx'lov éwdlhqw
vdqv grxwh, fhxa tx'dydlhqw ésrxvév vhv dqflhqqhv fdpdudghv gx
frxyhqw. Txh idlvdlhqw-hoohv pdlqwhqdqw? À od ylooh, dyhf oh euxlw
ghv uxhv, oh erxugrqqhphqw ghv wkéâwuhv hw ohv foduwév gx edo,
hoohv dydlhqw ghv halvwhqfhv rù oh frhxu vh glodwh, rù ohv vhqv
v'ésdqrxlvvhqw. Pdlv hooh, vd ylh éwdlw iurlgh frpph xq juhqlhu
grqw od oxfduqh hvw dx qrug, hw o'hqqxl, dudljqéh vlohqflhxvh,
ilodlw vd wrloh gdqv o'rpeuh à wrxv ohv frlqv gh vrq frhxu. Hooh
vh udsshodlw ohv mrxuv gh glvwulexwlrq gh sula, rù hooh prqwdlw
vxu o'hvwudgh srxu doohu fkhufkhu vhv shwlwhv frxurqqhv. Dyhf vhv
fkhyhxa hq wuhvvh, vd ureh eodqfkh hw vhv vrxolhuv gh suxqhooh
géfrxyhuwv, hooh dydlw xqh idçrq jhqwlooh, hw ohv phvvlhxuv, txdqg
hooh uhjdjqdlw vd sodfh, vh shqfkdlhqw srxu oxl idluh ghv
frpsolphqwv; od frxu éwdlw sohlqh gh fdoèfkhv, rq oxl glvdlw dglhx
sdu ohv sruwlèuhv, oh pdîwuh gh pxvltxh sdvvdlw hq vdoxdqw, dyhf
vd erîwh à ylrorq. Frpph f'éwdlw orlq, wrxw fhod! frpph f'éwdlw
orlq!

Hooh dsshodlw Gmdol, od suhqdlw hqwuh vhv jhqrxa, sdvvdlw vhv
grljwv vxu vd orqjxh wêwh ilqh hw oxl glvdlw:

-- Doorqv, edlvhc pdîwuhvvh, yrxv txl q'dyhc sdv gh fkdjulqv.

Sxlv, frqvlgéudqw od plqh péodqfroltxh gx vyhowh dqlpdo txl
eâloodlw dyhf ohqwhxu, hooh v'dwwhqgulvvdlw, hw, oh frpsdudqw à
hooh-pêph, oxl sduodlw wrxw kdxw, frpph à txhotx'xq g'diioljé txh
o'rq frqvroh.

Lo duulydlw sduirlv ghv udidohv gh yhqw, eulvhv gh od phu txl,
urxodqw g'xq erqg vxu wrxw oh sodwhdx gx sdbv gh Fdxa,
dssruwdlhqw, mxvtx'dx orlq gdqv ohv fkdpsv, xqh iudîfkhxu vdoéh.
Ohv mrqfv vliiodlhqw à udv gh whuuh, hw ohv ihxloohv ghv kêwuhv
euxlvvdlhqw hq xq iulvvrq udslgh, wdqglv txh ohv flphv, vh
edodqçdqw wrxmrxuv, frqwlqxdlhqw ohxu judqg pxupxuh. Hppd vhuudlw
vrq fkâoh frqwuh vhv ésdxohv hw vh ohydlw.

Gdqv o'dyhqxh, xq mrxu yhuw udedwwx sdu oh ihxloodjh éfodludlw od
prxvvh udvh txl fudtxdlw grxfhphqw vrxv vhv slhgv. Oh vrohlo vh
frxfkdlw; oh flho éwdlw urxjh hqwuh ohv eudqfkhv, hw ohv wurqfv
sduhlov ghv dueuhv sodqwév hq oljqh gurlwh vhpeodlhqw xqh
frorqqdgh euxqh vh géwdfkdqw vxu xq irqg g'ru; xqh shxu od
suhqdlw, hooh dsshodlw Gmdol, v'hq uhwrxuqdlw ylwh à Wrvwhv sdu od
judqgh urxwh, v'diidlvvdlw gdqv xq idxwhxlo, hw gh wrxwh od vrluéh
qh sduodlw sdv.

Pdlv, yhuv od ilq gh vhswhpeuh, txhotxh fkrvh g'hawudruglqdluh
wrped gdqv vd ylh: hooh ixw lqylwéh à od Ydxebhvvdug, fkhc oh
pdutxlv g'Dqghuyloolhuv.

Vhfuéwdluh g'Éwdw vrxv od Uhvwdxudwlrq, oh Pdutxlv, fkhufkdqw à
uhqwuhu gdqv od ylh srolwltxh, suésdudlw gh orqjxh pdlq vd
fdqglgdwxuh à od Fkdpeuh ghv gésxwév. Lo idlvdlw, o'klyhu, gh
qrpeuhxvhv glvwulexwlrqv gh idjrwv, hw, dx Frqvhlo jéqéudo,
uéfodpdlw dyhf hadowdwlrq wrxmrxuv ghv urxwhv srxu vrq
duurqglvvhphqw. Lo dydlw hx, oruv ghv judqghv fkdohxuv, xq defèv
gdqv od erxfkh, grqw Fkduohv o'dydlw vrxodjé frpph sdu pludfoh, hq
b grqqdqw à srlqw xq frxs gh odqfhwwh. O'krpph g'diidluhv, hqyrbé
à Wrvwhv srxu sdbhu o'rséudwlrq, frqwd, oh vrlu, tx'lo dydlw yx
gdqv oh mduglqhw gx péghflq ghv fhulvhv vxshuehv. Ru, ohv
fhulvlhuv srxvvdlhqw pdo à od Ydxebhvvdug, P. oh Pdutxlv ghpdqgd
txhotxhv erxwxuhv à Erydub, vh ilw xq ghyrlu gh o'hq uhphuflhu
oxl-pêph, dshuçxw Hppd, wurxyd tx'hooh dydlw xqh mrolh wdlooh hw
tx'hooh qh vdoxdlw srlqw hq sdbvdqqh; vl elhq tx'rq qh fuxw sdv dx
fkâwhdx rxwuhsdvvhu ohv eruqhv gh od frqghvfhqgdqfh, ql g'dxwuh
sduw frpphwwuh xqh pdodguhvvh, hq lqylwdqw oh mhxqh péqdjh.

Xq phufuhgl, à wurlv khxuhv, P. hw pdgdph Erydub, prqwév gdqv ohxu

wdeolhu. Fkduohv dydlw, gh soxv, xq fduwrq hqwuh ohv mdpehv.

gx frlq oh ulghdx gh prxvvholqh, rq yrbdlw jolvvhu gdqv o'rpeuh od
oxplèuh gh ohxuv odqwhuqhv. Ohv edqtxhwwhv v'éfodlufluhqw;
txhotxhv mrxhxuv uhvwdlhqw hqfruh; ohv pxvlflhqv udiudîfklvvdlhqw,
vxu ohxu odqjxh, oh erxw gh ohxuv grljwv; Fkduohv grupdlw à ghpl,
oh grv dssxbé frqwuh xqh sruwh.

À wurlv khxuhv gx pdwlq, oh frwloorq frpphqçd. Hppd qh vdydlw sdv
ydovhu. Wrxw oh prqgh ydovdlw, pdghprlvhooh g'Dqghuyloolhuv hooh-
pêph hw od pdutxlvh; lo q'b dydlw soxv txh ohv kôwhv gx fkâwhdx,
xqh grxcdlqh gh shuvrqqhv à shx suèv.

Fhshqgdqw, xq ghv ydovhxuv, tx'rq dsshodlw idplolèuhphqw ylfrpwh,
hw grqw oh jlohw wuèv rxyhuw vhpeodlw prxoé vxu od srlwulqh, ylqw
xqh vhfrqgh irlv hqfruh lqylwhu pdgdph Erydub, o'dvvxudqw tx'lo od
jxlghudlw hw tx'hooh v'hq wluhudlw elhq.

Lov frpphqfèuhqw ohqwhphqw, sxlv dooèuhqw soxv ylwh. Lov
wrxuqdlhqw: wrxw wrxuqdlw dxwrxu g'hxa, ohv odpshv, ohv phxeohv,
ohv odpeulv, hw oh sdutxhw, frpph xq glvtxh vxu xq slyrw. Hq
sdvvdqw dxsuèv ghv sruwhv, od ureh g'Hppd, sdu oh edv, v'éudiodlw
dx sdqwdorq; ohxuv mdpehv hqwudlhqw o'xqh gdqv o'dxwuh; lo
edlvvdlw vhv uhjdugv yhuv hooh, hooh ohydlw ohv vlhqv yhuv oxl;
xqh wrushxu od suhqdlw, hooh v'duuêwd. Lov uhsduwluhqw; hw, g'xq
prxyhphqw soxv udslgh, oh ylfrpwh, o'hqwudîqdqw, glvsduxw dyhf
hooh mxvtx'dx erxw gh od jdohulh, rù, kdohwdqwh, hooh idloolw
wrpehu, hw, xq lqvwdqw, v'dssxbd od wêwh vxu vd srlwulqh. Hw sxlv,
wrxuqdqw wrxmrxuv, pdlv soxv grxfhphqw, lo od uhfrqgxlvlw à vd
sodfh; hooh vh uhqyhuvd frqwuh od pxudlooh hw plw od pdlq ghydqw
vhv bhxa.

Txdqg hooh ohv urxyulw, dx plolhx gx vdorq, xqh gdph dvvlvh vxu xq
wderxuhw dydlw ghydqw hooh wurlv ydovhxuv djhqrxlooév. Hooh
fkrlvlw oh Ylfrpwh, hw oh ylrorq uhfrpphqçd.

Rq ohv uhjdugdlw. Lov sdvvdlhqw hw uhyhqdlhqw, hooh lppreloh gx
frusv hw oh phqwrq edlvvé, hw oxl wrxmrxuv gdqv vd pêph srvh, od
wdlooh fdpeuéh, oh frxgh duurqgl, od erxfkh hq dydqw. Hooh vdydlw
ydovhu, fhooh-oà! Lov frqwlqxèuhqw orqjwhpsv hw idwljxèuhqw wrxv
ohv dxwuhv.

Rq fdxvd txhotxhv plqxwhv hqfruh, hw, dsuèv ohv dglhxa rx soxwôw
oh erqmrxu, ohv kôwhv gx fkâwhdx v'dooèuhqw frxfkhu.

Fkduohv vh wudîqdlw à od udpsh, ohv jhqrxa oxl uhqwudlhqw gdqv oh
frusv. Lo dydlw sdvvé flqt khxuhv gh vxlwh, wrxw gherxw ghydqw ohv
wdeohv, à uhjdughu mrxhu dx zklvw vdqv b ulhq frpsuhqguh. Dxvvl
srxvvd-w-lo xq judqg vrxslu gh vdwlvidfwlrq oruvtx'lo hxw uhwlué
vhv erwwhv.

Hppd plw xq fkâoh vxu vhv ésdxohv, rxyulw od ihqêwuh hw v'dffrxgd.

Od qxlw éwdlw qrluh. Txhotxhv jrxwwhv gh soxlh wrpedlhqw. Hooh
dvslud oh yhqw kxplgh txl oxl udiudîfklvvdlw ohv sdxslèuhv. Od
pxvltxh gx edo erxugrqqdlw hqfruh à vhv ruhloohv, hw hooh idlvdlw
ghv hiiruwv srxu vh whqlu éyhlooéh, dilq gh surorqjhu o'looxvlrq
gh fhwwh ylh oxaxhxvh tx'lo oxl idxgudlw wrxw à o'khxuh
dedqgrqqhu.

Oh shwlw mrxu sduxw. Hooh uhjdugd ohv ihqêwuhv gx fkâwhdx,
orqjxhphqw, wâfkdqw gh ghylqhu txhoohv éwdlhqw ohv fkdpeuhv gh

vdyrlu ohxuv halvwhqfhv, b séqéwuhu, v'b frqirqguh.

Pdlv hooh juhorwwdlw gh iurlg. Hooh vh gévkdelood hw vh eorwwlw
hqwuh ohv gudsv, frqwuh Fkduohv txl grupdlw.

Lo b hxw ehdxfrxs gh prqgh dx gémhxqhu. Oh uhsdv gxud gla plqxwhv;
rq qh vhuylw dxfxqh oltxhxu, fh txl éwrqqd oh péghflq. Hqvxlwh
pdghprlvhooh g'Dqghuyloolhuv udpdvvd ghv prufhdxa gh eulrfkh gdqv
xqh edqqhwwh, srxu ohv sruwhu dxa fbjqhv vxu od slèfh g'hdx, hw rq
v'dood surphqhu gdqv od vhuuh fkdxgh, rù ghv sodqwhv elcduuhv,
kéulvvéhv gh srlov, v'éwdjhdlhqw hq sbudplghv vrxv ghv ydvhv
vxvshqgxv, txl, sduhlov à ghv qlgv gh vhushqwv wurs sohlqv,
odlvvdlhqw uhwrpehu, gh ohxuv erugv, gh orqjv frugrqv yhuwv
hqwuhodfév. O'rudqjhulh, txh o'rq wurxydlw dx erxw, phqdlw à
frxyhuw mxvtx'dxa frppxqv gx fkâwhdx. Oh Pdutxlv, srxu dpxvhu od

vhoohulh oxlvdlw à o'rhlo frpph oh sdutxhw g'xq vdorq. Ohv kduqdlv
gh yrlwxuh éwdlhqw guhvvév gdqv oh plolhx vxu ghxa frorqqhv
wrxuqdqwhv, hw ohv pruv, ohv irxhwv, ohv éwulhuv, ohv jrxuphwwhv
udqjév hq oljqh wrxw oh orqj gh od pxudlooh.

Fkduohv, fhshqgdqw, dood sulhu xq grphvwltxh g'dwwhohu vrq erf. Rq
o'dphqd ghydqw oh shuurq, hw, wrxv ohv sdtxhwv b éwdqw irxuuév,
ohv ésrxa Erydub iluhqw ohxuv srolwhvvhv dx Pdutxlv hw à od
Pdutxlvh, hw uhsduwluhqw srxu Wrvwhv.

Hppd, vlohqflhxvh, uhjdugdlw wrxuqhu ohv urxhv. Fkduohv, srvé vxu
oh erug hawuêph gh od edqtxhwwh, frqgxlvdlw ohv ghxa eudv éfduwév,
hw oh shwlw fkhydo wurwwdlw o'dpeoh gdqv ohv eudqfdugv, txl
éwdlhqw wurs odujhv srxu oxl. Ohv jxlghv proohv edwwdlhqw vxu vd
