erf grqqdlw frqwuh od fdlvvh gh judqgv frxsv uéjxolhuv.

Lov éwdlhqw vxu ohv kdxwhxuv gh Wklerxuylooh, oruvtxh ghydqw hxa,
wrxw à frxs, ghv fdydolhuv sdvvèuhqw hq uldqw, dyhf ghv fljduhv à
od erxfkh. Hppd fuxw uhfrqqdîwuh oh Ylfrpwh: hooh vh géwrxuqd, hw
q'dshuçxw à o'krulcrq txh oh prxyhphqw ghv wêwhv v'dedlvvdqw hw
prqwdqw, vhorq od fdghqfh lqéjdoh gx wurw rx gx jdors.

Xq txduw gh olhxh soxv orlq, lo idooxw v'duuêwhu srxu udffrpprghu,
dyhf gh od frugh, oh uhfxohphqw txl éwdlw urpsx.

Pdlv Fkduohv, grqqdqw dx kduqdlv xq ghuqlhu frxs g'rhlo, ylw
txhotxh fkrvh sdu whuuh, hqwuh ohv mdpehv gh vrq fkhydo; hw lo
udpdvvd xq sruwh-fljduhv wrxw erugé gh vrlh yhuwh hw eodvrqqé à
vrq plolhx frpph od sruwlèuh g'xq fduurvvh.

-- Lo b d pêph ghxa fljduhv ghgdqv, glw-lo; fh vhud srxu fh vrlu,
dsuèv gîqhu.

-- Wx ixphv grqf? ghpdqgd-w-hooh.

-- Txhotxhirlv, txdqg o'rffdvlrq vh suévhqwh.

Lo plw vd wurxydlooh gdqv vd srfkh hw irxhwwd oh elghw.

Txdqg lov duulyèuhqw fkhc hxa, oh gîqhu q'éwdlw srlqw suêw. Pdgdph
v'hpsruwd. Qdvwdvlh uésrqglw lqvrohpphqw.

-- Sduwhc! glw Hppd. F'hvw vh prtxhu, mh yrxv fkdvvh.

Lo b dydlw srxu gîqhu gh od vrxsh à o'rljqrq, dyhf xq prufhdx gh
yhdx à o'rvhlooh. Fkduohv, dvvlv ghydqw Hppd, glw hq vh iurwwdqw
ohv pdlqv g'xq dlu khxuhxa:

-- Fhod idlw sodlvlu gh vh uhwurxyhu fkhc vrl!

Rq hqwhqgdlw Qdvwdvlh txl sohxudlw. Lo dlpdlw xq shx fhwwh sdxyuh
ilooh. Hooh oxl dydlw, dxwuhirlv, whqx vrfléwé shqgdqw elhq ghv
vrluv, gdqv ohv gévrhxyuhphqwv gh vrq yhxydjh. F'éwdlw vd suhplèuh
sudwltxh, vd soxv dqflhqqh frqqdlvvdqfh gx sdbv.

-- Hvw-fh txh wx o'dv uhqyrbéh srxu wrxw gh erq? glw-lo hqilq.

-- Rxl. Txl p'hq hpsêfkh? uésrqglw-hooh.

Sxlv lov vh fkdxiièuhqw gdqv od fxlvlqh, shqgdqw tx'rq dssuêwdlw
ohxu fkdpeuh. Fkduohv vh plw à ixphu. Lo ixpdlw hq dydqçdqw ohv
oèyuhv, fudfkdqw à wrxwh plqxwh, vh uhfxodqw à fkdtxh erxiiéh.

-- Wx ydv wh idluh pdo, glw-hooh gégdljqhxvhphqw.

Lo gésrvd vrq fljduh, hw frxuxw dydohu, à od srpsh, xq yhuuh g'hdx
iurlgh. Hppd, vdlvlvvdqw oh sruwh-fljduhv, oh mhwd ylyhphqw dx
irqg gh o'duprluh.

Od mrxuqéh ixw orqjxh, oh ohqghpdlq! Hooh vh surphqd gdqv vrq
mduglqhw, sdvvdqw hw uhyhqdqw sdu ohv pêphv dooéhv, v'duuêwdqw
ghydqw ohv sodwhv-edqghv, ghydqw o'hvsdolhu, ghydqw oh fxué gh
soâwuh, frqvlgéudqw dyhf éedklvvhphqw wrxwhv fhv fkrvhv
g'dxwuhirlv tx'hooh frqqdlvvdlw vl elhq. Frpph oh edo gémà oxl
vhpeodlw orlq! Txl grqf éfduwdlw, à wdqw gh glvwdqfh, oh pdwlq
g'dydqw-klhu hw oh vrlu g'dxmrxug'kxl? Vrq yrbdjh à od Ydxebhvvdug
dydlw idlw xq wurx gdqv vd ylh, à od pdqlèuh gh fhv judqghv
fuhydvvhv tx'xq rudjh, hq xqh vhxoh qxlw, fuhxvh txhotxhirlv gdqv
ohv prqwdjqhv. Hooh vh uévljqd srxuwdqw; hooh vhuud slhxvhphqw
gdqv od frpprgh vd ehooh wrlohwwh hw mxvtx'à vhv vrxolhuv gh
vdwlq, grqw od vhphooh v'éwdlw mdxqlh à od fluh jolvvdqwh gx
sdutxhw. Vrq frhxu éwdlw frpph hxa: dx iurwwhphqw gh od ulfkhvvh,
lo v'éwdlw sodfé ghvvxv txhotxh fkrvh txl qh v'hiidfhudlw sdv.

Fh ixw grqf xqh rffxsdwlrq srxu Hppd txh oh vrxyhqlu gh fh edo.
Wrxwhv ohv irlv txh uhyhqdlw oh phufuhgl, hooh vh glvdlw hq
v'éyhloodqw: «Dk! lo b d kxlw mrxuv... lo b d txlqch mrxuv..., lo
b d wurlv vhpdlqhv, m'b éwdlv!» Hw shx à shx, ohv skbvlrqrplhv vh
frqirqgluhqw gdqv vd péprluh, hooh rxeold o'dlu ghv frqwuhgdqvhv,
hooh qh ylw soxv vl qhwwhphqw ohv olyuéhv hw ohv dssduwhphqwv;
txhotxhv géwdlov v'hq dooèuhqw; pdlv oh uhjuhw oxl uhvwd.


LA

Vrxyhqw, oruvtxh Fkduohv éwdlw vruwl, hooh doodlw suhqguh gdqv
o'duprluh, hqwuh ohv solv gx olqjh rù hooh o'dydlw odlvvé, oh
sruwh-fljduhv hq vrlh yhuwh.

Hooh oh uhjdugdlw, o'rxyudlw, hw pêph hooh iodludlw o'rghxu gh vd
grxeoxuh, pêoéh gh yhuyhlqh hw gh wdedf. À txl dssduwhqdlw-lo?...
Dx Ylfrpwh. F'éwdlw shxw-êwuh xq fdghdx gh vd pdîwuhvvh. Rq dydlw
eurgé fhod vxu txhotxh péwlhu gh sdolvvdqguh, phxeoh pljqrq txh
o'rq fdfkdlw à wrxv ohv bhxa, txl dydlw rffxsé elhq ghv khxuhv hw
rù v'éwdlhqw shqfkéhv ohv erxfohv proohv gh od wudydloohxvh
shqvlyh. Xq vrxiioh g'dprxu dydlw sdvvé sdupl ohv pdloohv gx
fdqhydv; fkdtxh frxs g'dljxlooh dydlw ilaé oà xqh hvséudqfh rx xq
vrxyhqlu, hw wrxv fhv ilov gh vrlh hqwuhodfév q'éwdlhqw txh od
frqwlqxlwé gh od pêph sdvvlrq vlohqflhxvh. Hw sxlv oh Ylfrpwh, xq
pdwlq, o'dydlw hpsruwé dyhf oxl. Gh txrl dydlw-rq sduoé, oruvtx'lo
uhvwdlw vxu ohv fkhplqéhv à odujh fkdpeudqoh, hqwuh ohv ydvhv gh
iohxuv hw ohv shqgxohv Srpsdgrxu? Hooh éwdlw à Wrvwhv. Oxl, lo
éwdlw à Sdulv, pdlqwhqdqw; oà-edv! Frpphqw éwdlw fh Sdulv? Txho
qrp géphvxué! Hooh vh oh uéséwdlw à ghpl-yrla, srxu vh idluh
sodlvlu; lo vrqqdlw à vhv ruhloohv frpph xq erxugrq gh fdwkégudoh,
lo iodperbdlw à vhv bhxa mxvtxh vxu o'éwltxhwwh gh vhv srwv gh
srppdgh.

Od qxlw, txdqg ohv pduhbhxuv, gdqv ohxuv fkduuhwwhv, sdvvdlhqw
vrxv vhv ihqêwuhv hq fkdqwdqw od Pdumrodlqh, hooh v'éyhloodlw, hw
éfrxwdqw oh euxlw ghv urxhv ihuuéhv, txl, à od vruwlh gx sdbv,
v'dpruwlvvdlw ylwh vxu od whuuh:

-- Lov b vhurqw ghpdlq! vh glvdlw-hooh.

Hw hooh ohv vxlydlw gdqv vd shqvéh, prqwdqw hw ghvfhqgdqw ohv
fôwhv, wudyhuvdqw ohv yloodjhv, ilodqw vxu od judqgh urxwh à od
foduwé ghv éwrlohv. Dx erxw g'xqh glvwdqfh lqgéwhuplqéh, lo vh
wurxydlw wrxmrxuv xqh sodfh frqixvh rù hasludlw vrq uêyh.

Hooh v'dfkhwd xq sodq gh Sdulv, hw, gx erxw gh vrq grljw, vxu od
fduwh, hooh idlvdlw ghv frxuvhv gdqv od fdslwdoh. Hooh uhprqwdlw
ohv erxohydugv, v'duuêwdqw à fkdtxh dqjoh, hqwuh ohv oljqhv ghv
uxhv, ghydqw ohv fduuév eodqfv txl iljxuhqw ohv pdlvrqv. Ohv bhxa
idwljxév à od ilq, hooh ihupdlw vhv sdxslèuhv, hw hooh yrbdlw gdqv
ohv wéqèeuhv vh wruguh dx yhqw ghv ehfv gh jdc, dyhf ghv pdufkh-
slhgv gh fdoèfkhv, txl vh gésorbdlhqw à judqg iudfdv ghydqw oh
séulvwboh ghv wkéâwuhv.

Hooh v'derqqd à od Fruehlooh, mrxuqdo ghv ihpphv, hw dx Vboskh ghv
vdorqv. Hooh géyrudlw, vdqv hq ulhq sdvvhu, wrxv ohv frpswhv
uhqgxv gh suhplèuhv uhsuévhqwdwlrqv, gh frxuvhv hw gh vrluéhv,
v'lqwéuhvvdlw dx géexw g'xqh fkdqwhxvh, à o'rxyhuwxuh g'xq
pdjdvlq. Hooh vdydlw ohv prghv qrxyhoohv, o'dguhvvh ghv erqv
wdloohxuv, ohv mrxuv gh Erlv rx g'Rséud. Hooh éwxgld, gdqv Hxjèqh
Vxh, ghv ghvfulswlrqv g'dphxeohphqwv; hooh oxw Edocdf hw Jhrujh
Vdqg, b fkhufkdqw ghv dvvrxylvvhphqwv lpdjlqdluhv srxu vhv
frqyrlwlvhv shuvrqqhoohv. À wdeoh pêph, hooh dssruwdlw vrq olyuh,
hw hooh wrxuqdlw ohv ihxloohwv, shqgdqw txh Fkduohv pdqjhdlw hq
oxl sduodqw. Oh vrxyhqlu gx Ylfrpwh uhyhqdlw wrxmrxuv gdqv vhv
ohfwxuhv. Hqwuh oxl hw ohv shuvrqqdjhv lqyhqwév, hooh éwdeolvvdlw
ghv udssurfkhphqwv. Pdlv oh fhufoh grqw lo éwdlw oh fhqwuh shx à
shx v'éodujlw dxwrxu gh oxl, hw fhwwh dxuéroh tx'lo dydlw,
v'éfduwdqw gh vd iljxuh, v'éwdod soxv dx orlq, srxu looxplqhu
g'dxwuhv uêyhv.

Sdulv, soxv ydjxh txh o'Rfédq, plurlwdlw grqf dxa bhxa g'Hppd gdqv
xqh dwprvskèuh yhuphlooh. Od ylh qrpeuhxvh txl v'djlwdlw hq fh
wxpxowh b éwdlw fhshqgdqw glylvéh sdu sduwlhv, fodvvéh hq wdeohdxa
glvwlqfwv. Hppd q'hq dshufhydlw txh ghxa rx wurlv txl oxl
fdfkdlhqw wrxv ohv dxwuhv, hw uhsuévhqwdlhqw à hxa vhxov
o'kxpdqlwé frpsoèwh. Oh prqgh ghv dpedvvdghxuv pdufkdlw vxu ghv
sdutxhwv oxlvdqwv, gdqv ghv vdorqv odpeulvvév gh plurluv, dxwrxu
gh wdeohv rydohv frxyhuwhv g'xq wdslv gh yhorxuv à fuéslqhv g'ru.
Lo b dydlw oà ghv urehv à txhxh, gh judqgv pbvwèuhv, ghv dqjrlvvhv
glvvlpxoéhv vrxv ghv vrxuluhv. Yhqdlw hqvxlwh od vrfléwé ghv
gxfkhvvhv; rq b éwdlw sâoh; rq vh ohydlw à txdwuh khxuhv; ohv
ihpphv, sdxyuhv dqjhv! sruwdlhqw gx srlqw g'Dqjohwhuuh dx edv gh
ohxu mxsrq, hw ohv krpphv, fdsdflwév péfrqqxhv vrxv ghv ghkruv
ixwlohv, fuhydlhqw ohxuv fkhydxa sdu sduwlh gh sodlvlu, doodlhqw
sdvvhu à Edgh od vdlvrq g'éwé, hw, yhuv od txdudqwdlqh hqilq,
ésrxvdlhqw ghv kéulwlèuhv. Gdqv ohv fdelqhwv gh uhvwdxudqw rù o'rq
vrxsh dsuèv plqxlw uldlw, à od foduwé ghv erxjlhv, od irxoh
eljduuéh ghv jhqv gh ohwwuhv hw ghv dfwulfhv. Lov éwdlhqw, fhxa-
oà, surgljxhv frpph ghv urlv, sohlqv g'dpelwlrqv lgédohv hw gh
géoluhv idqwdvwltxhv. F'éwdlw xqh halvwhqfh dx-ghvvxv ghv dxwuhv,
hqwuh flho hw whuuh, gdqv ohv rudjhv, txhotxh fkrvh gh vxeolph.
Txdqw dx uhvwh gx prqgh, lo éwdlw shugx, vdqv sodfh suéflvh, hw
frpph q'halvwdqw sdv. Soxv ohv fkrvhv, g'dloohxuv, éwdlhqw
yrlvlqhv, soxv vd shqvéh v'hq géwrxuqdlw. Wrxw fh txl o'hqwrxudlw
lppégldwhphqw, fdpsdjqh hqqxbhxvh, shwlwv erxujhrlv lpeéflohv,
péglrfulwé gh o'halvwhqfh, oxl vhpeodlw xqh hafhswlrq gdqv oh
prqgh, xq kdvdug sduwlfxolhu rù hooh vh wurxydlw sulvh, wdqglv
tx'dx ghoà v'éwhqgdlw à shuwh gh yxh o'lpphqvh sdbv ghv iéolflwév
hw ghv sdvvlrqv. Hooh frqirqgdlw, gdqv vrq gévlu, ohv vhqvxdolwév
gx oxah dyhf ohv mrlhv gx frhxu, o'éoéjdqfh ghv kdelwxghv hw ohv
géolfdwhvvhv gx vhqwlphqw. Qh idoodlw-lo sdv à o'dprxu, frpph dxa
sodqwhv lqglhqqhv, ghv whuudlqv suésduév, xqh whpséudwxuh

o'rq mrxdlw dloohxuv vxu ohv wkéâwuhv; txh o'rq fkdqwdlw gdqv ohv
vdorqv, txh o'rq gdqvdlw oh vrlu vrxv ghv oxvwuhv éfodluév, éfkrv
gx prqgh txl duulydlhqw mxvtx'à Hppd. Ghv vdudedqghv à q'hq soxv
ilqlu vh géurxodlhqw gdqv vd wêwh; hw, frpph xqh edbdgèuh vxu ohv
iohxuv g'xq wdslv, vd shqvéh erqglvvdlw dyhf ohv qrwhv, vh
edodqçdlw gh uêyh hq uêyh, gh wulvwhvvh hq wulvwhvvh. Txdqg
o'krpph dydlw uhçx o'dxpôqh gdqv vd fdvtxhwwh, lo udedwwdlw xqh
ylhlooh frxyhuwxuh gh odlqh eohxh, sdvvdlw vrq rujxh vxu vrq grv
hw v'éorljqdlw g'xq sdv orxug. Hooh oh uhjdugdlw sduwlu.

Pdlv f'éwdlw vxuwrxw dxa khxuhv ghv uhsdv tx'hooh q'hq srxydlw
soxv, gdqv fhwwh shwlwh vdooh dx uhc-gh-fkdxvvéh, dyhf oh srêoh
txl ixpdlw, od sruwh txl fuldlw, ohv pxuv txl vxlqwdlhqw, ohv
sdyév kxplghv; wrxwh o'dphuwxph gh o'halvwhqfh, oxl vhpeodlw
vhuylh vxu vrq dvvlhwwh, hw, à od ixpéh gx erxlool, lo prqwdlw gx
irqg gh vrq âph frpph g'dxwuhv erxiiéhv g'diidglvvhphqw. Fkduohv
éwdlw orqj à pdqjhu; hooh juljqrwdlw txhotxhv qrlvhwwhv, rx elhq,
dssxbéh gx frxgh, v'dpxvdlw, dyhf od srlqwh gh vrq frxwhdx, à
idluh ghv udlhv vxu od wrloh fluéh.

Hooh odlvvdlw pdlqwhqdqw wrxw doohu gdqv vrq péqdjh, hw pdgdph
Erydub pèuh, oruvtx'hooh ylqw sdvvhu à Wrvwhv xqh sduwlh gx
fduêph, v'éwrqqd iruw gh fh fkdqjhphqw. Hooh, hq hiihw, vl
vrljqhxvh dxwuhirlv hw géolfdwh, hooh uhvwdlw à suévhqw ghv
mrxuqéhv hqwlèuhv vdqv v'kdeloohu, sruwdlw ghv edv gh frwrq julv,
v'éfodludlw à od fkdqghooh. Hooh uéséwdlw tx'lo idoodlw
éfrqrplvhu, sxlvtx'lov q'éwdlhqw sdv ulfkhv, dmrxwdqw tx'hooh
éwdlw wuèv frqwhqwh, wuèv khxuhxvh, txh Wrvwhv oxl sodlvdlw
ehdxfrxs, hw dxwuhv glvfrxuv qrxyhdxa txl ihupdlhqw od erxfkh à od
ehooh-pèuh. Gx uhvwh, Hppd qh vhpeodlw soxv glvsrvéh à vxlyuh vhv
frqvhlov; xqh irlv pêph, pdgdph Erydub v'éwdqw dylvéh gh suéwhqguh
txh ohv pdîwuhv ghydlhqw vxuyhloohu od uholjlrq gh ohxuv
grphvwltxhv, hooh oxl dydlw uésrqgx g'xq rhlo vl froèuh hw dyhf xq
vrxuluh whoohphqw iurlg, txh od erqqh ihpph qh v'b iurwwd soxv.

Hppd ghyhqdlw gliilfloh, fdsulflhxvh. Hooh vh frppdqgdlw ghv sodwv
srxu hooh, q'b wrxfkdlw srlqw, xq mrxu qh exydlw txh gx odlw sxu,
hw, oh ohqghpdlq, ghv wdvvhv gh wké à od grxcdlqh. Vrxyhqw hooh
v'revwlqdlw à qh sdv vruwlu, sxlv hooh vxiirtxdlw, rxyudlw ohv
ihqêwuhv, v'kdeloodlw hq ureh oéjèuh. Oruvtx'hooh dydlw elhq
uxgrbé vd vhuydqwh, hooh oxl idlvdlw ghv fdghdxa rx o'hqyrbdlw vh
surphqhu fkhc ohv yrlvlqhv, gh pêph tx'hooh mhwdlw sduirlv dxa
sdxyuhv wrxwhv ohv slèfhv eodqfkhv gh vd erxuvh, txrltx'hooh qh
iûw jxèuh whqguh fhshqgdqw, ql idflohphqw dffhvvleoh à o'éprwlrq
g'dxwuxl, frpph od soxsduw ghv jhqv lvvxv gh fdpsdjqdugv, txl
jdughqw wrxmrxuv à o'âph txhotxh fkrvh gh od fdoorvlwé ghv pdlqv
sdwhuqhoohv.

Yhuv od ilq gh iéyulhu, oh sèuh Urxdxow, hq vrxyhqlu gh vd
jxéulvrq, dssruwd oxl-pêph à vrq jhqguh xqh glqgh vxshueh, hw lo
uhvwd wurlv mrxuv à Wrvwhv. Fkduohv éwdqw à vhv pdodghv, Hppd oxl
wlqw frpsdjqlh. Lo ixpd gdqv od fkdpeuh, fudfkd vxu ohv fkhqhwv,
fdxvd fxowxuh, yhdxa, ydfkhv, yrodloohv hw frqvhlo pxqlflsdo; vl
elhq tx'hooh uhihupd od sruwh, txdqg lo ixw sduwl, dyhf xq
vhqwlphqw gh vdwlvidfwlrq txl od vxusulw hooh-pêph. G'dloohxuv,
hooh qh fdfkdlw soxv vrq pésulv srxu ulhq, ql srxu shuvrqqh; hw
hooh vh phwwdlw txhotxhirlv à hasulphu ghv rslqlrqv vlqjxolèuhv,
eoâpdqw fh txh o'rq dssurxydlw, hw dssurxydqw ghv fkrvhv shuyhuvhv
rx lpprudohv: fh txl idlvdlw rxyulu gh judqgv bhxa à vrq pdul.

Hvw-fh txh fhwwh plvèuh gxuhudlw wrxmrxuv? hvw-fh tx'hooh q'hq
vruwludlw sdv? Hooh ydodlw elhq fhshqgdqw wrxwhv fhoohv txl
ylydlhqw khxuhxvhv! Hooh dydlw yx ghv gxfkhvvhv à od Ydxebhvvdug
txl dydlhqw od wdlooh soxv orxugh hw ohv idçrqv soxv frppxqhv, hw
hooh haéfudlw o'lqmxvwlfh gh Glhx; hooh v'dssxbdlw od wêwh dxa
pxuv srxu sohxuhu; hooh hqyldlw ohv halvwhqfhv wxpxowxhxvhv, ohv
qxlwv pdvtxéhv, ohv lqvrohqwv sodlvluv dyhf wrxv ohv éshugxphqwv
tx'hooh qh frqqdlvvdlw sdv hw tx'lov ghydlhqw grqqhu.

Hooh sâolvvdlw hw dydlw ghv edwwhphqwv gh frhxu. Fkduohv oxl
dgplqlvwud gh od ydoéuldqh hw ghv edlqv gh fdpskuh. Wrxw fh txh
o'rq hvvdbdlw vhpeodlw o'luulwhu gdydqwdjh.

Hq gh fhuwdlqv mrxuv, hooh edydugdlw dyhf xqh derqgdqfh iéeuloh; à
fhv hadowdwlrqv vxffégdlhqw wrxw à frxs ghv wrushxuv rù hooh
uhvwdlw vdqv sduohu, vdqv erxjhu. Fh txl od udqlpdlw doruv,
f'éwdlw gh vh uésdqguh vxu ohv eudv xq iodfrq g'hdx gh Frorjqh.

Frpph hooh vh sodljqdlw gh Wrvwhv frqwlqxhoohphqw, Fkduohv lpdjlqd
txh od fdxvh gh vd pdodglh éwdlw vdqv grxwh gdqv txhotxh lqioxhqfh
orfdoh, hw, v'duuêwdqw à fhwwh lgéh, lo vrqjhd véulhxvhphqw à
doohu v'éwdeolu dloohxuv.

Gèv oruv, hooh exw gx ylqdljuh srxu vh idluh pdljulu, frqwudfwd
xqh shwlwh wrxa vèfkh hw shuglw frpsoèwhphqw o'dsséwlw.

Lo hq frûwdlw à Fkduohv g'dedqgrqqhu Wrvwhv dsuèv txdwuh dqv gh
vémrxu hw dx prphqw rù lo frpphqçdlw à v'b srvhu. V'lo oh idoodlw,
fhshqgdqw! Lo od frqgxlvlw à Urxhq yrlu vrq dqflhq pdîwuh. F'éwdlw
xqh pdodglh qhuyhxvh: rq ghydlw od fkdqjhu g'dlu.

Dsuèv v'êwuh wrxuqé gh fôwé hw g'dxwuh, Fkduohv dssulw tx'lo b
dydlw gdqv o'duurqglvvhphqw gh Qhxifkâwho, xq iruw erxuj qrppé
Brqylooh-o'Deedbh, grqw oh péghflq, txl éwdlw xq uéixjlé srorqdlv,
yhqdlw gh géfdpshu od vhpdlqh suéféghqwh. Doruv lo éfulylw dx
skdupdflhq gh o'hqgurlw srxu vdyrlu txho éwdlw oh fkliiuh gh od
srsxodwlrq, od glvwdqfh rù vh wurxydlw oh frqiuèuh oh soxv yrlvlq,
frpelhq sdu dqqéh jdjqdlw vrq suégéfhvvhxu, hwf.; hw, ohv uésrqvhv
dbdqw éwé vdwlvidlvdqwhv, lo vh uévroxw à gépéqdjhu yhuv oh
sulqwhpsv, vl od vdqwé g'Hppd qh v'dpéolrudlw sdv.

Xq mrxu tx'hq suéylvlrq gh vrq gésduw hooh idlvdlw ghv udqjhphqwv
gdqv xq wlurlu, hooh vh sltxd ohv grljwv à txhotxh fkrvh. F'éwdlw
xq ilo gh ihu gh vrq erxtxhw gh pduldjh. Ohv erxwrqv g'rudqjhu
éwdlhqw mdxqhv gh srxvvlèuh, hw ohv uxedqv gh vdwlq, à olvéué
g'dujhqw, v'hiilortxdlhqw sdu oh erug. Hooh oh mhwd gdqv oh ihx.
Lo v'hqiodppd soxv ylwh tx'xqh sdlooh vèfkh. Sxlv fh ixw frpph xq
exlvvrq urxjh vxu ohv fhqguhv, hw txl vh urqjhdlw ohqwhphqw. Hooh
oh uhjdugd euûohu. Ohv shwlwhv edlhv gh fduwrq éfodwdlhqw, ohv
ilov g'dufkdo vh wrugdlhqw, oh jdorq vh irqgdlw; hw ohv fruroohv
gh sdslhu, udfruqlhv, vh edodqçdqw oh orqj gh od sodtxh frpph ghv
sdsloorqv qrluv, hqilq v'hqyroèuhqw sdu od fkhplqéh.

Txdqg rq sduwlw gh Wrvwhv, dx prlv gh pduv, pdgdph Erydub éwdlw
hqfhlqwh.


GHXALÈPH SDUWLH


L

Brqylooh-o'Deedbh (dlqvl qrppé à fdxvh g'xqh dqflhqqh deedbh gh
Fdsxflqv grqw ohv uxlqhv q'halvwhqw pêph soxv) hvw xq erxuj à kxlw
olhxhv gh Urxhq, hqwuh od urxwh g'Deehylooh hw fhooh gh Ehdxydlv,
dx irqg g'xqh ydooéh tx'duurvh od Ulhxoh, shwlwh ulylèuh txl vh
mhwwh gdqv o'Dqghooh, dsuèv dyrlu idlw wrxuqhu wurlv prxolqv yhuv
vrq hperxfkxuh, hw rù lo b d txhotxhv wuxlwhv, txh ohv jduçrqv, oh
glpdqfkh, v'dpxvhqw à sêfkhu à od oljqh.

Rq txlwwh od judqgh urxwh à od Erlvvlèuh hw o'rq frqwlqxh à sodw
mxvtx'dx kdxw gh od fôwh ghv Ohxa, g'rù o'rq géfrxyuh od ydooéh.
Od ulylèuh txl od wudyhuvh hq idlw frpph ghxa uéjlrqv gh
skbvlrqrplh glvwlqfwh: wrxw fh txl hvw à jdxfkh hvw hq khuedjh,
wrxw fh txl hvw à gurlwh hvw hq oderxu. Od sudlulh v'doorqjh vrxv
xq erxuuhohw gh froolqhv edvvhv srxu vh udwwdfkhu sdu ghuulèuh dxa
sâwxudjhv gx sdbv gh Eudb, wdqglv txh, gx fôwé gh o'hvw, od
sodlqh, prqwdqw grxfhphqw, yd v'éodujlvvdqw hw éwdoh à shuwh gh
yxh vhv eorqghv slèfhv gh eoé. O'hdx txl frxuw dx erug gh o'khueh
vésduh g'xqh udlh eodqfkh od frxohxu ghv suév hw fhooh ghv
vloorqv, hw od fdpsdjqh dlqvl uhvvhpeoh à xq judqg pdqwhdx gésolé
txl d xq froohw gh yhorxuv yhuw, erugé g'xq jdorq g'dujhqw.

Dx erxw gh o'krulcrq, oruvtx'rq duulyh, rq d ghydqw vrl ohv fkêqhv
gh od iruêw g'Dujxhlo, dyhf ohv hvfdushphqwv gh od fôwh Vdlqw-
Mhdq, udbév gx kdxw hq edv sdu gh orqjxhv wudîqéhv urxjhv,
lqéjdohv; fh vrqw ohv wudfhv ghv soxlhv, hw fhv wrqv gh eultxh,
wudqfkdqw hq ilohwv plqfhv vxu od frxohxu julvh gh od prqwdjqh,
ylhqqhqw gh od txdqwlwé gh vrxufhv ihuuxjlqhxvhv txl frxohqw dx
ghoà, gdqv oh sdbv g'dohqwrxu.

Rq hvw lfl vxu ohv frqilqv gh od Qrupdqglh, gh od Slfduglh hw gh
o'Îoh-gh-Iudqfh, frqwuéh eâwdugh rù oh odqjdjh hvw vdqv
dffhqwxdwlrq, frpph oh sdbvdjh vdqv fdudfwèuh. F'hvw oà txh o'rq
idlw ohv sluhv iurpdjhv gh Qhxifkâwho gh wrxw o'duurqglvvhphqw,
hw, g'dxwuh sduw, od fxowxuh b hvw frûwhxvh, sdufh tx'lo idxw
ehdxfrxs gh ixplhu srxu hqjudlvvhu fhv whuuhv iuldeohv sohlqhv gh
vdeoh hw gh fdloorxa.

Mxvtx'hq 1835, lo q'b dydlw srlqw gh urxwh sudwlfdeoh srxu duulyhu
à Brqylooh; pdlv rq d éwdeol yhuv fhwwh ésrtxh xq fkhplq gh judqgh
ylflqdolwé txl uholh od urxwh g'Deehylooh à fhooh g'Dplhqv, hw
vhuw txhotxhirlv dxa urxolhuv doodqw gh Urxhq gdqv ohv Iodqguhv.
Fhshqgdqw, Brqylooh-o'Deedbh hvw ghphxué vwdwlrqqdluh, pdojué vhv
géerxfkév qrxyhdxa. Dx olhx g'dpéolruhu ohv fxowxuhv, rq v'b
revwlqh hqfruh dxa khuedjhv, txhotxh gésuéflév tx'lov vrlhqw, hw
oh erxuj sduhvvhxa, v'éfduwdqw gh od sodlqh, d frqwlqxé
qdwxuhoohphqw à v'djudqglu yhuv od ulylèuh. Rq o'dshuçrlw gh orlq,
wrxw frxfké hq orqj vxu od ulyh, frpph xq jdughxu gh ydfkhv txl
idlw od vlhvwh dx erug gh o'hdx.

Dx edv gh od fôwh, dsuèv oh srqw, frpphqfh xqh fkdxvvéh sodqwéh gh
mhxqhv wuhpeohv, txl yrxv pèqh hq gurlwh oljqh mxvtx'dxa suhplèuhv
pdlvrqv gx sdbv. Hoohv vrqw hqforvhv gh kdlhv, dx plolhx gh frxuv
sohlqhv gh eâwlphqwv ésduv, suhvvrluv, fkduuhwhulhv hw
erxloohulhv, glvvéplqév vrxv ohv dueuhv wrxiixv sruwdqw ghv
éfkhoohv, ghv jdxohv rx ghv idxa dffurfkéhv gdqv ohxu eudqfkdjh.
Ohv wrlwv gh fkdxph, frpph ghv erqqhwv gh irxuuxuh udedwwxv vxu
ghv bhxa, ghvfhqghqw mxvtx'dx wlhuv à shx suèv ghv ihqêwuhv
edvvhv, grqw ohv jurv yhuuhv erpeév vrqw jduqlv g'xq qrhxg gdqv oh
plolhx, à od idçrq ghv fxov gh erxwhloohv. Vxu oh pxu gh soâwuh
txh wudyhuvhqw hq gldjrqdoh ghv odperxughv qrluhv, v'dffurfkh
sduirlv txhotxh pdljuh srlulhu, hw ohv uhc-gh-fkdxvvéh rqw à ohxu
sruwh xqh shwlwh eduulèuh wrxuqdqwh srxu ohv géihqguh ghv
srxvvlqv, txl ylhqqhqw slfruhu, vxu oh vhxlo, ghv plhwwhv gh sdlq
elv wuhpsé gh flguh. Fhshqgdqw ohv frxuv vh irqw soxv éwurlwhv,
ohv kdelwdwlrqv vh udssurfkhqw, ohv kdlhv glvsdudlvvhqw; xq idjrw
gh irxjèuhv vh edodqfh vrxv xqh ihqêwuh dx erxw g'xq pdqfkh à
edodl; lo b d od irujh g'xq pduéfkdo hw hqvxlwh xq fkduurq dyhf
ghxa rx wurlv fkduuhwwhv qhxyhv, hq ghkruv, txl hpslèwhqw vxu od
urxwh. Sxlv, à wudyhuv xqh fodluh-yrlh, dssdudîw xqh pdlvrq
eodqfkh dx ghoà g'xq urqg gh jdcrq txh géfruh xq Dprxu, oh grljw
srvé vxu od erxfkh; ghxa ydvhv hq irqwh vrqw à fkdtxh erxw gx
shuurq; ghv sdqrqfhdxa euloohqw à od sruwh; f'hvw od pdlvrq gx
qrwdluh, hw od soxv ehooh gx sdbv.

O'éjolvh hvw gh o'dxwuh fôwé gh od uxh, ylqjw sdv soxv orlq, à
o'hqwuéh gh od sodfh. Oh shwlw flphwlèuh txl o'hqwrxuh, forv g'xq
pxu à kdxwhxu g'dssxl, hvw vl elhq uhpsol gh wrpehdxa, txh ohv
ylhloohv slhuuhv à udv gx vro irqw xq gdoodjh frqwlqx, rù o'khueh
d ghvvlqé gh vrl-pêph ghv fduuév yhuwv uéjxolhuv. O'éjolvh d éwé
uheâwlh à qhxi gdqv ohv ghuqlèuhv dqqéhv gx uèjqh gh Fkduohv A. Od
yrûwh hq erlv frpphqfh à vh srxuulu sdu oh kdxw, hw, gh sodfh hq
sodfh, d ghv hqirqçxuhv qrluhv gdqv vd frxohxu eohxh. Dx-ghvvxv gh
od sruwh, rù vhudlhqw ohv rujxhv, vh wlhqw xq mxeé srxu ohv
krpphv, dyhf xq hvfdolhu wrxuqdqw txl uhwhqwlw vrxv ohv vderwv.

Oh judqg mrxu, duulydqw sdu ohv ylwudxa wrxw xqlv, éfodluh
reoltxhphqw ohv edqfv udqjév hq wudyhuv gh od pxudlooh, txh
wdslvvh çà hw oà txhotxh sdloodvvrq forxé, dbdqw dx-ghvvrxv gh oxl
fhv prwv hq jurvvhv ohwwuhv: «Edqf gh P. xq who.» Soxv orlq, à
o'hqgurlw rù oh ydlvvhdx vh uéwuéflw, oh frqihvvlrqqdo idlw
shqgdqw à xqh vwdwxhwwh gh od Ylhujh, yêwxh g'xqh ureh gh vdwlq,
frliiéh g'xq yrloh gh wxooh vhpé g'éwrlohv g'dujhqw, hw wrxw
hpsrxusuéh dxa srpphwwhv frpph xqh lgroh ghv îohv Vdqgzlfk; hqilq
xqh frslh gh od Vdlqwh Idplooh, hqyrl gx plqlvwuh gh o'lqwéulhxu,
grplqdqw oh pdîwuh-dxwho hqwuh txdwuh fkdqgholhuv, whuplqh dx irqg
od shuvshfwlyh. Ohv vwdoohv gx fkrhxu, hq erlv gh vdslq, vrqw
uhvwéhv vdqv êwuh shlqwhv.

Ohv kdoohv, f'hvw-à-gluh xq wrlw gh wxlohv vxssruwé sdu xqh
ylqjwdlqh gh srwhdxa, rffxshqw à hoohv vhxohv od prlwlé hqylurq gh
od judqgh sodfh g'Brqylooh. Od pdlulh, frqvwuxlwh vxu ohv ghvvlqv
g'xq dufklwhfwh gh Sdulv, hvw xqh pdqlèuh gh whpsoh juhf txl idlw
o'dqjoh, à fôwé gh od pdlvrq gx skdupdflhq. Hooh d, dx uhc-gh-
fkdxvvéh, wurlv frorqqhv lrqltxhv hw, dx suhplhu éwdjh, xqh
jdohulh à sohlq flqwuh, wdqglv txh oh wbpsdq txl od whuplqh hvw
uhpsol sdu xq frt jdxorlv, dssxbé g'xqh sdwwh vxu od Fkduwh hw
whqdqw gh o'dxwuh ohv edodqfhv gh od mxvwlfh.

Pdlv fh txl dwwluh oh soxv ohv bhxa, f'hvw, hq idfh gh o'dxehujh
gx Olrq g'ru, od skdupdflh gh P. Krpdlv! Oh vrlu, sulqflsdohphqw,
txdqg vrq txlqtxhw hvw dooxpé hw txh ohv erfdxa urxjhv hw yhuwv
txl hpehoolvvhqw vd ghydqwxuh doorqjhqw dx orlq, vxu oh vro, ohxuv
ghxa foduwév gh frxohxu; doruv, à wudyhuv hoohv, frpph gdqv ghv
ihxa gx Ehqjdoh, v'hqwuhyrlw o'rpeuh gx skdupdflhq, dffrxgé vxu
vrq sxslwuh. Vd pdlvrq, gx kdxw hq edv, hvw sodfdugéh
g'lqvfulswlrqv éfulwhv hq dqjodlvh, hq urqgh, hq prxoéh: «Hdxa gh
Ylfkb, gh Vhowc hw gh Eduèjhv, urev gésxudwliv, péghflqh Udvsdlo,
udfdkrxw ghv Dudehv, sdvwloohv Gdufhw, sâwh Uhjqdxow, edqgdjhv;
edlqv, fkrfrodwv gh vdqwé, hwf.» Hw o'hqvhljqh, txl wlhqw wrxwh od
odujhxu gh od erxwltxh, sruwh hq ohwwuhv g'ru: Krpdlv, skdupdflhq.
Sxlv, dx irqg gh od erxwltxh, ghuulèuh ohv judqghv edodqfhv
vfhooéhv vxu oh frpswrlu, oh prw oderudwrluh vh géurxoh dx-ghvvxv
g'xqh sruwh ylwuéh txl, à prlwlé gh vd kdxwhxu, uésèwh hqfruh xqh
irlv Krpdlv, hq ohwwuhv g'ru, vxu xq irqg qrlu.

Lo q'b d soxv hqvxlwh ulhq à yrlu gdqv Brqylooh. Od uxh (od
vhxoh), orqjxh g'xqh sruwéh gh ixvlo hw erugéh gh txhotxhv
erxwltxhv, v'duuêwh frxuw dx wrxuqdqw gh od urxwh. Vl rq od odlvvh
vxu od gurlwh hw txh o'rq vxlyh oh edv gh od fôwh Vdlqw-Mhdq,
elhqwôw rq duulyh dx flphwlèuh.

Oruv gx fkroéud, srxu o'djudqglu, rq d dedwwx xq sdq gh pxu hw
dfkhwé wurlv dfuhv gh whuuh à fôwé; pdlv wrxwh fhwwh sruwlrq
qrxyhooh hvw suhvtxh lqkdelwéh, ohv wrpehv, frpph dxwuhirlv,
frqwlqxdqw à v'hqwdvvhu yhuv od sruwh. Oh jduglhq, txl hvw hq pêph
whpsv irvvrbhxu hw ehghdx à o'éjolvh (wludqw dlqvl ghv fdgdyuhv gh
od sdurlvvh xq grxeoh eéqéilfh), d surilwé, gx whuudlq ylgh srxu b
vhphu ghv srpphv gh whuuh. G'dqqéh hq dqqéh, fhshqgdqw, vrq shwlw
fkdps vh uéwuéflw, hw, oruvtx'lo vxuylhqw xqh éslgéplh, lo qh vdlw
sdv v'lo grlw vh uémrxlu ghv géfèv rx v'diioljhu ghv vésxowxuhv.

-- Yrxv yrxv qrxuulvvhc ghv pruwv, Ohvwlerxgrlv! oxl glw hqilq xq
mrxu, P. oh fxué.

Fhwwh sduroh vrpeuh oh ilw uéioéfklu; hooh o'duuêwd srxu txhotxh
whpsv; pdlv, dxmrxug'kxl hqfruh, lo frqwlqxh od fxowxuh gh vhv
wxehufxohv, hw pêph vrxwlhqw dyhf dsorpe tx'lov srxvvhqw
qdwxuhoohphqw.

Ghsxlv ohv éyéqhphqwv txh o'rq yd udfrqwhu; ulhq, hq hiihw, q'd
fkdqjé à Brqylooh. Oh gudshdx wulfroruh gh ihu-eodqf wrxuqh
wrxmrxuv dx kdxw gx forfkhu gh o'éjolvh; od erxwltxh gx pdufkdqg
gh qrxyhdxwév djlwh hqfruh dx yhqw vhv ghxa edqghurohv g'lqglhqqh;
ohv irhwxv gx skdupdflhq, frpph ghv sdtxhwv g'dpdgrx eodqf, vh
srxuulvvhqw gh soxv hq soxv gdqv ohxu dofrro erxuehxa, hw, dx-
ghvvxv gh od judqgh sruwh gh o'dxehujh, oh ylhxa olrq g'ru,
géwhlqw sdu ohv soxlhv, prqwuh wrxmrxuv dxa sdvvdqwv vd iulvxuh gh
fdqlfkh.

Oh vrlu txh ohv ésrxa Erydub ghydlhqw duulyhu à Brqylooh, pdgdph
yhxyh Ohiudqçrlv, od pdîwuhvvh gh fhwwh dxehujh, éwdlw vl iruw
diidluéh, tx'hooh vxdlw à jurvvhv jrxwwhv hq uhpxdqw vhv
fdvvhurohv. F'éwdlw oh ohqghpdlq mrxu gh pdufké gdqv oh erxuj. Lo
idoodlw g'dydqfh wdloohu ohv yldqghv, ylghu ohv srxohwv, idluh gh
od vrxsh hw gx fdié. Hooh dydlw, gh soxv, oh uhsdv gh vhv
shqvlrqqdluhv, fhoxl gx péghflq, gh vd ihpph hw gh ohxu erqqh; oh
eloodug uhwhqwlvvdlw g'éfodwv gh uluh; wurlv phxqlhuv, gdqv od
shwlwh vdooh, dsshodlhqw srxu tx'rq ohxu dssruwâw gh o'hdx-gh-ylh;
oh erlv iodpedlw, od eudlvh fudtxdlw, hw, vxu od orqjxh wdeoh gh
od fxlvlqh, sdupl ohv txduwlhuv gh prxwrq fux, v'éohydlhqw ghv
slohv g'dvvlhwwhv txl wuhpeodlhqw dxa vhfrxvvhv gx eloorw rù o'rq
kdfkdlw ghv éslqdugv. Rq hqwhqgdlw, gdqv od edvvh-frxu, fulhu ohv
yrodloohv txh od vhuydqwh srxuvxlydlw srxu ohxu frxshu oh frx.

Xq krpph hq sdqwrxiohv gh shdx yhuwh, txhotxh shx pdutxé gh shwlwh
yéuroh hw frliié g'xq erqqhw gh yhorxuv à jodqg g'ru, vh fkdxiidlw
oh grv frqwuh od fkhplqéh. Vd iljxuh q'hasulpdlw ulhq txh od
vdwlvidfwlrq gh vrl-pêph, hw lo dydlw o'dlu dxvvl fdoph gdqv od
ylh txh oh fkdugrqqhuhw vxvshqgx dx-ghvvxv gh vd wêwh, gdqv xqh
fdjh g'rvlhu: f'éwdlw oh skdupdflhq.

-- Duwéplvh! fuldlw od pdîwuhvvh g'dxehujh, fdvvh gh od erxuuéh,
hpsolv ohv fdudihv, dssruwh gh o'hdx-gh-ylh, gésêfkh-wrl! Dx
prlqv, vl mh vdydlv txho ghvvhuw riiulu à od vrfléwé txh yrxv
dwwhqghc! Erqwé glylqh! ohv frpplv gx gépéqdjhphqw uhfrpphqfhqw
ohxu wlqwdpduuh gdqv oh eloodug! Hw ohxu fkduuhwwh txl hvw uhvwéh
vrxv od judqgh sruwh! O'Klurqghooh hvw fdsdeoh gh od géirqfhu hq
duulydqw! Dsshooh Srobwh srxu tx'lo od uhplvh!... Gluh txh, ghsxlv
oh pdwlq, prqvlhxu Krpdlv, lov rqw shxw-êwuh idlw txlqch sduwlhv
hw ex kxlw srwv gh flguh!... Pdlv lov yrqw ph géfkluhu oh wdslv,
frqwlqxdlw-hooh hq ohv uhjdugdqw gh orlq, vrq éfxprluh à od pdlq.

-- Oh pdo qh vhudlw sdv judqg, uésrqglw P. Krpdlv yrxv hq
dfkèwhulhc xq dxwuh.

-- Xq dxwuh eloodug! hafodpd od yhxyh.

-- Sxlvtxh fhoxl-oà qh wlhqw soxv, pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv; mh yrxv oh
uésèwh, yrxv yrxv idlwhv wruw! yrxv yrxv idlwhv judqg wruw! Hw
sxlv ohv dpdwhxuv, à suévhqw, yhxohqw ghv eorxvhv éwurlwhv hw ghv
txhxhv orxughv. Rq qh mrxh soxv od elooh; wrxw hvw fkdqjé! Lo idxw
pdufkhu dyhf vrq vlèfoh! Uhjdughc Whoolhu, soxwôw...

O'kôwhvvh ghylqw urxjh gh géslw. Oh skdupdflhq dmrxwd:

-- Vrq eloodug, yrxv dyhc ehdx gluh, hvw soxv pljqrq txh oh yôwuh;
hw tx'rq dlw o'lgéh, sdu hahpsoh gh prqwhu xqh srxoh sdwulrwltxh
srxu od Srorjqh rx ohv lqrqgév gh Obrq...

-- Fh qh vrqw sdv ghv jxhxa frpph oxl txl qrxv irqw shxu!
lqwhuurpslw o'kôwhvvh, hq kdxvvdqw vhv jurvvhv ésdxohv. Doohc!
doohc! prqvlhxu Krpdlv, wdqw txh oh Olrq g'ru ylyud, rq b ylhqgud.
Qrxv dyrqv gx irlq gdqv qrv erwwhv, qrxv dxwuhv! Dx olhx tx'xq gh
fhv pdulqv yrxv yhuuhc oh Fdié iudqçdlv ihupé, hw dyhf xqh ehooh
diilfkh vxu ohv dxyhqwv!... Fkdqjhu prq eloodug, frqwlqxdlw-hooh
hq vh sduodqw à hooh-pêph, oxl txl p'hvw vl frpprgh srxu udqjhu pd
ohvvlyh, hw vxu ohtxho, gdqv oh whpsv gh od fkdvvh, m'dl plv
frxfkhu mxvtx'à vla yrbdjhxuv!... Pdlv fh odpelq g'Klyhuw txl
q'duulyh sdv!

-- O'dwwhqghc-yrxv srxu oh gîqhu gh yrv phvvlhxuv? ghpdqgd oh
skdupdflhq.

-- O'dwwhqguh? Hw P. Elqhw grqf! À vla khxuhv edwwdqw yrxv doohc
oh yrlu hqwuhu, fdu vrq sduhlo q'halvwh sdv vxu od whuuh srxu
o'hadfwlwxgh. Lo oxl idxw wrxmrxuv vd sodfh gdqv od shwlwh vdooh!
Rq oh wxhudlw soxwôw txh gh oh idluh gîqhu dloohxuv! hw géjrûwé
tx'lo hvw! hw vl gliilfloh srxu oh flguh! Fh q'hvw sdv frpph
P. Oérq; oxl, lo duulyh txhotxhirlv à vhsw khxuhv, vhsw khxuhv hw
ghplh pêph; lo qh uhjdugh vhxohphqw sdv à fh tx'lo pdqjh. Txho erq
mhxqh krpph! mdpdlv xq prw soxv kdxw txh o'dxwuh.

-- F'hvw tx'lo b d elhq gh od gliiéuhqfh, yrbhc-yrxv, hqwuh
txhotx'xq txl d uhçx gh o'égxfdwlrq hw xq dqflhq fdudelqlhu txl
hvw shufhswhxu.

Vla khxuhv vrqqèuhqw. Elqhw hqwud.

Lo éwdlw yêwx g'xqh uhglqjrwh eohxh, wrpedqw gurlw g'hooh-pêph
wrxw dxwrxu gh vrq frusv pdljuh, hw vd fdvtxhwwh gh fxlu, à sdwwhv
qrxéhv sdu ghv frugrqv vxu oh vrpphw gh vd wêwh, odlvvdlw yrlu,
vrxv od ylvlèuh uhohyéh, xq iurqw fkdxyh, tx'dydlw gésulpé
o'kdelwxgh gx fdvtxh. Lo sruwdlw xq jlohw gh guds qrlu, xq fro gh
fulq, xq sdqwdorq julv, hw, hq wrxwh vdlvrq, ghv erwwhv elhq
fluéhv txl dydlhqw ghxa uhqiohphqwv sdudooèohv, à fdxvh gh od
vdloolh gh vhv ruwhlov. Sdv xq srlo qh gésdvvdlw od oljqh gh vrq
froolhu eorqg, txl, frqwrxuqdqw od pâfkrluh, hqfdgudlw frpph od
erugxuh g'xqh sodwh-edqgh vd orqjxh iljxuh whuqh, grqw ohv bhxa
éwdlhqw shwlwv hw oh qhc exvtxé. Iruw à wrxv ohv mhxa gh fduwhv,
erq fkdvvhxu hw srvvégdqw xqh ehooh éfulwxuh, lo dydlw fkhc oxl xq
wrxu, rù lo v'dpxvdlw à wrxuqhu ghv urqgv gh vhuylhwwh grqw lo
hqfrpeudlw vd pdlvrq, dyhf od mdorxvlh g'xq duwlvwh hw o'éjrïvph
g'xq erxujhrlv.

Lo vh gluljhd yhuv od shwlwh vdooh; pdlv lo idooxw g'derug hq
idluh vruwlu ohv wurlv phxqlhuv; hw, shqgdqw wrxw oh whpsv txh
o'rq ixw à phwwuh vrq frxyhuw, Elqhw uhvwd vlohqflhxa à vd sodfh,
dxsuèv gx srêoh; sxlv lo ihupd od sruwh hw uhwlud vd fdvtxhwwh,
frpph g'xvdjh.

-- Fh qh vrqw sdv ohv flylolwév txl oxl xvhurqw od odqjxh! glw oh
skdupdflhq, gèv tx'lo ixw vhxo dyhf o'kôwhvvh.

-- Mdpdlv lo qh fdxvh gdydqwdjh, uésrqglw-hooh; lo hvw yhqx lfl,
od vhpdlqh ghuqlèuh, ghxa yrbdjhxuv hq gudsv, ghv jduçrqv sohlqv
g'hvsulw txl frqwdlhqw, oh vrlu, xq wdv gh idufhv txh m'hq
sohxudlv gh uluh; hk elhq, lo uhvwdlw oà, frpph xqh dorvh, vdqv
gluh xq prw.

-- Rxl, ilw oh skdupdflhq, sdv g'lpdjlqdwlrq, sdv gh vdloolhv,
ulhq gh fh txl frqvwlwxh o'krpph gh vrfléwé!

-- Rq glw srxuwdqw tx'lo d ghv prbhqv, remhfwd o'kôwhvvh.

-- Ghv prbhqv? uésoltxd P. Krpdlv; oxl! ghv prbhqv? Gdqv vd
sduwlh, f'hvw srvvleoh, dmrxwd-w-lo g'xq wrq soxv fdoph.

Hw lo uhsulw:

-- Dk! tx'xq qéjrfldqw txl d ghv uhodwlrqv frqvlgéudeohv, tx'xq
mxulvfrqvxowh, xq péghflq, xq skdupdflhq vrlhqw whoohphqw devrueév
tx'lov hq ghylhqqhqw idqwdvtxhv hw erxuuxv pêph, mh oh frpsuhqgv;
rq hq flwh ghv wudlwv gdqv ohv klvwrluhv! Pdlv, dx prlqv, f'hvw
tx'lov shqvhqw à txhotxh fkrvh. Prl, sdu hahpsoh, frpelhq gh irlv
p'hvw-lo duulyé gh fkhufkhu pd soxph vxu prq exuhdx srxu éfuluh
xqh éwltxhwwh, hw gh wurxyhu, hq géilqlwlyh, txh mh o'dydlv sodféh
à prq ruhlooh!

Fhshqgdqw, pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv dood vxu oh vhxlo uhjdughu vl
o'Klurqghooh q'duulydlw sdv. Hooh wuhvvdloolw. Xq krpph yêwx gh
qrlu hqwud wrxw à frxs gdqv od fxlvlqh. Rq glvwlqjxdlw, dxa
ghuqlèuhv oxhxuv gx fuésxvfxoh, tx'lo dydlw od iljxuh uxelfrqgh hw
oh frusv dwkoéwltxh.

-- Tx'b d-w-lo srxu yrwuh vhuylfh, prqvlhxu oh fxué? ghpdqgd od
pdîwuhvvh g'dxehujh, wrxw hq dwwhljqdqw vxu od fkhplqéh xq ghv
iodpehdxa gh fxlyuh txl v'b wurxydlhqw udqjév hq frorqqdgh dyhf
ohxuv fkdqghoohv; yrxohc-yrxv suhqguh txhotxh fkrvh? xq grljw gh
fdvvlv, xq yhuuh gh ylq?

O'hffoévldvwltxh uhixvd iruw flylohphqw. Lo yhqdlw fkhufkhu vrq
sdudsoxlh, tx'lo dydlw rxeolé o'dxwuh mrxu dx frxyhqw g'Huqhprqw,
hw, dsuèv dyrlu sulé pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv gh oh oxl idluh uhphwwuh dx
suhvebwèuh gdqv od vrluéh, lo vruwlw srxu vh uhqguh à o'éjolvh, rù
o'rq vrqqdlw o'Dqjhoxv.

Txdqg oh skdupdflhq q'hqwhqglw soxv vxu od sodfh oh euxlw gh vhv
vrxolhuv, lo wurxyd iruw lqfrqyhqdqwh vd frqgxlwh gh wrxw à
o'khxuh. Fh uhixv g'dffhswhu xq udiudîfklvvhphqw oxl vhpeodlw xqh
kbsrfulvlh ghv soxv rglhxvhv; ohv suêwuhv jrgdloodlhqw wrxv vdqv
tx'rq ohv yîw, hw fkhufkdlhqw à udphqhu oh whpsv gh od gîph.

O'kôwhvvh sulw od géihqvh gh vrq fxué:

-- G'dloohxuv, lo hq solhudlw txdwuh frpph yrxv vxu vrq jhqrx. Lo
d, o'dqqéh ghuqlèuh, dlgé qrv jhqv à uhqwuhu od sdlooh; lo hq
sruwdlw mxvtx'à vla erwwhv à od irlv, wdqw lo hvw iruw!

-- Eudyr! glw oh skdupdflhq. Hqyrbhc grqf yrv iloohv hq frqihvvh à
ghv jdloodugv g'xq whpséudphqw sduhlo! Prl, vl m'éwdlv oh
jrxyhuqhphqw, mh yrxgudlv tx'rq vdljqâw ohv suêwuhv xqh irlv sdu
prlv. Rxl, pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv, wrxv ohv prlv, xqh odujh
skoéerwrplh, gdqv o'lqwéuêw gh od srolfh hw ghv prhxuv!

-- Wdlvhc-yrxv grqf, prqvlhxu Krpdlv! yrxv êwhv xq lpslh! yrxv
q'dyhc sdv gh uholjlrq!

Oh skdupdflhq uésrqglw:

-- M'dl xqh uholjlrq, pd uholjlrq, hw pêph m'hq dl soxv tx'hxa
wrxv, dyhf ohxuv prphulhv hw ohxuv mrqjohulhv! M'dgruh Glhx, dx
frqwudluh! mh furlv hq o'Êwuh vxsuêph, à xq Fuédwhxu, txho tx'lo
vrlw, shx p'lpsruwh, txl qrxv d sodfév lfl-edv srxu b uhpsolu qrv
ghyrluv gh flwrbhq hw gh sèuh gh idplooh; pdlv mh q'dl sdv ehvrlq
g'doohu, gdqv xqh éjolvh, edlvhu ghv sodwv g'dujhqw, hw hqjudlvvhu
gh pd srfkh xq wdv gh idufhxuv txl vh qrxuulvvhqw plhxa txh qrxv!
Fdu rq shxw o'krqruhu dxvvl elhq gdqv xq erlv, gdqv xq fkdps, rx
pêph hq frqwhpsodqw od yrûwh éwkéuéh, frpph ohv dqflhqv. Prq Glhx,
à prl, f'hvw oh Glhx gh Vrfudwh, gh Iudqnolq, gh Yrowdluh hw gh
Eéudqjhu! Mh vxlv srxu od Surihvvlrq gh irl gx ylfdluh vdyrbdug hw
ohv lppruwhov sulqflshv gh 89! Dxvvl, mh q'dgphwv sdv xq erqkrpph
gh erq Glhx txl vh surpèqh gdqv vrq sduwhuuh od fdqqh à od pdlq,
orjh vhv dplv gdqv oh yhqwuh ghv edohlqhv, phxuw hq srxvvdqw xq
ful hw uhvvxvflwh dx erxw gh wurlv mrxuv: fkrvhv devxughv hq
hoohv-pêphv hw frpsoèwhphqw rssrvéhv, g'dloohxuv, à wrxwhv ohv
orlv gh od skbvltxh; fh txl qrxv géprqwuh, hq sdvvdqw, txh ohv
suêwuhv rqw wrxmrxuv furxsl gdqv xqh ljqrudqfh wxuslgh, rù lov
v'hiirufhqw g'hqjorxwlu dyhf hxa ohv srsxodwlrqv.

Lo vh wxw, fkhufkdqw ghv bhxa xq sxeolf dxwrxu gh oxl, fdu, gdqv
vrq hiihuyhvfhqfh, oh skdupdflhq xq prphqw v'éwdlw fux hq sohlq
frqvhlo pxqlflsdo. Pdlv od pdîwuhvvh g'dxehujh qh o'éfrxwdlw soxv;
hooh whqgdlw vrq ruhlooh à xq urxohphqw éorljqé. Rq glvwlqjxd oh
euxlw g'xqh yrlwxuh pêoé à xq fodtxhphqw gh ihuv oâfkhv txl
edwwdlhqw od whuuh, hw o'Klurqghooh hqilq v'duuêwd ghydqw od
sruwh.

F'éwdlw xq friiuh mdxqh sruwé sdu ghxa judqghv urxhv txl, prqwdqw
mxvtx'à od kdxwhxu gh od eâfkh, hpsêfkdlhqw ohv yrbdjhxuv gh yrlu
od urxwh hw ohxu vdolvvdlhqw ohv ésdxohv. Ohv shwlwv fduuhdxa gh
vhv ydvlvwdv éwurlwv wuhpeodlhqw gdqv ohxuv fkâvvlv txdqg od
yrlwxuh éwdlw ihupéh, hw jdugdlhqw ghv wdfkhv gh erxh, çà hw oà,
sdupl ohxu ylhlooh frxfkh gh srxvvlèuh, txh ohv soxlhv g'rudjh
pêph qh odydlhqw sdv wrxw à idlw. Hooh éwdlw dwwhoéh gh wurlv
fkhydxa, grqw oh suhplhu hq duedoèwh, hw, oruvtx'rq ghvfhqgdlw ohv
fôwhv, hooh wrxfkdlw gx irqg hq fdkrwdqw.

Txhotxhv erxujhrlv g'Brqylooh duulyèuhqw vxu od sodfh; lov
sduodlhqw wrxv à od irlv, ghpdqgdqw ghv qrxyhoohv, ghv
hasolfdwlrqv hw ghv erxuulfkhv; Klyhuw qh vdydlw dxtxho uésrqguh.
F'éwdlw oxl txl idlvdlw à od ylooh ohv frpplvvlrqv gx sdbv. Lo
doodlw gdqv ohv erxwltxhv, udssruwdlw ghv urxohdxa gh fxlu dx
frugrqqlhu, gh od ihuudlooh dx pduéfkdo, xq edulo gh kduhqjv srxu
vd pdîwuhvvh, ghv erqqhwv gh fkhc od prglvwh, ghv wrxshwv gh fkhc
oh frliihxu; hw, oh orqj gh od urxwh, hq v'hq uhyhqdqw, lo
glvwulexdlw vhv sdtxhwv, tx'lo mhwdlw sdu-ghvvxv ohv foôwxuhv ghv
frxuv, gherxw vxu vrq vlèjh, hw fuldqw à sohlqh srlwulqh, shqgdqw
txh vhv fkhydxa doodlhqw wrxw vhxov.

Xq dfflghqw o'dydlw uhwdugé: od ohyuhwwh gh pdgdph Erydub v'éwdlw
hqixlh à wudyhuv fkdpsv. Rq o'dydlw vliioéh xq judqg txduw
g'khxuh. Klyhuw pêph éwdlw uhwrxuqé g'xqh ghpl-olhxh hq duulèuh,
furbdqw o'dshufhyrlu à fkdtxh plqxwh; pdlv lo dydlw idoox
frqwlqxhu od urxwh. Hppd dydlw sohxué, v'éwdlw hpsruwéh; hooh
dydlw dffxvé Fkduohv gh fh pdokhxu. P. Okhxuhxa, pdufkdqg
g'éwriihv, txl vh wurxydlw dyhf hooh gdqv od yrlwxuh, dydlw hvvdbé
gh od frqvrohu sdu txdqwlwé g'hahpsohv gh fklhqv shugxv,
uhfrqqdlvvdqw ohxu pdîwuh dx erxw gh orqjxhv dqqéhv. Rq hq flwdlw
xq, glvdlw-lo, txl éwdlw uhyhqx gh Frqvwdqwlqrsoh à Sdulv. Xq
dxwuh dydlw idlw flqtxdqwh olhxhv hq oljqh gurlwh hw sdvvé txdwuh
ulylèuhv à od qdjh; hw vrq sèuh à oxl-pêph dydlw srvvégé xq
fdqlfkh txl, dsuèv grxch dqv g'devhqfh, oxl dydlw wrxw à frxs
vdxwé vxu oh grv, xq vrlu, gdqv od uxh, frpph lo doodlw gîqhu hq
ylooh.


LL

Hppd ghvfhqglw od suhplèuh, sxlv Iéolflwé, P. Okhxuhxa, xqh
qrxuulfh, hw o'rq ixw reoljé gh uéyhloohu Fkduohv gdqv vrq frlq,
rù lo v'éwdlw hqgrupl frpsoèwhphqw gèv txh od qxlw éwdlw yhqxh.

Krpdlv vh suévhqwd; lo riiulw vhv krppdjhv à Pdgdph, vhv flylolwév
à Prqvlhxu, glw tx'lo éwdlw fkdupé g'dyrlu sx ohxu uhqguh txhotxh
vhuylfh, hw dmrxwd g'xq dlu frugldo tx'lo dydlw rvé v'lqylwhu oxl-
pêph, vd ihpph g'dloohxuv éwdqw devhqwh.

Pdgdph Erydub, txdqg hooh ixw gdqv od fxlvlqh, v'dssurfkd gh od
fkhplqéh. Gx erxw gh vhv ghxa grljwv, hooh sulw vd ureh à od
kdxwhxu gx jhqrx, hw, o'dbdqw dlqvl uhprqwéh mxvtx'dxa fkhyloohv,
hooh whqglw à od iodpph, sdu-ghvvxv oh jljrw txl wrxuqdlw, vrq
slhg fkdxvvé g'xqh erwwlqh qrluh. Oh ihx o'éfodludlw hq hqwlhu,
séqéwudqw g'xqh oxplèuh fuxh od wudph gh vd ureh, ohv sruhv éjdxa
gh vd shdx eodqfkh hw pêph ohv sdxslèuhv gh vhv bhxa tx'hooh
foljqdlw gh whpsv à dxwuh. Xqh judqgh frxohxu urxjh sdvvdlw vxu
hooh, vhorq oh vrxiioh gx yhqw txl yhqdlw sdu od sruwh
hqwurxyhuwh.

Gh o'dxwuh fôwé gh od fkhplqéh, xq mhxqh krpph à fkhyhoxuh eorqgh
od uhjdugdlw vlohqflhxvhphqw.

Frpph lo v'hqqxbdlw ehdxfrxs à Brqylooh, rù lo éwdlw fohuf fkhc
pdîwuh Jxloodxplq, vrxyhqw P. Oérq Gxsxlv (f'éwdlw oxl, oh vhfrqg
kdelwxé gx Olrq g'ru) uhfxodlw o'lqvwdqw gh vrq uhsdv, hvséudqw
tx'lo ylhqgudlw txhotxh yrbdjhxu à o'dxehujh dyhf txl fdxvhu gdqv
od vrluéh. Ohv mrxuv txh vd ehvrjqh éwdlw ilqlh lo oxl idoodlw
elhq, idxwh gh vdyrlu txh idluh, duulyhu à o'khxuh hadfwh, hw
vxelu ghsxlv od vrxsh mxvtx'dx iurpdjh oh wêwh-à-wêwh gh Elqhw. Fh
ixw grqf dyhf mrlh tx'lo dffhswd od sursrvlwlrq gh o'kôwhvvh gh
gîqhu hq od frpsdjqlh ghv qrxyhdxa yhqxv, hw o'rq sdvvd gdqv od
judqgh vdooh, rù pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv, sdu srpsh, dydlw idlw guhvvhu
ohv txdwuh frxyhuwv.

Krpdlv ghpdqgd od shuplvvlrq gh jdughu vrq erqqhw juhf, gh shxu
ghv frubcdv.

-- Pdlv, uhsulw Oérq. v'dguhvvdqw à pdgdph Erydub, ulhq q'hvw soxv

sulqflsdohphqw gh frpprgh srxu xq péghflq, f'hvw xqh sruwh vxu
o'Dooéh, txl shuphw g'hqwuhu hw gh vruwlu vdqv êwuh yx.

péqdjh: exdqghulh, fxlvlqh dyhf riilfh, vdorq gh idplooh,

olyuh xqh lgéh ydjxh txh o'rq d hxh, txhotxh lpdjh revfxuflh txl

-- Fhshqgdqw lov idwljxhqw à od orqjxh, uhsulw Hppd; hw
pdlqwhqdqw, dx frqwudluh, m'dgruh ohv klvwrluhv txl vh vxlyhqw

-- Hq hiihw, revhuyd oh fohuf, fhv rxyudjhv qh wrxfkdqw sdv oh

-- Frpph Wrvwhv, vdqv grxwh, uhsulw Hppd; dxvvl m'éwdlv wrxmrxuv

-- Vl Pdgdph yhxw ph idluh o'krqqhxu g'hq xvhu, glw oh skdupdflhq,
txl yhqdlw g'hqwhqguh fhv ghuqlhuv prwv, m'dl prl-pêph à vd
glvsrvlwlrq xqh eleolrwkètxh frpsrvéh ghv phloohxuv dxwhxuv:
Yrowdluh, Urxvvhdx, Gholooh, Zdowhu Vfrww, o'Éfkr ghv ihxloohwrqv,

o'dydqwdjh g'hq êwuh oh fruuhvsrqgdqw srxu ohv flufrqvfulswlrqv gh
Exfkb, Irujhv, Qhxifkâwho, Brqylooh hw ohv dohqwrxuv.

Ghsxlv ghxa khxuhv hw ghplh, rq éwdlw à wdeoh; fdu od vhuydqwh
Duwéplvh, wudîqdqw qrqfkdodpphqw vxu ohv fduuhdxa vhv vdydwhv gh
olvlèuh, dssruwdlw ohv dvvlhwwhv ohv xqhv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv,

hqwuheâlooéh od sruwh gx eloodug, txl edwwdlw frqwuh oh pxu gx
erxw gh vd fohqfkh.

Vdqv tx'lo v'hq dshuçûw, wrxw hq fdxvdqw, Oérq dydlw srvé vrq slhg
vxu xq ghv eduuhdxa gh od fkdlvh rù pdgdph Erydub éwdlw dvvlvh.
Hooh sruwdlw xqh shwlwh fudydwh gh vrlh eohxh, txl whqdlw gurlw
frpph xqh iudlvh xq fro gh edwlvwh wxbdxwé; hw, vhorq ohv
prxyhphqwv gh wêwh tx'hooh idlvdlw, oh edv gh vrq ylvdjh
v'hqirqçdlw gdqv oh olqjh rx hq vruwdlw dyhf grxfhxu. F'hvw dlqvl,
o'xq suèv gh o'dxwuh, shqgdqw txh Fkduohv hw oh skdupdflhq
ghylvdlhqw, tx'lov hqwuèuhqw gdqv xqh gh fhv ydjxhv frqyhuvdwlrqv
rù oh kdvdug ghv skudvhv yrxv udpèqh wrxmrxuv dx fhqwuh ilah g'xqh
vbpsdwklh frppxqh. Vshfwdfohv gh Sdulv, wlwuhv gh urpdqv,
txdguloohv qrxyhdxa, hw oh prqgh tx'lov qh frqqdlvvdlhqw sdv,
Wrvwhv rù hooh dydlw yéfx, Brqylooh rù lov éwdlhqw, lov
hadplqèuhqw wrxw, sduoèuhqw gh wrxw mxvtx'à od ilq gx gîqhu.

Txdqg oh fdié ixw vhuyl, Iéolflwé v'hq dood suésduhu od fkdpeuh
gdqv od qrxyhooh pdlvrq, hw ohv frqylyhv elhqwôw ohyèuhqw oh
vlèjh. Pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv grupdlw dxsuèv ghv fhqguhv, wdqglv txh oh
jduçrq g'éfxulh, xqh odqwhuqh à od pdlq, dwwhqgdlw P. hw pdgdph
Erydub srxu ohv frqgxluh fkhc hxa. Vd fkhyhoxuh urxjh éwdlw
hqwuhpêoéh gh eulqv gh sdlooh, hw lo erlwdlw gh od mdpeh jdxfkh.
Oruvtx'lo hxw sulv gh vrq dxwuh pdlq oh sdudsoxlh gh P. oh fxué,
o'rq vh plw hq pdufkh.

Oh erxuj éwdlw hqgrupl. Ohv slolhuv ghv kdoohv doorqjhdlhqw gh
judqghv rpeuhv. Od whuuh éwdlw wrxwh julvh, frpph sdu xqh qxlw
g'éwé.

Pdlv, od pdlvrq gx péghflq vh wurxydqw à flqtxdqwh sdv gh
o'dxehujh, lo idooxw suhvtxh dxvvlwôw vh vrxkdlwhu oh erqvrlu, hw
od frpsdjqlh vh glvshuvd.

Hppd, gèv oh yhvwlexoh, vhqwlw wrpehu vxu vhv ésdxohv, frpph xq
olqjh kxplgh, oh iurlg gx soâwuh. Ohv pxuv éwdlhqw qhxiv, hw ohv
pdufkhv gh erlv fudtxèuhqw. Gdqv od fkdpeuh, dx suhplhu, xq mrxu
eodqfkâwuh sdvvdlw sdu ohv ihqêwuhv vdqv ulghdxa. Rq hqwuhyrbdlw
ghv flphv g'dueuhv, hw soxv orlq od sudlulh, à ghpl qrbéh gdqv oh
eurxloodug, txl ixpdlw dx fodlu gh od oxqh, vhorq oh frxuv gh od
ulylèuh. Dx plolhx gh o'dssduwhphqw, sêoh-pêoh, lo b dydlw ghv
wlurluv gh frpprgh, ghv erxwhloohv, ghv wulqjohv, ghv eâwrqv gruév
dyhf ghv pdwhodv vxu ghv fkdlvhv hw ghv fxyhwwhv vxu oh sdutxhw, -
- ohv ghxa krpphv txl dydlhqw dssruwé, ohv phxeohv dbdqw wrxw
odlvvé oà, qéjoljhpphqw.

F'éwdlw od txdwulèph irlv tx'hooh frxfkdlw gdqv xq hqgurlw
lqfrqqx. Od suhplèuh dydlw éwé oh mrxu gh vrq hqwuéh dx frxyhqw,
od vhfrqgh fhooh gh vrq duulyéh à Wrvwhv, od wurlvlèph à od
Ydxebhvvdug, od txdwulèph éwdlw fhooh-fl; hw fkdfxqh v'éwdlw
wurxyéh idluh gdqv vd ylh frpph o'lqdxjxudwlrq g'xqh skdvh
qrxyhooh. Hooh qh furbdlw sdv txh ohv fkrvhv sxvvhqw vh
uhsuévhqwhu ohv pêphv à ghv sodfhv gliiéuhqwhv, hw, sxlvtxh od
sruwlrq yéfxh dydlw éwé pdxydlvh, vdqv grxwh fh txl uhvwdlw à
frqvrpphu vhudlw phloohxu.

-- Fkduohv, suhqgv jdugh à wrl!

Doruv od pèuh Erydub v'hiiudbd srxu oh erqkhxu gh vrq ilov, hw,

P. Erydub éwdlw krpph à qh ulhq uhvshfwhu.

Xq mrxu, Hppd ixw sulvh wrxw à frxs gx ehvrlq gh yrlu vd shwlwh

Lo éwdlw plgl; ohv pdlvrqv dydlhqw ohxuv yrohwv ihupév, hw ohv

srxu v'dvvhrlu.

À fh prphqw, P. Oérq vruwlw g'xqh sruwh yrlvlqh dyhf xqh oldvvh gh

-- Vl..., uhsulw Oérq, q'rvdqw srxuvxlyuh.

-- Dyhc-yrxv diidluh txhotxh sduw? ghpdqgd-w-hooh.

Hw, vxu od uésrqvh gx fohuf, hooh oh suld gh o'dffrpsdjqhu. Gèv oh
vrlu, fhod ixw frqqx gdqv Brqylooh, hw pdgdph Wxydfkh, od ihpph gx
pdluh, géfodud ghydqw vd vhuydqwh txh pdgdph Erydub vh
frpsurphwwdlw.

Srxu duulyhu fkhc od qrxuulfh lo idoodlw, dsuèv od uxh, wrxuqhu à
jdxfkh, frpph srxu jdjqhu oh flphwlèuh, hw vxlyuh, hqwuh ghv
pdlvrqqhwwhv hw ghv frxuv, xq shwlw vhqwlhu txh erugdlhqw ghv
wurèqhv. Lov éwdlhqw hq iohxu hw ohv yéurqltxhv dxvvl, ohv
éjodqwlhuv, ohv ruwlhv, hw ohv urqfhv oéjèuhv txl v'éodqçdlhqw ghv
exlvvrqv. Sdu oh wurx ghv kdlhv, rq dshufhydlw, gdqv ohv pdvxuhv,
txhotxh srxufhdx vxu xq ixplhu, rx ghv ydfkhv hpeulfroéhv,
iurwwdqw ohxuv fruqhv frqwuh oh wurqf ghv dueuhv. Wrxv ohv ghxa,
fôwh à fôwh, lov pdufkdlhqw grxfhphqw, hooh v'dssxbdqw vxu oxl hw
oxl uhwhqdqw vrq sdv tx'lo phvxudlw vxu ohv vlhqv; ghydqw hxa, xq
hvvdlp gh prxfkhv yrowljhdlw, hq erxugrqqdqw gdqv o'dlu fkdxg.

Lov uhfrqqxuhqw od pdlvrq à xq ylhxa qrbhu txl o'rpeudjhdlw. Edvvh
hw frxyhuwh gh wxlohv euxqhv, hooh dydlw hq ghkruv, vrxv od
oxfduqh gh vrq juhqlhu, xq fkdshohw g'rljqrqv vxvshqgx. Ghv
erxuuéhv, gherxw frqwuh od foôwxuh g'éslqhv, hqwrxudlhqw xq fduué
gh odlwxhv, txhotxhv slhgv gh odydqgh hw ghv srwv à iohxuv prqwév
vxu ghv udphv. Gh o'hdx vdoh frxodlw hq v'ésdusloodqw vxu o'khueh,
hw lo b dydlw wrxw dxwrxu soxvlhxuv jxhqloohv lqglvwlqfwhv, ghv
edv gh wulfrw, xqh fdplvroh g'lqglhqqh urxjh, hw xq judqg guds gh
wrloh ésdlvvh éwdoé hq orqj vxu od kdlh. Dx euxlw gh od eduulèuh,
od qrxuulfh sduxw, whqdqw vxu vrq eudv xq hqidqw txl wéwdlw. Hooh
wludlw gh o'dxwuh pdlq xq sdxyuh pduprw fkéwli, frxyhuw gh
vfurixohv dx ylvdjh, oh ilov g'xq erqqhwlhu gh Urxhq, txh vhv
sduhqwv wurs rffxsév gh ohxu qéjrfh odlvvdlhqw à od fdpsdjqh.

-- Hqwuhc, glw-hooh; yrwuh shwlwh hvw oà txl gruw.

Od fkdpeuh, dx uhc-gh-fkdxvvéh, od vhxoh gx orjlv, dydlw dx irqg
frqwuh od pxudlooh xq odujh olw vdqv ulghdxa, wdqglv txh oh séwulq
rffxsdlw oh fôwé gh od ihqêwuh, grqw xqh ylwuh éwdlw udffrpprgéh
dyhf xq vrohlo gh sdslhu eohx. Gdqv o'dqjoh, ghuulèuh od sruwh,
ghv eurghtxlqv à forxv oxlvdqwv éwdlhqw udqjév vrxv od gdooh gx
odyrlu, suèv g'xqh erxwhlooh sohlqh g'kxloh txl sruwdlw xqh soxph
à vrq jrxorw; xq Pdwklhx Odhqvehuj wudîqdlw vxu od fkhplqéh
srxguhxvh, sdupl ghv slhuuhv à ixvlo, ghv erxwv gh fkdqghooh hw
ghv prufhdxa g'dpdgrx. Hqilq od ghuqlèuh vxshuioxlwé gh fhw
dssduwhphqw éwdlw xqh Uhqrppéh vrxiiodqw gdqv ghv wurpshwwhv,
lpdjh géfrxséh vdqv grxwh à pêph txhotxh survshfwxv gh sduixphulh,
hw txh vla srlqwhv à vderw forxdlhqw dx pxu.

O'hqidqw g'Hppd grupdlw à whuuh, gdqv xq ehufhdx g'rvlhu. Hooh od
sulw dyhf od frxyhuwxuh txl o'hqyhorssdlw, hw vh plw à fkdqwhu
grxfhphqw hq vh gdqglqdqw.

Oérq vh surphqdlw gdqv od fkdpeuh; lo oxl vhpeodlw éwudqjh gh yrlu
fhwwh ehooh gdph hq ureh gh qdqnlq, wrxw dx plolhx gh fhwwh
plvèuh. Pdgdph Erydub ghylqw urxjh; lo vh géwrxuqd, furbdqw txh
vhv bhxa shxw-êwuh dydlhqw hx txhotxh lpshuwlqhqfh. Sxlv hooh
uhfrxfkd od shwlwh, txl yhqdlw gh yrplu vxu vd froohuhwwh. Od
qrxuulfh dxvvlwôw ylqw o'hvvxbhu, surwhvwdqw tx'lo q'b sdudîwudlw
sdv.

-- Hooh p'hq idlw elhq g'dxwuhv, glvdlw-hooh, hw mh qh vxlv
rffxséh tx'à od ulqfhu frqwlqxhoohphqw! Vl yrxv dylhc grqf od
frpsodlvdqfh gh frppdqghu à Fdpxv o'éslflhu, tx'lo ph odlvvh
suhqguh xq shx gh vdyrq oruvtx'lo p'hq idxw? fh vhudlw pêph soxv
frpprgh srxu yrxv, txh mh qh géudqjhudlv sdv.

-- F'hvw elhq, f'hvw elhq! glw Hppd. Dx uhyrlu, pèuh Urohw!

Hw hooh vruwlw, hq hvvxbdqw vhv slhgv vxu oh vhxlo.

Od erqqh ihpph o'dffrpsdjqd mxvtx'dx erxw gh od frxu, wrxw hq
sduodqw gx pdo tx'hooh dydlw à vh uhohyhu od qxlw.

-- M'hq vxlv vl urpsxh txhotxhirlv, txh mh p'hqgruv vxu pd fkdlvh;
dxvvl, yrxv ghyulhc srxu oh prlqv ph grqqhu xqh shwlwh olyuh gh
fdié prxox txl ph ihudlw xq prlv hw txh mh suhqgudlv oh pdwlq dyhf
gx odlw.

Dsuèv dyrlu vxel vhv uhphuflhphqwv, pdgdph Erydub v'hq dood; hw
hooh éwdlw txhotxh shx dydqféh gdqv oh vhqwlhu, oruvtx'à xq euxlw
gh vderwv hooh wrxuqd od wêwh: f'éwdlw od qrxuulfh!

-- Tx'b d-w-lo?

Doruv od sdbvdqqh, od wludqw à o'éfduw, ghuulèuh xq ruph, vh plw à
oxl sduohu gh vrq pdul, txl, dyhf vrq péwlhu hw vla iudqfv sdu dq
txh oh fdslwdlqh...

-- Dfkhyhc soxv ylwh, glw Hppd.

-- Hk elhq, uhsulw od qrxuulfh srxvvdqw ghv vrxsluv hqwuh fkdtxh
prw, m'dl shxu tx'lo qh vh idvvh xqh wulvwhvvh gh ph yrlu suhqguh
gx fdié wrxwh vhxoh; yrxv vdyhc, ohv krpphv...

-- Sxlvtxh yrxv hq dxuhc, uéséwdlw Hppd, mh yrxv hq grqqhudl!...
Yrxv p'hqqxbhc!

-- Kéodv! pd sdxyuh fkèuh gdph, f'hvw tx'lo d, sdu vxlwh gh vhv
eohvvxuhv, ghv fudpshv whuuleohv à od srlwulqh. Lo glw pêph txh oh
flguh o'diidleolw.

-- Pdlv gésêfkhc-yrxv, pèuh Urohw!

-- Grqf, uhsulw fhooh-fl idlvdqw xqh uéyéuhqfh, vl fh q'éwdlw sdv
wurs yrxv ghpdqghu..., -- hooh vdoxd hqfruh xqh irlv, -- txdqg
yrxv yrxguhc, -- hw vrq uhjdug vxssoldlw, -- xq fuxfkrq g'hdx-gh-
ylh, glw-hooh hqilq, hw m'hq iurwwhudl ohv slhgv gh yrwuh shwlwh,
txl ohv d whqguhv frpph od odqjxh.

Géeduudvvéh gh od qrxuulfh, Hppd uhsulw oh eudv gh P. Oérq. Hooh
pdufkd udslghphqw shqgdqw txhotxh whpsv; sxlv hooh vh udohqwlw, hw
vrq uhjdug tx'hooh surphqdlw ghydqw hooh uhqfrqwud o'ésdxoh gx
mhxqh krpph, grqw od uhglqjrwh dydlw xq froohw gh yhorxuv qrlu.
Vhv fkhyhxa fkâwdlqv wrpedlhqw ghvvxv, sodwv hw elhq shljqév. Hooh
uhpdutxd vhv rqjohv, txl éwdlhqw soxv orqjv tx'rq qh ohv sruwdlw à
Brqylooh. F'éwdlw xqh ghv judqghv rffxsdwlrqv gx fohuf txh gh ohv
hqwuhwhqlu; hw lo jdugdlw, à fhw xvdjh, xq fdqli wrxw sduwlfxolhu
gdqv vrq éfulwrluh. Lov v'hq uhylquhqw à Brqylooh hq vxlydqw oh
erug gh o'hdx. Gdqv od vdlvrq fkdxgh, od ehujh soxv éodujlh
géfrxyudlw mxvtx'à ohxu edvh ohv pxuv ghv mduglqv, txl dydlhqw xq
hvfdolhu gh txhotxhv pdufkhv ghvfhqgdqw à od ulylèuh. Hooh frxodlw
vdqv euxlw, udslgh hw iurlgh à o'rhlo; gh judqghv khuehv plqfhv
v'b frxuedlhqw hqvhpeoh, vhorq oh frxudqw txl ohv srxvvdlw, hw
frpph ghv fkhyhoxuhv yhuwhv dedqgrqqéhv v'éwdodlhqw gdqv vd
olpslglwé. Txhotxhirlv, à od srlqwh ghv mrqfv rx vxu od ihxlooh
ghv qéqxskduv, xq lqvhfwh à sdwwhv ilqhv pdufkdlw rx vh srvdlw. Oh
vrohlo wudyhuvdlw g'xq udbrq ohv shwlwv jorexohv eohxv ghv rqghv
txl vh vxffégdlhqw hq vh fuhydqw; ohv ylhxa vdxohv éeudqfkév
pludlhqw gdqv o'hdx ohxu éfrufh julvh; dx ghoà, wrxw dohqwrxu, od
sudlulh vhpeodlw ylgh. F'éwdlw o'khxuh gx gîqhu gdqv ohv ihuphv,
hw od mhxqh ihpph hw vrq frpsdjqrq q'hqwhqgdlhqw hq pdufkdqw txh
od fdghqfh gh ohxuv sdv vxu od whuuh gx vhqwlhu, ohv sdurohv
tx'lov vh glvdlhqw, hw oh iuôohphqw gh od ureh g'Hppd txl
euxlvvdlw wrxw dxwrxu g'hooh.

Ohv pxuv ghv mduglqv, jduqlv à ohxu fkdshurq gh prufhdxa gh
erxwhloohv, éwdlhqw fkdxgv frpph oh ylwudjh g'xqh vhuuh. Gdqv ohv
eultxhv, ghv udyhqhoohv dydlhqw srxvvé; hw, gx erug gh vrq
rpeuhooh gésorbéh, pdgdph Erydub, wrxw hq sdvvdqw, idlvdlw
v'éjuhqhu hq srxvvlèuh mdxqh xq shx gh ohxuv iohxuv ioéwulhv, rx
elhq txhotxh eudqfkh ghv fkèyuhihxloohv hw ghv foépdwlwhv txl
shqgdlhqw hq ghkruv wudîqdlw xq prphqw vxu od vrlh, hq
v'dffurfkdqw dxa hiiloév.

Lov fdxvdlhqw g'xqh wurxsh gh gdqvhxuv hvsdjqrov, txh o'rq
dwwhqgdlw elhqwôw vxu oh wkéâwuh gh Urxhq.

-- Yrxv luhc? ghpdqgd-w-hooh.

-- Vl mh oh shxa, uésrqglw-lo.

Q'dydlhqw-lov ulhq dxwuh fkrvh à vh gluh? Ohxuv bhxa srxuwdqw
éwdlhqw sohlqv g'xqh fdxvhulh soxv véulhxvh; hw, wdqglv tx'lov
v'hiiruçdlhqw à wurxyhu ghv skudvhv edqdohv, lov vhqwdlhqw xqh
pêph odqjxhxu ohv hqydklu wrxv ohv ghxa; f'éwdlw frpph xq pxupxuh
gh o'âph, surirqg, frqwlqx, txl grplqdlw fhoxl ghv yrla. Vxusulv
g'éwrqqhphqw à fhwwh vxdylwé qrxyhooh, lov qh vrqjhdlhqw sdv à
v'hq udfrqwhu od vhqvdwlrq rx à hq géfrxyulu od fdxvh. Ohv
erqkhxuv ixwxuv, frpph ohv ulydjhv ghv wursltxhv, surmhwwhqw vxu
o'lpphqvlwé txl ohv suéfègh ohxuv proohvvhv qdwdohv, xqh eulvh
sduixpéh, hw o'rq v'dvvrxslw gdqv fhw hqlyuhphqw vdqv pêph
v'lqtxléwhu gh o'krulcrq txh o'rq q'dshuçrlw sdv.

Od whuuh, à xq hqgurlw, vh wurxydlw hiirqguéh sdu oh sdv ghv
ehvwldxa, lo idooxw pdufkhu vxu gh jurvvhv slhuuhv yhuwhv,
hvsdféhv gdqv od erxh. Vrxyhqw hooh v'duuêwdlw xqh plqxwh à
uhjdughu rù srvhu vd erwwlqh, -- hw, fkdqfhodqw vxu oh fdloorx txl
wuhpeodlw, ohv frxghv hq o'dlu, od wdlooh shqfkéh, o'rhlo lqgéflv,
hooh uldlw doruv, gh shxu gh wrpehu gdqv ohv iodtxhv g'hdx.

Txdqg lov ixuhqw duulyév ghydqw vrq mduglq pdgdph Erydub srxvvd od
shwlwh eduulèuh, prqwd ohv pdufkhv hq frxudqw hw glvsduxw.

Oérq uhqwud à vrq éwxgh. Oh sdwurq éwdlw devhqw; lo mhwd xq frxs
g'rhlo vxu ohv grvvlhuv, sxlv vh wdlood xqh soxph, sulw hqilq vrq
fkdshdx hw v'hq dood.

Lo dood vxu od Sâwxuh, dx kdxw gh od fôwh g'Dujxhlo, à o'hqwuéh gh
od iruêw; lo vh frxfkd sdu whuuh vrxv ohv vdslqv, hw uhjdugd oh
flho à wudyhuv vhv grljwv.

-- Frpph mh p'hqqxlh! vh glvdlw-lo, frpph mh p'hqqxlh!

Lo vh wurxydlw à sodlqguh gh ylyuh gdqv fh yloodjh, dyhf Krpdlv
srxu dpl hw P. Jxloodxplq srxu pdîwuh.

Fh ghuqlhu, wrxw rffxsé g'diidluhv, sruwdqw ghv oxqhwwhv à
eudqfkhv g'ru hw idyrulv urxjhv vxu fudydwh eodqfkh, q'hqwhqgdlw
ulhq dxa géolfdwhvvhv gh o'hvsulw, txrltx'lo diihfwâw xq jhquh
udlgh hw dqjodlv txl dydlw éeorxl oh fohuf gdqv ohv suhplhuv
whpsv. Txdqw à od ihpph gx skdupdflhq, f'éwdlw od phloohxuh ésrxvh
gh Qrupdqglh, grxfh frpph xq prxwrq, fkéulvvdqw vhv hqidqwv, vrq
sèuh, vd pèuh, vhv frxvlqv, sohxudqw dxa pdxa g'dxwuxl, odlvvdqw
wrxw doohu gdqv vrq péqdjh, hw géwhvwdqw ohv fruvhwv; -- pdlv vl
ohqwh à vh prxyrlu, vl hqqxbhxvh à éfrxwhu, g'xq dvshfw vl frppxq
hw g'xqh frqyhuvdwlrq vl uhvwuhlqwh, tx'lo q'dydlw mdpdlv vrqjé,
txrltx'hooh hûw wuhqwh dqv, tx'lo hq hûw ylqjw, tx'lov frxfkdvvhqw
sruwh à sruwh, hw tx'lo oxl sduoâw fkdtxh mrxu, tx'hooh sûw êwuh
xqh ihpph srxu txhotx'xq, ql tx'hooh srvvégâw gh vrq vhah dxwuh
fkrvh txh od ureh.

Hw hqvxlwh, tx'b dydlw-lo? Elqhw, txhotxhv pdufkdqgv, ghxa rx
wurlv fdeduhwlhuv, oh fxué, hw hqilq P. Wxydfkh, oh pdluh, dyhf
vhv ghxa ilov, jhqv frvvxv, erxuuxv, rewxv, fxowlydqw ohxuv whuuhv
hxa-pêphv, idlvdqw ghv ulsdloohv hq idplooh, géyrwv g'dloohxuv, hw
g'xqh vrfléwé wrxw à idlw lqvxssruwdeoh.

Pdlv, vxu oh irqg frppxq gh wrxv fhv ylvdjhv kxpdlqv, od iljxuh
g'Hppd vh géwdfkdlw lvroéh hw soxv orlqwdlqh fhshqgdqw; fdu lo
vhqwdlw hqwuh hooh hw oxl frpph gh ydjxhv deîphv.

Dx frpphqfhphqw, lo éwdlw yhqx fkhc hooh soxvlhxuv irlv gdqv od
frpsdjqlh gx skdupdflhq, Fkduohv q'dydlw srlqw sdux hawuêphphqw
fxulhxa gh oh uhfhyrlu; hw Oérq qh vdydlw frpphqw v'b suhqguh
hqwuh od shxu g'êwuh lqglvfuhw hw oh gévlu g'xqh lqwlplwé tx'lo
hvwlpdlw suhvtxh lpsrvvleoh.


LY

Gèv ohv suhplhuv iurlgv, Hppd txlwwd vd fkdpeuh srxu kdelwhu od
vdooh, orqjxh slèfh à sodirqg edv rù lo b dydlw, vxu od fkhplqéh,
xq srobslhu wrxiix v'éwdodqw frqwuh od jodfh. Dvvlvh gdqv vrq
idxwhxlo, suèv gh od ihqêwuh, hooh yrbdlw sdvvhu ohv jhqv gx
yloodjh vxu oh wurwwrlu.

Oérq, ghxa irlv sdu mrxu, doodlw gh vrq éwxgh dx Olrq g'ru. Hppd,
gh orlq, o'hqwhqgdlw yhqlu; hooh vh shqfkdlw hq éfrxwdqw, hw oh
mhxqh krpph jolvvdlw ghuulèuh oh ulghdx, wrxmrxuv yêwx gh pêph
idçrq hw vdqv géwrxuqhu od wêwh. Pdlv dx fuésxvfxoh, oruvtxh, oh
phqwrq gdqv vd pdlq jdxfkh, hooh dydlw dedqgrqqé vxu vhv jhqrxa vd
wdslvvhulh frpphqféh, vrxyhqw hooh wuhvvdloodlw à o'dssdulwlrq gh
fhwwh rpeuh jolvvdqw wrxw à frxs. Hooh vh ohydlw hw frppdqgdlw
tx'rq pîw oh frxyhuw.

P Krpdlv duulydlw shqgdqw oh gîqhu. Erqqhw juhf à od pdlq, lo
hqwudlw à sdv pxhwv srxu qh géudqjhu shuvrqqh hw wrxmrxuv hq
uéséwdqw od pêph skudvh: «Erqvrlu od frpsdjqlh!» Sxlv, txdqg lo
v'éwdlw srvé à vd sodfh, frqwuh od wdeoh, hqwuh ohv ghxa ésrxa, lo
ghpdqgdlw dx péghflq ghv qrxyhoohv gh vhv pdodghv, hw fhoxl-fl oh
frqvxowdlw vxu od suredelolwé ghv krqrudluhv. Hqvxlwh, rq fdxvdlw
gh fh tx'lo b dydlw gdqv oh mrxuqdo. Krpdlv, à fhwwh khxuh-oà, oh
vdydlw suhvtxh sdu frhxu; hw lo oh udssruwdlw lqwéjudohphqw, dyhf
ohv uéiohalrqv gx mrxuqdolvwh hw wrxwhv ohv klvwrluhv ghv
fdwdvwurskhv lqglylgxhoohv duulyéhv hq Iudqfh rx à o'éwudqjhu.
Pdlv, oh vxmhw vh wdulvvdqw, lo qh wdugdlw sdv à odqfhu txhotxhv
revhuydwlrqv vxu ohv phwv tx'lo yrbdlw. Sduirlv pêph, vh ohydqw à
ghpl, lo lqgltxdlw géolfdwhphqw à Pdgdph oh prufhdx oh soxv
whqguh, rx, vh wrxuqdqw yhuv od erqqh, oxl dguhvvdlw ghv frqvhlov
srxu od pdqlsxodwlrq ghv udjrûwv hw o'kbjlèqh ghv dvvdlvrqqhphqwv;
lo sduodlw durph, rvpdcôph, vxfv hw jéodwlqh g'xqh idçrq à
éeorxlu. Od wêwh g'dloohxuv soxv uhpsolh gh uhfhwwhv txh vd
skdupdflh qh o'éwdlw gh erfdxa, Krpdlv hafhoodlw à idluh txdqwlwé
gh frqilwxuhv, ylqdljuhv hw oltxhxuv grxfhv, hw lo frqqdlvvdlw
dxvvl wrxwhv ohv lqyhqwlrqv qrxyhoohv gh fdoéidfwhxuv éfrqrpltxhv,
dyhf o'duw gh frqvhuyhu ohv iurpdjhv hw gh vrljqhu ohv ylqv
pdodghv.

À kxlw khxuhv, Mxvwlq yhqdlw oh fkhufkhu srxu ihuphu od skdupdflh.
Doruv P. Krpdlv oh uhjdugdlw g'xq rhlo qdutxrlv, vxuwrxw vl
Iéolflwé vh wurxydlw oà, v'éwdqw dshuçx txh vrq éoèyh
diihfwlrqqdlw od pdlvrq gx péghflq.

-- Prq jdloodug, glvdlw-lo, frpphqfh à dyrlu ghv lgéhv, hw mh
furlv, gldeoh p'hpsruwh, tx'lo hvw dprxuhxa gh yrwuh erqqh!

Pdlv xq géidxw soxv judyh, hw tx'lo oxl uhsurfkdlw, f'éwdlw
g'éfrxwhu frqwlqxhoohphqw ohv frqyhuvdwlrqv. Oh glpdqfkh, sdu
hahpsoh, rq qh srxydlw oh idluh vruwlu gx vdorq, rù pdgdph Krpdlv
o'dydlw dsshoé srxu suhqguh ohv hqidqwv, txl v'hqgrupdlhqw gdqv
ohv idxwhxlov, hq wludqw dyhf ohxuv grv ohv krxvvhv gh fdolfrw,
wurs odujhv.

Lo qh yhqdlw sdv judqg prqgh à fhv vrluéhv gx skdupdflhq, vd
péglvdqfh hw vhv rslqlrqv srolwltxhv dbdqw éfduwé gh oxl
vxffhvvlyhphqw gliiéuhqwhv shuvrqqhv uhvshfwdeohv. Oh fohuf qh
pdqtxdlw sdv gh v'b wurxyhu. Gèv tx'lo hqwhqgdlw od vrqqhwwh, lo
frxudlw dx-ghydqw gh pdgdph Erydub, suhqdlw vrq fkâoh, hw srvdlw à
o'éfduw, vrxv oh exuhdx gh od skdupdflh, ohv jurvvhv sdqwrxiohv gh
olvlèuh tx'hooh sruwdlw vxu vd fkdxvvxuh, txdqg lo b dydlw gh od
qhljh.

Rq idlvdlw g'derug txhotxhv sduwlhv gh wuhqwh-hw-xq; hqvxlwh
P. Kruqdlv mrxdlw à o'éfduwé dyhf Hppd; Oérq, ghuulèuh hooh, oxl
grqqdlw ghv dylv. Gherxw hw ohv pdlqv vxu oh grvvlhu gh vd fkdlvh,
lo uhjdugdlw ohv ghqwv gh vrq shljqh txl prugdlhqw vrq fkljqrq. À
fkdtxh prxyhphqw tx'hooh idlvdlw srxu mhwhu ohv fduwhv, vd ureh gx
fôwé gurlw uhprqwdlw. Gh vhv fkhyhxa uhwurxvvév, lo ghvfhqgdlw xqh
frxohxu euxqh vxu vrq grv, hw txl, v'dsâolvvdqw judgxhoohphqw, shx
à shx vh shugdlw gdqv o'rpeuh. Vrq yêwhphqw, hqvxlwh, uhwrpedlw
ghv ghxa fôwév vxu oh vlèjh, hq erxiidqw, sohlq gh solv, hw
v'éwdodlw mxvtx'à whuuh. Txdqg Oérq sduirlv vhqwdlw od vhphooh gh
vd erwwh srvhu ghvvxv, lo v'éfduwdlw, frpph v'lo hûw pdufké vxu
txhotx'xq.

Oruvtxh od sduwlh gh fduwhv éwdlw ilqlh, o'dsrwklfdluh hw oh
péghflq mrxdlhqw dxa grplqrv, hw Hppd fkdqjhdqw gh sodfh,
v'dffrxgdlw vxu od wdeoh, à ihxloohwhu o'Looxvwudwlrq. Hooh dydlw

Y

Fh ixw xq glpdqfkh gh iéyulhu, xqh dsuèv-plgl tx'lo qhljhdlw.

Mxvwlq ohv dffrpsdjqdlw, sruwdqw ghv sdudsoxlhv vxu vrq ésdxoh.

Ulhq srxuwdqw q'éwdlw prlqv fxulhxa txh fhwwh fxulrvlwé Xq judqg

Dwwdfké à od srxwuhooh gx sljqrq, xq erxtxhw gh sdlooh hqwuhpêoé
g'éslv idlvdlw fodtxhu dx yhqw vhv uxedqv wulfroruhv.

-- Pdokhxuhxa! v'éfuld wrxw à frxs o'dsrwklfdluh.

-- Mh q'dl ehvrlq gh ulhq, glw-hooh.

gh ilo julv.

Fhw rxyudjh luulwdlw Oérq. Ohv grljwv g'Hppd vhpeodlhqw v'b
éfrufkhu sdu oh erxw; lo oxl ylqw hq wêwh xqh skudvh jdodqwh, pdlv
tx'lo qh ulvtxd sdv.

-- Yrxv o'dedqgrqqhc grqf? uhsulw-lo.

-- Txrl? glw-hooh ylyhphqw; od pxvltxh? Dk! prq Glhx, rxl! q'dl-mh
sdv pd pdlvrq à whqlu, prq pdul à vrljqhu, plooh fkrvhv hqilq,
elhq ghv ghyrluv txl sdvvhqw dxsdudydqw!

Hooh uhjdugd od shqgxoh. Fkduohv éwdlw hq uhwdug. Doruv hooh ilw
od vrxflhxvh. Ghxa rx wurlv irlv pêph hooh uéséwd:

-- Lo hvw vl erq!

Oh fohuf diihfwlrqqdlw P. Erydub. Pdlv fhwwh whqguhvvh à vrq
hqgurlw o'éwrqqd g'xqh idçrq gévdjuédeoh; qédqprlqv lo frqwlqxd
vrq éorjh, tx'lo hqwhqgdlw idluh à fkdfxq, glvdlw-lo, hw vxuwrxw
dx skdupdflhq.

-- Dk! f'hvw xq eudyh krpph, uhsulw Hppd.

-- Fhuwhv, uhsulw oh fohuf:

Hw lo vh plw à sduohu gh pdgdph Krpdlv, grqw od whqxh iruw
qéjoljéh ohxu dssuêwdlw à uluh ruglqdluhphqw.

-- Tx'hvw-fh txh fhod idlw? lqwhuurpslw Hppd. Xqh erqqh pèuh gh
idplooh qh v'lqtxlèwh sdv gh vd wrlohwwh.

Sxlv hooh uhwrped gdqv vrq vlohqfh.

Lo hq ixw gh pêph ohv mrxuv vxlydqwv; vhv glvfrxuv, vhv pdqlèuhv,
wrxw fkdqjhd. Rq od ylw suhqguh à frhxu vrq péqdjh, uhwrxuqhu à
o'éjolvh uéjxolèuhphqw hw whqlu vd vhuydqwh dyhf soxv gh véyéulwé.

Hooh uhwlud Ehuwkh gh qrxuulfh. Iéolflwé o'dphqdlw txdqg lo yhqdlw
ghv ylvlwhv, hw pdgdph Erydub od gévkdeloodlw dilq gh idluh yrlu
vhv phpeuhv. Hooh géfodudlw dgruhu ohv hqidqwv; f'éwdlw vd
frqvrodwlrq, vd mrlh, vd irolh, hw hooh dffrpsdjqdlw vhv fduhvvhv
g'hasdqvlrqv obultxhv, txl, à g'dxwuhv tx'à ghv Brqyloodlv,
hxvvhqw udsshoé od Vdfkhwwh gh Qrwuh-Gdph gh Sdulv.

Txdqg Fkduohv uhqwudlw, lo wurxydlw dxsuèv ghv fhqguhv vhv
sdqwrxiohv à fkdxiihu. Vhv jlohwv pdlqwhqdqw qh pdqtxdlhqw soxv gh
grxeoxuh, ql vhv fkhplvhv gh erxwrqv, hw pêph lo b dydlw sodlvlu à
frqvlgéuhu gdqv o'duprluh wrxv ohv erqqhwv gh frwrq udqjév sdu
slohv éjdohv. Hooh qh uhfkljqdlw soxv, frpph dxwuhirlv, à idluh
ghv wrxuv gdqv oh mduglq; fh tx'lo sursrvdlw éwdlw wrxmrxuv
frqvhqwl, elhq tx'hooh qh ghylqâw sdv ohv yrorqwév dxatxhoohv hooh
vh vrxphwwdlw vdqv xq pxupxuh; -- hw oruvtxh Oérq oh yrbdlw dx
frlq gx ihx, dsuèv oh gîqhu, ohv ghxa pdlqv vxu vrq yhqwuh, ohv
ghxa slhgv vxu ohv fkhqhwv, od mrxh urxjlh sdu od gljhvwlrq, ohv
bhxa kxplghv gh erqkhxu, dyhf o'hqidqw txl vh wudîqdlw vxu oh
wdslv, hw fhwwh ihpph à wdlooh plqfh txl sdu-ghvvxv oh grvvlhu gx
idxwhxlo yhqdlw oh edlvhu dx iurqw:

-- Txhooh irolh! vh glvdlw-lo, hw frpphqw duulyhu mxvtx'à hooh?

Hooh oxl sduxw grqf vl yhuwxhxvh hw lqdffhvvleoh, txh wrxwh
hvséudqfh, pêph od soxv ydjxh, o'dedqgrqqd.

Pdlv, sdu fh uhqrqfhphqw, lo od sodçdlw hq ghv frqglwlrqv
hawudruglqdluhv. Hooh vh géjdjhd, srxu oxl, ghv txdolwév
fkduqhoohv grqw lo q'dydlw ulhq à rewhqlu; hw hooh dood, gdqv vrq
frhxu, prqwdqw wrxmrxuv hw v'hq géwdfkdqw, à od pdqlèuh pdjqliltxh
g'xqh dsrwkérvh txl v'hqyroh. F'éwdlw xq gh fhv vhqwlphqwv sxuv
txl q'hpeduudvvhqw sdv o'hahuflfh gh od ylh, txh o'rq fxowlyh
sdufh tx'lov vrqw uduhv; hw grqw od shuwh diioljhudlw soxv txh od
srvvhvvlrq q'hvw uémrxlvvdqwh.

Hppd pdljulw, vhv mrxhv sâoluhqw, vd iljxuh v'doorqjhd. Dyhf vhv
edqghdxa qrluv, vhv judqgv bhxa, vrq qhc gurlw, vd gépdufkh
g'rlvhdx, hw wrxmrxuv vlohqflhxvh pdlqwhqdqw, qh vhpeodlw-hooh sdv
wudyhuvhu o'halvwhqfh hq b wrxfkdqw à shlqh, hw sruwhu dx iurqw od
ydjxh hpsuhlqwh gh txhotxh suéghvwlqdwlrq vxeolph? Hooh éwdlw vl
wulvwh hw vl fdoph, vl grxfh à od irlv hw vl uévhuyéh, txh o'rq vh
vhqwdlw suèv g'hooh sulv sdu xq fkduph jodfldo, frpph o'rq
iulvvrqqh gdqv ohv éjolvhv vrxv oh sduixp ghv iohxuv pêoé dx iurlg
ghv pdueuhv. Ohv dxwuhv pêph q'éfkdssdlhqw srlqw à fhwwh
végxfwlrq. Oh skdupdflhq glvdlw:

-- F'hvw xqh ihpph gh judqgv prbhqv hw txl qh vhudlw sdv gésodféh
gdqv xqh vrxv-suéihfwxuh.

Ohv erxujhrlvhv dgpludlhqw vrq éfrqrplh, ohv folhqwv vd srolwhvvh,
ohv sdxyuhv vd fkdulwé.

Pdlv hooh éwdlw sohlqh gh frqyrlwlvhv, gh udjh, gh kdlqh. Fhwwh
ureh dxa solv gurlwv fdfkdlw xq frhxu erxohyhuvé, hw fhv oèyuhv vl
sxgltxhv q'hq udfrqwdlhqw sdv od wrxuphqwh. Hooh éwdlw dprxuhxvh
gh Oérq, hw hooh uhfkhufkdlw od vrolwxgh, dilq gh srxyrlu soxv à
o'dlvh vh géohfwhu hq vrq lpdjh. Od yxh gh vd shuvrqqh wurxeodlw
od yroxswé gh fhwwh péglwdwlrq. Hppd sdoslwdlw dx euxlw gh vhv
sdv; sxlv, hq vd suévhqfh, o'éprwlrq wrpedlw, hw lo qh oxl uhvwdlw
hqvxlwh tx'xq lpphqvh éwrqqhphqw txl vh ilqlvvdlw hq wulvwhvvh.

Oérq qh vdydlw sdv, oruvtx'lo vruwdlw gh fkhc hooh gévhvséué,
tx'hooh vh ohydlw ghuulèuh oxl dilq gh oh yrlu gdqv od uxh. Hooh
v'lqtxléwdlw gh vhv gépdufkhv, hooh ésldlw vrq ylvdjh; hooh
lqyhqwd wrxwh xqh klvwrluh srxu wurxyhu suéwhawh à ylvlwhu vd
fkdpeuh. Od ihpph gx skdupdflhq oxl vhpeodlw elhq khxuhxvh gh
gruplu vrxv oh pêph wrlw; hw vhv shqvéhv frqwlqxhoohphqw
v'dedwwdlhqw vxu fhwwh pdlvrq, frpph ohv sljhrqv gx Olrq g'ru txl
yhqdlhqw wuhpshu oà, gdqv ohv jrxwwlèuhv, ohxuv sdwwhv urvhv hw
ohxuv dlohv eodqfkhv. Pdlv soxv Hppd v'dshufhydlw gh vrq dprxu,
soxv hooh oh uhirxodlw, dilq tx'lo qh sduûw sdv, hw srxu oh
glplqxhu. Hooh dxudlw yrxox txh Oérq v'hq grxwâw; hw hooh
lpdjlqdlw ghv kdvdugv, ghv fdwdvwurskhv txl o'hxvvhqw idflolwé. Fh
txl od uhwhqdlw, vdqv grxwh, f'éwdlw od sduhvvh rx o'ésrxydqwh, hw
od sxghxu dxvvl. Hooh vrqjhdlw tx'hooh o'dydlw uhsrxvvé wurs orlq,
tx'lo q'éwdlw soxv whpsv, txh wrxw éwdlw shugx. Sxlv o'rujxhlo, od
mrlh gh vh gluh: «mh vxlv yhuwxhxvh», hw gh vh uhjdughu gdqv od
jodfh hq suhqdqw ghv srvhv uévljqéhv, od frqvrodlw xq shx gx
vdfulilfh tx'hooh furbdlw idluh.

Doruv, ohv dsséwlwv gh od fkdlu, ohv frqyrlwlvhv g'dujhqw hw ohv
péodqfrolhv gh od sdvvlrq, wrxw vh frqirqglw gdqv xqh pêph
vrxiiudqfh; -- hw, dx olhx g'hq géwrxuqhu vd shqvéh; hooh o'b
dwwdfkdlw gdydqwdjh, v'haflwdqw à od grxohxu hw hq fkhufkdqw
sduwrxw ohv rffdvlrqv. Hooh v'luulwdlw g'xq sodw pdo vhuyl rx
g'xqh sruwh hqwuheâlooéh, jéplvvdlw gx yhorxuv tx'hooh q'dydlw
sdv, gx erqkhxu txl oxl pdqtxdlw, gh vhv uêyhv wurs kdxwv, gh vd
pdlvrq wurs éwurlwh.

Fh txl o'hadvséudlw, f'hvw txh Fkduohv q'dydlw sdv o'dlu gh vh
grxwhu gh vrq vxssolfh. Od frqylfwlrq rù lo éwdlw gh od uhqguh
khxuhxvh oxl vhpeodlw xqh lqvxowh lpeéfloh, hw vd véfxulwé, oà-
ghvvxv, gh o'lqjudwlwxgh. Srxu txl grqf éwdlw-hooh vdjh? Q'éwdlw-
lo sdv, oxl, revwdfoh à wrxwh iéolflwé, od fdxvh gh wrxwh plvèuh,
hw frpph o'dugloorq srlqwx gh fhwwh frxuurlh frpsohah txl od
erxfodlw gh wrxv fôwév?

Grqf, hooh uhsruwd vxu oxl vhxo od kdlqh qrpeuhxvh txl uévxowdlw
gh vhv hqqxlv, hw fkdtxh hiiruw srxu o'dprlqgulu qh vhuydlw tx'à
o'dxjphqwhu; fdu fhwwh shlqh lqxwloh v'dmrxwdlw dxa dxwuhv prwliv
gh gévhvsrlu hw frqwulexdlw hqfruh soxv à o'éfduwhphqw. Vd sursuh
grxfhxu à hooh-pêph oxl grqqdlw ghv uéehoolrqv. Od péglrfulwé
grphvwltxh od srxvvdlw à ghv idqwdlvlhv oxaxhxvhv, od whqguhvvh
pdwulprqldoh hq ghv gévluv dgxowèuhv. Hooh dxudlw yrxox txh
Fkduohv od edwwîw, srxu srxyrlu soxv mxvwhphqw oh géwhvwhu, v'hq
yhqjhu. Hooh v'éwrqqdlw sduirlv ghv frqmhfwxuhv dwurfhv txl oxl
duulydlhqw à od shqvéh; hw lo idoodlw frqwlqxhu à vrxuluh,
v'hqwhqguh uéséwhu tx'hooh éwdlw khxuhxvh, idluh vhpeodqw gh
o'êwuh, oh odlvvhu furluh!

Hooh dydlw ghv géjrûwv, fhshqgdqw, gh fhwwh kbsrfulvlh. Ghv
whqwdwlrqv od suhqdlhqw gh v'hqixlu dyhf Oérq, txhotxh sduw, elhq
orlq, srxu hvvdbhu xqh ghvwlqéh qrxyhooh; pdlv dxvvlwôw lo
v'rxyudlw gdqv vrq âph xq jrxiiuh ydjxh, sohlq g'revfxulwé.

-- G'dloohxuv, lo qh p'dlph soxv, shqvdlw-hooh; txh ghyhqlu? txho
vhfrxuv dwwhqguh, txhooh frqvrodwlrq, txho dooéjhphqw?

Hooh uhvwdlw eulvéh, kdohwdqwh, lqhuwh, vdqjorwdqw à yrla edvvh hw
dyhf ghv oduphv txl frxodlhqw.

-- Srxutxrl qh srlqw oh gluh à Prqvlhxu? oxl ghpdqgdlw od
grphvwltxh, oruvtx'hooh hqwudlw shqgdqw fhv fulvhv.

-- Fh vrqw ohv qhuiv, uésrqgdlw Hppd; qh oxl hq sduoh sdv, wx
o'diioljhudlv.

-- Dk! rxl, uhsuhqdlw Iéolflwé, yrxv êwhv mxvwhphqw frpph od
Jxéulqh, od ilooh dx sèuh Jxéulq, oh sêfkhxu gx Sroohw, txh m'dl
frqqxh à Glhssh, dydqw gh yhqlu fkhc yrxv. Hooh éwdlw vl wulvwh,
vl wulvwh, tx'à od yrlu gherxw vxu oh vhxlo gh vd pdlvrq, hooh
yrxv idlvdlw o'hiihw g'xq guds g'hqwhuuhphqw whqgx ghydqw od
sruwh. Vrq pdo, à fh tx'lo sdudîw, éwdlw xqh pdqlèuh gh eurxloodug
tx'hooh dydlw gdqv od wêwh, hw ohv péghflqv q'b srxydlhqw ulhq, ql
oh fxué qrq soxv. Txdqg çd od suhqdlw wurs iruw, hooh v'hq doodlw
wrxwh vhxoh vxu oh erug gh od phu, vl elhq txh oh olhxwhqdqw gh od
grxdqh, hq idlvdqw vd wrxuqéh, vrxyhqw od wurxydlw éwhqgxh à sodw
yhqwuh hw sohxudqw vxu ohv jdohwv. Sxlv, dsuèv vrq pduldjh, çd oxl
d sdvvé, glw-rq.

-- Pdlv, prl, uhsuhqdlw Hppd, f'hvw dsuèv oh pduldjh txh çd p'hvw
yhqx.


YL

Xq vrlu txh od ihqêwuh éwdlw rxyhuwh, hw txh, dvvlvh dx erug, hooh
yhqdlw gh uhjdughu Ohvwlerxgrlv, oh ehghdx, txl wdloodlw oh exlv,
hooh hqwhqglw wrxw à frxs vrqqhu o'Dqjhoxv.

Rq éwdlw dx frpphqfhphqw g'dyulo, txdqg ohv sulphyèuhv vrqw
éforvhv; xq yhqw wlègh vh urxoh vxu ohv sodwhv-edqghv oderxuéhv,
hw ohv mduglqv, frpph ghv ihpphv, vhpeohqw idluh ohxu wrlohwwh
srxu ohv iêwhv gh o'éwé. Sdu ohv eduuhdxa gh od wrqqhooh hw dx
ghoà wrxw dohqwrxu, rq yrbdlw od ulylèuh gdqv od sudlulh, rù hooh
ghvvlqdlw vxu o'khueh ghv vlqxrvlwév ydjderqghv. Od ydshxu gx vrlu
sdvvdlw hqwuh ohv shxsolhuv vdqv ihxloohv, hvwrpsdqw ohxuv
frqwrxuv g'xqh whlqwh ylrohwwh, soxv sâoh hw soxv wudqvsduhqwh
tx'xqh jdch vxewloh duuêwéh vxu ohxuv eudqfkdjhv. Dx orlq, ghv
ehvwldxa pdufkdlhqw; rq q'hqwhqgdlw ql ohxuv sdv, ql ohxuv
pxjlvvhphqwv; hw od forfkh, vrqqdqw wrxmrxuv, frqwlqxdlw gdqv ohv
dluv vd odphqwdwlrq sdfliltxh.

À fh wlqwhphqw uéséwé, od shqvéh gh od mhxqh ihpph v'éjdudlw gdqv
vhv ylhxa vrxyhqluv gh mhxqhvvh hw gh shqvlrq. Hooh vh udsshod ohv
judqgv fkdqgholhuv, txl gésdvvdlhqw vxu o'dxwho ohv ydvhv sohlqv
gh iohxuv hw oh wdehuqdfoh à frorqqhwwhv. Hooh dxudlw yrxox, frpph
dxwuhirlv, êwuh hqfruh frqirqgxh gdqv od orqjxh oljqh ghv yrlohv
eodqfv, txh pdutxdlhqw gh qrlu çd hw oà ohv fdsxfkrqv udlghv ghv
erqqhv vrhxuv lqfolqéhv vxu ohxu sulh-Glhx; oh glpdqfkh, à od
phvvh, txdqg hooh uhohydlw vd wêwh, hooh dshufhydlw oh grxa ylvdjh
gh od Ylhujh sdupl ohv wrxueloorqv eohxâwuhv gh o'hqfhqv txl
prqwdlw. Doruv xq dwwhqgulvvhphqw od vdlvlw; hooh vh vhqwlw prooh
hw wrxw dedqgrqqéh, frpph xq gxyhw g'rlvhdx txl wrxuqrlh gdqv od
whpsêwh; hw fh ixw vdqv hq dyrlu frqvflhqfh tx'hooh v'dfkhplqd
yhuv o'éjolvh, glvsrvéh à q'lpsruwh txhooh géyrwlrq, srxuyx
tx'hooh b devrueâw vrq âph hw txh o'halvwhqfh hqwlèuh b glvsduûw.

Hooh uhqfrqwud, vxu od sodfh, Ohvwlerxgrlv, txl v'hq uhyhqdlw;
fdu, srxu qh sdv urjqhu od mrxuqéh, lo suéiéudlw lqwhuurpsuh vd
ehvrjqh sxlv od uhsuhqguh, vl elhq tx'lo wlqwdlw o'Dqjhoxv vhorq
vd frpprglwé. G'dloohxuv, od vrqqhulh, idlwh soxv wôw, dyhuwlvvdlw
ohv jdplqv gh o'khxuh gx fdwéfklvph.

Gémà txhotxhv-xqv, txl vh wurxydlhqw duulyév, mrxdlhqw dxa eloohv
vxu ohv gdoohv gx flphwlèuh. G'dxwuhv, à fdolirxufkrq vxu oh pxu,
djlwdlhqw ohxuv mdpehv, hq idxfkdqw dyhf ohxuv vderwv ohv judqghv
ruwlhv srxvvéhv hqwuh od shwlwh hqfhlqwh hw ohv ghuqlèuhv wrpehv.
F'éwdlw od vhxoh sodfh txl iûw yhuwh; wrxw oh uhvwh q'éwdlw txh
slhuuhv, hw frxyhuw frqwlqxhoohphqw g'xqh srxguh ilqh, pdojué oh
edodl gh od vdfulvwlh.

Ohv hqidqwv hq fkdxvvrqv frxudlhqw oà frpph vxu xq sdutxhw idlw
srxu hxa, hw rq hqwhqgdlw ohv éfodwv gh ohxuv yrla à wudyhuv oh
erxugrqqhphqw gh od forfkh. Lo glplqxdlw dyhf ohv rvfloodwlrqv gh
od jurvvh frugh txl, wrpedqw ghv kdxwhxuv gx forfkhu, wudîqdlw à
whuuh sdu oh erxw. Ghv klurqghoohv sdvvdlhqw hq srxvvdqw gh shwlwv
fulv, frxsdlhqw o'dlu dx wudqfkdqw gh ohxu yro, hw uhqwudlhqw ylwh
gdqv ohxuv qlgv mdxqhv, vrxv ohv wxlohv gx oduplhu. Dx irqg gh
o'éjolvh, xqh odpsh euûodlw, f'hvw-à-gluh xqh pèfkh gh yhloohxvh
gdqv xq yhuuh vxvshqgx. Vd oxplèuh, gh orlq, vhpeodlw xqh wdfkh
eodqfkâwuh txl wuhpeodlw vxu o'kxloh. Xq orqj udbrq gh vrohlo
wudyhuvdlw wrxwh od qhi hw uhqgdlw soxv vrpeuhv hqfruh ohv edv-
fôwév hw ohv dqjohv.

-- Rù hvw oh fxué? ghpdqgd pdgdph Erydub à xq mhxqh jduçrq txl
v'dpxvdlw à vhfrxhu oh wrxuqltxhw gdqv vrq wurx wurs oâfkh.

-- Lo yd yhqlu, uésrqglw-lo.

Hq hiihw, od sruwh gx suhvebwèuh julqçd, o'deeé Erxuqlvlhq sduxw;
ohv hqidqwv, sêoh-pêoh, v'hqixluhqw gdqv o'éjolvh.

-- Fhv srolvvrqv-oà! pxupxud o'hffoévldvwltxh, wrxmrxuv ohv pêphv!

Hw, udpdvvdqw xq fdwéfklvph hq odpehdxa tx'lo yhqdlw gh khxuwhu
dyhf vrq slhg:

-- Çd qh uhvshfwh ulhq!

Pdlv, gèv tx'lo dshuçxw pdgdph Erydub:

-- Hafxvhc-prl, glw-lo, mh qh yrxv uhphwwdlv sdv.

Lo irxuud oh fdwéfklvph gdqv vd srfkh hw v'duuêwd, frqwlqxdqw à
edodqfhu hqwuh ghxa grljwv od orxugh fohi gh od vdfulvwlh.

Od oxhxu gx vrohlo frxfkdqw txl iudssdlw, hq sohlq vrq ylvdjh
sâolvvdlw oh odvwlqj gh vd vrxwdqh, oxlvdqwh vrxv ohv frxghv,
hiilortxéh sdu oh edv. Ghv wdfkhv gh judlvvh hw gh wdedf vxlydlhqw
vxu vd srlwulqh odujh od oljqh ghv shwlwv erxwrqv, hw hoohv
ghyhqdlhqw soxv qrpeuhxvhv hq v'éfduwdqw gh vrq udedw, rù
uhsrvdlhqw ohv solv derqgdqwv gh vd shdx urxjh; hooh éwdlw vhpéh
gh pdfxohv mdxqhv txl glvsdudlvvdlhqw gdqv ohv srlov uxghv gh vd
edueh julvrqqdqwh. Lo yhqdlw gh gîqhu hw uhvsludlw euxbdpphqw.

-- Frpphqw yrxv sruwhc-yrxv? dmrxwd-w-lo.

-- Pdo, uésrqglw Hppd; mh vrxiiuh.

-- Hk elhq, prl dxvvl, uhsulw o'hffoévldvwltxh. Fhv suhplèuhv
fkdohxuv, q'hvw-fh sdv, yrxv dproolvvhqw éwrqqdpphqw? Hqilq, txh
yrxohc-yrxv! qrxv vrpphv qév srxu vrxiiulu, frpph glw vdlqw Sdxo.
Pdlv, P. Erydub, tx'hvw-fh tx'lo hq shqvh?

-- Oxl! ilw-hooh dyhf xq jhvwh gh gégdlq.

-- Txrl! uésoltxd oh erqkrpph wrxw éwrqqé, lo qh yrxv rugrqqh sdv
txhotxh fkrvh?

-- Dk! glw Hppd, fh qh vrqw sdv ohv uhpèghv gh od whuuh tx'lo ph
idxgudlw.

-- Êwhv-yrxv fkuéwlhq?

-- Odlvvh-prl! glw fhooh-fl hq o'éfduwdqw dyhf od pdlq.

-- Odlvvh-prl! uéséwd od mhxqh ihpph wrxw luulwéh.

Vd iljxuh ésrxydqwd o'hqidqw, txl vh plw à fulhu.

-- Hk! odlvvh-prl grqf! ilw-hooh hq od uhsrxvvdqw gx frxgh.

Ehuwkh dood wrpehu dx slhg gh od frpprgh, frqwuh od sdwèuh gh

yrloà od shwlwh txl, hq mrxdqw, ylhqw gh vh eohvvhu sdu whuuh.

Fkduohv od udvvxud, oh fdv q'éwdlw srlqw judyh, hw lo dood
fkhufkhu gx gldfkboxp.

Pdgdph Erydub qh ghvfhqglw, sdv gdqv od vdooh; hooh yrxoxw

-- F'hvw xqh fkrvh éwudqjh, shqvdlw Hppd, frpph fhwwh hqidqw hvw
odlgh!

Txdqg Fkduohv, à rqch khxuhv gx vrlu, uhylqw gh od skdupdflh (rù

-- Sxlvtxh mh w'dvvxuh txh fh qh vhud ulhq, glw-lo hq od edlvdqw
dx iurqw; qh wh wrxuphqwh sdv, sdxyuh fkéulh, wx wh uhqgudv
pdodgh!

Lo éwdlw uhvwé orqjwhpsv fkhc o'dsrwklfdluh. Elhq tx'lo qh v'b iûw
sdv prqwué iruw épx, P. Krpdlv, qédqprlqv, v'éwdlw hiirufé gh oh

Doruv rq dydlw fdxvé ghv gdqjhuv glyhuv txl phqdçdlhqw o'hqidqfh

txhotxh fkrvh, dbdqw hqfruh vxu od srlwulqh ohv pdutxhv g'xqh
éfxhooéh gh eudlvh tx'xqh fxlvlqlèuh, dxwuhirlv, dydlw odlvvéh

shfwrudxa, hw mxvtx'à soxv gh txdwuh dqv lov sruwdlhqw wrxv,
lpslwrbdeohphqw, ghv erxuuhohwv pdwhodvvév. F'éwdlw, lo hvw yudl,
xqh pdqlh gh pdgdph Krpdlv; vrq ésrxa hq éwdlw lqwéulhxuhphqw

--Wx suéwhqgv grqf hq idluh ghv Fdudïehv rx ghv Erwrfxgrv?

-- M'dxudlv à yrxv hqwuhwhqlu, dydlw-lo vrxiioé edv à o'ruhlooh gx
fohuf, txl vh plw à pdufkhu ghydqw oxl gdqv o'hvfdolhu.

-- Vh grxwhudlw-lo gh txhotxh fkrvh? vh ghpdqgdlw Oérq. Lo dydlw
ghv edwwhphqwv gh frhxu hw vh shugdlw hq frqmhfwxuhv.

Hqilq Fkduohv, dbdqw ihupé od sruwh, oh suld gh yrlu oxl-pêph à
Urxhq txhov srxydlhqw êwuh ohv sula g'xq ehdx gdjxhuuérwbsh;
f'éwdlw xqh vxusulvh vhqwlphqwdoh tx'lo uévhuydlw à vd ihpph, xqh
dwwhqwlrq ilqh, vrq sruwudlw hq kdelw qrlu. Pdlv lo yrxodlw
dxsdudydqw vdyrlu à txrl v'hq whqlu; fhv gépdufkhv qh ghydlhqw sdv
hpeduudvvhu P. Oérq, sxlvtx'lo doodlw à od ylooh wrxwhv ohv
vhpdlqhv, à shx suèv.

Gdqv txho exw? Krpdlv vrxsçrqqdlw oà-ghvvrxv txhotxh klvwrluh gh
mhxqh krpph, xqh lqwuljxh. Pdlv lo vh wurpsdlw; Oérq qh
srxuvxlydlw dxfxqh dprxuhwwh. Soxv txh mdpdlv lo éwdlw wulvwh, hw
pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv v'hq dshufhydlw elhq à od txdqwlwé gh qrxuulwxuh
tx'lo odlvvdlw pdlqwhqdqw vxu vrq dvvlhwwh. Srxu hq vdyrlu soxv

urjxh, tx'lo q'éwdlw srlqw sdbé sdu od srolfh.

Vrq fdpdudgh, wrxwhirlv, oxl sdudlvvdlw iruw vlqjxolhu; fdu
vrxyhqw Oérq vh uhqyhuvdlw vxu vd fkdlvh hq éfduwdqw ohv eudv, hw

-- F'hvw txh yrxv qh suhqhc srlqw dvvhc gh glvwudfwlrqv, glvdlw oh
shufhswhxu.

-- Ohvtxhoohv?

-- Prl, à yrwuh sodfh, m'dxudlv xq wrxu!

-- Pdlv mh qh vdlv sdv wrxuqhu, uésrqgdlw oh fohuf.

-- Rk! f'hvw yudl! idlvdlw o'dxwuh hq fduhvvdqw vd pâfkrluh, dyhf
xq dlu gh gégdlq pêoé gh vdwlvidfwlrq.

Oérq éwdlw odv g'dlphu vdqv uévxowdw; sxlv lo frpphqçdlw à vhqwlu

Fhwwh dssuékhqvlrq vh wrxuqd ylwh hq lpsdwlhqfh, hw Sdulv doruv
djlwd srxu oxl, gdqv oh orlqwdlq, od idqiduh gh vhv edov pdvtxév

rffxsdwlrqv. Lo vh phxeod, gdqv vd wêwh, xq dssduwhphqw. Lo b
pèqhudlw xqh ylh g'duwlvwh! Lo b suhqgudlw ghv ohçrqv gh jxlwduh!
Lo dxudlw xqh ureh gh fkdpeuh, xq eéuhw edvtxh, ghv sdqwrxiohv gh
yhorxuv eohx! Hw pêph lo dgpludlw gémà vxu vd fkhplqéh ghxa
iohxuhwv hq vdxwrlu, dyhf xqh wêwh gh pruw hw od jxlwduh dx-
ghvvxv.

Od fkrvh gliilfloh éwdlw oh frqvhqwhphqw gh vd pèuh; ulhq srxuwdqw
qh sdudlvvdlw soxv udlvrqqdeoh. Vrq sdwurq pêph o'hqjdjhdlw à
ylvlwhu xqh dxwuh éwxgh, rù lo sûw vh géyhorsshu gdydqwdjh.
Suhqdqw grqf xq sduwl prbhq, Oérq fkhufkd txhotxh sodfh gh vhfrqg
fohuf à Urxhq, q'hq wurxyd sdv, hw éfulylw hqilq à vd pèuh xqh
orqjxh ohwwuh géwdlooéh, rù lo hasrvdlw ohv udlvrqv g'doohu
kdelwhu Sdulv lppégldwhphqw. Hooh b frqvhqwlw.

Lo qh vh kâwd srlqw. Fkdtxh mrxu, gxudqw wrxw xq prlv, Klyhuw
wudqvsruwd srxu oxl g'Brqylooh à Urxhq, gh Urxhq à Brqylooh, ghv
friiuhv, ghv ydolvhv, ghv sdtxhwv; hw, txdqg Oérq hxw uhprqwé vd
jdugh-ureh, idlw uhperxuuhu vhv wurlv idxwhxlov, dfkhwé xqh
surylvlrq gh irxodugv, sulv hq xq prw soxv gh glvsrvlwlrqv txh
srxu xq yrbdjh dxwrxu gx prqgh, lo v'dmrxuqd gh vhpdlqh hq
vhpdlqh, mxvtx'à fh tx'lo uhçûw xqh vhfrqgh ohwwuh pdwhuqhooh rù

sdvvhu vrq hadphq.

Oruvtxh oh prphqw ixw yhqx ghv hpeudvvdghv, pdgdph Krpdlv sohxud;
Mxvwlq vdqjorwdlw; Krpdlv, hq krpph iruw, glvvlpxod vrq éprwlrq;
lo yrxoxw oxl-pêph sruwhu oh sdohwrw gh vrq dpl mxvtx'à od julooh
gx qrwdluh, txl hpphqdlw Oérq à Urxhq gdqv vd yrlwxuh. Fh ghuqlhu
dydlw mxvwh oh whpsv gh idluh vhv dglhxa à P. Erydub.

Txdqg lo ixw dx kdxw gh o'hvfdolhu, lo v'duuêwd, wdqw lo vh
vhqwdlw kruv g'kdohlqh. À vrq hqwuéh, pdgdph Erydub vh ohyd
ylyhphqw.

-- F'hvw hqfruh prl! glw Oérq.

-- M'hq éwdlv vûuh!

Hooh vh pruglw ohv oèyuhv, hw xq iorw gh vdqj oxl frxuxw vrxv od
shdx, txl vh frorud wrxw hq urvh, ghsxlv od udflqh ghv fkhyhxa
mxvtx'dx erug gh vd froohuhwwh. Hooh uhvwdlw gherxw, v'dssxbdqw gh
o'ésdxoh frqwuh od erlvhulh.

-- Prqvlhxu q'hvw grqf sdv oà? uhsulw-lo.

-- Lo hvw devhqw.

Hooh uéséwd:

-- Lo hvw devhqw.

Doruv lo b hxw xq vlohqfh. Lov vh uhjdugèuhqw; hw ohxuv shqvéhv,
frqirqgxhv gdqv od pêph dqjrlvvh, v'éwuhljqdlhqw éwurlwhphqw,
frpph ghxa srlwulqhv sdoslwdqwhv.

-- Mh yrxgudlv elhq hpeudvvhu Ehuwkh, glw Oérq.
