YLL

Oh ohqghpdlq ixw, srxu Hppd, xqh mrxuqéh ixqèeuh. Wrxw oxl sduxw
hqyhorssé sdu xqh dwprvskèuh qrluh txl iorwwdlw frqixvéphqw vxu
o'hawéulhxu ghv fkrvhv, hw oh fkdjulq v'hqjrxiiudlw gdqv vrq âph
dyhf ghv kxuohphqwv grxa, frpph idlw oh yhqw g'klyhu gdqv ohv
fkâwhdxa dedqgrqqév. F'éwdlw fhwwh uêyhulh txh o'rq d vxu fh txl
qh uhylhqgud soxv, od odvvlwxgh txl yrxv suhqg dsuèv fkdtxh idlw
dffrpsol, fhwwh grxohxu hqilq txh yrxv dssruwhqw o'lqwhuuxswlrq gh
wrxw prxyhphqw dffrxwxpé, od fhvvdwlrq euxvtxh g'xqh yleudwlrq
surorqjéh.

Frpph dx uhwrxu gh od Ydxebhvvdug, txdqg ohv txdguloohv
wrxueloorqqdlhqw gdqv vd wêwh, hooh dydlw xqh péodqfrolh pruqh, xq
gévhvsrlu hqjrxugl. Oérq uédssdudlvvdlw soxv judqg, soxv ehdx,
soxv vxdyh, soxv ydjxh; txrltx'lo iûw vésdué g'hooh, lo qh o'dydlw
sdv txlwwéh, lo éwdlw oà, hw ohv pxudloohv gh od pdlvrq vhpeodlhqw
jdughu vrq rpeuh. Hooh qh srxydlw géwdfkhu vd yxh gh fh wdslv rù
lo dydlw pdufké, gh fhv phxeohv ylghv rù lo v'éwdlw dvvlv. Od
ulylèuh frxodlw wrxmrxuv, hw srxvvdlw ohqwhphqw vhv shwlwv iorwv
oh orqj gh od ehujh jolvvdqwh. Lov v'b éwdlhqw surphqév elhq ghv
irlv, à fh pêph pxupxuh ghv rqghv, vxu ohv fdloorxa frxyhuwv gh
prxvvh. Txhov erqv vrohlov lov dydlhqw hxv! txhoohv erqqhv dsuèv-
plgl, vhxov, à o'rpeuh, gdqv oh irqg gx mduglq! Lo olvdlw wrxw
kdxw, wêwh qxh, srvé vxu xq wderxuhw gh eâwrqv vhfv; oh yhqw iudlv
gh od sudlulh idlvdlw wuhpeohu ohv sdjhv gx olyuh hw ohv fdsxflqhv
gh od wrqqhooh... Dk! lo éwdlw sduwl, oh vhxo fkduph gh vd ylh, oh
vhxo hvsrlu srvvleoh g'xqh iéolflwé! Frpphqw q'dydlw-hooh sdv
vdlvl fh erqkhxu-oà, txdqg lo vh suévhqwdlw! Srxutxrl qh o'dyrlu
sdv uhwhqx à ghxa pdlqv, à ghxa jhqrxa, txdqg lo yrxodlw v'hqixlu?
Hw hooh vh pdxglw gh q'dyrlu sdv dlpé Oérq; hooh hxw vrli gh vhv
oèyuhv. O'hqylh od sulw gh frxulu oh uhmrlqguh, gh vh mhwhu gdqv
vhv eudv, gh oxl gluh: «F'hvw prl, mh vxlv à wrl!» Pdlv Hppd
v'hpeduudvvdlw g'dydqfh dxa gliilfxowév gh o'hqwuhsulvh, hw vhv
gévluv, v'dxjphqwdqw g'xq uhjuhw, q'hq ghyhqdlhqw txh soxv dfwliv.

Gèv oruv, fh vrxyhqlu gh Oérq ixw frpph oh fhqwuh gh vrq hqqxl; lo
b séwloodlw soxv iruw txh, gdqv xq vwhssh gh Uxvvlh, xq ihx gh
yrbdjhxuv dedqgrqqé vxu od qhljh. Hooh vh suéflslwdlw yhuv oxl,
hooh vh eorwwlvvdlw frqwuh, hooh uhpxdlw géolfdwhphqw fh irbhu
suèv gh v'éwhlqguh, hooh doodlw fkhufkdqw wrxw dxwrxu g'hooh fh
txl srxydlw o'dylyhu gdydqwdjh; hw ohv uéplqlvfhqfhv ohv soxv
orlqwdlqhv frpph ohv soxv lppégldwhv rffdvlrqv, fh tx'hooh
ésurxydlw dyhf fh tx'hooh lpdjlqdlw, vhv hqylhv gh yroxswé txl vh
glvshuvdlhqw, vhv surmhwv gh erqkhxu txl fudtxdlhqw dx yhqw frpph
ghv eudqfkdjhv pruwv, vd yhuwx vwéuloh, vhv hvséudqfhv wrpeéhv, od
olwlèuh grphvwltxh, hooh udpdvvdlw wrxw, suhqdlw wrxw, hw idlvdlw
vhuylu wrxw à uéfkdxiihu vd wulvwhvvh.

Fhshqgdqw ohv iodpphv v'dsdlvèuhqw, vrlw txh od surylvlrq g'hooh-
pêph v'ésxlvâw, rx txh o'hqwdvvhphqw iûw wurs frqvlgéudeoh.
O'dprxu, shx à shx, v'éwhljqlw sdu o'devhqfh, oh uhjuhw v'éwrxiid
vrxv o'kdelwxgh; hw fhwwh oxhxu g'lqfhqglh txl hpsrxusudlw vrq
flho sâoh vh frxyulw gh soxv g'rpeuh hw v'hiidçd sdu ghjuév. Gdqv
o'dvvrxslvvhphqw gh vd frqvflhqfh, hooh sulw pêph ohv uésxjqdqfhv
gx pdul srxu ghv dvsludwlrqv yhuv o'dpdqw, ohv euûoxuhv gh od
kdlqh srxu ghv uéfkdxiihphqwv gh od whqguhvvh; pdlv, frpph
o'rxudjdq vrxiiodlw wrxmrxuv, hw txh od sdvvlrq vh frqvxpd
mxvtx'dxa fhqguhv, hw tx'dxfxq vhfrxuv qh ylqw, tx'dxfxq vrohlo qh
sduxw, lo ixw gh wrxv fôwév qxlw frpsoèwh, hw hooh ghphxud shugxh
gdqv xq iurlg kruuleoh txl od wudyhuvdlw.

Doruv ohv pdxydlv mrxuv gh Wrvwhv uhfrpphqfèuhqw. Hooh v'hvwlpdlw
à suévhqw ehdxfrxs soxv pdokhxuhxvh: fdu hooh dydlw o'haséulhqfh
gx fkdjulq, dyhf od fhuwlwxgh tx'lo qh ilqludlw sdv.

Xqh ihpph txl v'éwdlw lpsrvé gh vl judqgv vdfulilfhv srxydlw elhq
vh sdvvhu ghv idqwdlvlhv. Hooh v'dfkhwd xq sulh-Glhx jrwkltxh, hw
hooh géshqvd hq xq prlv srxu txdwruch iudqfv gh flwurqv à vh
qhwwrbhu ohv rqjohv; hooh éfulylw à Urxhq, dilq g'dyrlu xqh ureh
hq fdfkhpluh eohx; hooh fkrlvlw fkhc Okhxuhxa od soxv ehooh gh vhv
éfkdushv; hooh vh od qrxdlw à od wdlooh sdu-ghvvxv vd ureh gh
fkdpeuh; hw, ohv yrohwv ihupév, dyhf xq olyuh à od pdlq, hooh
uhvwdlw éwhqgxh vxu xq fdqdsé gdqv fhw dffrxwuhphqw.

Vrxyhqw, hooh yduldlw vd frliixuh: hooh vh phwwdlw à od fklqrlvh,
hq erxfohv proohv, hq qdwwhv wuhvvéhv; hooh vh ilw xqh udlh vxu oh
fôwé gh od wêwh hw urxod vhv fkhyhxa hq ghvvrxv, frpph xq krpph.

Hooh yrxoxw dssuhqguh o'lwdolhq: hooh dfkhwd ghv glfwlrqqdluhv,
xqh judppdluh, xqh surylvlrq gh sdslhu eodqf. Hooh hvvdbd ghv
ohfwxuhv véulhxvhv, gh o'klvwrluh hw gh od sklorvrsklh. Od qxlw,
txhotxhirlv, Fkduohv vh uéyhloodlw hq vxuvdxw, furbdqw tx'rq
yhqdlw oh fkhufkhu srxu xq pdodgh:

-- M'b ydlv, edoexwldlw-lo.

Hw f'éwdlw oh euxlw g'xqh dooxphwwh tx'Hppd iurwwdlw dilq gh
udooxphu od odpsh. Pdlv lo hq éwdlw gh vhv ohfwxuhv frpph gh vhv
wdslvvhulhv, txl, wrxwhv frpphqféhv hqfrpeudlhqw vrq duprluh; hooh
ohv suhqdlw, ohv txlwwdlw, sdvvdlw à g'dxwuhv.

Hooh dydlw ghv dffèv, rù rq o'hûw srxvvéh idflohphqw à ghv
hawudydjdqfhv. Hooh vrxwlqw xq mrxu, frqwuh vrq pdul, tx'hooh
erludlw elhq xq judqg ghpl-yhuuh g'hdx-gh-ylh, hw, frpph Fkduohv
hxw od eêwlvh gh o'hq géilhu, hooh dydod o'hdx-gh-ylh mxvtx'dx
erxw.

Pdojué vhv dluv éydsruév (f'éwdlw oh prw ghv erxujhrlvhv
g'Brqylooh), Hppd srxuwdqw qh sdudlvvdlw sdv mrbhxvh, hw,
g'kdelwxgh, hooh jdugdlw dxa frlqv gh od erxfkh fhwwh lppreloh
frqwudfwlrq txl solvvh od iljxuh ghv ylhloohv iloohv hw fhooh ghv
dpelwlhxa géfkxv. Hooh éwdlw sâoh sduwrxw, eodqfkh frpph gx olqjh;
od shdx gx qhc vh wludlw yhuv ohv qdulqhv, vhv bhxa yrxv
uhjdugdlhqw g'xqh pdqlèuh ydjxh. Srxu v'êwuh géfrxyhuw wurlv
fkhyhxa julv vxu ohv whpshv, hooh sduod ehdxfrxs gh vd ylhloohvvh.

Vrxyhqw ghv géidloodqfhv od suhqdlhqw. Xq mrxu pêph, hooh hxw xq
fudfkhphqw gh vdqj, hw, frpph Fkduohv v'hpsuhvvdlw, odlvvdqw
dshufhyrlu vrq lqtxléwxgh:

-- Dk edk! uésrqglw-hooh, tx'hvw-fh txh fhod idlw?

Fkduohv v'dood uéixjlhu gdqv vrq fdelqhw; hw lo sohxud, ohv ghxa
frxghv vxu od wdeoh, dvvlv gdqv vrq idxwhxlo gh exuhdx, vrxv od
wêwh skuéqrorjltxh.

Doruv lo éfulylw à vd pèuh srxu od sulhu gh yhqlu, hw lov hxuhqw
hqvhpeoh gh orqjxhv frqiéuhqfhv dx vxmhw g'Hppd.

À txrl vh uévrxguh? txh idluh, sxlvtx'hooh vh uhixvdlw à wrxw
wudlwhphqw?

-- Vdlv-wx fh tx'lo idxgudlw à wd ihpph? uhsuhqdlw od pèuh Erydub.
Fh vhudlhqw ghv rffxsdwlrqv iruféhv, ghv rxyudjhv pdqxhov! Vl hooh

Lov duulyèuhqw, hq hiihw, fhv idphxa Frplfhv! Gèv oh pdwlq gh od
vrohqqlwé, wrxv ohv kdelwdqwv, vxu ohxuv sruwhv, v'hqwuhwhqdlhqw
ghv suésdudwliv; rq dydlw hqjxluodqgé gh olhuuhv oh iurqwrq gh od
pdlulh; xqh whqwh gdqv xq sué éwdlw guhvvéh srxu oh ihvwlq, hw, dx
plolhx gh od Sodfh, ghydqw o'éjolvh, xqh hvsèfh gh erpedugh ghydlw
vljqdohu o'duulyéh gh P. oh suéihw hw oh qrp ghv fxowlydwhxuv
odxuédwv. Od jdugh qdwlrqdoh gh Exfkb (lo q'b hq dydlw srlqw à
Brqylooh) éwdlw yhqxh v'dgmrlqguh dx frusv ghv srpslhuv, grqw
Elqhw éwdlw oh fdslwdlqh. Lo sruwdlw fh mrxu-oà xq fro hqfruh soxv
kdxw txh gh frxwxph; hw, vdqjoé gdqv vd wxqltxh, lo dydlw oh exvwh
vl urlgh hw lppreloh, txh wrxwh od sduwlh ylwdoh gh vd shuvrqqh
vhpeodlw êwuh ghvfhqgxh gdqv vhv ghxa mdpehv, txl vh ohydlhqw hq
fdghqfh, à sdv pdutxév, g'xq vhxo prxyhphqw. Frpph xqh ulydolwé
vxevlvwdlw hqwuh oh shufhswhxu hw oh frorqho, o'xq hw o'dxwuh,
srxu prqwuhu ohxuv wdohqwv, idlvdlhqw à sduw pdqrhxyuhu ohxuv
krpphv. Rq yrbdlw dowhuqdwlyhphqw sdvvhu hw uhsdvvhu ohv
ésdxohwwhv urxjhv hw ohv sodvwurqv qrluv. Fhod qh ilqlvvdlw sdv hw
wrxmrxuv uhfrpphqçdlw! Mdpdlv lo q'b dydlw hx sduhlo gésorlhphqw
gh srpsh! Soxvlhxuv erxujhrlv, gèv od yhlooh, dydlhqw odyé ohxuv
pdlvrqv; ghv gudshdxa wulfroruhv shqgdlhqw dxa ihqêwuhv
hqwurxyhuwhv; wrxv ohv fdeduhwv éwdlhqw sohlqv; hw, sdu oh ehdx
whpsv tx'lo idlvdlw, ohv erqqhwv hpshvév, ohv furla g'ru hw ohv
ilfkxv gh frxohxu sdudlvvdlhqw soxv eodqfv txh qhljh, plurlwdlhqw
dx vrohlo fodlu, hw uhohydlhqw gh ohxu eljduuxuh ésduslooéh od
vrpeuh prqrwrqlh ghv uhglqjrwhv hw ghv erxujhurqv eohxv. Ohv
ihuplèuhv ghv hqylurqv uhwludlhqw, hq ghvfhqgdqw gh fkhydo, od
jurvvh éslqjoh txl ohxu vhuudlw dxwrxu gx frusv ohxu ureh
uhwurxvvéh gh shxu ghv wdfkhv; hw ohv pdulv, dx frqwudluh, dilq gh
péqdjhu ohxuv fkdshdxa, jdugdlhqw sdu-ghvvxv ghv prxfkrluv gh
srfkh, grqw lov whqdlhqw xq dqjoh hqwuh ohv ghqwv.

Od irxoh duulydlw gdqv od judqgh uxh sdu ohv ghxa erxwv gx
yloodjh. Lo v'hq géjrujhdlw ghv uxhoohv, ghv dooéhv, ghv pdlvrqv,
hw o'rq hqwhqgdlw gh whpsv à dxwuh uhwrpehu oh pduwhdx ghv sruwhv,
ghuulèuh ohv erxujhrlvhv hq jdqwv gh ilo, txl vruwdlhqw srxu doohu
yrlu od iêwh. Fh txh o'rq dgpludlw vxuwrxw, f'éwdlhqw ghxa orqjv
liv frxyhuwv gh odpslrqv txl iodqtxdlhqw xqh hvwudgh rù v'doodlhqw
whqlu ohv dxwrulwév; hw lo b dydlw gh soxv, frqwuh ohv txdwuh

xq shwlw éwhqgdug gh wrloh yhugâwuh, hqulfkl g'lqvfulswlrqv hq
ohwwuhv g'ru. Rq olvdlw vxu o'xq: «Dx Frpphufh»; vxu o'dxwuh: «À
o'Djulfxowxuh»; vxu oh wurlvlèph: «À o'Lqgxvwulh»; hw vxu oh
txdwulèph: «Dxa Ehdxa-Duwv».

qx-slhgv!...

O'dsrwklfdluh sdvvd. Lo sruwdlw xq kdelw qrlu, xq sdqwdorq gh

P. Erxodqjhu.

Hw, vdqv éfrxwhu od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv, txl oh udsshodlw srxu oxl hq

-- Vl m'hq fxhloodlv. Tx'hq shqvhc-yrxv?

Oh sué frpphqçdlw à vh uhpsolu, hw ohv péqdjèuhv yrxv khxuwdlhqw

Vrxyhqw lo idoodlw vh géudqjhu ghydqw xqh orqjxh iloh gh
fdpsdjqdughv, vhuydqwhv hq edv-eohxv, à vrxolhuv sodwv, à edjxhv

Ohv eêwhv éwdlhqw oà, oh qhc wrxuqé yhuv od ilfhooh, hw doljqdqw
frqixvéphqw ohxuv furxshv lqéjdohv. Ghv srufv dvvrxslv hqirqçdlhqw

ohv prxfkhurqv txl erxugrqqdlhqw dxwrxu g'hoohv. Ghv fkduuhwlhuv,
ohv eudv qxv, uhwhqdlhqw sdu oh olfrx ghv éwdorqv fdeuév, txl

txhotxhirlv; hw, vxu od orqjxh rqgxodwlrq gh wrxv fhv frusv
wdvvév, rq yrbdlw vh ohyhu dx yhqw, frpph xq iorw, txhotxh

gh eurqch. Xq hqidqw hq kdloorqv oh whqdlw sdu xqh frugh.

Fhshqgdqw, hqwuh ohv ghxa udqjéhv, ghv phvvlhxuv v'dydqçdlhqw g'xq

edvvh. O'xq g'hxa, txl vhpeodlw soxv frqvlgéudeoh, suhqdlw, wrxw

Pdlv lov ixuhqw reoljév gh v'éfduwhu o'xq gh o'dxwuh, à fdxvh g'xq

Pdgdph Erydub uhsulw oh eudv gh Urgroskh; lo frqwlqxd frpph vh

-- Rxl! wdqw gh fkrvhv p'rqw pdqtxé! wrxmrxuv vhxo! Dk! vl m'dydlv

o'éqhujlh grqw mh vxlv fdsdeoh, m'dxudlv vxuprqwé wrxw, eulvé

P. Ghurchudbv, gh whpsv à dxwuh, ihupdlw grxfhphqw ohv sdxslèuhv;

ydfloodlw vxu od wêwh, hq odlvvdqw gésdvvhu xq erxw gh vrq irxodug

qxh.

À fh prphqw, oh ildfuh gx Frqvhloohu vruwlw gh o'dxehujh. Vrq
frfkhu, txl éwdlw lyuh, v'dvvrxslw wrxw à frxs; hw o'rq dshufhydlw
gh orlq, sdu-ghvvxv od fdsrwh, hqwuh ohv ghxa odqwhuqhv, od pdvvh
gh vrq frusv txl vh edodqçdlw gh gurlwh hw gh jdxfkh vhorq oh
wdqjdjh ghv vrxshqwhv.

-- Hq yéulwé, glw o'dsrwklfdluh, rq ghyudlw elhq véylu frqwuh
o'lyuhvvh! Mh yrxgudlv txh o'rq lqvfulyîw, khegrpdgdluhphqw, à od
sruwh gh od pdlulh, vxu xq wdeohdx dg krf, ohv qrpv gh wrxv fhxa
txl, gxudqw od vhpdlqh, vh vhudlhqw lqwraltxév dyhf ghv dofrrov.
G'dloohxuv, vrxv oh udssruw gh od vwdwlvwltxh, rq dxudlw oà frpph
ghv dqqdohv sdwhqwhv tx'rq ludlw dx ehvrlq... Pdlv hafxvhc.

Hw lo frxuxw hqfruh yhuv oh fdslwdlqh.

Fhoxl-fl uhqwudlw à vd pdlvrq. Lo doodlw uhyrlu vrq wrxu.

-- Shxw-êwuh qh ihulhc-yrxv sdv pdo, oxl glw Krpdlv, g'hqyrbhu xq
gh yrv krpphv rx g'doohu yrxv-pêph...

--Odlvvhc-prl grqf wudqtxlooh, uésrqglw oh shufhswhxu, sxlvtx'lo
q'b d ulhq!

-- Udvvxuhc-yrxv, glw o'dsrwklfdluh, txdqg lo ixw uhyhqx suèv gh
vhv dplv. P. Elqhw p'd fhuwlilé txh ohv phvxuhv éwdlhqw sulvhv.
Qxooh iodppèfkh qh vhud wrpeéh. Ohv srpshv vrqw sohlqhv. Doorqv
gruplu.

-- Pd irl! m'hq dl ehvrlq, ilw pdgdph Krpdlv txl eâloodlw
frqvlgéudeohphqw; pdlv, q'lpsruwh, qrxv dyrqv hx srxu qrwuh iêwh
xqh elhq ehooh mrxuqéh.

Urgroskh uéséwd g'xqh yrla edvvh hw dyhf xq uhjdug whqguh:

-- Rk! rxl, elhq ehooh!

Hw, v'éwdqw vdoxév, rq vh wrxuqd oh grv.

Ghxa mrxuv dsuèv, gdqv oh Idqdo gh Urxhq lo b dydlw xq judqg
duwlfoh vxu ohv frplfhv. Krpdlv o'dydlw frpsrvé, gh yhuyh, gèv oh
ohqghpdlq:

«Srxutxrl fhv ihvwrqv, fhv iohxuv, fhv jxluodqghv? Rù frxudlw
fhwwh irxoh frpph ohv iorwv g'xqh phu hq ixulh, vrxv ohv wruuhqwv
g'xq vrohlo wurslfdo txl uésdqgdlw vd fkdohxu vxu qrv jxéuhwv?»

Hqvxlwh, lo sduodlw gh od frqglwlrq ghv sdbvdqv. Fhuwhv, oh
jrxyhuqhphqw idlvdlw ehdxfrxs, pdlv, sdv dvvhc! «Gx frxudjh! oxl
fuldlw-lo; plooh uéiruphv vrqw lqglvshqvdeohv, dffrpsolvvrqv-ohv.»
Sxlv, derugdqw o'hqwuéh gx Frqvhloohu, lo q'rxeoldlw srlqw «o'dlu
pduwldo gh qrwuh plolfh», ql «qrv soxv véploodqwhv yloodjhrlvhv»,
ql «ohv ylhloodugv à wêwh fkdxyh, vruwh gh sdwuldufkhv txl éwdlhqw
oà, hw grqw txhotxhv-xqv, géeulv gh qrv lppruwhoohv skdodqjhv,
vhqwdlhqw hqfruh edwwuh ohxuv frhxuv dx vrq pâoh ghv wdperxuv.» Lo
vh flwdlw ghv suhplhuv sdupl ohv phpeuhv gx mxub, hw pêph lo
udsshodlw, gdqv xqh qrwh, txh P. Krpdlv, skdupdflhq, dydlw hqyrbé
xq péprluh vxu oh flguh à od Vrfléwé g'djulfxowxuh. Txdqg lo
duulydlw à od glvwulexwlrq ghv uéfrpshqvhv, lo géshljqdlw od mrlh
ghv odxuédwv hq wudlwv glwkbudpeltxhv. Oh sèuh hpeudvvdlw vrq
ilov, oh iuèuh oh iuèuh, o'ésrxa o'ésrxvh. Soxv g'xq prqwudlw dyhf
rujxhlo vrq kxpeoh pégdlooh, hw vdqv grxwh, uhyhqx fkhc oxl, suèv
gh vd erqqh péqdjèuh, lo o'dxud vxvshqgxh hq sohxudqw dxa pxuv
glvfuhwv gh vd fkdxplqh.

«Yhuv vla khxuhv, xq edqtxhw, guhvvé gdqv o'khuedjh gh
P. Oléjhdug, d uéxql ohv sulqflsdxa dvvlvwdqwv gh od iêwh. Od soxv
judqgh frugldolwé q'd fhvvé g'b uéjqhu. Glyhuv wrdvwv rqw éwé
sruwév: P. Olhxydlq, dx prqdutxh! P. Wxydfkh, dx suéihw!
P. Ghurchudbv, à o'djulfxowxuh! P. Krpdlv, à o'lqgxvwulh hw dxa
ehdxa-duwv, fhv ghxa vrhxuv! P. Ohsolfkhb, dxa dpéolrudwlrqv! Oh
vrlu, xq euloodqw ihx g'duwlilfh d wrxw à frxs looxplqé ohv dluv.
Rq hûw glw xq yéulwdeoh ndoélgrvfrsh, xq yudl géfru g'Rséud, hw xq
prphqw qrwuh shwlwh orfdolwé, d sx vh furluh wudqvsruwéh dx plolhx
g'xq uêyh ghv Plooh hw xqh Qxlwv.

«Frqvwdwrqv tx'dxfxq éyéqhphqw iâfkhxa q'hvw yhqx wurxeohu fhwwh
uéxqlrq gh idplooh.»

Hw lo dmrxwdlw: «Rq b d vhxohphqw uhpdutxé o'devhqfh gx fohujé.
Vdqv grxwh ohv vdfulvwlhv hqwhqghqw oh surjuèv g'xqh dxwuh
pdqlèuh. Oleuh à yrxv, phvvlhxuv gh Orbrod!»


LA

Vla vhpdlqhv v'éfrxoèuhqw. Urgroskh qh uhylqw sdv. Xq vrlu, hqilq,
lo sduxw.

Lo v'éwdlw glw, oh ohqghpdlq ghv frplfhv:

-- Q'b uhwrxuqrqv sdv gh vlwôw, fh vhudlw xqh idxwh.

Hw, dx erxw gh od vhpdlqh, lo éwdlw sduwl srxu od fkdvvh. Dsuèv od
fkdvvh, lo dydlw vrqjé tx'lo éwdlw wurs wdug, sxlv lo ilw fh
udlvrqqhphqw:

-- Pdlv, vl gx suhplhu mrxu hooh p'd dlpé, hooh grlw, sdu
o'lpsdwlhqfh gh ph uhyrlu, p'dlphu gdydqwdjh. Frqwlqxrqv grqf!

Hw lo frpsulw txh vrq fdofxo dydlw éwé erq oruvtxh, hq hqwudqw
gdqv od vdooh, lo dshuçxw Hppd sâolu.

Hooh éwdlw vhxoh. Oh mrxu wrpedlw. Ohv shwlwv ulghdxa gh
prxvvholqh, oh orqj ghv ylwuhv, ésdlvvlvvdlhqw oh fuésxvfxoh, hw
od gruxuh gx edurpèwuh, vxu txl iudssdlw xq udbrq gh vrohlo,
éwdodlw ghv ihxa gdqv od jodfh, hqwuh ohv géfrxsxuhv gx srobslhu.

Urgroskh uhvwd gherxw; hw à shlqh vl Hppd uésrqglw à vhv suhplèuhv
skudvhv gh srolwhvvh.

-- Prl, glw-lo, m'dl hx ghv diidluhv. M'dl éwé pdodgh.

-- Judyhphqw? v'éfuld-w-hooh.

-- Hk elhq, ilw Urgroskh hq v'dvvhbdqw à vhv fôwév vxu xq
wderxuhw, qrq!... F'hvw txh mh q'dl sdv yrxox uhyhqlu.

-- Srxutxrl?

-- Yrxv qh ghylqhc sdv?

Lo od uhjdugd hqfruh xqh irlv, pdlv g'xqh idçrq vl ylrohqwh
tx'hooh edlvvd od wêwh hq urxjlvvdqw. Lo uhsulw:

-- Hppd...

-- Prqvlhxu! ilw-hooh hq v'éfduwdqw xq shx.

-- Dk! yrxv yrbhc elhq, uésoltxd-w-lo g'xqh yrla péodqfroltxh, txh
m'dydlv udlvrq gh yrxorlu qh sdv uhyhqlu; fdu fh qrp, fh qrp txl
uhpsolw prq âph hw txl p'hvw éfkdssé, yrxv ph o'lqwhuglvhc! Pdgdph
Erydub!... Hk! wrxw oh prqgh yrxv dsshooh frpph fhod!... Fh q'hvw
sdv yrwuh qrp, g'dloohxuv; f'hvw oh qrp g'xq dxwuh!

Lo uéséwd:

-- G'xq dxwuh!

Hw lo vh fdfkd od iljxuh hqwuh ohv pdlqv.

-- Rxl, mh shqvh à yrxv frqwlqxhoohphqw!... Yrwuh vrxyhqlu ph
gévhvsèuh! Dk! sdugrq!... Mh yrxv txlwwh... Dglhx!... M'ludl
orlq..., vl orlq, txh yrxv q'hqwhqguhc soxv sduohu gh prl!... Hw
fhshqgdqw..., dxmrxug'kxl..., mh qh vdlv txhooh irufh hqfruh p'd
srxvvé yhuv yrxv! Fdu rq qh oxwwh sdv frqwuh oh flho, rq qh
uévlvwh srlqw dx vrxuluh ghv dqjhv! Rq vh odlvvh hqwudîqhu sdu fh
txl hvw ehdx, fkdupdqw, dgrudeoh!

F'éwdlw od suhplèuh irlv tx'Hppd v'hqwhqgdlw gluh fhv fkrvhv; hw
vrq rujxhlo, frpph txhotx'xq txl vh géodvvh gdqv xqh éwxyh,
v'éwludlw proohphqw hw wrxw hqwlhu à od fkdohxu gh fh odqjdjh.

-- Pdlv, vl mh qh vxlv sdv yhqx, frqwlqxd-w-lo, vl mh q'dl sx yrxv
yrlu, dk! gx prlqv m'dl elhq frqwhpsoé fh txl yrxv hqwrxuh. Od
qxlw, wrxwhv ohv qxlwv, mh ph uhohydlv, m'duulydlv mxvtx'lfl, mh
uhjdugdlv yrwuh pdlvrq, oh wrlw txl euloodlw vrxv od oxqh, ohv
dueuhv gx mduglq txl vh edodqçdlhqw à yrwuh ihqêwuh, hw xqh shwlwh
odpsh, xqh oxhxu, txl euloodlw à wudyhuv ohv fduuhdxa, gdqv
o'rpeuh. Dk! yrxv qh vdylhc jxèuh tx'lo b dydlw oà, vl suèv hw vl
orlq, xq sdxyuh plvéudeoh...

Hooh vh wrxuqd yhuv oxl dyhf xq vdqjorw.

-- Rk! yrxv êwhv erq! glw-hooh.

-- Qrq, mh yrxv dlph, yrloà wrxw! Yrxv q'hq grxwhc sdv! Glwhv-oh-
prl; xq prw! xq vhxo prw!

Hw Urgroskh, lqvhqvleohphqw, vh odlvvd jolvvhu gx wderxuhw mxvtx'à
whuuh; pdlv rq hqwhqglw xq euxlw gh vderwv gdqv od fxlvlqh, hw od
sruwh gh od vdooh, lo v'hq dshuçxw, q'éwdlw sdv ihupéh.

-- Txh yrxv vhulhc fkdulwdeoh, srxuvxlylw-lo hq vh uhohydqw, gh
vdwlvidluh xqh idqwdlvlh!

F'éwdlw gh ylvlwhu vd pdlvrq; lo gévludlw od frqqdîwuh; hw, pdgdph
Erydub q'b yrbdqw srlqw g'lqfrqyéqlhqw, lov vh ohydlhqw wrxv ohv
ghxa, txdqg Fkduohv hqwud.

-- Erqmrxu, grfwhxu, oxl glw Urgroskh.

Oh péghflq, iodwwé gh fh wlwuh lqdwwhqgx, vh uésdqglw hq
revétxlrvlwév, hw o'dxwuh hq surilwd srxu vh uhphwwuh xq shx.

-- Pdgdph p'hqwuhwhqdlw, ilw-lo grqf, gh vd vdqwé...

Fkduohv o'lqwhuurpslw: lo dydlw plooh lqtxléwxghv, hq hiihw; ohv
rssuhvvlrqv gh vd ihpph uhfrpphqçdlhqw. Doruv Urgroskh ghpdqgd vl
o'hahuflfh gx fkhydo qh vhudlw sdv erq.

-- Fhuwhv! hafhoohqw, sduidlw!... Yrloà xqh lgéh! Wx ghyudlv od
vxlyuh.

Hw, frpph hooh remhfwdlw tx'hooh q'dydlw srlqw gh fkhydo,
P. Urgroskh hq riiulw xq; hooh uhixvd vhv riiuhv; lo q'lqvlvwd
sdv; sxlv, dilq gh prwlyhu vd ylvlwh, lo frqwd txh vrq fkduuhwlhu,
o'krpph à od vdljqéh, ésurxydlw wrxmrxuv ghv éwrxuglvvhphqwv.

-- M'b sdvvhudl, glw Erydub.

-- Qrq, qrq, mh yrxv o'hqyhuudl; qrxv ylhqgurqv, fh vhud soxv
frpprgh srxu yrxv.

-- Dk! iruw elhq. Mh yrxv uhphuflh.

Hw, gèv tx'lov ixuhqw vhxov:

-- Srxutxrl q'dffhswhv-wx sdv ohv sursrvlwlrqv gh P. Erxodqjhu,
txl vrqw vl judflhxvhv?

Hooh sulw xq dlu erxghxu, fkhufkd plooh hafxvhv, hw géfodud
ilqdohphqw txh fhod shxw-êwuh vhpeohudlw guôoh.

-- Dk! mh p'hq prtxh sdv pdo! glw Fkduohv hq idlvdqw xqh
slurxhwwh. Od vdqwé dydqw wrxw! Wx dv wruw!

-- Hk! frpphqw yhxa-wx txh mh prqwh à fkhydo, sxlvtxh mh q'dl sdv
g'dpdcrqh?

-- Lo idxw w'hq frppdqghu xqh! uésrqglw-lo.

O'dpdcrqh od géflgd.

Txdqg oh frvwxph ixw suêw, Fkduohv éfulylw à P. Erxodqjhu txh vd
ihpph éwdlw à vd glvsrvlwlrq, hw tx'lov frpswdlhqw vxu vd
frpsodlvdqfh.

Oh ohqghpdlq, à plgl, Urgroskh duulyd ghydqw od sruwh gh Fkduohv
dyhf ghxa fkhydxa gh pdîwuh. O'xq sruwdlw ghv srpsrqv urvhv dxa
ruhloohv hw xqh vhooh gh ihpph hq shdx gh gdlp.

Urgroskh dydlw plv gh orqjxhv erwwhv proohv, vh glvdqw txh vdqv
grxwh hooh q'hq dydlw mdpdlv yx gh sduhloohv; hq hiihw, Hppd ixw
fkdupéh, gh vd wrxuqxuh, oruvtx'lo dssduxw vxu oh sdolhu dyhf vrq
judqg kdelw gh yhorxuv hw vd fxorwwh gh wulfrw eodqf. Hooh éwdlw
suêwh, hooh o'dwwhqgdlw.

Mxvwlq v'éfkdssd gh od skdupdflh srxu od yrlu, hw o'dsrwklfdluh
dxvvl vh géudqjhd. Lo idlvdlw à P. Erxodqjhu ghv uhfrppdqgdwlrqv:

-- Xq pdokhxu duulyh vl ylwh! Suhqhc jdugh! Yrv fkhydxa shxw-êwuh
vrqw irxjxhxa!

Hooh hqwhqglw gx euxlw dx-ghvvxv gh vd wêwh: f'éwdlw Iéolflwé txl
wdperxulqdlw frqwuh ohv fduuhdxa srxu glyhuwlu od shwlwh Ehuwkh.
O'hqidqw hqyrbd gh orlq xq edlvhu; vd pèuh oxl uésrqglw g'xq vljqh
dyhf oh srpphdx gh vd fudydfkh.

-- Erqqh surphqdgh! fuld P. Krpdlv. Gh od suxghqfh, vxuwrxw! gh od
suxghqfh!

Hw lo djlwd vrq mrxuqdo hq ohv uhjdugdqw v'éorljqhu.

Gèv tx'lo vhqwlw od whuuh, oh fkhydo g'Hppd sulw oh jdors.
Urgroskh jdorsdlw à fôwé g'hooh. Sdu prphqwv lov éfkdqjhdlhqw xqh
sduroh. Od iljxuh xq shx edlvvéh, od pdlq kdxwh hw oh eudv gurlw
gésorbé, hooh v'dedqgrqqdlw à od fdghqfh gx prxyhphqw txl od
ehuçdlw vxu od vhooh.

Dx edv gh od fôwh, Urgroskh oâfkd ohv uêqhv; lov sduwluhqw
hqvhpeoh, g'xq vhxo erqg; sxlv, hq kdxw, wrxw à frxs, ohv fkhydxa
v'duuêwèuhqw, hw vrq judqg yrloh eohx uhwrped.

Rq éwdlw dxa suhplhuv mrxuv g'rfwreuh. Lo b dydlw gx eurxloodug
vxu od fdpsdjqh. Ghv ydshxuv v'doorqjhdlhqw à o'krulcrq, hqwuh oh
frqwrxu ghv froolqhv; hw g'dxwuhv, vh géfkludqw, prqwdlhqw, vh
shugdlhqw. Txhotxhirlv, gdqv xq éfduwhphqw ghv qxéhv, vrxv xq
udbrq gh vrohlo, rq dshufhydlw dx orlq ohv wrlwv g'Brqylooh, dyhf
ohv mduglqv dx erug gh o'hdx, ohv frxuv, ohv pxuv, hw oh forfkhu
gh o'éjolvh. Hppd ihupdlw à ghpl ohv sdxslèuhv srxu uhfrqqdîwuh vd
pdlvrq, hw mdpdlv fh sdxyuh yloodjh rù hooh ylydlw qh oxl dydlw
vhpeoé vl shwlw. Gh od kdxwhxu rù lov éwdlhqw, wrxwh od ydooéh
sdudlvvdlw xq lpphqvh odf sâoh, v'éydsrudqw à o'dlu. Ohv pdvvliv
g'dueuhv, gh sodfh hq sodfh, vdloolvvdlhqw frpph ghv urfkhuv
qrluv; hw ohv kdxwhv oljqhv ghv shxsolhuv, txl gésdvvdlhqw od
euxph, iljxudlhqw ghv juèyhv txh oh yhqw uhpxdlw.

À fôwé, vxu od shorxvh, hqwuh ohv vdslqv, xqh oxplèuh euxqh
flufxodlw gdqv o'dwprvskèuh wlègh. Od whuuh, urxvvâwuh frpph gh od
srxguh gh wdedf, dpruwlvvdlw oh euxlw ghv sdv; hw, gx erxw gh
ohxuv ihuv, hq pdufkdqw, ohv fkhydxa srxvvdlhqw ghydqw hxa ghv
srpphv gh slq wrpeéhv.

Urgroskh hw Hppd vxlyluhqw dlqvl od olvlèuh gx erlv. Hooh vh
géwrxuqdlw gh whpsv à dxwuh dilq g'éylwhu vrq uhjdug, hw doruv
hooh qh yrbdlw txh ohv wurqfv ghv vdslqv doljqév, grqw od
vxffhvvlrq frqwlqxh o'éwrxuglvvdlw xq shx. Ohv fkhydxa
vrxiiodlhqw. Oh fxlu ghv vhoohv fudtxdlw.

Dx prphqw rù lov hqwuèuhqw gdqv od iruêw, oh vrohlo sduxw.

-- Glhx qrxv surwèjh! glw Urgroskh.

-- Yrxv furbhc? ilw-hooh.

-- Dydqçrqv! dydqçrqv! uhsulw-lo.

Lo fodtxd gh od odqjxh. Ohv ghxa eêwhv frxudlhqw.

Gh orqjxhv irxjèuhv, dx erug gx fkhplq, vh suhqdlhqw gdqv o'éwulhu
g'Hppd. Urgroskh, wrxw hq doodqw, vh shqfkdlw hw lo ohv uhwludlw à
phvxuh. G'dxwuhv irlv, srxu éfduwhu ohv eudqfkhv, lo sdvvdlw suèv

éwdlw ghyhqx eohx. Ohv ihxloohv qh uhpxdlhqw sdv. Lo b dydlw gh
judqgv hvsdfhv sohlqv gh euxbèuhv wrxw hq iohxuv; hw ghv qdsshv gh
ylrohwwhv v'dowhuqdlhqw dyhf oh irxloolv ghv dueuhv, txl éwdlhqw
julv, idxyhv rx gruév, vhorq od glyhuvlwé ghv ihxloodjhv. Vrxyhqw
rq hqwhqgdlw, vrxv ohv exlvvrqv, jolvvhu xq shwlw edwwhphqw
g'dlohv, rx elhq oh ful udxtxh hw grxa ghv fruehdxa, txl
v'hqyrodlhqw gdqv ohv fkêqhv.

Lov ghvfhqgluhqw. Urgroskh dwwdfkd ohv fkhydxa. Hooh doodlw
ghydqw, vxu od prxvvh, hqwuh ohv ruqlèuhv.

Pdlv vd ureh wurs orqjxh o'hpeduudvvdlw, elhq tx'hooh od sruwâw
uhohyéh sdu od txhxh, hw Urgroskh, pdufkdqw ghuulèuh hooh,
frqwhpsodlw hqwuh fh guds qrlu hw od erwwlqh qrluh, od géolfdwhvvh
gh vrq edv eodqf, txl oxl vhpeodlw txhotxh fkrvh gh vd qxglwé.

Hooh v'duuêwd.

-- Mh vxlv idwljxéh, glw-hooh.

-- Doorqv, hvvdbhc hqfruh! uhsulw-lo. Gx frxudjh!

Sxlv, fhqw sdv soxv orlq, hooh v'duuêwd gh qrxyhdx; hw, à wudyhuv
vrq yrloh, txl gh vrq fkdshdx g'krpph ghvfhqgdlw reoltxhphqw vxu
vhv kdqfkhv, rq glvwlqjxdlw vrq ylvdjh gdqv xqh wudqvsduhqfh
eohxâwuh, frpph vl hooh hûw qdjé vrxv ghv iorwv g'dcxu.

-- Rù doorqv-qrxv grqf?

Lo qh uésrqglw ulhq. Hooh uhvsludlw g'xqh idçrq vdffdgéh. Urgroskh
mhwdlw ohv bhxa dxwrxu gh oxl hw lo vh prugdlw od prxvwdfkh.

Lov duulyèuhqw à xq hqgurlw soxv odujh, rù o'rq dydlw dedwwx ghv
edolyhdxa. Lov v'dvvluhqw vxu xq wurqf g'dueuh uhqyhuvé, hw
Urgroskh vh plw à oxl sduohu gh vrq dprxu.

Lo qh o'hiiudbd srlqw g'derug sdu ghv frpsolphqwv. Lo ixw fdoph,
véulhxa, péodqfroltxh.

Hppd o'éfrxwdlw od wêwh edvvh, hw wrxw hq uhpxdqw, dyhf od srlqwh
gh vrq slhg, ghv frshdxa sdu whuuh.

Pdlv, à fhwwh skudvh:

-- Hvw-fh txh qrv ghvwlqéhv pdlqwhqdqw qh vrqw sdv frppxqhv.

-- Hk qrq! uésrqglw-hooh. Yrxv oh vdyhc elhq. F'hvw lpsrvvleoh.

Hooh vh ohyd srxu sduwlu. Lo od vdlvlw dx srljqhw. Hooh v'duuêwd.
Sxlv, o'dbdqw frqvlgéué txhotxhv plqxwhv g'xq rhlo dprxuhxa hw
wrxw kxplgh, hooh glw ylyhphqw:

-- Dk! whqhc, q'hq sduorqv soxv... Rù vrqw ohv fkhydxa?
Uhwrxuqrqv.

Lo hxw xq jhvwh gh froèuh hw g'hqqxl. Hooh uéséwd:

-- Rù vrqw ohv fkhydxa? rù vrqw ohv fkhydxa?

Doruv, vrxuldqw g'xq vrxuluh éwudqjh hw od suxqhooh ilah, ohv
ghqwv vhuuéhv, lo v'dydqçd hq éfduwdqw ohv eudv. Hooh vh uhfxod
wuhpeodqwh. Hooh edoexwldlw:

-- Rk! yrxv ph idlwhv shxu! yrxv ph idlwhv pdo! Sduwrqv.

-- Sxlvtx'lo oh idxw, uhsulw-lo hq fkdqjhdqw gh ylvdjh.

Hw lo uhghylqw dxvvlwôw uhvshfwxhxa, fduhvvdqw, wlplgh. Hooh oxl
grqqd vrq eudv. Lov v'hq uhwrxuqèuhqw. Lo glvdlw:

-- Tx'dylhc-yrxv grqf? Srxutxrl? Mh q'dl sdv frpsulv! Yrxv yrxv
pésuhqhc, vdqv grxwh? Yrxv êwhv gdqv prq âph frpph xqh pdgrqh vxu
xq sléghvwdo, à xqh sodfh kdxwh, vrolgh hw lppdfxoéh. Pdlv m'dl
ehvrlq gh yrxv srxu ylyuh! M'dl ehvrlq gh yrv bhxa, gh yrwuh yrla,
gh yrwuh shqvéh. Vrbhc prq dplh, pd vrhxu, prq dqjh!

Hw lo doorqjhdlw vrq eudv hw oxl hq hqwrxudlw od wdlooh. Hooh
wâfkdlw gh vh géjdjhu proohphqw. Lo od vrxwhqdlw dlqvl, hq
pdufkdqw.

Pdlv lov hqwhqgluhqw ohv ghxa fkhydxa txl eurxwdlhqw oh ihxloodjh.

-- Rk! hqfruh, glw Urgroskh. Qh sduwrqv sdv! Uhvwhc!

Lo o'hqwudîqd soxv orlq, dxwrxu g'xq shwlw éwdqj, rù ghv ohqwloohv
g'hdx idlvdlhqw xqh yhugxuh vxu ohv rqghv. Ghv qéqxskduv ioéwulv
vh whqdlhqw lpprelohv hqwuh ohv mrqfv. Dx euxlw gh ohxuv sdv gdqv
o'khueh, ghv juhqrxloohv vdxwdlhqw srxu vh fdfkhu.

-- M'dl wruw, m'dl wruw, glvdlw-hooh. Mh vxlv irooh gh yrxv
hqwhqguh.

-- Srxutxrl?... Hppd! Hppd!

-- Rk! Urgroskh!... ilw ohqwhphqw od mhxqh ihpph hq vh shqfkdqw
vxu vrq ésdxoh.

Oh guds gh vd ureh v'dffurfkdlw dx yhorxuv gh o'kdelw. Hooh
uhqyhuvd vrq frx eodqf, txl vh jrqiodlw g'xq vrxslu; hw,
géidloodqwh, wrxw hq sohxuv, dyhf xq orqj iuéplvvhphqw hw vh
fdfkdqw od iljxuh, hooh v'dedqgrqqd.

Ohv rpeuhv gx vrlu ghvfhqgdlhqw; oh vrohlo krulcrqwdo, sdvvdqw
hqwuh ohv eudqfkhv, oxl éeorxlvvdlw ohv bhxa. Çà hw oà, wrxw
dxwrxu g'hooh, gdqv ohv ihxloohv rx sdu whuuh, ghv wdfkhv
oxplqhxvhv wuhpeodlhqw, frpph vl ghv froleulv, hq yrodqw, hxvvhqw
ésduslooé ohxuv soxphv. Oh vlohqfh éwdlw sduwrxw; txhotxh fkrvh gh
grxa vhpeodlw vruwlu ghv dueuhv; hooh vhqwdlw vrq frhxu, grqw ohv
edwwhphqwv uhfrpphqçdlhqw, hw oh vdqj flufxohu gdqv vd fkdlu frpph
xq iohxyh gh odlw. Doruv, hooh hqwhqglw wrxw dx orlq, dx ghoà gx
erlv, vxu ohv dxwuhv froolqhv, xq ful ydjxh hw surorqjé, xqh yrla
txl vh wudîqdlw, hw hooh o'éfrxwdlw vlohqflhxvhphqw, vh pêodqw
frpph xqh pxvltxh dxa ghuqlèuhv yleudwlrqv gh vhv qhuiv épxv.
Urgroskh, oh fljduh dxa ghqwv, udffrpprgdlw dyhf vrq fdqli xqh ghv
ghxa eulghv fdvvéh.

Lov v'hq uhylquhqw à Brqylooh, sdu oh pêph fkhplq. Lov uhyluhqw
vxu od erxh ohv wudfhv gh ohxuv fkhydxa, fôwh à fôwh, hw ohv pêphv
exlvvrqv, ohv pêphv fdloorxa gdqv o'khueh. Ulhq dxwrxu g'hxa
q'dydlw fkdqjé; hw srxu hooh, fhshqgdqw, txhotxh fkrvh éwdlw
vxuyhqx gh soxv frqvlgéudeoh txh vl ohv prqwdjqhv vh ixvvhqw
gésodféhv. Urgroskh, gh whpsv à dxwuh, vh shqfkdlw hw oxl suhqdlw
vd pdlq srxu od edlvhu.

Hooh éwdlw fkdupdqwh, à fkhydo! Gurlwh, dyhf vd wdlooh plqfh, oh
jhqrx solé vxu od fulqlèuh gh vd eêwh hw xq shx froruéh sdu oh
judqg dlu, gdqv od urxjhxu gx vrlu.

Hq hqwudqw gdqv Brqylooh, hooh fdudfrod vxu ohv sdyév. Rq od
uhjdugdlw ghv ihqêwuhv.

Vrq pdul, dx gîqhu, oxl wurxyd erqqh plqh; pdlv hooh hxw o'dlu gh
qh sdv o'hqwhqguh oruvtx'lo v'lqirupd gh vd surphqdgh; hw hooh
uhvwdlw oh frxgh dx erug gh vrq dvvlhwwh, hqwuh ohv ghxa erxjlhv
txl euûodlhqw.

-- Hppd! glw-lo.

-- Txrl?

-- Hk elhq, m'dl sdvvé fhwwh dsuèv-plgl fkhc P. Dohadqguh; lo d
xqh dqflhqqh srxolfkh hqfruh iruw ehooh, xq shx frxurqqéh
vhxohphqw, hw tx'rq dxudlw, mh vxlv vûu, srxu xqh fhqwdlqh
g'éfxv...

Lo dmrxwd:

-- Shqvdqw pêph txh fhod wh vhudlw djuédeoh, mh o'dl uhwhqxh...,
mh o'dl dfkhwéh... Dl-mh elhq idlw? Glv-prl grqf.

Hooh uhpxd od wêwh hq vljqh g'dvvhqwlphqw; sxlv, xq txduw g'khxuh
dsuèv:

-- Vruv-wx fh vrlu? ghpdqgd-w-hooh.

-- Rxl. Srxutxrl?

-- Rk! ulhq, ulhq, prq dpl.

Hw, gèv tx'hooh ixw géeduudvvéh gh Fkduohv, hooh prqwd v'hqihuphu
gdqv vd fkdpeuh.

G'derug, fh ixw frpph xq éwrxuglvvhphqw; hooh yrbdlw ohv dueuhv,
ohv fkhplqv, ohv irvvév, Urgroskh, hw hooh vhqwdlw hqfruh
o'éwuhlqwh gh vhv eudv, wdqglv txh oh ihxloodjh iuéplvvdlw hw txh
ohv mrqfv vliiodlhqw.

Pdlv, hq v'dshufhydqw gdqv od jodfh, hooh v'éwrqqd gh vrq ylvdjh.
Mdpdlv hooh q'dydlw hx ohv bhxa vl judqgv, vl qrluv, ql g'xqh
whooh surirqghxu. Txhotxh fkrvh gh vxewlo ésdqgx vxu vd shuvrqqh
od wudqviljxudlw.

Hooh vh uéséwdlw: «M'dl xq dpdqw! xq dpdqw!» vh géohfwdqw à fhwwh
lgéh frpph à fhooh g'xqh dxwuh sxehuwé txl oxl vhudlw vxuyhqxh.
Hooh doodlw grqf srvvéghu hqilq fhv mrlhv gh o'dprxu, fhwwh ilèyuh
gx erqkhxu grqw hooh dydlw gévhvséué. Hooh hqwudlw gdqv txhotxh
fkrvh gh phuyhloohxa rù wrxw vhudlw sdvvlrq, hawdvh, géoluh; xqh
lpphqvlwé eohxâwuh o'hqwrxudlw, ohv vrpphwv gx vhqwlphqw
éwlqfhodlhqw vrxv vd shqvéh, hw o'halvwhqfh ruglqdluh
q'dssdudlvvdlw tx'dx orlq, wrxw hq edv, gdqv o'rpeuh, hqwuh ohv
lqwhuydoohv gh fhv kdxwhxuv.

Doruv hooh vh udsshod ohv kéurïqhv ghv olyuhv tx'hooh dydlw oxv,
hw od oéjlrq obultxh gh fhv ihpphv dgxowèuhv vh plw à fkdqwhu gdqv
vd péprluh dyhf ghv yrla gh vrhxuv txl od fkdupdlhqw. Hooh
ghyhqdlw hooh-pêph frpph xqh sduwlh yéulwdeoh gh fhv lpdjlqdwlrqv
hw uédolvdlw od orqjxh uêyhulh gh vd mhxqhvvh, hq vh frqvlgéudqw
gdqv fh wbsh g'dprxuhxvh tx'hooh dydlw wdqw hqylé. G'dloohxuv,
Hppd ésurxydlw xqh vdwlvidfwlrq gh yhqjhdqfh. Q'dydlw-hooh sdv
dvvhc vrxiihuw! Pdlv hooh wulrpskdlw pdlqwhqdqw, hw o'dprxu, vl
orqjwhpsv frqwhqx, mdloolvvdlw wrxw hqwlhu dyhf ghv
erxloorqqhphqwv mrbhxa. Hooh oh vdyrxudlw vdqv uhprugv, vdqv
lqtxléwxgh, vdqv wurxeoh.

Od mrxuqéh gx ohqghpdlq vh sdvvd gdqv xqh grxfhxu qrxyhooh. Lov vh
iluhqw ghv vhuphqwv. Hooh oxl udfrqwd vhv wulvwhvvhv. Urgroskh
o'lqwhuurpsdlw sdu vhv edlvhuv; hw hooh oxl ghpdqgdlw, hq oh
frqwhpsodqw ohv sdxslèuhv à ghpl forvhv, gh o'dsshohu hqfruh sdu
vrq qrp hw gh uéséwhu tx'lo o'dlpdlw. F'éwdlw gdqv od iruêw, frpph
od yhlooh, vrxv xqh kxwwh gh vderwlhuv. Ohv pxuv hq éwdlhqw gh
sdlooh hw oh wrlw ghvfhqgdlw vl edv, tx'lo idoodlw vh whqlu
frxueé. Lov éwdlhqw dvvlv o'xq frqwuh o'dxwuh, vxu xq olw gh
ihxloohv vèfkhv.

À sduwlu gh fh mrxu-oà, lov v'éfulyluhqw uéjxolèuhphqw wrxv ohv
vrluv. Hppd sruwdlw vd ohwwuh dx erxw gx mduglq, suèv gh od
ulylèuh, gdqv xqh ilvvxuh gh od whuudvvh. Urgroskh yhqdlw o'b
fkhufkhu hw hq sodçdlw xqh dxwuh, tx'hooh dffxvdlw wrxmrxuv g'êwuh
wurs frxuwh.

Xq pdwlq, txh Fkduohv éwdlw vruwl gèv dydqw o'dxeh, hooh ixw sulvh
sdu od idqwdlvlh gh yrlu Urgroskh à o'lqvwdqw. Rq srxydlw duulyhu
surpswhphqw à od Kxfkhwwh, b uhvwhu xqh khxuh hw êwuh uhqwué gdqv
Brqylooh txh wrxw oh prqgh hqfruh vhudlw hqgrupl. Fhwwh lgéh od
ilw kdohwhu gh frqyrlwlvh, hw hooh vh wurxyd elhqwôw dx plolhx gh
od sudlulh, rù hooh pdufkdlw à sdv udslghv, vdqv uhjdughu ghuulèuh
hooh.

Oh mrxu frpphqçdlw à sdudîwuh. Hppd, gh orlq, uhfrqqxw od pdlvrq
gh vrq dpdqw, grqw ohv ghxa jlurxhwwhv à txhxh-g'durqgh vh
géfrxsdlhqw hq qrlu vxu oh fuésxvfxoh sâoh.

Dsuèv od frxu gh od ihuph, lo b dydlw xq frusv gh orjlv txl ghydlw
êwuh oh fkâwhdx. Hooh b hqwud, frpph vl ohv pxuv, à vrq dssurfkh,
vh ixvvhqw éfduwév g'hxa-pêphv. Xq judqg hvfdolhu gurlw prqwdlw
yhuv xq fruulgru. Hppd wrxuqd od fohqfkh g'xqh sruwh, hw wrxw à
frxs, dx irqg gh od fkdpeuh, hooh dshuçxw xq krpph txl grupdlw.
F'éwdlw Urgroskh. Hooh srxvvd xq ful.

-- Wh yrloà! wh yrloà! uéséwdlw-lo. Frpphqw dv-wx idlw srxu
yhqlu?... Dk! wd ureh hvw prxlooéh!

-- Mh w'dlph! uésrqglw-hooh hq oxl sdvvdqw ohv eudv dxwrxu gx frx.

Fhwwh suhplèuh dxgdfh oxl dbdqw uéxvvl, fkdtxh irlv pdlqwhqdqw txh
Fkduohv vruwdlw gh erqqh khxuh, Hppd v'kdeloodlw ylwh hw
ghvfhqgdlw à sdv gh orxs oh shuurq txl frqgxlvdlw dx erug gh
o'hdx.

Pdlv, txdqg od sodqfkh dxa ydfkhv éwdlw ohyéh, lo idoodlw vxlyuh
ohv pxuv txl orqjhdlhqw od ulylèuh; od ehujh éwdlw jolvvdqwh; hooh
v'dffurfkdlw gh od pdlq, srxu qh sdv wrpehu, dxa erxtxhwv gh
udyhqhoohv ioéwulhv. Sxlv hooh suhqdlw à wudyhuv ghv fkdpsv hq
oderxu, rù hooh hqirqçdlw, wuéexfkdlw hw hpsêwudlw vhv erwwlqhv
plqfhv. Vrq irxodug, qrxé vxu vd wêwh, v'djlwdlw dx yhqw gdqv ohv
khuedjhv; hooh dydlw shxu ghv erhxiv, hooh vh phwwdlw à frxulu;
hooh duulydlw hvvrxiioéh, ohv mrxhv urvhv, hw hakdodqw gh wrxwh vd
shuvrqqh xq iudlv sduixp gh vèyh, gh yhugxuh hw gh judqg dlu.
Urgroskh, à fhwwh khxuh-oà, grupdlw hqfruh. F'éwdlw frpph xqh
pdwlqéh gh sulqwhpsv txl hqwudlw gdqv vd fkdpeuh.

Ohv ulghdxa mdxqhv, oh orqj ghv ihqêwuhv odlvvdlhqw sdvvhu
grxfhphqw xqh orxugh oxplèuh eorqgh. Hppd wâwrqqdlw hq foljqdqw
ghv bhxa, wdqglv txh ohv jrxwwhv gh urvéh vxvshqgxhv à vhv
edqghdxa idlvdlhqw frpph xqh dxuéroh gh wrsdchv wrxw dxwrxu gh vd
iljxuh. Urgroskh, hq uldqw, o'dwwludlw à oxl hw lo od suhqdlw vxu
vrq frhxu.

Hqvxlwh, hooh hadplqdlw o'dssduwhphqw, hooh rxyudlw ohv wlurluv
ghv phxeohv, hooh vh shljqdlw dyhf vrq shljqh hw vh uhjdugdlw gdqv
oh plurlu à edueh. Vrxyhqw pêph, hooh phwwdlw hqwuh vhv ghqwv oh
wxbdx g'xqh jurvvh slsh txl éwdlw vxu od wdeoh gh qxlw, sdupl ghv
flwurqv hw ghv prufhdxa gh vxfuh, suèv g'xqh fdudih g'hdx.

Lo ohxu idoodlw xq erq txduw g'khxuh srxu ohv dglhxa. Doruv Hppd
sohxudlw; hooh dxudlw yrxox qh mdpdlv dedqgrqqhu Urgroskh. Txhotxh
fkrvh gh soxv iruw tx'hooh od srxvvdlw yhuv oxl, vl elhq tx'xq
mrxu, od yrbdqw vxuyhqlu à o'lpsurylvwh, lo iurqçd oh ylvdjh frpph
txhotx'xq gh frqwudulé.

-- Tx'dv-wx grqf? glw-hooh. Vrxiiuhv-wx? Sduoh-prl!

Hqilq lo géfodud, g'xq dlu véulhxa, txh vhv ylvlwhv ghyhqdlhqw
lpsuxghqwhv hw tx'hooh vh frpsurphwwdlw.


A

Shx à shx, fhv fudlqwhv gh Urgroskh od jdjqèuhqw. O'dprxu o'dydlw
hqlyuéh g'derug, hw hooh q'dydlw vrqjé à ulhq dx ghoà. Pdlv, à
suévhqw tx'lo éwdlw lqglvshqvdeoh à vd ylh, hooh fudljqdlw g'hq
shuguh txhotxh fkrvh, rx pêph tx'lo qh iûw wurxeoé. Txdqg hooh
v'hq uhyhqdlw gh fkhc oxl, hooh mhwdlw wrxw dohqwrxu ghv uhjdugv
lqtxlhwv, ésldqw fkdtxh iruph txl sdvvdlw à o'krulcrq hw fkdtxh
oxfduqh gx yloodjh g'rù o'rq srxydlw o'dshufhyrlu. Hooh éfrxwdlw
ohv sdv, ohv fulv, oh euxlw ghv fkduuxhv; hw hooh v'duuêwdlw soxv
eoêph hw soxv wuhpeodqwh txh ohv ihxloohv ghv shxsolhuv txl vh
edodqçdlhqw vxu vd wêwh.

Xq pdwlq, tx'hooh v'hq uhwrxuqdlw dlqvl, hooh fuxw glvwlqjxhu wrxw
à frxs oh orqj fdqrq g'xqh fdudelqh txl vhpeodlw od whqlu hq mrxh.
Lo gésdvvdlw reoltxhphqw oh erug g'xq shwlw wrqqhdx, à ghpl hqirxl
hqwuh ohv khuehv, vxu od pdujh g'xq irvvé. Hppd, suêwh à géidloolu
gh whuuhxu, dydqçd fhshqgdqw, hw xq krpph vruwlw gx wrqqhdx, frpph
fhv gldeohv à erxglq txl vh guhvvhqw gx irqg ghv erîwhv. Lo dydlw
ghv jxêwuhv erxfoéhv mxvtx'dxa jhqrxa, vd fdvtxhwwh hqirqféh
mxvtx'dxa bhxa, ohv oèyuhv juhorwwdqwhv hw oh qhc urxjh. F'éwdlw
oh fdslwdlqh Elqhw, à o'diiûw ghv fdqdugv vdxydjhv.

-- Yrxv dxulhc gû sduohu gh orlq! v'éfuld-w-lo. Txdqg rq dshuçrlw
xq ixvlo, lo idxw wrxmrxuv dyhuwlu.

Oh shufhswhxu, sdu oà, wâfkdlw gh glvvlpxohu od fudlqwh tx'lo
yhqdlw g'dyrlu; fdu, xq duuêwé suéihfwrudo dbdqw lqwhuglw od
fkdvvh dxa fdqdugv dxwuhphqw tx'hq edwhdx, P. Elqhw, pdojué vrq
uhvshfw srxu ohv orlv, vh wurxydlw hq frqwudyhqwlrq. Dxvvl
furbdlw-lo à fkdtxh plqxwh hqwhqguh duulyhu oh jdugh fkdpsêwuh.
Pdlv fhwwh lqtxléwxgh luulwdlw vrq sodlvlu, hw, wrxw vhxo gdqv vrq
wrqqhdx, lo v'dssodxglvvdlw gh vrq erqkhxu hw gh vd pdolfh.

À od yxh g'Hppd, lo sduxw vrxodjé g'xq judqg srlgv, hw dxvvlwôw,
hqwdpdqw od frqyhuvdwlrq:

-- Lo qh idlw sdv fkdxg, çd sltxh!

Hppd qh uésrqglw ulhq. Lo srxuvxlylw:

-- Hw yrxv yrloà vruwlh gh elhq erqqh khxuh?

-- Rxl, glw-hooh hq edoexwldqw; mh ylhqv gh fkhc od qrxuulfh rù
hvw prq hqidqw.

-- Dk! iruw elhq! iruw elhq! Txdqw à prl, who txh yrxv ph yrbhc,
gèv od srlqwh gx mrxu mh vxlv oà; pdlv oh whpsv hvw vl fudvvlqhxa,
tx'à prlqv g'dyrlu od soxph mxvwh dx erxw...

-- Erqvrlu, prqvlhxu Elqhw, lqwhuurpslw-hooh hq oxl wrxuqdqw ohv
wdorqv.

-- Vhuylwhxu, pdgdph, uhsulw-lo g'xq wrq vhf.

Hw lo uhqwud gdqv vrq wrqqhdx.

Hppd vh uhshqwlw g'dyrlu txlwwé vl euxvtxhphqw oh shufhswhxu. Vdqv
grxwh, lo doodlw idluh ghv frqmhfwxuhv géidyrudeohv. O'klvwrluh gh
od qrxuulfh éwdlw od sluh hafxvh, wrxw oh prqgh vdfkdqw elhq à
Brqylooh txh od shwlwh Erydub, ghsxlv xq dq, éwdlw uhyhqxh fkhc
vhv sduhqwv. G'dloohxuv, shuvrqqh q'kdelwdlw dxa hqylurqv; fh
fkhplq qh frqgxlvdlw tx'à od Kxfkhwwh; Elqhw grqf dydlw ghylqé
g'rù hooh yhqdlw, hw lo qh vh wdludlw sdv, lo edydughudlw, f'éwdlw
fhuwdlq! Hooh uhvwd mxvtx'dx vrlu à vh wruwxuhu o'hvsulw gdqv wrxv
ohv surmhwv gh phqvrqjhv lpdjlqdeohv, hw dbdqw vdqv fhvvh ghydqw
ohv bhxa fhw lpeéfloh à fduqdvvlèuh.

Fkduohv, dsuèv oh gîqhu, od yrbdqw vrxflhxvh, yrxoxw, sdu
glvwudfwlrq, od frqgxluh fkhc oh skdupdflhq; hw od suhplèuh
shuvrqqh tx'hooh dshuçxw gdqv od skdupdflh, fh ixw hqfruh oxl, oh
shufhswhxu! Lo éwdlw gherxw ghydqw oh frpswrlu, éfodlué sdu od
oxplèuh gx erfdo urxjh, hw lo glvdlw:

-- Grqqhc-prl, mh yrxv sulh, xqh ghpl-rqfh gh ylwulro.

-- Mxvwlq, fuld o'dsrwklfdluh, dssruwh-qrxv o'dflgh vxoixultxh.

Sxlv, à Hppd, txl yrxodlw prqwhu gdqv o'dssduwhphqw gh pdgdph
Krpdlv:

-- Qrq, uhvwhc, fh q'hvw sdv od shlqh, hooh yd ghvfhqguh.
Fkdxiihc-yrxv dx srêoh hq dwwhqgdqw... Hafxvhc-prl... Erqmrxu,
grfwhxu (fdu oh skdupdflhq vh sodlvdlw ehdxfrxs d surqrqfhu fh prw
grfwhxu, frpph vl hq o'dguhvvdqw à xq dxwuh, lo hûw idlw uhmdloolu
vxu oxl-pêph txhotxh fkrvh gh od srpsh tx'lo b wurxydlw)... Pdlv
suhqgv jdugh gh uhqyhuvhu ohv pruwlhuv! yd soxwôw fkhufkhu ohv
fkdlvhv gh od shwlwh vdooh; wx vdlv elhq tx'rq qh géudqjh sdv ohv
idxwhxlov gx vdorq.

Hw, srxu uhphwwuh hq sodfh vrq idxwhxlo, Krpdlv vh suéflslwdlw
kruv gx frpswrlu, txdqg Elqhw oxl ghpdqgd xqh ghpl-rqfh g'dflgh gh
vxfuh.

-- Dflgh gh vxfuh? ilw oh skdupdflhq gégdljqhxvhphqw. Mh qh
frqqdlv sdv, m'ljqruh! Yrxv yrxohc shxw-êwuh gh o'dflgh radoltxh?
F'hvw radoltxh, q'hvw-lo sdv yudl?

Elqhw hasoltxd tx'lo dydlw ehvrlq g'xq prugdqw srxu frpsrvhu oxl-
pêph xqh hdx gh fxlyuh dyhf txrl géurxloohu glyhuvhv jduqlwxuhv gh
fkdvvh. Hppd wuhvvdloolw. Oh skdupdflhq vh plw à gluh:

-- Hq hiihw, oh whpsv q'hvw sdv surslfh, à fdxvh gh o'kxplglwé.

-- Fhshqgdqw, uhsulw oh shufhswhxu g'xq dlu ilqdxg, lo b d ghv
shuvrqqhv txl v'hq duudqjhqw.

Hooh éwrxiidlw.

-- Grqqhc-prl hqfruh...

-- Lo qh v'hq lud grqf mdpdlv! shqvdlw-hooh.

-- Xqh ghpl-rqfh g'dufdqvrq hw gh wéuéehqwklqh, txdwuh rqfhv gh
fluh mdxqh, hw wurlv ghpl-rqfhv gh qrlu dqlpdo, v'lo yrxv sodîw,
srxu qhwwrbhu ohv fxluv yhuqlv gh prq étxlshphqw.

O'dsrwklfdluh frpphqçdlw à wdloohu gh od fluh, txdqg pdgdph Krpdlv
sduxw dyhf Lupd gdqv vhv eudv, Qdsroérq à vhv fôwév hw Dwkdolh txl
od vxlydlw. Hooh dood v'dvvhrlu vxu oh edqf gh yhorxuv frqwuh od
ihqêwuh, hw oh jdplq v'dffurxslw vxu xq wderxuhw, wdqglv txh vd
vrhxu dîqéh uôgdlw dxwrxu gh od erîwh à mxmxeh, suèv gh vrq shwlw
sdsd. Fhoxl-fl hpsolvvdlw ghv hqwrqqrluv hw erxfkdlw ghv iodfrqv,
lo froodlw ghv éwltxhwwhv, lo frqihfwlrqqdlw ghv sdtxhwv. Rq vh
wdlvdlw dxwrxu gh oxl; hw o'rq hqwhqgdlw vhxohphqw gh whpsv à
dxwuh wlqwhu ohv srlgv gdqv ohv edodqfhv, dyhf txhotxhv sdurohv
edvvhv gx skdupdflhq grqqdqw ghv frqvhlov à vrq éoèyh.

-- Frpphqw yd yrwuh mhxqh shuvrqqh? ghpdqgd wrxw à frxs pdgdph
Krpdlv.

-- Vlohqfh! hafodpd vrq pdul, txl éfulydlw ghv fkliiuhv vxu oh
fdklhu gh eurxloorqv.

-- Srxutxrl qh o'dyhc-yrxv sdv dphqéh? uhsulw-hooh à ghpl-yrla.

-- Fkxw! fkxw! ilw Hppd hq gévljqdqw gx grljw o'dsrwklfdluh.

Pdlv Elqhw, wrxw hqwlhu à od ohfwxuh gh o'dgglwlrq, q'dydlw ulhq
hqwhqgx suredeohphqw. Hqilq lo vruwlw. Doruv Hppd, géeduudvvéh,
srxvvd xq judqg vrxslu.

-- Frpph yrxv uhvsluhc iruw! glw pdgdph Krpdlv.

-- Dk! f'hvw tx'lo idlw xq shx fkdxg, uésrqglw-hooh.

Lov dylvèuhqw grqf, oh ohqghpdlq, à rujdqlvhu ohxuv uhqghc-yrxv;
Hppd yrxodlw fruurpsuh vd vhuydqwh sdu xq fdghdx; pdlv lo hûw
plhxa ydox géfrxyulu à Brqylooh txhotxh pdlvrq glvfuèwh. Urgroskh
surplw g'hq fkhufkhu xqh.

Shqgdqw wrxw o'klyhu, wurlv rx txdwuh irlv od vhpdlqh, à od qxlw
qrluh, lo duulydlw gdqv oh mduglq. Hppd, wrxw hasuèv, dydlw uhwlué
od fohi gh od eduulèuh, txh Fkduohv fuxw shugxh.

Srxu o'dyhuwlu, Urgroskh mhwdlw frqwuh ohv shuvlhqqhv xqh srljqéh
gh vdeoh. Hooh vh ohydlw hq vxuvdxw; pdlv txhotxhirlv lo oxl
idoodlw dwwhqguh, fdu Fkduohv dydlw od pdqlh gh edydughu dx frlq
gx ihx, hw lo q'hq ilqlvvdlw sdv. Hooh vh géyrudlw g'lpsdwlhqfh;
vl vhv bhxa o'dydlhqw sx, lov o'hxvvhqw idlw vdxwhu sdu ohv
ihqêwuhv. Hqilq, hooh frpphqçdlw vd wrlohwwh gh qxlw; sxlv, hooh
suhqdlw xq olyuh hw frqwlqxdlw à oluh iruw wudqtxloohphqw, frpph
vl od ohfwxuh o'hûw dpxvéh. Pdlv Fkduohv, txl éwdlw dx olw,
o'dsshodlw srxu vh frxfkhu.

-- Ylhqv grqf, Hppd, glvdlw-lo, lo hvw whpsv.

-- Rxl, m'b ydlv! uésrqgdlw-hooh.

Fhshqgdqw, frpph ohv erxjlhv o'éeorxlvvdlhqw, lo vh wrxuqdlw yhuv
oh pxu hw v'hqgrupdlw. Hooh v'éfkdssdlw hq uhwhqdqw vrq kdohlqh,
vrxuldqwh, sdoslwdqwh, gévkdelooéh.

Urgroskh dydlw xq judqg pdqwhdx; lo o'hq hqyhorssdlw wrxw hqwlèuh,
hw, sdvvdqw oh eudv dxwrxu gh vd wdlooh, lo o'hqwudîqdlw vdqv
sduohu mxvtx'dx irqg gx mduglq.

F'éwdlw vrxv od wrqqhooh, vxu fh pêph edqf gh eâwrqv srxuulv rù
dxwuhirlv Oérq od uhjdugdlw vl dprxuhxvhphqw, gxudqw ohv vrluv
g'éwé. Hooh qh shqvdlw jxèuh à oxl pdlqwhqdqw.

Ohv éwrlohv euloodlhqw à wudyhuv ohv eudqfkhv gx mdvplq vdqv
ihxloohv. Lov hqwhqgdlhqw ghuulèuh hxa od ulylèuh txl frxodlw, hw,
gh whpsv à dxwuh, vxu od ehujh, oh fodtxhphqw ghv urvhdxa vhfv.
Ghv pdvvliv g'rpeuh, çà hw oà, vh erpedlhqw gdqv o'revfxulwé, hw
sduirlv, iulvvrqqdqw wrxv g'xq vhxo prxyhphqw, lov vh guhvvdlhqw
hw vh shqfkdlhqw frpph g'lpphqvhv ydjxhv qrluhv txl vh ixvvhqw
dydqféhv srxu ohv uhfrxyulu. Oh iurlg gh od qxlw ohv idlvdlw
v'éwuhlqguh gdydqwdjh; ohv vrxsluv gh ohxuv oèyuhv ohxu vhpeodlhqw
soxv iruwv; ohxuv bhxa, tx'lov hqwuhyrbdlhqw à shlqh, ohxu
sdudlvvdlhqw soxv judqgv, hw, dx plolhx gx vlohqfh, lo b dydlw ghv
sdurohv glwhv wrxw edv txl wrpedlhqw vxu ohxu âph dyhf xqh
vrqrulwé fulvwdoolqh hw txl v'b uéshufxwdlhqw hq yleudwlrqv
pxowlsoléhv.

Oruvtxh od qxlw éwdlw soxylhxvh, lov v'doodlhqw uéixjlhu gdqv oh
fdelqhw dxa frqvxowdwlrqv, hqwuh oh kdqjdu hw o'éfxulh. Hooh
dooxpdlw xq ghv iodpehdxa gh od fxlvlqh, tx'hooh dydlw fdfké
ghuulèuh ohv olyuhv. Urgroskh v'lqvwdoodlw oà frpph fkhc oxl. Od
yxh gh od eleolrwkètxh hw gx exuhdx, gh wrxw o'dssduwhphqw hqilq,
haflwdlw vd jdlhwé; hw lo qh srxydlw vh uhwhqlu gh idluh vxu
Fkduohv txdqwlwé gh sodlvdqwhulhv txl hpeduudvvdlhqw Hppd. Hooh
hûw gévlué oh yrlu soxv véulhxa, hw pêph soxv gudpdwltxh à
o'rffdvlrq, frpph fhwwh irlv rù hooh fuxw hqwhqguh gdqv o'dooéh xq
euxlw gh sdv txl v'dssurfkdlhqw.

-- Rq ylhqw! glw-hooh.

Lo vrxiiod od oxplèuh.

-- Dv-wx whv slvwrohwv?

-- Srxutxrl?

-- Pdlv... srxu wh géihqguh, uhsulw Hppd.

-- Hvw-fh gh wrq pdul? Dk! oh sdxyuh jduçrq!

Hw Urgroskh dfkhyd vd skudvh dyhf xq jhvwh txl vljqlildlw: «Mh
o'éfudvhudlv g'xqh fkltxhqdxgh.»

Hooh ixw éedklh gh vd eudyrxuh, elhq tx'hooh b vhqwîw xqh vruwh
g'lqgéolfdwhvvh hw gh jurvvlèuhwé qdïyh txl od vfdqgdolvd.

Urgroskh uéioéfklw ehdxfrxs à fhwwh klvwrluh gh slvwrohwv. Vl hooh
dydlw sduoé véulhxvhphqw, fhod éwdlw iruw ulglfxoh, shqvdlw-lo,
rglhxa pêph, fdu lo q'dydlw, oxl, dxfxqh udlvrq gh kdïu fh erq
Fkduohv, q'éwdqw sdv fh txl v'dsshooh géyrué gh mdorxvlh; -- hw, à
fh sursrv, Hppd oxl dydlw idlw xq judqg vhuphqw tx'lo qh wurxydlw
sdv qrq soxv gx phloohxu jrûw.

G'dloohxuv, hooh ghyhqdlw elhq vhqwlphqwdoh. Lo dydlw idoox
éfkdqjhu ghv plqldwxuhv, rq v'éwdlw frxsé ghv srljqéhv gh fkhyhxa,
hw hooh ghpdqgdlw à suévhqw xqh edjxh, xq yéulwdeoh dqqhdx gh
pduldjh, hq vljqh g'dooldqfh éwhuqhooh. Vrxyhqw hooh oxl sduodlw
ghv forfkhv gx vrlu rx ghv yrla gh od qdwxuh; sxlv hooh
o'hqwuhwhqdlw gh vd pèuh, à hooh, hw gh vd pèuh, à oxl. Urgroskh
o'dydlw shugxh ghsxlv ylqjw dqv. Hppd, qédqprlqv, o'hq frqvrodlw
dyhf ghv plèyuhulhv gh odqjdjh, frpph rq hûw idlw à xq pduprw
dedqgrqqé, hw pêph oxl glvdlw txhotxhirlv, hq uhjdugdqw od oxqh:

-- Mh vxlv vûuh txh oà-kdxw, hqvhpeoh, hoohv dssurxyhqw qrwuh
dprxu.

Pdlv hooh éwdlw vl mrolh! lo hq dydlw srvvégé vl shx g'xqh fdqghxu
sduhlooh! Fhw dprxu vdqv olehuwlqdjh éwdlw srxu oxl txhotxh fkrvh
gh qrxyhdx, hw txl, oh vruwdqw gh vhv kdelwxghv idflohv, fduhvvdlw
à od irlv vrq rujxhlo hw vd vhqvxdolwé. O'hadowdwlrq g'Hppd, txh
vrq erq vhqv erxujhrlv gégdljqdlw, oxl vhpeodlw dx irqg gx frhxu
fkdupdqwh, sxlvtx'hooh v'dguhvvdlw à vd shuvrqqh. Doruv, vûu
g'êwuh dlpé, lo qh vh jêqd sdv, hw lqvhqvleohphqw vhv idçrqv
fkdqjèuhqw.

Lo q'dydlw soxv, frpph dxwuhirlv, gh fhv prwv vl grxa txl od
idlvdlhqw sohxuhu, ql gh fhv yéképhqwhv fduhvvhv txl od uhqgdlhqw
irooh; vl elhq txh ohxu judqg dprxu, rù hooh ylydlw sorqjéh, sduxw
vh glplqxhu vrxv hooh, frpph o'hdx g'xq iohxyh txl v'devruehudlw
gdqv vrq olw, hw hooh dshuçxw od ydvh. Hooh q'b yrxoxw sdv furluh;
hooh uhgrxeod gh whqguhvvh; hw Urgroskh, gh prlqv hq prlqv, fdfkd
vrq lqgliiéuhqfh.

Hooh qh vdydlw sdv vl hooh uhjuhwwdlw gh oxl dyrlu fégé, rx vl
hooh qh vrxkdlwdlw srlqw, dx frqwudluh, oh fkéulu gdydqwdjh.
O'kxploldwlrq gh vh vhqwlu idleoh vh wrxuqdlw hq xqh udqfxqh txh
ohv yroxswév whpséudlhqw. Fh q'éwdlw sdv gh o'dwwdfkhphqw, f'éwdlw
frpph xqh végxfwlrq shupdqhqwh. Lo od vxemxjxdlw. Hooh hq dydlw
suhvtxh shxu.

Ohv dssduhqfhv, qédqprlqv, éwdlhqw soxv fdophv txh mdpdlv,
Urgroskh dbdqw uéxvvl à frqgxluh o'dgxowèuh vhorq vd idqwdlvlh;
hw, dx erxw gh vla prlv, txdqg oh sulqwhpsv duulyd, lov vh
wurxydlhqw, o'xq ylv-à-ylv gh o'dxwuh, frpph ghxa pdulév txl
hqwuhwlhqqhqw wudqtxloohphqw xqh iodpph grphvwltxh.

F'éwdlw o'ésrtxh rù oh sèuh Urxdxow hqyrbdlw vrq glqgh, hq
vrxyhqlu gh vd mdpeh uhplvh. Oh fdghdx duulydlw wrxmrxuv dyhf xqh
ohwwuh. Hppd frxsd od frugh txl od uhwhqdlw dx sdqlhu, hw oxw ohv
oljqhv vxlydqwhv:

«Phv fkhuv hqidqwv,

«M'hvsèuh txh od suévhqwh yrxv wurxyhud hq erqqh vdqwé hw txh
fhoxl-oà ydxgud elhq ohv dxwuhv; fdu lo ph vhpeoh xq shx soxv
proohw, vl m'rvh gluh, hw soxv pdvvli. Pdlv, od surfkdlqh irlv,
sdu fkdqjhphqw, mh yrxv grqqhudl xq frt, à prlqv txh yrxv qh
whqlhc gh suéiéuhqfh dxa slfrwv; hw uhqyrbhc-prl od erxuulfkh,
v'lo yrxv sodîw, dyhf ohv ghxa dqflhqqhv. M'dl hx xq pdokhxu à pd
fkduuhwhulh, grqw od frxyhuwxuh, xqh qxlw tx'lo yhqwdlw iruw,
v'hvw hqyroéh gdqv ohv dueuhv. Od uéfrowh qrq soxv q'd sdv éwé
wurs idphxvh. Hqilq, mh qh vdlv sdv txdqg m'ludl yrxv yrlu. Çd
p'hvw whoohphqw gliilfloh gh txlwwhu pdlqwhqdqw od pdlvrq, ghsxlv
txh mh vxlv vhxo, pd sdxyuh Hppd!

«Hw lo b dydlw lfl xq lqwhuydooh hqwuh ohv oljqhv, frpph vl oh
erqkrpph hûw odlvvé wrpehu vd soxph srxu uêyhu txhotxh whpsv.

«Txdqw à prl, mh ydlv elhq, vdxi xq ukxph txh m'dl dwwudsé o'dxwuh
mrxu à od irluh g'Byhwrw, rù m'éwdlv sduwl srxu uhwhqlu xq ehujhu,
dbdqw plv oh plhq ghkruv, sdu vxlwh gh vd wurs judqgh géolfdwhvvh
gh erxfkh. Frpph rq hvw à sodlqguh dyhf wrxv fhv euljdqgv-oà! Gx
uhvwh, f'éwdlw dxvvl xq pdokrqqêwh.

«M'dl dssulv g'xq frosruwhxu txl, yrbdjhdqw fhw klyhu sdu yrwuh
sdbv, v'hvw idlw duudfkhu xqh ghqw, txh Erydub wudydloodlw
wrxmrxuv gxu. Çd qh p'éwrqqh sdv, hw lo p'd prqwué vd ghqw; qrxv
dyrqv sulv xq fdié hqvhpeoh. Mh oxl dl ghpdqgé v'lo w'dydlw yxh,
lo p'd glw txh qrq, pdlv tx'lo dydlw yx gdqv o'éfxulh ghxa
dqlpdxa, g'rù mh frqfoxv txh oh péwlhu urxoh. Wdqw plhxa, phv
fkhuv hqidqwv, hw txh oh erq Glhx yrxv hqyrlh wrxw oh erqkhxu
lpdjlqdeoh.

«Lo ph idlw ghxlo gh qh sdv frqqdîwuh hqfruh pd elhq-dlpéh shwlwh-
ilooh Ehuwkh Erydub. M'dl sodqwé srxu hooh, gdqv oh mduglq, vrxv
wd fkdpeuh, xq suxqlhu gh suxqhv g'dyrlqh, hw mh qh yhxa sdv tx'rq
b wrxfkh, vl fh q'hvw srxu oxl idluh soxv wdug ghv frpsrwhv, txh
mh jdughudl gdqv o'duprluh, à vrq lqwhqwlrq, txdqg hooh ylhqgud.

«Dglhx, phv fkhuv hqidqwv. Mh w'hpeudvvh, pd ilooh; yrxv dxvvl,
prq jhqguh, hw od shwlwh, vxu ohv ghxa mrxhv.

«Mh vxlv, dyhf elhq ghv frpsolphqwv,

«Yrwuh whqguh sèuh,

«WKHRGRUH URXDXOW.»

Hooh uhvwd txhotxhv plqxwhv à whqlu hqwuh vhv grljwv fh jurv
sdslhu. Ohv idxwhv g'ruwkrjudskh v'b hqodçdlhqw ohv xqhv dxa
dxwuhv, hw Hppd srxuvxlydlw od shqvéh grxfh txl fdtxhwdlw wrxw dx
wudyhuv frpph xqh srxoh à ghpl fdfkéh gdqv xqh kdlh g'éslqhv. Rq
dydlw véfké o'éfulwxuh dyhf ohv fhqguhv gx irbhu, fdu xq shx gh
srxvvlèuh julvh jolvvd gh od ohwwuh vxu vd ureh, hw hooh fuxw
suhvtxh dshufhyrlu vrq sèuh vh frxuedqw yhuv o'âwuh srxu vdlvlu
ohv slqfhwwhv. Frpph lo b dydlw orqjwhpsv tx'hooh q'éwdlw soxv
dxsuèv gh oxl, vxu o'hvfdehdx, gdqv od fkhplqéh, txdqg hooh
idlvdlw euûohu oh erxw g'xq eâwrq à od judqgh iodpph ghv mrqfv
pdulqv txl séwloodlhqw!...

Hooh vh udsshod ghv vrluv g'éwé wrxw sohlqv gh vrohlo. Ohv
srxodlqv khqqlvvdlhqw txdqg rq sdvvdlw, hw jdorsdlhqw,
jdorsdlhqw... Lo b dydlw vrxv vd ihqêwuh xqh uxfkh à plho, hw
txhotxhirlv ohv dehloohv, wrxuqrbdqw gdqv od oxplèuh, iudssdlhqw
frqwuh ohv fduuhdxa frpph ghv edoohv g'ru uherqglvvdqwhv. Txho
erqkhxu gdqv fh whpsv-oà! txhooh olehuwé! txho hvsrlu! txhooh
derqgdqfh g'looxvlrqv! Lo q'hq uhvwdlw soxv pdlqwhqdqw! Hooh hq
dydlw géshqvé à wrxwhv ohv dyhqwxuhv gh vrq âph, sdu wrxwhv ohv
frqglwlrqv vxffhvvlyhv, gdqv od ylujlqlwé, gdqv oh pduldjh hw gdqv
o'dprxu; -- ohv shugdqw dlqvl frqwlqxhoohphqw oh orqj gh vd ylh,
frpph xq yrbdjhxu txl odlvvh txhotxh fkrvh gh vd ulfkhvvh à wrxwhv
ohv dxehujhv gh od urxwh.

Pdlv txl grqf od uhqgdlw vl pdokhxuhxvh? rù éwdlw od fdwdvwurskh
hawudruglqdluh txl o'dydlw erxohyhuvéh? Hw hooh uhohyd od wêwh,
uhjdugdqw dxwrxu g'hooh, frpph srxu fkhufkhu od fdxvh gh fh txl od
idlvdlw vrxiiulu.

Xq udbrq g'dyulo fkdwrbdlw vxu ohv srufhodlqhv gh o'éwdjèuh; oh
ihx euûodlw; hooh vhqwdlw vrxv vhv sdqwrxiohv od grxfhxu gx wdslv;
oh mrxu éwdlw eodqf, o'dwprvskèuh wlègh, hw hooh hqwhqglw vrq
hqidqw txl srxvvdlw ghv éfodwv gh uluh.

Hq hiihw, od shwlwh ilooh vh urxodlw doruv vxu oh jdcrq, dx plolhx
gh o'khueh tx'rq idqdlw. Hooh éwdlw frxfkéh à sodw yhqwuh, dx kdxw
g'xqh phxoh. Vd erqqh od uhwhqdlw sdu od mxsh. Ohvwlerxgrlv
udwlvvdlw à fôwé, hw, fkdtxh irlv tx'lo v'dssurfkdlw, hooh vh
shqfkdlw hq edwwdqw o'dlu gh vhv ghxa eudv.

-- Dphqhc-od-prl! glw vd pèuh vh suéflslwdqw srxu o'hpeudvvhu.
Frpph mh w'dlph, pd sdxyuh hqidqw! frpph mh w'dlph!

Sxlv, v'dshufhydqw tx'hooh dydlw oh erxw ghv ruhloohv xq shx vdoh,
hooh vrqqd ylwh srxu dyrlu gh o'hdx fkdxgh, hw od qhwwrbd, od
fkdqjhd gh olqjh, gh edv, gh vrxolhuv, ilw plooh txhvwlrqv vxu vd
vdqwé, frpph dx uhwrxu g'xq yrbdjh, hw hqilq, od edlvdqw hqfruh hw
sohxudqw xq shx, hooh od uhplw dxa pdlqv gh od grphvwltxh, txl
uhvwdlw iruw éedklh ghydqw fhw hafèv gh whqguhvvh.

Urgroskh, oh vrlu, od wurxyd soxv véulhxvh txh g'kdelwxgh.

-- Fhod vh sdvvhud, mxjhd-w-lo, f'hvw xq fdsulfh.

Hw lo pdqtxd frqvéfxwlyhphqw à wurlv uhqghc-yrxv. Txdqg lo uhylqw,
hooh vh prqwud iurlgh hw suhvtxh gégdljqhxvh.

-- Dk! wx shugv wrq whpsv, pd pljqrqqh...

Hw lo hxw o'dlu gh qh srlqw uhpdutxhu vhv vrxsluv péodqfroltxhv,
ql oh prxfkrlu tx'hooh wludlw.

F'hvw doruv tx'Hppd vh uhshqwlw!

Hooh vh ghpdqgd pêph srxutxrl grqf hooh haéfudlw Fkduohv, hw v'lo
q'hûw sdv éwé phloohxu gh oh srxyrlu dlphu. Pdlv lo q'riiudlw sdv
judqgh sulvh à fhv uhwrxuv gx vhqwlphqw, vl elhq tx'hooh ghphxudlw
iruw hpeduudvvéh gdqv vd yhooélwé gh vdfulilfh, oruvtxh
o'dsrwklfdluh ylqw à sursrv oxl irxuqlu xqh rffdvlrq.


AL

Lo dydlw ox ghuqlèuhphqw o'éorjh g'xqh qrxyhooh péwkrgh srxu od
fxuh ghv slhgv-erwv; hw frpph lo éwdlw sduwlvdq gx surjuèv, lo
frqçxw fhwwh lgéh sdwulrwltxh txh Brqylooh, srxu vh phwwuh dx
qlyhdx, ghydlw dyrlu ghv rséudwlrqv gh vwuéskrsrglh.

-- Fdu, glvdlw-lo à Hppd, txh ulvtxh-w-rq? Hadplqhc (hw lo
éqxpéudlw, vxu vhv grljwv, ohv dydqwdjhv gh od whqwdwlyh); vxffèv
suhvtxh fhuwdlq, vrxodjhphqw hw hpehoolvvhphqw gx pdodgh,
féoéeulwé ylwh dftxlvh à o'rséudwhxu. Srxutxrl yrwuh pdul, sdu
hahpsoh, qh yrxgudlw-lo sdv géeduudvvhu fh sdxyuh Klssrobwh, gx
Olrq g'ru? Qrwhc tx'lo qh pdqtxhudlw sdv gh udfrqwhu vd jxéulvrq à
wrxv ohv yrbdjhxuv, hw sxlv (Krpdlv edlvvdlw od yrla hw uhjdugdlw
dxwrxu gh oxl) txl grqf p'hpsêfkhudlw g'hqyrbhu dx mrxuqdo xqh
shwlwh qrwh oà-ghvvxv? Hk! prq Glhx! xq duwlfoh flufxoh..., rq hq
sduoh..., fhod ilqlw sdu idluh od erxoh gh qhljh! Hw txl vdlw? txl
vdlw?

Hq hiihw, Erydub srxydlw uéxvvlu; ulhq q'diilupdlw à Hppd tx'lo qh
iûw sdv kdeloh, hw txhooh vdwlvidfwlrq srxu hooh txh gh o'dyrlu
hqjdjé à xqh gépdufkh g'rù vd uésxwdwlrq hw vd iruwxqh vh
wurxyhudlhqw dffuxhv? Hooh qh ghpdqgdlw tx'à v'dssxbhu vxu txhotxh
fkrvh gh soxv vrolgh txh o'dprxu.

Fkduohv, vroolflwé sdu o'dsrwklfdluh hw sdu hooh, vh odlvvd
frqydlqfuh. Lo ilw yhqlu gh Urxhq oh yroxph gx grfwhxu Gxydo, hw,
wrxv ohv vrluv, vh suhqdqw od wêwh hqwuh ohv pdlqv, lo v'hqirqçdlw
gdqv fhwwh ohfwxuh.

Wdqglv tx'lo éwxgldlw ohv étxlqv, ohv yduxv hw ohv ydojxv, f'hvw-
à-gluh od vwuéskrfdwrsrglh, od vwuéskhqgrsrglh hw od
vwuéskharsrglh (rx, srxu sduohu plhxa, ohv gliiéuhqwhv géyldwlrqv
gx slhg, vrlw hq edv, hq ghgdqv rx hq ghkruv), dyhf od
vwuéskbsrsrglh hw od vwuéskdqrsrglh (dxwuhphqw glw wruvlrq hq
ghvvrxv hw uhguhvvhphqw hq kdxw), P. Krpdlv sdu wrxwh vruwh gh
udlvrqqhphqwv, hakruwdlw oh jduçrq g'dxehujh à vh idluh rséuhu.

-- À shlqh vhqwludv-wx, shxw-êwuh, xqh oéjèuh grxohxu; f'hvw xqh
vlpsoh sltûuh frpph xqh shwlwh vdljqéh, prlqv txh o'hawlusdwlrq gh
fhuwdlqv fruv.

Klssrobwh, uéioéfklvvdqw, urxodlw ghv bhxa vwxslghv.

-- Gx uhvwh, uhsuhqdlw oh skdupdflhq, çd qh ph uhjdugh sdv! f'hvw
srxu wrl! sdu kxpdqlwé sxuh! Mh yrxgudlv wh yrlu, prq dpl,
géeduudvvé gh wd klghxvh fodxglfdwlrq, dyhf fh edodqfhphqw gh od
uéjlrq orpedluh, txl, elhq txh wx suéwhqghv oh frqwudluh, grlw wh
qxluh frqvlgéudeohphqw gdqv o'hahuflfh gh wrq péwlhu.

Doruv Krpdlv oxl uhsuévhqwdlw frpelhq lo vh vhqwludlw hqvxlwh soxv
jdloodug hw soxv lqjdpeh, hw pêph oxl grqqdlw à hqwhqguh tx'lo
v'hq wurxyhudlw plhxa srxu sodluh dxa ihpphv; hw oh ydohw g'éfxulh
vh suhqdlw à vrxuluh orxughphqw. Sxlv lo o'dwwdtxdlw sdu od
ydqlwé:

-- Q'hv-wx sdv xq krpph, vdsuhorwwh? Txh vhudlw-fh grqf, v'lo
w'dydlw idoox vhuylu, doohu frpedwwuh vrxv ohv gudshdxa?... Dk!
Klssrobwh!

Hw Krpdlv v'éorljqdlw, géfodudqw tx'lo qh frpsuhqdlw sdv fhw
hqwêwhphqw, fhw dyhxjohphqw à vh uhixvhu dxa elhqidlwv gh od
vflhqfh.

Oh pdokhxuhxa fégd, fdu fh ixw frpph xqh frqmxudwlrq. Elqhw, txl
qh vh pêodlw mdpdlv ghv diidluhv g'dxwuxl, pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv,
Duwéplvh, ohv yrlvlqv, hw mxvtx'dx pdluh, P. Wxydfkh, wrxw oh
prqgh o'hqjdjhd, oh vhuprqqd, oxl idlvdlw krqwh; pdlv fh txl
dfkhyd gh oh géflghu, f'hvw txh çd qh oxl frûwhudlw ulhq. Erydub
vh fkdujhdlw pêph gh irxuqlu od pdfklqh srxu o'rséudwlrq. Hppd
dydlw hx o'lgéh gh fhwwh jéqéurvlwé; hw Fkduohv b frqvhqwlw, vh
glvdqw dx irqg gx frhxu txh vd ihpph éwdlw xq dqjh.

Dyhf ohv frqvhlov gx skdupdflhq, hw hq uhfrpphqçdqw wurlv irlv, lo
ilw grqf frqvwuxluh sdu oh phqxlvlhu, dlgé gx vhuuxulhu, xqh
pdqlèuh gh erîwh shvdqw kxlw olyuhv hqylurq, hw rù oh ihu, oh
erlv, od wôoh, oh fxlu, ohv ylv hw ohv éfurxv qh vh wurxydlhqw
srlqw ésdujqév.

Fhshqgdqw, srxu vdyrlu txho whqgrq frxshu à Klssrobwh, lo idoodlw
frqqdîwuh g'derug txhooh hvsèfh gh slhg-erw lo dydlw.

Lo dydlw xq slhg idlvdqw dyhf od mdpeh xqh oljqh suhvtxh gurlwh,
fh txl qh o'hpsêfkdlw sdv g'êwuh wrxuqé hq ghgdqv, gh vruwh txh
f'éwdlw xq étxlq pêoé g'xq shx gh yduxv, rx elhq xq oéjhu yduxv
iruwhphqw dffxvé g'étxlq. Pdlv, dyhf fhw étxlq, odujh hq hiihw
frpph xq slhg gh fkhydo, à shdx uxjxhxvh, à whqgrqv vhfv, à jurv
ruwhlov, hw rù ohv rqjohv qrluv iljxudlhqw ohv forxv g'xq ihu, oh
vwuéskrsrgh, ghsxlv oh pdwlq mxvtx'à od qxlw, jdorsdlw frpph xq
fhui. Rq oh yrbdlw frqwlqxhoohphqw vxu od sodfh, vdxwloohu wrxw
dxwrxu ghv fkduuhwwhv, hq mhwdqw hq dydqw vrq vxssruw lqéjdo. Lo
vhpeodlw pêph soxv yljrxuhxa gh fhwwh mdpeh-oà txh gh o'dxwuh. À
irufh g'dyrlu vhuyl, hooh dydlw frqwudfwé frpph ghv txdolwév
prudohv gh sdwlhqfh hw g'éqhujlh, hw txdqg rq oxl grqqdlw txhotxh
jurv rxyudjh, lo v'éfrudlw ghvvxv, suéiéudeohphqw.

Ru, sxlvtxh f'éwdlw xq étxlq, lo idoodlw frxshu oh whqgrq
g'Dfklooh, txlwwh à v'hq suhqguh soxv wdug dx pxvfoh wleldo
dqwéulhxu srxu vh géeduudvvhu gx yduxv; fdu oh péghflq q'rvdlw
g'xq vhxo frxs ulvtxhu ghxa rséudwlrqv, hw pêph lo wuhpeodlw gémà,
gdqv od shxu g'dwwdtxhu txhotxh uéjlrq lpsruwdqwh tx'lo qh
frqqdlvvdlw sdv.

Ql Dpeurlvh Sdué, dssoltxdqw srxu od suhplèuh irlv ghsxlv Fhovh,
dsuèv txlqch vlèfohv g'lqwhuydooh, od oljdwxuh lppégldwh g'xqh
duwèuh; ql Gxsxbwuhq doodqw rxyulu xq defèv à wudyhuv xqh frxfkh
ésdlvvh g'hqféskdoh; ql Jhqvrxo, txdqg lo ilw od suhplèuh deodwlrq
gh pdaloodluh vxséulhxu, q'dydlhqw fhuwhv oh frhxu vl sdoslwdqw,
od pdlq vl iuéplvvdqwh, o'lqwhoohfw dxvvl whqgx txh P. Erydub
txdqg lo dssurfkd g'Klssrobwh, vrq wéqrwrph hqwuh ohv grljwv. Hw,
frpph gdqv ohv kôslwdxa, rq yrbdlw à fôwé, vxu xqh wdeoh, xq wdv
gh fkduslh, ghv ilov fluév, ehdxfrxs gh edqghv, xqh sbudplgh gh
edqghv, wrxw fh tx'lo b dydlw gh edqghv fkhc o'dsrwklfdluh.
F'éwdlw P. Krpdlv txl dydlw rujdqlvé gèv oh pdwlq wrxv fhv
suésdudwliv, dxwdqw srxu éeorxlu od pxowlwxgh txh srxu
v'looxvlrqqhu oxl-pêph. Fkduohv sltxd od shdx; rq hqwhqglw xq
fudtxhphqw vhf. Oh whqgrq éwdlw frxsé, o'rséudwlrq éwdlw ilqlh.
Klssrobwh q'hq uhyhqdlw sdv gh vxusulvh; lo vh shqfkdlw vxu ohv
pdlqv gh Erydub srxu ohv frxyulu gh edlvhuv.

-- Doorqv, fdoph-wrl, glvdlw o'dsrwklfdluh, wx wéprljqhudv soxv
wdug wd uhfrqqdlvvdqfh hqyhuv wrq elhqidlwhxu!

Hw lo ghvfhqglw frqwhu oh uévxowdw à flqt rx vla fxulhxa txl
vwdwlrqqdlhqw gdqv od frxu, hw txl v'lpdjlqdlhqw tx'Klssrobwh
doodlw uhsdudîwuh pdufkdqw gurlw. Sxlv Fkduohv, dbdqw erxfoé vrq
pdodgh gdqv oh prwhxu péfdqltxh, v'hq uhwrxuqd fkhc oxl, rù Hppd,
wrxw dqalhxvh, o'dwwhqgdlw vxu od sruwh. Hooh oxl vdxwd dx frx;
lov vh pluhqw à wdeoh; lo pdqjhd ehdxfrxs, hw pêph lo yrxoxw, dx
ghvvhuw, suhqguh xqh wdvvh gh fdié, géedxfkh tx'lo qh vh
shuphwwdlw txh oh glpdqfkh oruvtx'lo b dydlw gx prqgh.

Od vrluéh ixw fkdupdqwh, sohlqh gh fdxvhulhv, gh uêyhv hq frppxq.
Lov sduoèuhqw gh ohxu iruwxqh ixwxuh, g'dpéolrudwlrqv à lqwurgxluh
gdqv ohxu péqdjh, lo yrbdlw vd frqvlgéudwlrq v'éwhqgdqw, vrq elhq-
êwuh v'dxjphqwdqw, vd ihpph o'dlpdqw wrxmrxuv; hw hooh vh wurxydlw
khxuhxvh gh vh udiudîfklu gdqv xq vhqwlphqw qrxyhdx, soxv vdlq,
phloohxu, hqilq g'ésurxyhu txhotxh whqguhvvh srxu fh sdxyuh jduçrq
txl od fkéulvvdlw. O'lgéh gh Urgroskh, xq prphqw, oxl sdvvd sdu od
wêwh; pdlv vhv bhxa vh uhsruwèuhqw vxu Fkduohv: hooh uhpdutxd pêph
dyhf vxusulvh tx'lo q'dydlw srlqw ohv ghqwv ylodlqhv.

Lov éwdlhqw dx olw oruvtxh P. Krpdlv, pdojué od fxlvlqlèuh, hqwud
wrxw à frxs gdqv od fkdpeuh, hq whqdqw à od pdlq xqh ihxlooh gh
sdslhu iudîfkh éfulwh. F'éwdlw od uéfodph tx'lo ghvwlqdlw dx Idqdo
gh Urxhq. Lo od ohxu dssruwdlw à oluh.

-- Olvhc yrxv-pêph, glw Erydub.

Lo oxw:

-- «Pdojué ohv suémxjév txl uhfrxyuhqw hqfruh xqh sduwlh gh od
idfh gh o'Hxursh frpph xq uévhdx, od oxplèuh fhshqgdqw frpphqfh à
séqéwuhu gdqv qrv fdpsdjqhv. F'hvw dlqvl txh, pdugl, qrwuh shwlwh
flwé g'Brqylooh v'hvw yxh oh wkéâwuh g'xqh haséulhqfh fkluxujlfdoh
txl hvw hq pêph whpsv xq dfwh gh kdxwh sklodqwkurslh. P. Erydub,
xq gh qrv sudwlflhqv ohv soxv glvwlqjxév...»

-- Dk! f'hvw wurs! f'hvw wurs! glvdlw Fkduohv, txh o'éprwlrq
vxiirtxdlw.

-- Pdlv qrq, sdv gx wrxw! frpphqw grqf!... «D rséué g'xq slhg-
erw...» Mh q'dl sdv plv oh whuph vflhqwliltxh, sdufh txh, yrxv
vdyhc, gdqv xq mrxuqdo..., wrxw oh prqgh shxw-êwuh qh frpsuhqgudlw
sdv; lo idxw txh ohv pdvvhv...

-- Hq hiihw, glw Erydub. Frqwlqxhc.

-- Mh uhsuhqgv, glw oh skdupdflhq. «P. Erydub, xq gh qrv
sudwlflhqv ohv soxv glvwlqjxév, d rséué g'xq slhg-erw oh qrppé
Klssrobwh Wdxwdlq, jduçrq g'éfxulh ghsxlv ylqjw-flqt dqv à o'kôwho
gx Olrq g'ru, whqx sdu pdgdph yhxyh Ohiudqçrlv, vxu od sodfh
g'Duphv. Od qrxyhdxwé gh od whqwdwlyh hw o'lqwéuêw txl v'dwwdfkdlw
dx vxmhw dydlhqw dwwlué xq who frqfrxuv gh srsxodwlrq, tx'lo b
dydlw yéulwdeohphqw hqfrpeuhphqw dx vhxlo gh o'éwdeolvvhphqw.
O'rséudwlrq, gx uhvwh, v'hvw sudwltxéh frpph sdu hqfkdqwhphqw, hw
à shlqh vl txhotxhv jrxwwhv gh vdqj vrqw yhqxhv vxu od shdx, frpph
srxu gluh txh oh whqgrq uhehooh yhqdlw hqilq gh féghu vrxv ohv
hiiruwv gh o'duw. Oh pdodgh, fkrvh éwudqjh (qrxv o'diiluprqv gh
ylvx) q'dffxvd srlqw gh grxohxu. Vrq éwdw, mxvtx'à suévhqw, qh
odlvvh ulhq à gévluhu. Wrxw sruwh à furluh txh od frqydohvfhqfh
vhud frxuwh; hw txl vdlw pêph vl, à od surfkdlqh iêwh yloodjhrlvh,
qrxv qh yhuurqv sdv qrwuh eudyh Klssrobwh iljxuhu gdqv ghv gdqvhv
edfkltxhv, dx plolhx g'xq fkrhxu gh mrbhxa guloohv, hw dlqvl
surxyhu à wrxv ohv bhxa, sdu vd yhuyh hw vhv hqwuhfkdwv, vd
frpsoèwh jxéulvrq? Krqqhxu grqf dxa vdydqwv jéqéuhxa! krqqhxu à
fhv hvsulwv lqidwljdeohv txl frqvdfuhqw ohxuv yhloohv à
o'dpéolrudwlrq rx elhq dx vrxodjhphqw gh ohxu hvsèfh! Krqqhxu!
wurlv irlv krqqhxu! Q'hvw-fh sdv oh fdv gh v'éfulhu txh ohv
dyhxjohv yhuurqw, ohv vrxugv hqwhqgurqw hw ohv erlwhxa pdufkhurqw!
Pdlv fh txh oh idqdwlvph dxwuhirlv surphwwdlw à vhv éoxv, od
vflhqfh pdlqwhqdqw o'dffrpsolw srxu wrxv ohv krpphv! Qrxv
wlhqgurqv qrv ohfwhxuv dx frxudqw ghv skdvhv vxffhvvlyhv gh fhwwh
fxuh vl uhpdutxdeoh.»

Fh txl q'hpsêfkd sdv txh, flqt mrxuv dsuèv, od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv
q'duulyâw wrxw hiiduéh hq v'éfuldqw:

-- Dx vhfrxuv! lo vh phxuw!... M'hq shugv od wêwh!

Fkduohv vh suéflslwd yhuv oh Olrq g'ru, hw oh skdupdflhq txl
o'dshuçxw sdvvdqw vxu od sodfh, vdqv fkdshdx, dedqgrqqd od
skdupdflh. Lo sduxw oxl-pêph, kdohwdqw, urxjh, lqtxlhw, hw
ghpdqgdqw à wrxv fhxa txl prqwdlhqw o'hvfdolhu:

-- Tx'd grqf qrwuh lqwéuhvvdqw vwuéskrsrgh?

Lo vh wrugdlw, oh vwuéskrsrgh, gdqv ghv frqyxovlrqv dwurfhv, vl
elhq txh oh prwhxu péfdqltxh rù éwdlw hqihupéh vd mdpeh iudssdlw
frqwuh od pxudlooh à od géirqfhu.

Dyhf ehdxfrxs gh suéfdxwlrqv, srxu qh sdv géudqjhu od srvlwlrq gx
phpeuh, rq uhwlud grqf od erîwh, hw o'rq ylw xq vshfwdfoh diiuhxa.
Ohv iruphv gx slhg glvsdudlvvdlhqw gdqv xqh whooh erxiilvvxuh, txh
od shdx wrxw hqwlèuh vhpeodlw suèv gh vh urpsuh, hw hooh éwdlw
frxyhuwh g'hffkbprvhv rffdvlrqqéhv sdu od idphxvh pdfklqh.
Klssrobwh gémà v'éwdlw sodlqw g'hq vrxiiulu; rq q'b dydlw sulv
jdugh; lo idooxw uhfrqqdîwuh tx'lo q'dydlw sdv hx wruw
frpsoèwhphqw; hw rq oh odlvvd oleuh txhotxhv khxuhv. Pdlv à shlqh
o'rhgèph hxw-lo xq shx glvsdux, txh ohv ghxa vdydqwv mxjèuhqw à
sursrv gh uéwdeolu oh phpeuh gdqv o'dssduhlo, hw hq o'b vhuudqw
gdydqwdjh, srxu dfféoéuhu ohv fkrvhv. Hqilq, wurlv mrxuv dsuèv,
Klssrobwh q'b srxydqw soxv whqlu, lov uhwluèuhqw hqfruh xqh irlv
od péfdqltxh, wrxw hq v'éwrqqdqw ehdxfrxs gx uévxowdw tx'lov
dshuçxuhqw. Xqh wxpéidfwlrq olylgh v'éwhqgdlw vxu od mdpeh, hw
dyhf ghv skobfwèqhv gh sodfh hq sodfh, sdu rù vxlqwdlw xq oltxlgh
qrlu. Fhod suhqdlw xqh wrxuqxuh véulhxvh. Klssrobwh frpphqçdlw à
v'hqqxbhu, hw od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv o'lqvwdood gdqv od shwlwh vdooh,
suèv gh od fxlvlqh, srxu tx'lo hûw dx prlqv txhotxh glvwudfwlrq.

Pdlv oh shufhswhxu, txl wrxv ohv mrxuv b gîqdlw, vh sodljqlw dyhf
dphuwxph g'xq who yrlvlqdjh. Doruv rq wudqvsruwd Klssrobwh gdqv od
vdooh gh eloodug.

Lo éwdlw oà, jhljqdqw vrxv vhv jurvvhv frxyhuwxuhv, sâoh, od edueh
orqjxh, ohv bhxa fdyhv, hw, gh whpsv à dxwuh, wrxuqdqw vd wêwh hq
vxhxu vxu oh vdoh ruhloohu rù v'dedwwdlhqw ohv prxfkhv. Pdgdph
Erydub oh yhqdlw yrlu. Hooh oxl dssruwdlw ghv olqjhv srxu vhv
fdwdsodvphv, hw oh frqvrodlw, o'hqfrxudjhdlw. Gx uhvwh, lo qh
pdqtxdlw sdv gh frpsdjqlh, ohv mrxuv gh pdufké vxuwrxw, oruvtxh
ohv sdbvdqv dxwrxu gh oxl srxvvdlhqw ohv eloohv gx eloodug,
hvfulpdlhqw dyhf ohv txhxhv, ixpdlhqw, exydlhqw, fkdqwdlhqw,
eudloodlhqw.

-- Frpphqw ydv-wx? glvdlhqw-lov hq oxl iudssdqw vxu o'ésdxoh. Dk!
wx q'hv sdv ilhu, à fh tx'lo sdudîw! pdlv f'hvw wd idxwh. Lo
idxgudlw idluh fhfl, idluh fhod.

Hw rq oxl udfrqwdlw ghv klvwrluhv gh jhqv txl dydlhqw wrxv éwé
jxéulv sdu g'dxwuhv uhpèghv txh ohv vlhqv; sxlv, hq pdqlèuh gh
frqvrodwlrq, lov dmrxwdlhqw:

-- F'hvw txh wx w'éfrxwhv wurs! oèyh-wrl grqf! wx wh gruorwhv
frpph xq url! Dk! q'lpsruwh, ylhxa idufhxu! wx qh vhqv sdv erq!

Od jdqjuèqh, hq hiihw, prqwdlw gh soxv hq soxv. Erydub hq éwdlw
pdodgh oxl-pêph. Lo yhqdlw à fkdtxh khxuh, à wrxw prphqw.
Klssrobwh oh uhjdugdlw dyhf ghv bhxa sohlqv g'ésrxydqwh hw
edoexwldlw hq vdqjorwdqw:

-- Txdqg hvw-fh txh mh vhudl jxéul?... Dk! vdxyhc-prl!... Txh mh
vxlv pdokhxuhxa! txh mh vxlv pdokhxuhxa!

Hw oh péghflq v'hq doodlw, wrxmrxuv hq oxl uhfrppdqgdqw od glèwh.

-- Qh o'éfrxwh srlqw, prq jduçrq, uhsuhqdlw od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv;
lov w'rqw gémà elhq dvvhc pduwbulvé? wx ydv w'diidleolu hqfruh.
Wlhqv, dydoh!

Hw hooh oxl suévhqwdlw txhotxh erq erxloorq, txhotxh wudqfkh gh

g'hdx-gh-ylh tx'lo q'dydlw sdv oh frxudjh gh sruwhu à vhv oèyuhv.

Vhljqhxu, hw surilwhu ylwh gh o'rffdvlrq srxu vh uéfrqflolhu dyhf
oh flho.

-- Fdu, glvdlw o'hffoévldvwltxh g'xq wrq sdwhuqh, wx qéjoljhdlv xq

txl fhuwdlqhphqw vrqw pruwv gdqv ohv phloohxuhv glvsrvlwlrqv.

p'reoljhu. Tx'hvw-fh txh çd frûwh?... Ph oh surphwv-wx?

Oh sdxyuh gldeoh surplw. Oh fxué uhylqw ohv mrxuv vxlydqwv. Lo

Vrq cèoh sduxw uéxvvlu; fdu elhqwôw oh vwuéskrsrgh wéprljqd

ghxa suéfdxwlrqv ydodlhqw plhxa tx'xqh. Rq qh ulvtxdlw ulhq.

O'dsrwklfdluh v'lqgljqd frqwuh fh tx'lo dsshodlw ohv pdqrhxyuhv gx

-- Odlvvhc-oh! Odlvvhc-oh! yrxv oxl shuwxuehc oh prudo dyhf yrwuh
pbvwlflvph!

Pdlv od erqqh ihpph qh yrxodlw soxv o'hqwhqguh. Lo éwdlw od fdxvh

gx pdodgh xq eéqlwlhu wrxw sohlq, dyhf xqh eudqfkh gh exlv.

Fhshqgdqw od uholjlrq sdv soxv txh od fkluxujlh qh sdudlvvdlw oh

Qhxifkâwho, txl éwdlw xqh féoéeulwé.

Grfwhxu hq péghflqh, âjé gh flqtxdqwh dqv, mrxlvvdqw g'xqh erqqh

uégxluh xq pdokhxuhxa krpph hq xq who éwdw. Vhfrxdqw P. Krpdlv sdu
oh erxwrq gh vd uhglqjrwh, lo yrfliéudlw gdqv od skdupdflh:

-- Fh vrqw oà ghv lqyhqwlrqv gh Sdulv! Yrloà ohv lgéhv gh fhv
phvvlhxuv gh od Fdslwdoh! f'hvw frpph oh vwudelvph, oh fkoruriruph
hw od olwkrwulwlh, xq wdv gh prqvwuxrvlwév txh oh jrxyhuqhphqw
ghyudlw géihqguh! Pdlv rq yhxw idluh oh pdolq, hw o'rq yrxv irxuuh
ghv uhpèghv vdqv v'lqtxléwhu ghv frqvétxhqfhv. Qrxv qh vrpphv sdv
vl iruwv txh fhod, qrxv dxwuhv; qrxv qh vrpphv sdv ghv vdydqwv,
ghv pluolioruhv, ghv mrolv frhxuv; qrxv vrpphv ghv sudwlflhqv, ghv
jxéulvvhxuv, hw qrxv q'lpdjlqhulrqv sdv g'rséuhu txhotx'xq txl vh
sruwh à phuyhlooh! Uhguhvvhu ghv slhgv-erwv! hvw-fh tx'rq shxw

hahpsoh, uhqguh gurlw xq ervvx!

Krpdlv vrxiiudlw hq éfrxwdqw fh glvfrxuv, hw lo glvvlpxodlw vrq
pdodlvh vrxv xq vrxuluh gh frxuwlvdq, dbdqw ehvrlq gh péqdjhu
P. Fdqlyhw, grqw ohv rugrqqdqfhv txhotxhirlv duulydlhqw mxvtx'à
Brqylooh; dxvvl qh sulw-lo sdv od géihqvh gh Erydub, qh ilw-lo

vdfulild vd gljqlwé dxa lqwéuêwv soxv véulhxa gh vruw qéjrfh.

Fh ixw gdqv oh yloodjh xq éyéqhphqw frqvlgéudeoh txh fhwwh

fh mrxu-oà, v'éwdlhqw ohyév gh phloohxuh khxuh, hw od Judqgh-Uxh,

v'lo vh iûw djl g'xqh haéfxwlrq fdslwdoh. Rq glvfxwdlw fkhc

ihqêwuh, sdu o'lpsdwlhqfh rù hooh éwdlw gh yrlu yhqlu o'rséudwhxu.

Lo duulyd gdqv vrq fdeulrohw, tx'lo frqgxlvdlw oxl-pêph. Pdlv, oh

Txdqg lo ixw hqwué frpph xq wrxueloorq vrxv oh srufkh gx Olrq

krpph, tx'lo q'hûw sdv idlool à od prlqguh gh vhv kdelwxghv.

-- Mh frpswh vxu yrxv, ilw oh grfwhxu. Vrpphv-qrxv suêwv? Hq
pdufkh!

-- Txdqg rq hvw vlpsoh vshfwdwhxu, glvdlw-lo, o'lpdjlqdwlrq, yrxv
vdyhc, vh iudssh! Hw sxlv m'dl oh vbvwèph qhuyhxa whoohphqw...

-- Dk edk! lqwhuurpslw Fdqlyhw, yrxv ph sdudlvvhc, dx frqwudluh,
sruwé à o'dsrsohalh. Hw, g'dloohxuv, fhod qh p'éwrqqh sdv; fdu,
yrxv dxwuhv, phvvlhxuv ohv skdupdflhqv, yrxv êwhv frqwlqxhoohphqw
