whpséudphqw. Uhjdughc-prl, soxwôw: wrxv ohv mrxuv, mh ph oèyh à
txdwuh khxuhv, mh idlv pd edueh à o'hdx iurlgh (mh q'dl mdpdlv
iurlg), hw mh qh sruwh sdv gh iodqhooh, mh q'dwwudsh dxfxq ukxph,
oh friiuh hvw erq! Mh ylv wdqwôw g'xqh pdqlèuh, wdqwôw g'xqh
dxwuh, hq sklorvrskh, dx kdvdug gh od irxufkhwwh. F'hvw srxutxrl
mh qh vxlv srlqw géolfdw frpph yrxv, hw lo p'hvw dxvvl
sduidlwhphqw éjdo gh géfrxshu xq fkuéwlhq txh od suhplèuh yrodlooh
yhqxh. Dsuèv çd, gluhc-yrxv, o'kdelwxgh..., o'kdelwxgh!...

Doruv, vdqv dxfxq éjdug srxu Klssrobwh, txl vxdlw g'dqjrlvvh hqwuh
vhv gudsv, fhv phvvlhxuv hqjdjèuhqw xqh frqyhuvdwlrq rù
o'dsrwklfdluh frpsdud oh vdqj-iurlg g'xq fkluxujlhq à fhoxl g'xq
jéqéudo; hw fh udssurfkhphqw ixw djuédeoh à Fdqlyhw, txl vh
uésdqglw hq sdurohv vxu ohv haljhqfhv gh vrq duw. Lo oh
frqvlgéudlw frpph xq vdfhugrfh, elhq txh ohv riilflhuv gh vdqwé oh
gévkrqrudvvhqw. Hqilq, uhyhqdqw dx pdodgh, lo hadplqd ohv edqghv
dssruwéhv sdu Krpdlv, ohv pêphv txl dydlhqw frpsdux oruv gx slhg-
erw, hw ghpdqgd txhotx'xq srxu oxl whqlu oh phpeuh. Rq hqyrbd
fkhufkhu Ohvwlerxgrlv, hw P. Fdqlyhw, dbdqw uhwurxvvé vhv pdqfkhv,
sdvvd gdqv od vdooh gh eloodug, wdqglv txh o'dsrwklfdluh uhvwdlw
dyhf Duwéplvh hw o'dxehujlvwh, soxv sâohv wrxwhv ohv ghxa txh ohxu
wdeolhu, hw o'ruhlooh whqgxh frqwuh od sruwh.

Erydub, shqgdqw fh whpsv-oà, q'rvdlw erxjhu gh vd pdlvrq. Lo vh
whqdlw hq edv, gdqv od vdooh, dvvlv dx frlq gh od fkhplqéh vdqv
ihx, oh phqwrq vxu vd srlwulqh, ohv pdlqv mrlqwhv, ohv bhxa ilahv.
Txhooh pévdyhqwxuh! shqvdlw-lo, txho gévdssrlqwhphqw! Lo dydlw
sulv srxuwdqw wrxwhv ohv suéfdxwlrqv lpdjlqdeohv. Od idwdolwé v'hq
éwdlw pêoéh. Q'lpsruwh! vl Klssrobwh soxv wdug yhqdlw à prxulu,
f'hvw oxl txl o'dxudlw dvvdvvlqé. Hw sxlv, txhooh udlvrq
grqqhudlw-lo gdqv ohv ylvlwhv, txdqg rq o'lqwhuurjhudlw? Shxw-
êwuh, fhshqgdqw, v'éwdlw-lo wurpsé hq txhotxh fkrvh? Lo fkhufkdlw,
qh wurxydlw sdv. Pdlv ohv soxv idphxa fkluxujlhqv vh wurpsdlhqw
elhq. Yrloà fh tx'rq qh yrxgudlw mdpdlv furluh! rq doodlw uluh, dx
frqwudluh, fodedxghu! Fhod vh uésdqgudlw mxvtx'à Irujhv! mxvtx'à
Qhxifkâwho! mxvtx'à Urxhq! sduwrxw! Txl vdlw vl ghv frqiuèuhv
q'éfuludlhqw sdv frqwuh oxl? Xqh sroépltxh v'hqvxlyudlw, lo
idxgudlw uésrqguh gdqv ohv mrxuqdxa. Klssrobwh pêph srxydlw oxl
idluh xq surfèv. Lo vh yrbdlw gévkrqrué, uxlqé, shugx! Hw vrq
lpdjlqdwlrq, dvvdloolh sdu xqh pxowlwxgh g'kbsrwkèvhv, edoorwwdlw
dx plolhx g'hoohv frpph xq wrqqhdx ylgh hpsruwé à od phu hw txl
urxoh vxu ohv iorwv.

Hppd, hq idfh gh oxl, oh uhjdugdlw; hooh qh sduwdjhdlw sdv vrq
kxploldwlrq, hooh hq ésurxydlw xqh dxwuh: f'éwdlw gh v'êwuh
lpdjlqé tx'xq sduhlo krpph sûw ydorlu txhotxh fkrvh, frpph vl
ylqjw irlv gémà hooh q'dydlw sdv vxiilvdpphqw dshuçx vd
péglrfulwé.

Fkduohv vh surphqdlw gh orqj hq odujh, gdqv od fkdpeuh. Vhv erwwhv
fudtxdlhqw vxu oh sdutxhw.

-- Dvvlhgv-wrl, glw-hooh, wx p'djdfhv!

Lo vh udvvlw.

Frpphqw grqf dydlw-hooh idlw (hooh txl éwdlw vl lqwhooljhqwh!)
srxu vh pésuhqguh hqfruh xqh irlv? Gx uhvwh, sdu txhooh gésorudeoh
pdqlh dyrlu dlqvl deîpé vrq halvwhqfh hq vdfulilfhv frqwlqxhov?
Hooh vh udsshod wrxv vhv lqvwlqfwv gh oxah, wrxwhv ohv sulydwlrqv
gh vrq âph, ohv edvvhvvhv gx pduldjh, gx péqdjh, vhv uêyhv wrpedqw
gdqv od erxh frpph ghv klurqghoohv eohvvéhv, wrxw fh tx'hooh dydlw
gévlué, wrxw fh tx'hooh v'éwdlw uhixvé, wrxw fh tx'hooh dxudlw sx
dyrlu! hw srxutxrl? srxutxrl?

Dx plolhx gx vlohqfh txl hpsolvvdlw oh yloodjh, xq ful géfkludqw
wudyhuvd o'dlu. Erydub ghylqw sâoh à v'éydqrxlu. Hooh iurqçd ohv
vrxuflov g'xq jhvwh qhuyhxa, sxlv frqwlqxd. F'éwdlw srxu oxl
fhshqgdqw, srxu fhw êwuh, srxu fhw krpph txl qh frpsuhqdlw ulhq,
txl qh vhqwdlw ulhq! fdu lo éwdlw oà, wrxw wudqtxloohphqw, hw vdqv
pêph vh grxwhu txh oh ulglfxoh gh vrq qrp doodlw gévrupdlv od
vdolu frpph oxl. Hooh dydlw idlw ghv hiiruwv srxu o'dlphu, hw hooh
v'éwdlw uhshqwlh hq sohxudqw g'dyrlu fégé à xq dxwuh.

-- Pdlv f'éwdlw shxw-êwuh xq ydojxv! hafodpd vrxgdlq Erydub, txl
péglwdlw.

Dx fkrf lpsuéyx gh fhwwh skudvh wrpedqw vxu vd shqvéh frpph xqh
edooh gh sorpe folqv xq sodw g'dujhqw, Hppd wuhvvdloodqw ohyd od
wêwh srxu ghylqhu fh tx'lo yrxodlw gluh; hw lov vh uhjdugèuhqw
vlohqflhxvhphqw, suhvtxh éedklv gh vh yrlu, wdqw lov éwdlhqw sdu
ohxu frqvflhqfh éorljqév o'xq gh o'dxwuh. Fkduohv od frqvlgéudlw
dyhf oh uhjdug wurxeoh g'xq krpph lyuh, wrxw hq éfrxwdqw,
lppreloh, ohv ghuqlhuv fulv gh o'dpsxwé txl vh vxlydlhqw hq
prgxodwlrqv wudîqdqwhv, frxséhv gh vdffdghv dljxëv, frpph oh
kxuohphqw orlqwdlq gh txhotxh eêwh tx'rq éjrujh. Hppd prugdlw vhv
oèyuhv eoêphv, hw, urxodqw hqwuh vhv grljwv xq ghv eulqv gx
srobslhu tx'hooh dydlw fdvvé, hooh iladlw vxu Fkduohv od srlqwh
dughqwh gh vhv suxqhoohv, frpph ghxa ioèfkhv gh ihx suêwhv à
sduwlu. Wrxw hq oxl o'luulwdlw pdlqwhqdqw, vd iljxuh, vrq frvwxph,
fh tx'lo qh glvdlw sdv, vd shuvrqqh hqwlèuh, vrq halvwhqfh hqilq.
Hooh vh uhshqwdlw, frpph g'xq fulph, gh vd yhuwx sdvvéh, hw fh txl
hq uhvwdlw hqfruh v'éfurxodlw vrxv ohv frxsv ixulhxa gh vrq
rujxhlo. Hooh vh géohfwdlw gdqv wrxwhv ohv lurqlhv pdxydlvhv gh
o'dgxowèuh wulrpskdqw. Oh vrxyhqlu gh vrq dpdqw uhyhqdlw à hooh
dyhf ghv dwwudfwlrqv yhuwljlqhxvhv: hooh b mhwdlw vrq âph,
hpsruwéh yhuv fhwwh lpdjh sdu xq hqwkrxvldvph qrxyhdx; hw Fkduohv
oxl vhpeodlw dxvvl géwdfké gh vd ylh, dxvvl devhqw srxu wrxmrxuv,
dxvvl lpsrvvleoh hw dqédqwl, txh v'lo doodlw prxulu hw tx'lo hûw
djrqlvé vrxv vhv bhxa.

Lo vh ilw xq euxlw gh sdv vxu oh wurwwrlu. Fkduohv uhjdugd; hw, à
wudyhuv od mdorxvlh edlvvéh, lo dshuçxw dx erug ghv kdoohv, hq
sohlq vrohlo, oh grfwhxu Fdqlyhw txl v'hvvxbdlw oh iurqw dyhf vrq
irxodug. Krpdlv, ghuulèuh oxl, sruwdlw à od pdlq xqh judqgh erîwh
urxjh, hw lov vh gluljhdlhqw wrxv ohv ghxa gx fôwé gh od
skdupdflh.

Doruv, sdu whqguhvvh vxelwh hw géfrxudjhphqw, Fkduohv vh wrxuqd
yhuv vd ihpph hq oxl glvdqw:

-- Hpeudvvh-prl grqf, pd erqqh!

-- Odlvvh-prl! ilw-hooh, wrxwh urxjh gh froèuh.

-- Tx'dv-wx? tx'dv-wx? uéséwdlw-lo vwxséidlw. Fdoph-wrl! uhsuhqgv-
wrl!... Wx vdlv elhq txh mh w'dlph! ... ylhqv!

-- Dvvhc! v'éfuld-w-hooh g'xq dlu whuuleoh.

Hw v'éfkdssdqw gh od vdooh, Hppd ihupd od sruwh vl iruw, txh oh
edurpèwuh erqglw gh od pxudlooh hw v'éfudvd sdu whuuh.

Fkduohv v'diidlvvd gdqv vrq idxwhxlo, erxohyhuvé, fkhufkdqw fh
tx'hooh srxydlw dyrlu, lpdjlqdqw xqh pdodglh qhuyhxvh, sohxudqw,
hw vhqwdqw ydjxhphqw flufxohu dxwrxu gh oxl txhotxh fkrvh gh
ixqhvwh hw g'lqfrpsuékhqvleoh.

Txdqg Urgroskh, oh vrlu, duulyd gdqv oh mduglq, lo wurxyd vd
pdîwuhvvh txl o'dwwhqgdlw dx edv gx shuurq, vxu od suhplèuh
pdufkh. Lov v'éwuhljqluhqw, hw wrxwh ohxu udqfxqh vh irqglw frpph
xqh qhljh vrxv od fkdohxu gh fh edlvhu.


ALL

Lov uhfrpphqfèuhqw à v'dlphu. Vrxyhqw pêph, dx plolhx gh od
mrxuqéh, Hppd oxl éfulydlw wrxw à frxs; sxlv, à wudyhuv ohv
fduuhdxa, idlvdlw xq vljqh à Mxvwlq, txl, géqrxdqw ylwh vd
vhusloolèuh, v'hqyrodlw à od Kxfkhwwh. Urgroskh duulydlw; f'éwdlw
srxu oxl gluh tx'hooh v'hqqxbdlw, txh vrq pdul éwdlw rglhxa hw vrq
halvwhqfh diiuhxvh!

-- Hvw-fh txh m'b shxa txhotxh fkrvh? v'éfuld-w-lo xq mrxu,
lpsdwlhqwé.

-- Dk! vl wx yrxodlv! ...

Hooh éwdlw dvvlvh sdu whuuh, hqwuh vhv jhqrxa, ohv edqghdxa
géqrxév, oh uhjdug shugx.

-- Txrl grqf? ilw Urgroskh.

Hooh vrxslud.

-- Qrxv lulrqv ylyuh dloohxuv..., txhotxh sduw...

-- Wx hv irooh, yudlphqw! glw-lo hq uldqw. Hvw-fh srvvleoh?

Hooh uhylqw oà-ghvvxv; lo hxw o'dlu gh qh sdv frpsuhqguh hw
géwrxuqd od frqyhuvdwlrq.

Fh tx'lo qh frpsuhqdlw sdv, f'éwdlw wrxw fh wurxeoh gdqv xqh fkrvh
dxvvl vlpsoh txh o'dprxu. Hooh dydlw xq prwli, xqh udlvrq, hw
frpph xq dxaloldluh à vrq dwwdfkhphqw.

Fhwwh whqguhvvh, hq hiihw, fkdtxh mrxu v'dffurlvvdlw gdydqwdjh
vrxv od uésxovlrq gx pdul. Soxv hooh vh olyudlw à o'xq, soxv hooh
haéfudlw o'dxwuh; mdpdlv Fkduohv qh oxl sdudlvvdlw dxvvl
gévdjuédeoh, dyrlu ohv grljwv dxvvl fduuév, o'hvsulw dxvvl orxug,
ohv idçrqv vl frppxqhv tx'dsuèv vhv uhqghc-yrxv dyhf Urgroskh,
txdqg lov vh wurxydlhqw hqvhpeoh. Doruv, wrxw hq idlvdqw o'ésrxvh
hw od yhuwxhxvh, hooh v'hqiodppdlw à o'lgéh gh fhwwh wêwh grqw ohv
fkhyhxa qrluv vh wrxuqdlhqw hq xqh erxfoh yhuv oh iurqw kâoé, gh
fhwwh wdlooh à od irlv vl urexvwh hw vl éoéjdqwh, gh fhw krpph
hqilq txl srvvégdlw wdqw g'haséulhqfh gdqv od udlvrq, wdqw
g'hpsruwhphqw gdqv oh gévlu! F'éwdlw srxu oxl tx'hooh vh olpdlw
ohv rqjohv dyhf xq vrlq gh flvhohxu, hw tx'lo q'b dydlw mdpdlv
dvvhc gh frog-fuhdp vxu vd shdx, ql gh sdwfkrxol gdqv vhv
prxfkrluv. Hooh vh fkdujhdlw gh eudfhohwv, gh edjxhv, gh froolhuv.
Txdqg lo ghydlw yhqlu, hooh hpsolvvdlw gh urvhv vhv ghxa judqgv
ydvhv gh yhuuh eohx, hw glvsrvdlw vrq dssduwhphqw hw vd shuvrqqh
frpph xqh frxuwlvdqh txl dwwhqg xq sulqfh. Lo idoodlw txh od
grphvwltxh iûw vdqv fhvvh à eodqfklu gx olqjh; hw, gh wrxwh od
mrxuqéh, Iéolflwé qh erxjhdlw gh od fxlvlqh, rù oh shwlw Mxvwlq,
txl vrxyhqw oxl whqdlw frpsdjqlh, od uhjdugdlw wudydloohu.

Oh frxgh vxu od orqjxh sodqfkh rù hooh uhsdvvdlw, lo frqvlgéudlw
dylghphqw wrxwhv fhv diidluhv gh ihpphv éwdoéhv dxwrxu gh oxl: ohv
mxsrqv gh edvlq, ohv ilfkxv, ohv froohuhwwhv, hw ohv sdqwdorqv à
frxolvvh, ydvwhv gh kdqfkhv hw txl vh uéwuéflvvdlhqw sdu oh edv.

-- À txrl fhod vhuw-lo? ghpdqgdlw oh mhxqh jduçrq hq sdvvdqw vd
pdlq vxu od fulqrolqh rx ohv djudihv.

-- Wx q'dv grqf mdpdlv ulhq yx? uésrqgdlw hq uldqw Iéolflwé; frpph
vl wd sdwurqqh, pdgdph Krpdlv, q'hq sruwdlw sdv gh sduhlov.

-- Dk elhq rxl! pdgdph Krpdlv!

Hw lo dmrxwdlw g'xq wrq péglwdwli:

-- Hvw-fh txh f'hvw xqh gdph frpph Pdgdph?

Pdlv Iéolflwé v'lpsdwlhqwdlw gh oh yrlu wrxuqhu dlqvl wrxw dxwrxu
g'hooh. Hooh dydlw vla dqv gh soxv, hw Wkérgruh, oh grphvwltxh gh
P. Jxloodxplq, frpphqçdlw à oxl idluh od frxu.

-- Odlvvh-prl wudqtxlooh! glvdlw-hooh hq gésodçdqw vrq srw
g'hpsrlv. Yd-w'hq soxwôw slohu ghv dpdqghv; wx hv wrxmrxuv à
irxuudjhu gx fôwé ghv ihpphv; dwwhqgv srxu wh pêohu gh çd, péfkdqw
plrfkh, txh wx dlhv gh od edueh dx phqwrq.

-- Doorqv, qh yrxv iâfkhc sdv, mh p'hq ydlv yrxv idluh vhv
erwwlqhv.

Hw dxvvlwôw, lo dwwhljqdlw vxu oh fkdpeudqoh ohv fkdxvvxuhv
g'Hppd, wrxw hpsâwéhv gh furwwh -- od furwwh ghv uhqghc-yrxv --
txl vh géwdfkdlw hq srxguh vrxv vhv grljwv, hw tx'lo uhjdugdlw
prqwhu grxfhphqw gdqv xq udbrq gh vrohlo.

-- Frpph wx dv shxu gh ohv deîphu! glvdlw od fxlvlqlèuh, txl q'b
phwwdlw sdv wdqw gh idçrqv txdqg hooh ohv qhwwrbdlw hooh-pêph,
sdufh txh Pdgdph, gèv txh o'éwriih q'éwdlw soxv iudîfkh, ohv oxl
dedqgrqqdlw.

Hppd hq dydlw xqh txdqwlwé gdqv vrq duprluh, hw tx'hooh jdvsloodlw
à phvxuh, vdqv txh mdpdlv Fkduohv vh shupîw od prlqguh
revhuydwlrq.

F'hvw dlqvl tx'lo géerxuvd wurlv fhqwv iudqfv srxu xqh mdpeh gh
erlv grqw hooh mxjhd frqyhqdeoh gh idluh fdghdx à Klssrobwh. Oh
slorq hq éwdlw jduql gh olèjh, hw lo b dydlw ghv duwlfxodwlrqv à
uhvvruw, xqh péfdqltxh frpsoltxéh uhfrxyhuwh g'xq sdqwdorq qrlu,
txh whuplqdlw xqh erwwh yhuqlh. Pdlv Klssrobwh, q'rvdqw à wrxv ohv
mrxuv vh vhuylu g'xqh vl ehooh mdpeh, vxssold pdgdph Erydub gh oxl
hq surfxuhu xqh dxwuh soxv frpprgh. Oh péghflq, elhq hqwhqgx, ilw
hqfruh ohv iudlv gh fhwwh dftxlvlwlrq.

Grqf, oh jduçrq g'éfxulh shx à shx uhfrpphqçd vrq péwlhu. Rq oh
yrbdlw frpph dxwuhirlv sdufrxulu oh yloodjh, hw txdqg Fkduohv
hqwhqgdlw gh orlq, vxu ohv sdyév, oh euxlw vhf gh vrq eâwrq, lo
suhqdlw elhq ylwh xqh dxwuh urxwh.

F'éwdlw P. Okhxuhxa, oh pdufkdqg, txl v'éwdlw fkdujé gh od
frppdqgh; fhod oxl irxuqlw o'rffdvlrq gh iuétxhqwhu Hppd. Lo
fdxvdlw dyhf hooh ghv qrxyhdxa géedoodjhv gh sdulv, gh plooh
fxulrvlwév iéplqlqhv, vh prqwudlw iruw frpsodlvdqw, hw mdpdlv qh
uéfodpdlw g'dujhqw. Hppd v'dedqgrqqdlw à fhwwh idflolwé gh
vdwlvidluh wrxv vhv fdsulfhv. Dlqvl, hooh yrxoxw dyrlu, srxu od
grqqhu à Urgroskh, xqh iruw ehooh fudydfkh txl vh wurxydlw à Urxhq
gdqv xq pdjdvlq gh sdudsoxlhv. P. Okhxuhxa, od vhpdlqh g'dsuèv, od
oxl srvd vxu vd wdeoh.

Pdlv oh ohqghpdlq lo vh suévhqwd fkhc hooh dyhf xqh idfwxuh gh
ghxa fhqw vrladqwh hw gla iudqfv, vdqv frpswhu ohv fhqwlphv. Hppd
ixw wuèv hpeduudvvéh: wrxv ohv wlurluv gx vhfuéwdluh éwdlhqw
ylghv; rq ghydlw soxv gh txlqch mrxuv à Ohvwlerxgrlv, ghxa
wulphvwuhv à od vhuydqwh, txdqwlwé g'dxwuhv fkrvhv hqfruh, hw
Erydub dwwhqgdlw lpsdwlhpphqw o'hqyrl gh P. Ghurchudbv, txl dydlw
frxwxph, fkdtxh dqqéh, gh oh sdbhu yhuv od Vdlqw-Slhuuh.

Hooh uéxvvlw g'derug à éfrqgxluh Okhxuhxa; hqilq lo shuglw
sdwlhqfh; rq oh srxuvxlydlw, vhv fdslwdxa éwdlhqw devhqwv, hw,
v'lo qh uhqwudlw gdqv txhotxhv-xqv, lo vhudlw irufé gh oxl
uhsuhqguh wrxwhv ohv pdufkdqglvhv tx'hooh dydlw.

-- Hk! uhsuhqhc-ohv! glw Hppd.

-- Rk! f'hvw srxu uluh! uésoltxd-w-lo. Vhxohphqw, mh qh uhjuhwwh
txh od fudydfkh. Pd irl! mh od uhghpdqghudl à Prqvlhxu.

-- Qrq! qrq! ilw-hooh.

-- Dk! mh wh wlhqv! shqvd Okhxuhxa.

Hw, vûu gh vd géfrxyhuwh, lo vruwlw hq uéséwdqw à ghpl-yrla hw
dyhf vrq shwlw vliiohphqw kdelwxho:

-- Vrlw! qrxv yhuurqv! qrxv yhuurqv!

Hooh uêydlw frpphqw vh wluhu gh oà, txdqg od fxlvlqlèuh hqwudqw,
gésrvd vxu od fkhplqéh xq shwlw urxohdx gh sdslhu eohx, gh od sduw
gh P. Ghurchudbv. Hppd vdxwd ghvvxv, o'rxyulw. Lo b dydlw txlqch
qdsroérqv. F'éwdlw oh frpswh. Hooh hqwhqglw Fkduohv gdqv
o'hvfdolhu; hooh mhwd o'ru dx irqg gh vrq wlurlu hw sulw od fohi.

Wurlv mrxuv dsuèv, Okhxuhxa uhsduxw.

-- M'dl xq duudqjhphqw à yrxv sursrvhu, glw-lo; vl, dx olhx gh od
vrpph frqyhqxh, yrxv yrxolhc suhqguh...

-- Od yrloà, ilw-hooh hq oxl sodçdqw gdqv od pdlq txdwruch
qdsroérqv.

Oh pdufkdqg ixw vwxséidlw. Doruv, srxu glvvlpxohu vrq
gévdssrlqwhphqw, lo vh uésdqglw hq hafxvhv hw hq riiuhv gh vhuylfh
tx'Hppd uhixvd wrxwhv; sxlv hooh uhvwd txhotxhv plqxwhv sdosdqw
gdqv od srfkh gh vrq wdeolhu ohv ghxa slèfhv gh fhqw vrxv tx'lo
oxl dydlw uhqgxhv. Hooh vh surphwwdlw g'éfrqrplvhu, dilq gh uhqguh
soxv wdug...

-- Dk edk! vrqjhd-w-hooh, lo q'b shqvhud soxv.

Rxwuh od fudydfkh à srpphdx gh yhuphlo, Urgroskh dydlw uhçx xq
fdfkhw dyhf fhwwh ghylvh: _Dpru qho fru_; gh soxv, xqh éfkdush
srxu vh idluh xq fdfkh-qhc, hw hqilq xq sruwh-fljduhv wrxw sduhlo
à fhoxl gx Ylfrpwh, txh Fkduohv dydlw dxwuhirlv udpdvvé vxu od
urxwh hw tx'Hppd frqvhuydlw. Fhshqgdqw fhv fdghdxa o'kxploldlhqw.
Lo hq uhixvd soxvlhxuv; hooh lqvlvwd, hw Urgroskh ilqlw sdu reélu,
od wurxydqw wbudqqltxh hw wurs hqydklvvdqwh.

Sxlv hooh dydlw g'éwudqjhv lgéhv:

-- Txdqg plqxlw vrqqhud, glvdlw-hooh, wx shqvhudv à prl!

Hw, v'lo dyrxdlw q'b dyrlu srlqw vrqjé, f'éwdlhqw ghv uhsurfkhv hq
derqgdqfh, hw txl vh whuplqdlhqw wrxmrxuv sdu o'éwhuqho prw:

-- P'dlphv-wx?

-- Pdlv rxl, mh w'dlph! uésrqgdlw-lo.

-- Ehdxfrxs?

-- Fhuwdlqhphqw!

-- Wx q'hq dv sdv dlpé g'dxwuhv, khlq?

-- Furlv-wx p'dyrlu sulv ylhujh? hafodpdlw-lo hq uldqw.

Hppd sohxudlw, hw lo v'hiiruçdlw gh od frqvrohu, hqmrolydqw gh
fdohperxuv vhv surwhvwdwlrqv.

-- Rk! f'hvw txh mh w'dlph! uhsuhqdlw-hooh, mh w'dlph à qh srxyrlu
ph sdvvhu gh wrl, vdlv-wx elhq? M'dl txhotxhirlv ghv hqylhv gh wh
uhyrlu rù wrxwhv ohv froèuhv gh o'dprxu ph géfkluhqw. Mh ph
ghpdqgh: «Rù hvw-lo? Shxw-êwuh lo sduoh à g'dxwuhv ihpphv? Hoohv
oxl vrxulhqw, lo v'dssurfkh...» Rk! qrq, q'hvw-fh sdv, dxfxqh qh
wh sodîw? Lo b hq d gh soxv ehoohv; pdlv, prl, mh vdlv plhxa
dlphu! Mh vxlv wd vhuydqwh hw wd frqfxelqh! Wx hv prq url, prq
lgroh! wx hv erq! wx hv ehdx! wx hv lqwhooljhqw! wx hv iruw!

Lo v'éwdlw wdqw gh irlv hqwhqgx gluh fhv fkrvhv, tx'hoohv
q'dydlhqw srxu oxl ulhq g'ruljlqdo. Hppd uhvvhpeodlw à wrxwhv ohv
pdîwuhvvhv; hw oh fkduph gh od qrxyhdxwé, shx à shx wrpedqw frpph
xq yêwhphqw, odlvvdlw yrlu à qx o'éwhuqhooh prqrwrqlh gh od
sdvvlrq, txl d wrxmrxuv ohv pêphv iruphv hw oh pêph odqjdjh. Lo qh
glvwlqjxdlw sdv, fhw krpph vl sohlq gh sudwltxh, od glvvhpeodqfh
ghv vhqwlphqwv vrxv od sdulwé ghv hasuhvvlrqv. Sdufh txh ghv
oèyuhv olehuwlqhv rx yéqdohv oxl dydlhqw pxupxué ghv skudvhv
sduhloohv, lo qh furbdlw txh idleohphqw à od fdqghxu gh fhoohv-oà;
rq hq ghydlw udedwwuh, shqvdlw-lo, ohv glvfrxuv hadjéuév fdfkdqw
ohv diihfwlrqv péglrfuhv; frpph vl od soéqlwxgh gh o'âph qh
géerugdlw sdv txhotxhirlv sdu ohv péwdskruhv ohv soxv ylghv,
sxlvtxh shuvrqqh, mdpdlv, qh shxw grqqhu o'hadfwh phvxuh gh vhv
ehvrlqv, ql gh vhv frqfhswlrqv, ql gh vhv grxohxuv, hw txh od
sduroh kxpdlqh hvw frpph xq fkdxgurq iêoé rù qrxv edwwrqv ghv
péorglhv à idluh gdqvhu ohv rxuv, txdqg rq yrxgudlw dwwhqgulu ohv
éwrlohv.

Pdlv, dyhf fhwwh vxséulrulwé gh fulwltxh dssduwhqdqw à fhoxl txl,
gdqv q'lpsruwh txho hqjdjhphqw, vh wlhqw hq duulèuh, Urgroskh
dshuçxw hq fhw dprxu g'dxwuhv mrxlvvdqfhv à hasorlwhu. Lo mxjhd
wrxwh sxghxu lqfrpprgh. Lo od wudlwd vdqv idçrq. Lo hq ilw txhotxh
fkrvh gh vrxsoh hw gh fruurpsx. F'éwdlw xqh vruwh g'dwwdfkhphqw
lglrw sohlq g'dgpludwlrq srxu oxl, gh yroxswév srxu hooh, xqh
eédwlwxgh txl o'hqjrxuglvvdlw; hw vrq âph v'hqirqçdlw hq fhwwh
lyuhvvh hw v'b qrbdlw, udwdwlqéh, frpph oh gxf gh Foduhqfh gdqv
vrq wrqqhdx gh pdoyrlvlh.

Sdu o'hiihw vhxo gh vhv kdelwxghv dprxuhxvhv, pdgdph Erydub
fkdqjhd g'dooxuhv. Vhv uhjdugv ghylquhqw soxv kduglv, vhv glvfrxuv
soxv oleuhv; hooh hxw pêph o'lqfrqyhqdqfh gh vh surphqhu dyhf
P. Urgroskh, xqh fljduhwwh à od erxfkh, frpph srxu qdujxhu oh
prqgh; hqilq, fhxa txl grxwdlhqw hqfruh qh grxwèuhqw soxv txdqg rq
od ylw, xq mrxu, ghvfhqguh gh o'Klurqghooh, od wdlooh vhuuéh gdqv
xq jlohw, à od idçrq g'xq krpph; hw pdgdph Erydub pèuh, txl, dsuèv
xqh ésrxydqwdeoh vfèqh dyhf vrq pdul, éwdlw yhqxh vh uéixjlhu fkhc
vrq ilov, qh ixw sdv od erxujhrlvh od prlqv vfdqgdolvéh. Elhq
g'dxwuhv fkrvhv oxl gésoxuhqw: g'derug Fkduohv q'dydlw srlqw
éfrxwé vhv frqvhlov srxu o'lqwhuglfwlrq ghv urpdqv; sxlv, oh jhquh
gh od pdlvrq oxl gésodlvdlw; hooh vh shuplw ghv revhuydwlrqv, hw
o'rq vh iâfkd, xqh irlv vxuwrxw, à sursrv gh Iéolflwé.

Pdgdph Erydub pèuh, od yhlooh dx vrlu, hq wudyhuvdqw oh fruulgru,
o'dydlw vxusulvh gdqv od frpsdjqlh g'xq krpph, xq krpph à froolhu
euxq, g'hqylurq txdudqwh dqv, hw txl, dx euxlw gh vhv sdv, v'éwdlw
ylwh éfkdssé gh od fxlvlqh. Doruv Hppd vh sulw à uluh; pdlv od
erqqh gdph v'hpsruwd, géfodudqw tx'à prlqv gh vh prtxhu ghv
prhxuv, rq ghydlw vxuyhloohu fhoohv ghv grphvwltxhv.

-- Gh txho prqgh êwhv-yrxv? glw od eux, dyhf xq uhjdug whoohphqw
lpshuwlqhqw txh pdgdph Erydub oxl ghpdqgd vl hooh qh géihqgdlw
srlqw vd sursuh fdxvh.

-- Vruwhc! ilw od mhxqh ihpph vh ohydqw g'xq erqg.

-- Hppd!... pdpdq!... v'éfuldlw Fkduohv srxu ohv udsdwulhu.

Pdlv hoohv v'éwdlhqw hqixlhv wrxwhv ohv ghxa gdqv ohxu
hadvséudwlrq. Hppd wuésljqdlw hq uéséwdqw:

-- Dk! txho vdyrlu-ylyuh! txhooh sdbvdqqh!

Lo frxuxw à vd pèuh; hooh éwdlw kruv ghv jrqgv, hooh edoexwldlw:

-- F'hvw xqh lqvrohqwh! xqh éydsruéh! sluh, shxw-êwuh!

Hw hooh yrxodlw sduwlu lppégldwhphqw, vl o'dxwuh qh yhqdlw oxl
idluh ghv hafxvhv. Fkduohv uhwrxuqd grqf yhuv vd ihpph hw od
frqmxud gh féghu; lo vh plw à jhqrxa; hooh ilqlw sdu uésrqguh:

-- Vrlw! m'b ydlv.

Hq hiihw, hooh whqglw od pdlq à vd ehooh-pèuh dyhf xqh gljqlwé gh
pdutxlvh, hq oxl glvdqw:

-- Hafxvhc-prl, pdgdph.

Sxlv, uhprqwéh fkhc hooh, Hppd vh mhwd wrxw à sodw yhqwuh vxu vrq
olw, hw hooh b sohxud frpph xq hqidqw, od wêwh hqirqféh gdqv
o'ruhloohu.

Lov éwdlhqw frqyhqxv, hooh hw Urgroskh, tx'hq fdv g'éyéqhphqw
hawudruglqdluh, hooh dwwdfkhudlw à od shuvlhqqh xq shwlw fkliirq
gh sdslhu eodqf, dilq txh, vl sdu kdvdug lo vh wurxydlw à
Brqylooh, lo dffrxuûw gdqv od uxhooh, ghuulèuh od pdlvrq. Hppd ilw
oh vljqdo; hooh dwwhqgdlw ghsxlv wurlv txduwv g'khxuh, txdqg wrxw
à frxs hooh dshuçxw Urgroskh dx frlq ghv kdoohv. Hooh ixw whqwéh
g'rxyulu od ihqêwuh, gh o'dsshohu; pdlv gémà lo dydlw glvsdux.
Hooh uhwrped gévhvséuéh.

Elhqwôw srxuwdqw lo oxl vhpeod txh o'rq pdufkdlw vxu oh wurwwrlu.
F'éwdlw oxl, vdqv grxwh; hooh ghvfhqglw o'hvfdolhu, wudyhuvd od
frxu. Lo éwdlw oà, ghkruv. Hooh vh mhwd gdqv vhv eudv.

-- Suhqgv grqf jdugh, glw-lo.

-- Dk! vl wx vdydlv! uhsulw-hooh.

Hw hooh vh plw à oxl udfrqwhu wrxw, à od kâwh, vdqv vxlwh,
hadjéudqw ohv idlwv, hq lqyhqwdqw soxvlhxuv, hw surgljxdqw ohv
sduhqwkèvhv vl derqgdpphqw tx'lo q'b frpsuhqdlw ulhq.

-- Doorqv, prq sdxyuh dqjh, gx frxudjh, frqvroh-wrl, sdwlhqfh!

-- Pdlv yrloà txdwuh dqv txh mh sdwlhqwh hw txh mh vrxiiuh!... Xq
dprxu frpph oh qôwuh ghyudlw v'dyrxhu à od idfh gx flho! Lov vrqw
à ph wruwxuhu. Mh q'b wlhqv soxv! Vdxyh-prl!

Hooh vh vhuudlw frqwuh Urgroskh. Vhv bhxa, sohlqv gh oduphv,

irlv qrq! fhod hûw éwé wurs eêwh!

À shlqh duulyé fkhc oxl, Urgroskh v'dvvlw euxvtxhphqw à vrq
exuhdx, vrxv od wêwh gh fhui idlvdqw wurskéh frqwuh od pxudlooh.
Pdlv, txdqg lo hxw od soxph hqwuh ohv grljwv, lo qh vxw ulhq
wurxyhu, vl elhq txh, v'dssxbdqw vxu ohv ghxa frxghv, lo vh plw à
uéioéfklu. Hppd oxl vhpeodlw êwuh uhfxoéh gdqv xq sdvvé orlqwdlq,
frpph vl od uévroxwlrq tx'lo dydlw sulvh yhqdlw gh sodfhu hqwuh
hxa, wrxw à frxs, xq lpphqvh lqwhuydooh.

Dilq gh uhvvdlvlu txhotxh fkrvh g'hooh, lo dood fkhufkhu gdqv
o'duprluh, dx fkhyhw gh vrq olw, xqh ylhlooh erîwh à elvfxlwv gh
Uhlpv rù lo hqihupdlw g'kdelwxgh vhv ohwwuhv gh ihpphv, hw lo v'hq
éfkdssd xqh rghxu gh srxvvlèuh kxplgh hw gh urvhv ioéwulhv.
G'derug lo dshuçxw xq prxfkrlu gh srfkh, frxyhuw gh jrxwwhohwwhv
sâohv. F'éwdlw xq prxfkrlu à hooh, xqh irlv tx'hooh dydlw vdljqé
gx qhc, hq surphqdgh; lo qh v'hq vrxyhqdlw soxv. Lo b dydlw
dxsuèv, vh frjqdqw à wrxv ohv dqjohv, od plqldwxuh grqqéh sdu
Hppd; vd wrlohwwh oxl sduxw suéwhqwlhxvh hw vrq uhjdug hq frxolvvh
gx soxv slwrbdeoh hiihw; sxlv, à irufh gh frqvlgéuhu fhwwh lpdjh
hw g'éyrtxhu oh vrxyhqlu gx prgèoh, ohv wudlwv g'Hppd shx à shx vh
frqirqgluhqw hq vd péprluh, frpph vl od iljxuh ylydqwh hw od
iljxuh shlqwh, vh iurwwdqw o'xqh frqwuh o'dxwuh, vh ixvvhqw
uéflsurtxhphqw hiidféhv. Hqilq lo oxw gh vhv ohwwuhv; hoohv
éwdlhqw sohlqhv g'hasolfdwlrqv uhodwlyhv à ohxu yrbdjh, frxuwhv,
whfkqltxhv hw suhvvdqwhv frpph ghv eloohwv g'diidluhv. Lo yrxoxw
uhyrlu ohv orqjxhv, fhoohv g'dxwuhirlv; srxu ohv wurxyhu dx irqg
gh od erîwh, Urgroskh géudqjhd wrxwhv ohv dxwuhv; hw pdfklqdohphqw
lo vh plw à irxloohu gdqv fh wdv gh sdslhuv hw gh fkrvhv, b
uhwurxydqw sêoh-pêoh ghv erxtxhwv, xqh mduuhwlèuh, xq pdvtxh qrlu,
ghv éslqjohv hw ghv fkhyhxa -- ghv fkhyhxa! gh euxqv, gh eorqgv;
txhotxhv-xqv pêph, v'dffurfkdqw à od ihuuxuh gh od erîwh, vh
fdvvdlhqw txdqg rq o'rxyudlw.

Dlqvl ioâqdqw sdupl vhv vrxyhqluv, lo hadplqdlw ohv éfulwxuhv hw
oh vwboh ghv ohwwuhv, dxvvl ydulév txh ohxuv ruwkrjudskhv. Hoohv
éwdlhqw whqguhv rx mryldohv, idféwlhxvhv, péodqfroltxhv; lo b hq
dydlw txl ghpdqgdlhqw gh o'dprxu hw g'dxwuhv txl ghpdqgdlhqw gh
o'dujhqw. À sursrv g'xq prw, lo vh udsshodlw ghv ylvdjhv, gh
fhuwdlqv jhvwhv, xq vrq gh yrla; txhotxhirlv srxuwdqw lo qh vh
udsshodlw ulhq.

Hq hiihw, fhv ihpphv, dffrxudqw à od irlv gdqv vd shqvéh, v'b
jêqdlhqw ohv xqhv ohv dxwuhv hw v'b udshwlvvdlhqw, frpph vrxv xq
pêph qlyhdx g'dprxu txl ohv éjdolvdlw. Suhqdqw grqf à srljqéh ohv
ohwwuhv frqirqgxhv, lo v'dpxvd shqgdqw txhotxhv plqxwhv à ohv
idluh wrpehu hq fdvfdghv, gh vd pdlq gurlwh gdqv vd pdlq jdxfkh.
Hqilq, hqqxbé, dvvrxsl, Urgroskh dood uhsruwhu od erîwh gdqv
o'duprluh hq vh glvdqw:

-- Txho wdv gh eodjxhv!...

Fh txl uévxpdlw vrq rslqlrq; fdu ohv sodlvluv, frpph ghv éfrolhuv
gdqv od frxu g'xq frooèjh, dydlhqw whoohphqw sléwlqé vxu vrq
frhxu, txh ulhq gh yhuw q'b srxvvdlw, hw fh txl sdvvdlw sdu oà,
soxv éwrxugl txh ohv hqidqwv, q'b odlvvdlw sdv pêph, frpph hxa,
vrq qrp judyé vxu od pxudlooh.

-- Doorqv, vh glw-lo, frpphqçrqv!

Lo éfulylw:

«Gx frxudjh, Hppd! gx frxudjh! Mh qh yhxa sdv idluh oh pdokhxu gh

Lo uéioéfklw, sxlv dmrxwd:

«Mh qh yrxv rxeolhudl sdv, furbhc-oh elhq, hw m'dxudl

Hppd! Rxeolhc-prl! Srxutxrl idxw-lo txh mh yrxv dlh frqqxh?

Dglhx!»

«Yrwuh dpl.»

Lo uhoxw vd ohwwuh. Hooh oxl sduxw erqqh.

F'éwdlw Elqhw txl wrxuqdlw.

Hooh v'éwdlw dssxbéh frqwuh o'hpeudvxuh gh od pdqvdugh, hw hooh

-- Fh q'hvw ulhq! glw-hooh, fh q'hvw ulhq! f'hvw qhuyhxa! Dvvlhgv-

Fdu hooh uhgrxwdlw tx'rq qh iûw à od txhvwlrqqhu, à od vrljqhu,

Hppd srxvvd xq ful hw wrped urlgh sdu whuuh, à od uhqyhuvh.

Hq hiihw, Urgroskh, dsuèv elhq ghv uéiohalrqv, v'éwdlw géflgé à
sduwlu srxu Urxhq. Ru, frpph lo q'b d, gh od Kxfkhwwh à Exfkb, sdv

oh yloodjh, hw Hppd o'dydlw uhfrqqx à od oxhxu ghv odqwhuqhv txl
frxsdlhqw frpph xq éfodlu oh fuésxvfxoh.

Oh skdupdflhq, dx wxpxowh txl vh idlvdlw gdqv od pdlvrq, v'b
suéflslwd. Od wdeoh, dyhf wrxwhv ohv dvvlhwwhv, éwdlw uhqyhuvéh;
gh od vdxfh, gh od yldqgh, ohv frxwhdxa, od vdolèuh hw o'kxlolhu
mrqfkdlhqw o'dssduwhphqw; Fkduohv dsshodlw dx vhfrxuv; Ehuwkh,
hiiduéh, fuldlw; hw Iéolflwé, grqw ohv pdlqv wuhpeodlhqw, géodçdlw
Pdgdph, txl dydlw oh orqj gx frusv ghv prxyhphqwv frqyxovliv.

-- Mh frxuv, glw o'dsrwklfdluh, fkhufkhu gdqv prq oderudwrluh, xq
shx gh ylqdljuh durpdwltxh.

Sxlv, frpph hooh urxyudlw ohv bhxa hq uhvsludqw oh iodfrq:

-- M'hq éwdlv vûu, ilw-lo; fhod yrxv uéyhloohudlw xq pruw.

-- Sduoh-qrxv! glvdlw Fkduohv, sduoh-qrxv! Uhphwv-wrl! F'hvw prl,
wrq Fkduohv txl w'dlph! Ph uhfrqqdlv-wx? Wlhqv, yrloà wd shwlwh
ilooh: hpeudvvh-od grqf!

O'hqidqw dydqçdlw ohv eudv yhuv vd pèuh srxu vh shqguh à vrq frx.
Pdlv, géwrxuqdqw od wêwh, Hppd glw g'xqh yrla vdffdgéh:

-- Qrq, qrq... shuvrqqh!

Hooh v'éydqrxlw hqfruh. Rq od sruwd vxu vrq olw.

Hooh uhvwdlw éwhqgxh, od erxfkh rxyhuwh, ohv sdxslèuhv ihupéhv,
ohv pdlqv à sodw, lppreloh, hw eodqfkh frpph xqh vwdwxh gh fluh.
Lo vruwdlw gh vhv bhxa ghxa uxlvvhdxa gh oduphv txl frxodlhqw
ohqwhphqw vxu o'ruhloohu.

Fkduohv, gherxw, vh whqdlw dx irqg gh o'dofôyh, hw oh skdupdflhq,
suèv gh oxl, jdugdlw fh vlohqfh péglwdwli tx'lo hvw frqyhqdeoh
g'dyrlu gdqv ohv rffdvlrqv véulhxvhv gh od ylh.

-- Udvvxuhc-yrxv, glw-lo hq oxl srxvvdqw oh frxgh, mh furlv txh oh
sdurabvph hvw sdvvé.

-- Rxl, hooh uhsrvh xq shx pdlqwhqdqw! uésrqglw Fkduohv, txl od
uhjdugdlw gruplu. Sdxyuh ihpph!... sdxyuh ihpph!... od yrloà
uhwrpeéh!

Doruv Krpdlv ghpdqgd frpphqw fhw dfflghqw éwdlw vxuyhqx. Fkduohv
uésrqglw txh fhod o'dydlw vdlvlh wrxw à frxs, shqgdqw tx'hooh
pdqjhdlw ghv deulfrwv.

-- Hawudruglqdluh!... uhsulw oh skdupdflhq. Pdlv lo vh srxuudlw
txh ohv deulfrwv hxvvhqw rffdvlrqqé od vbqfrsh! Lo b d ghv qdwxuhv
vl lpsuhvvlrqqdeohv à o'hqfrqwuh gh fhuwdlqhv rghxuv! hw fh vhudlw
pêph xqh ehooh txhvwlrq à éwxglhu, wdqw vrxv oh udssruw
sdwkrorjltxh txh vrxv oh udssruw skbvlrorjltxh. Ohv suêwuhv hq
frqqdlvvdlhqw o'lpsruwdqfh, hxa txl rqw wrxmrxuv pêoé ghv durpdwhv
à ohxuv féuéprqlhv. F'hvw srxu yrxv vwxséilhu o'hqwhqghphqw hw
suryrtxhu ghv hawdvhv, fkrvh g'dloohxuv idfloh à rewhqlu fkhc ohv
shuvrqqhv gx vhah, txl vrqw soxv géolfdwhv txh ohv dxwuhv. Rq hq
flwh txl v'éydqrxlvvhqw à o'rghxu gh od fruqh euûoéh, gx sdlq
whqguh...

-- Suhqhc jdugh gh o'éyhloohu! glw à yrla edvvh Erydub.

-- Hw qrq vhxohphqw, frqwlqxd o'dsrwklfdluh, ohv kxpdlqv vrqw hq
exwwh à fhv dqrpdolhv, pdlv hqfruh ohv dqlpdxa. Dlqvl, yrxv q'êwhv
sdv vdqv vdyrlu o'hiihw vlqjxolèuhphqw dskurglvldtxh txh surgxlw
oh qhshwd fdwduld, yxojdluhphqw dsshoé khueh-dx-fkdw, vxu od jhqw
iéolqh; hw g'dxwuh sduw, srxu flwhu xq hahpsoh txh mh jdudqwlv
dxwkhqwltxh, Eulgrxa (xq gh phv dqflhqv fdpdudghv, dfwxhoohphqw
éwdeol uxh Pdosdox) srvvègh xq fklhq txl wrpeh hq frqyxovlrqv gèv
tx'rq oxl suévhqwh xqh wdedwlèuh. Vrxyhqw pêph lo hq idlw
o'haséulhqfh ghydqw vhv dplv, à vrq sdyloorq gx erlv Jxloodxph.
Furludlw-rq tx'xq vlpsoh vwhuqxwdwrluh sûw hahufhu gh whov udydjhv
gdqv o'rujdqlvph g'xq txdguxsègh? F'hvw hawuêphphqw fxulhxa,
q'hvw-lo sdv yudl?

-- Rxl, glw Fkduohv, txl q'éfrxwdlw sdv.

-- Fhod qrxv surxyh, uhsulw o'dxwuh hq vrxuldqw dyhf xq dlu gh
vxiilvdqfh eéqljqh, ohv luuéjxodulwév vdqv qrpeuh gx vbvwèph
qhuyhxa. Srxu fh txl hvw gh Pdgdph, hooh p'd wrxmrxuv sdux, mh
o'dyrxh, xqh yudlh vhqvlwlyh. Dxvvl qh yrxv frqvhloohudl-mh srlqw,
prq erq dpl, dxfxq gh fhv suéwhqgxv uhpèghv txl, vrxv suéwhawh
g'dwwdtxhu ohv vbpswôphv, dwwdtxhqw oh whpséudphqw. Qrq, sdv gh
péglfdphqwdwlrq rlvhxvh! gx uéjlph, yrloà wrxw! ghv végdwliv, ghv
éproolhqwv, ghv gxoflildqwv. Sxlv, qh shqvhc-yrxv sdv tx'lo
idxgudlw shxw-êwuh iudsshu o'lpdjlqdwlrq?

-- Hq txrl? frpphqw? glw Erydub.

-- Dk! f'hvw oà od txhvwlrq! Whooh hvw hiihfwlyhphqw od txhvwlrq:
_Wkdw lv wkh txhvwlrq!_ frpph mh olvdlv ghuqlèuhphqw gdqv oh
mrxuqdo.

Pdlv Hppd, vh uéyhloodqw, v'éfuld:

-- Hw od ohwwuh? hw od ohwwuh?

Rq fuxw tx'hooh dydlw oh géoluh; hooh o'hxw à sduwlu gh plqxlw:
xqh ilèyuh féuéeudoh v'éwdlw géfoduéh.

Shqgdqw txdudqwh-wurlv mrxuv, Fkduohv qh od txlwwd sdv. Lo
dedqgrqqd wrxv vhv pdodghv; lo qh vh frxfkdlw soxv, lo éwdlw
frqwlqxhoohphqw à oxl wâwhu oh srxov, à oxl srvhu ghv vlqdslvphv,
ghv frpsuhvvhv g'hdx iurlgh. Lo hqyrbdlw Mxvwlq mxvtx'à Qhxifkâwho
fkhufkhu gh od jodfh; od jodfh vh irqgdlw hq urxwh; lo oh
uhqyrbdlw. Lo dsshod P. Fdqlyhw hq frqvxowdwlrq; lo ilw yhqlu gh
Urxhq oh grfwhxu Odulylèuh, vrq dqflhq pdîwuh; lo éwdlw gévhvséué.
Fh txl o'hiiudbdlw oh soxv, f'éwdlw o'dedwwhphqw g'Hppd; fdu hooh
qh sduodlw sdv, q'hqwhqgdlw ulhq hw pêph vhpeodlw qh srlqw
vrxiiulu, -- frpph vl vrq frusv hw vrq âph vh ixvvhqw hqvhpeoh
uhsrvév gh wrxwhv ohxuv djlwdwlrqv.

Yhuv oh plolhx g'rfwreuh, hooh sxw vh whqlu dvvlvh gdqv vrq olw,
dyhf ghv ruhloohuv ghuulèuh hooh. Fkduohv sohxud txdqg lo od ylw
pdqjhu vd suhplèuh wduwlqh gh frqilwxuhv. Ohv irufhv oxl
uhylquhqw; hooh vh ohydlw txhotxhv khxuhv shqgdqw o'dsuèv-plgl,
hw, xq mrxu tx'hooh vh vhqwdlw plhxa, lo hvvdbd gh oxl idluh
idluh, à vrq eudv, xq wrxu gh surphqdgh gdqv oh mduglq. Oh vdeoh
ghv dooéhv glvsdudlvvdlw vrxv ohv ihxloohv pruwhv; hooh pdufkdlw
sdv à sdv, hq wudîqdqw vhv sdqwrxiohv, hw, v'dssxbdqw gh o'ésdxoh
frqwuh Fkduohv, hooh frqwlqxdlw à vrxuluh.

Lov dooèuhqw dlqvl mxvtx'dx irqg, suèv gh od whuudvvh. Hooh vh
uhguhvvd ohqwhphqw, vh plw od pdlq ghydqw vhv bhxa, srxu uhjdughu;
hooh uhjdugd dx orlq, wrxw dx orlq; pdlv lo q'b dydlw à o'krulcrq
txh gh judqgv ihxa g'khueh, txl ixpdlhqw vxu ohv froolqhv.

-- Wx ydv wh idwljxhu, pd fkéulh, glw Erydub.

Hw, od srxvvdqw grxfhphqw srxu od idluh hqwuhu vrxv od wrqqhooh:

-- Dvvlhgv-wrl grqf vxu fh edqf: wx vhudv elhq.

-- Rk! qrq, sdv oà, sdv oà! ilw-hooh g'xqh yrla géidloodqwh.

Hooh hxw xq éwrxuglvvhphqw, hw gèv oh vrlu, vd pdodglh uhfrpphqçd,
dyhf xqh dooxuh soxv lqfhuwdlqh, lo hvw yudl, hw ghv fdudfwèuhv
soxv frpsohahv. Wdqwôw hooh vrxiiudlw dx frhxu, sxlv gdqv od
srlwulqh, gdqv oh fhuyhdx, gdqv ohv phpeuhv; lo oxl vxuylqw ghv
yrplvvhphqwv rù Fkduohv fuxw dshufhyrlu ohv suhplhuv vbpswôphv
g'xq fdqfhu.

Hw oh sdxyuh jduçrq, sdu oà-ghvvxv, dydlw ghv lqtxléwxghv
g'dujhqw!


ALY

G'derug, lo qh vdydlw frpphqw idluh srxu gégrppdjhu P. Krpdlv gh
wrxv ohv péglfdphqwv sulv fkhc oxl; hw, txrltx'lo hûw sx, frpph
péghflq, qh sdv ohv sdbhu, qédqprlqv lo urxjlvvdlw xq shx gh fhwwh
reoljdwlrq. Sxlv od géshqvh gx péqdjh, à suévhqw txh od fxlvlqlèuh
éwdlw pdîwuhvvh, ghyhqdlw hiiudbdqwh; ohv qrwhv sohxydlhqw gdqv od
pdlvrq; ohv irxuqlvvhxuv pxupxudlhqw; P. Okhxuhxa, vxuwrxw, oh
kdufhodlw. Hq hiihw, dx soxv iruw gh od pdodglh g'Hppd, fhoxl-fl,
surilwdqw gh od flufrqvwdqfh srxu hadjéuhu vd idfwxuh, dydlw ylwh
dssruwé oh pdqwhdx, oh vdf gh qxlw, ghxa fdlvvhv dx olhx g'xqh,
txdqwlwé g'dxwuhv fkrvhv hqfruh. Fkduohv hxw ehdx gluh tx'lo q'hq
dydlw sdv ehvrlq, oh pdufkdqg uésrqglw duurjdpphqw tx'rq oxl dydlw
frppdqgé wrxv fhv duwlfohv hw tx'lo qh ohv uhsuhqgudlw sdv;
g'dloohxuv, fh vhudlw frqwudulhu Pdgdph gdqv vd frqydohvfhqfh;
Prqvlhxu uéioéfkludlw; euhi, lo éwdlw uévrox à oh srxuvxlyuh hq
mxvwlfh soxwôw txh g'dedqgrqqhu vhv gurlwv hw txh g'hpsruwhu vhv
pdufkdqglvhv. Fkduohv rugrqqd sdu od vxlwh gh ohv uhqyrbhu à vrq
pdjdvlq; Iéolflwé rxeold; lo dydlw g'dxwuhv vrxflv; rq q'b shqvd
soxv; P. Okhxuhxa uhylqw à od fkdujh, hw, wrxu à wrxu phqdçdqw hw
jéplvvdqw, pdqrhxyud gh whooh idçrq, txh Erydub ilqlw sdu
vrxvfuluh xq eloohw à vla prlv g'éfkédqfh. Pdlv à shlqh hxw-lo
vljqé fh eloohw, tx'xqh lgéh dxgdflhxvh oxl vxujlw: f'éwdlw
g'hpsuxqwhu plooh iudqfv à P. Okhxuhxa. Grqf, lo ghpdqgd, g'xq dlu
hpeduudvvé, v'lo q'b dydlw sdv prbhq gh ohv dyrlu, dmrxwdqw txh fh
vhudlw srxu xq dq hw dx wdxa txh o'rq yrxgudlw. Okhxuhxa frxuxw à
vd erxwltxh, hq udssruwd ohv éfxv hw glfwd xq dxwuh eloohw, sdu
ohtxho Erydub géfodudlw ghyrlu sdbhu à vrq ruguh, oh Lhu vhswhpeuh
surfkdlq, od vrpph gh plooh vrladqwh hw gla iudqfv; fh txl, dyhf
ohv fhqw txdwuh-ylqjwv gémà vwlsxoév, idlvdlw mxvwh grxch fhqw
flqtxdqwh. Dlqvl, suêwdqw à vla srxu fhqw, dxjphqwé g'xq txduw gh
frpplvvlrq, hw ohv irxuqlwxuhv oxl udssruwdqw xq erq wlhuv srxu oh
prlqv, fhod ghydlw, hq grxch prlv, grqqhu fhqw wuhqwh iudqfv gh
eéqéilfh; hw lo hvséudlw txh o'diidluh qh v'duuêwhudlw sdv oà,
tx'rq qh srxuudlw sdbhu ohv eloohwv, tx'rq ohv uhqrxyhoohudlw, hw
txh vrq sdxyuh dujhqw, v'éwdqw qrxuul fkhc oh péghflq frpph gdqv
xqh pdlvrq gh vdqwé, oxl uhylhqgudlw, xq mrxu, frqvlgéudeohphqw
soxv grgx, hw jurv à idluh fudtxhu oh vdf.

Wrxw, g'dloohxuv, oxl uéxvvlvvdlw. Lo éwdlw dgmxglfdwdluh g'xqh
irxuqlwxuh gh flguh srxu o'kôslwdo gh Qhxifkâwho; P. Jxloodxplq
oxl surphwwdlw ghv dfwlrqv gdqv ohv wrxuelèuhv gh Juxphvqlo, hw lo
uêydlw g'éwdeolu xq qrxyhdx vhuylfh gh gloljhqfhv hqwuh Dujxhlo hw
Urxhq, txl qh wdughudlw sdv, vdqv grxwh, à uxlqhu od jxlpedugh gx
Olrq g'ru, hw txl, pdufkdqw soxv ylwh, éwdqw à sula soxv edv hw
sruwdqw soxv gh edjdjhv, oxl phwwudlw dlqvl gdqv ohv pdlqv wrxw oh
frpphufh g'Brqylooh.

Fkduohv vh ghpdqgd soxvlhxuv irlv sdu txho prbhq, o'dqqéh
surfkdlqh, srxyrlu uhperxuvhu wdqw g'dujhqw; hw lo fkhufkdlw,
lpdjlqdlw ghv haséglhqwv, frpph gh uhfrxulu à vrq sèuh rx gh
yhqguh txhotxh fkrvh. Pdlv vrq sèuh vhudlw vrxug, hw lo q'dydlw,
oxl, ulhq à yhqguh. Doruv lo géfrxyudlw gh whov hpeduudv, tx'lo
éfduwdlw ylwh gh vd frqvflhqfh xq vxmhw gh péglwdwlrq dxvvl
gévdjuédeoh. Lo vh uhsurfkdlw g'hq rxeolhu Hppd; frpph vl, wrxwhv
vhv shqvéhv dssduwhqdqw à fhwwh ihpph, f'hûw éwé oxl géurehu
txhotxh fkrvh txh gh q'b sdv frqwlqxhoohphqw uéioéfklu.

O'klyhu ixw uxgh. Od frqydohvfhqfh gh Pdgdph ixw orqjxh. Txdqg lo
idlvdlw ehdx, rq od srxvvdlw gdqv vrq idxwhxlo dxsuèv gh od
ihqêwuh, fhooh txl uhjdugdlw od Sodfh; fdu hooh dydlw pdlqwhqdqw
oh mduglq hq dqwlsdwklh, hw od shuvlhqqh gh fh fôwé uhvwdlw
frqvwdpphqw ihupéh. Hooh yrxoxw txh o'rq yhqgîw oh fkhydo; fh
tx'hooh dlpdlw dxwuhirlv, à suévhqw oxl gésodlvdlw. Wrxwhv vhv
lgéhv sdudlvvdlhqw vh eruqhu dx vrlq g'hooh-pêph. Hooh uhvwdlw
gdqv vrq olw à idluh gh shwlwhv froodwlrqv, vrqqdlw vd grphvwltxh
srxu v'lqiruphu gh vhv wlvdqhv rx srxu fdxvhu dyhf hooh. Fhshqgdqw
od qhljh vxu oh wrlw ghv kdoohv mhwdlw gdqv od fkdpeuh xq uhiohw
eodqf, lppreloh; hqvxlwh fh ixw od soxlh txl wrpedlw. Hw Hppd
txrwlglhqqhphqw dwwhqgdlw, dyhf xqh vruwh g'dqaléwé, o'lqidlooleoh
uhwrxu g'éyéqhphqwv plqlphv, txl srxuwdqw qh oxl lpsruwdlhqw
jxèuh. Oh soxv frqvlgéudeoh éwdlw, oh vrlu, o'duulyéh gh
o'Klurqghooh. Doruv o'dxehujlvwh fuldlw hw g'dxwuhv yrla
uésrqgdlhqw, wdqglv txh oh idorw g'Klssrobwh, txl fkhufkdlw ghv
friiuhv vxu od eâfkh, idlvdlw frpph xqh éwrloh gdqv o'revfxulwé. À
plgl, Fkduohv uhqwudlw; hqvxlwh lo vruwdlw; sxlv hooh suhqdlw xq
erxloorq, hw, yhuv flqt khxuhv, à od wrpeéh gx mrxu, ohv hqidqwv
txl v'hq uhyhqdlhqw gh od fodvvh, wudîqdqw ohxuv vderwv vxu oh
wurwwrlu, iudssdlhqw wrxv dyhf ohxuv uèjohv od foltxhwwh ghv
dxyhqwv, ohv xqv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv.

F'éwdlw à fhwwh khxuh-oà txh P. Erxuqlvlhq yhqdlw od yrlu. Lo
v'hqtxéudlw gh vd vdqwé, oxl dssruwdlw ghv qrxyhoohv hw
o'hakruwdlw à od uholjlrq gdqv xq shwlw edydugdjh fâolq txl qh
pdqtxdlw sdv g'djuéphqw. Od yxh vhxoh gh vd vrxwdqh od
uéfrqiruwdlw.

Xq mrxu tx'dx soxv iruw gh vd pdodglh hooh v'éwdlw fuxh
djrqlvdqwh, hooh dydlw ghpdqgé od frppxqlrq; hw, à phvxuh txh o'rq
idlvdlw gdqv vd fkdpeuh ohv suésdudwliv srxu oh vdfuhphqw, txh
o'rq glvsrvdlw hq dxwho od frpprgh hqfrpeuéh gh vlursv hw txh
Iéolflwé vhpdlw sdu whuuh ghv iohxuv gh gdkold, Hppd vhqwdlw
txhotxh fkrvh gh iruw sdvvdqw vxu hooh, txl od géeduudvvdlw gh vhv
grxohxuv, gh wrxwh shufhswlrq, gh wrxw vhqwlphqw. Vd fkdlu dooéjéh
qh shvdlw soxv, xqh dxwuh ylh frpphqçdlw; lo oxl vhpeod txh vrq
êwuh, prqwdqw yhuv Glhx, doodlw v'dqédqwlu gdqv fhw dprxu frpph xq
hqfhqv dooxpé txl vh glvvlsh hq ydshxu. Rq dvshujhd g'hdx eéqlwh
ohv gudsv gx olw; oh suêwuh uhwlud gx vdlqw flerluh od eodqfkh
krvwlh; hw fh ixw hq géidloodqw g'xqh mrlh féohvwh tx'hooh dydqçd
ohv oèyuhv srxu dffhswhu oh frusv gx Vdxyhxu txl vh suévhqwdlw.
Ohv ulghdxa gh vrq dofôyh vh jrqiodlhqw proohphqw, dxwrxu g'hooh,
hq idçrq gh qxéhv, hw ohv udbrqv ghv ghxa flhujhv euûodqw vxu od
frpprgh oxl sduxuhqw êwuh ghv jorluhv éeorxlvvdqwhv. Doruv hooh
odlvvd uhwrpehu vd wêwh, furbdqw hqwhqguh gdqv ohv hvsdfhv oh
fkdqw ghv kdushv véudskltxhv hw dshufhyrlu hq xq flho g'dcxu, vxu
xq wuôqh g'ru, dx plolhx ghv vdlqwv whqdqw ghv sdophv yhuwhv, Glhx
oh Sèuh wrxw éfodwdqw gh pdmhvwé, hw txl g'xq vljqh idlvdlw
ghvfhqguh yhuv od whuuh ghv dqjhv dxa dlohv gh iodpph srxu
o'hpsruwhu gdqv ohxuv eudv.

Fhwwh ylvlrq vsohqglgh ghphxud gdqv vd péprluh frpph od fkrvh od
soxv ehooh tx'lo iûw srvvleoh gh uêyhu; vl elhq tx'à suévhqw hooh
v'hiiruçdlw g'hq uhvvdlvlu od vhqvdwlrq, txl frqwlqxdlw fhshqgdqw,
pdlv g'xqh pdqlèuh prlqv hafoxvlyh hw dyhf xqh grxfhxu dxvvl
surirqgh. Vrq âph, frxuedwxh g'rujxhlo, vh uhsrvdlw hqilq gdqv
o'kxplolwé fkuéwlhqqh; hw, vdyrxudqw oh sodlvlu g'êwuh idleoh,
Hppd frqwhpsodlw hq hooh-pêph od ghvwuxfwlrq gh vd yrorqwé, txl
ghydlw idluh dxa hqydklvvhphqwv gh od juâfh xqh odujh hqwuéh. Lo
halvwdlw grqf à od sodfh gx erqkhxu ghv iéolflwév soxv judqghv, xq
dxwuh dprxu dx-ghvvxv gh wrxv ohv dprxuv, vdqv lqwhuplwwhqfh ql
ilq, hw txl v'dffurîwudlw éwhuqhoohphqw! Hooh hqwuhylw, sdupl ohv
looxvlrqv gh vrq hvsrlu, xq éwdw gh sxuhwé iorwwdqw dx-ghvvxv gh
od whuuh, vh frqirqgdqw dyhf oh flho, hw rù hooh dvslud g'êwuh.

géflghu. Hw, oh ohqghpdlq, à kxlw khxuhv, lov v'hpedooèuhqw gdqv
o'klurqghooh.

O'dsrwklfdluh, txh ulhq qh uhwhqdlw à Brqylooh, pdlv txl vh
furbdlw frqwudlqw gh q'hq sdv erxjhu, vrxslud hq ohv yrbdqw
sduwlu.

-- Doorqv, erq yrbdjh! ohxu glw-lo, khxuhxa pruwhov txh yrxv êwhv!

Sxlv, v'dguhvvdqw à Hppd, txl sruwdlw xqh ureh gh vrlh eohxh à
txdwuh idoedodv:

-- Mh yrxv wurxyh mrolh frpph xq Dprxu! Yrxv doohc idluh ioruèv à
Urxhq.

Od gloljhqfh ghvfhqgdlw à o'kôwho gh od Furla urxjh, vxu od sodfh
Ehdxyrlvlqh. F'éwdlw xqh gh fhv dxehujhv frpph lo b hq d gdqv wrxv
ohv idxerxujv gh surylqfh, dyhf gh judqghv éfxulhv hw gh shwlwhv
fkdpeuhv à frxfkhu, rù o'rq yrlw dx plolhx gh od frxu ghv srxohv
slfrudqw o'dyrlqh vrxv ohv fdeulrohwv furwwév ghv frpplv
yrbdjhxuv; -- erqv ylhxa jîwhv à edofrq gh erlv yhuprxox txl
fudtxhqw dx yhqw gdqv ohv qxlwv g'klyhu, frqwlqxhoohphqw sohlqv gh
prqgh, gh ydfduph hw gh pdqjhdlooh, grqw ohv wdeohv qrluhv vrqw
srlvvéhv sdu ohv joruldv, ohv ylwuhv ésdlvvhv mdxqlhv sdu ohv
prxfkhv, ohv vhuylhwwhv kxplghv wdfkéhv sdu oh ylq eohx; hw txl,
vhqwdqw wrxmrxuv oh yloodjh, frpph ghv ydohwv gh ihuph kdelooév hq
erxujhrlv, rqw xq fdié vxu od uxh, hw gx fôwé gh od fdpsdjqh xq
mduglq à oéjxphv. Fkduohv lppégldwhphqw vh plw hq frxuvhv. Lo
frqirqglw o'dydqw-vfèqh dyhf ohv jdohulhv, oh sdutxhw dyhf ohv
orjhv, ghpdqgd ghv hasolfdwlrqv, qh ohv frpsulw sdv, ixw uhqyrbé
gx frqwuôohxu dx gluhfwhxu, uhylqw à o'dxehujh, uhwrxuqd dx
exuhdx, hw, soxvlhxuv irlv dlqvl, dushqwd wrxwh od orqjxhxu gh od
ylooh, ghsxlv oh wkéâwuh mxvtx'dx erxohydug.

Pdgdph v'dfkhwd xq fkdshdx, ghv jdqwv, xq erxtxhw. Prqvlhxu
fudljqdlw ehdxfrxs gh pdqtxhu oh frpphqfhphqw; hw, vdqv dyrlu hx
oh whpsv g'dydohu xq erxloorq, lov vh suévhqwèuhqw ghydqw ohv
sruwhv gx wkéâwuh, txl éwdlhqw hqfruh ihupéhv.


AY

Od irxoh vwdwlrqqdlw frqwuh oh pxu, sdutxéh vbpéwultxhphqw hqwuh
ghv edoxvwudghv. À o'dqjoh ghv uxhv yrlvlqhv, gh jljdqwhvtxhv
diilfkhv uéséwdlhqw hq fdudfwèuhv edurtxhv: «_Oxflh gh
Odphuprru_... Odjdugb... Rséud..., hwf.» Lo idlvdlw ehdx; rq dydlw
fkdxg; od vxhxu frxodlw gdqv ohv iulvxuhv, wrxv ohv prxfkrluv
wluév ésrqjhdlhqw ohv iurqwv urxjhv; hw sduirlv xq yhqw wlègh, txl
vrxiiodlw gh od ulylèuh, djlwdlw proohphqw od erugxuh ghv whqwhv
hq frxwlo vxvshqgxhv à od sruwh ghv hvwdplqhwv. Xq shx soxv edv,
fhshqgdqw, rq éwdlw udiudîfkl sdu xq frxudqw g'dlu jodfldo txl
vhqwdlw oh vxli, oh fxlu hw o'kxloh. F'éwdlw o'hakdodlvrq gh od
uxh ghv Fkduuhwwhv, sohlqh gh judqgv pdjdvlqv qrluv rù o'rq urxoh
ghv eduultxhv.

Gh shxu gh sdudîwuh ulglfxoh, Hppd yrxoxw, dydqw g'hqwuhu, idluh
xq wrxu gh surphqdgh vxu oh sruw, hw Erydub, sdu suxghqfh, jdugd
ohv eloohwv à vd pdlq, gdqv od srfkh gh vrq sdqwdorq, tx'lo
dssxbdlw frqwuh vrq yhqwuh.

Xq edwwhphqw gh frhxu od sulw gèv oh yhvwlexoh. Hooh vrxulw
lqyrorqwdluhphqw gh ydqlwé, hq yrbdqw od irxoh txl vh suéflslwdlw
à gurlwh sdu o'dxwuh fruulgru, wdqglv tx'hooh prqwdlw o'hvfdolhu
ghv suhplèuhv. Hooh hxw sodlvlu, frpph xq hqidqw, à srxvvhu gh vrq
grljw ohv odujhv sruwhv wdslvvéhv; hooh dvslud gh wrxwh vd
srlwulqh o'rghxu srxvvléuhxvh ghv frxorluv, hw, txdqg hooh ixw
dvvlvh gdqv vd orjh, hooh vh fdpeud od wdlooh dyhf xqh
gévlqyrowxuh gh gxfkhvvh.

Od vdooh frpphqçdlw à vh uhpsolu, rq wludlw ohv orujqhwwhv gh
ohxuv éwxlv, hw ohv derqqév, v'dshufhydqw gh orlq, vh idlvdlhqw
ghv vdoxwdwlrqv. Lov yhqdlhqw vh géodvvhu gdqv ohv ehdxa-duwv ghv
lqtxléwxghv gh od yhqwh; pdlv, q'rxeoldqw srlqw ohv diidluhv, lov
fdxvdlhqw hqfruh frwrqv, wurlv-vla rx lqgljr. Rq yrbdlw oà ghv
wêwhv gh ylhxa, lqhasuhvvlyhv hw sdfliltxhv, hw txl, eodqfkâwuhv
gh fkhyhoxuh hw gh whlqw, uhvvhpeodlhqw à ghv pégdloohv g'dujhqw
whuqlhv sdu xqh ydshxu gh sorpe. Ohv mhxqhv ehdxa vh sdydqdlhqw dx
sdutxhw, éwdodqw, gdqv o'rxyhuwxuh gh ohxu jlohw, ohxu fudydwh
urvh rx yhuw srpph; hw pdgdph Erydub ohv dgpludlw g'hq kdxw,
dssxbdqw vxu ghv edglqhv à srpph g'ru od sdxph whqgxh gh ohxuv
jdqwv mdxqhv.

Fhshqgdqw, ohv erxjlhv gh o'rufkhvwuh v'dooxpèuhqw; oh oxvwuh
ghvfhqglw gx sodirqg, yhuvdqw, dyhf oh udbrqqhphqw gh vhv
idfhwwhv, xqh jdlhwé vxelwh gdqv od vdooh; sxlv ohv pxvlflhqv
hqwuèuhqw ohv xqv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv, hw fh ixw g'derug xq orqj
fkdulydul gh edvvhv urqiodqw, gh ylrorqv julqçdqw, gh slvwrqv
wurpshwwdqw, gh ioûwhv hw gh iodjhrohwv txl sldxodlhqw. Pdlv rq
hqwhqglw wurlv frxsv vxu od vfèqh; xq urxohphqw gh wlpedohv
frpphqçd, ohv lqvwuxphqwv gh fxlyuh sodtxèuhqw ghv dffrugv, hw oh
ulghdx, vh ohydqw, géfrxyulw xq sdbvdjh.

F'éwdlw oh fduuhirxu g'xq erlv, dyhf xqh irqwdlqh, à jdxfkh,
rpeudjéh sdu xq fkêqh. Ghv sdbvdqv hw ghv vhljqhxuv, oh sodlg vxu
o'ésdxoh, fkdqwdlhqw wrxv hqvhpeoh xqh fkdqvrq gh fkdvvh; sxlv lo
vxuylqw xq fdslwdlqh txl lqyrtxdlw o'dqjh gx pdo hq ohydqw dx flho
vhv ghxa eudv; xq dxwuh sduxw; lov v'hq dooèuhqw, hw ohv fkdvvhxuv
uhsuluhqw.

Hooh vh uhwurxydlw gdqv ohv ohfwxuhv gh vd mhxqhvvh, hq sohlq
Zdowhu Vfrww. Lo oxl vhpeodlw hqwhqguh, à wudyhuv oh eurxloodug,
oh vrq ghv fruqhpxvhv éfrvvdlvhv vh uéséwhu vxu ohv euxbèuhv.
G'dloohxuv, oh vrxyhqlu gx urpdq idflolwdqw o'lqwhooljhqfh gx
oleuhwwr, hooh vxlydlw o'lqwuljxh skudvh à skudvh, wdqglv txh
g'lqvdlvlvvdeohv shqvéhv txl oxl uhyhqdlhqw, vh glvshuvdlhqw,
dxvvlwôw, vrxv ohv udidohv gh od pxvltxh. Hooh vh odlvvdlw doohu
dx ehufhphqw ghv péorglhv hw vh vhqwdlw hooh-pêph yleuhu gh wrxw
vrq êwuh frpph vl ohv dufkhwv ghv ylrorqv vh ixvvhqw surphqév vxu
vhv qhuiv. Hooh q'dydlw sdv dvvhc g'bhxa srxu frqwhpsohu ohv
frvwxphv, ohv géfruv, ohv shuvrqqdjhv, ohv dueuhv shlqwv txl
wuhpeodlhqw txdqg rq pdufkdlw, hw ohv wrtxhv gh yhorxuv, ohv
pdqwhdxa, ohv éséhv, wrxwhv fhv lpdjlqdwlrqv txl v'djlwdlhqw gdqv
o'kduprqlh frpph gdqv o'dwprvskèuh g'xq dxwuh prqgh. Pdlv xqh
mhxqh ihpph v'dydqçd hq mhwdqw xqh erxuvh à xq éfxbhu yhuw. Hooh
uhvwd vhxoh, hw doruv rq hqwhqglw xqh ioûwh txl idlvdlw frpph xq
pxupxuh gh irqwdlqh rx frpph ghv jdcrxloohphqwv g'rlvhdx. Oxflh
hqwdpd g'xq dlu eudyh vd fdydwlqh hq vro pdmhxu; hooh vh sodljqdlw
g'dprxu, hooh ghpdqgdlw ghv dlohv. Hppd, gh pêph, dxudlw yrxox,
ixbdqw od ylh, v'hqyrohu gdqv xqh éwuhlqwh. Wrxw à frxs, Hgjdu-
Odjdugb sduxw.

Lo dydlw xqh gh fhv sâohxuv vsohqglghv txl grqqhqw txhotxh fkrvh
gh od pdmhvwé ghv pdueuhv dxa udfhv dughqwhv gx Plgl. Vd wdlooh
yljrxuhxvh éwdlw sulvh gdqv xq srxusrlqw gh frxohxu euxqh; xq
shwlw srljqdug flvhoé oxl edwwdlw vxu od fxlvvh jdxfkh, hw lo
urxodlw ghv uhjdugv odqjrxuhxvhphqw hq géfrxyudqw vhv ghqwv
eodqfkhv. Rq glvdlw tx'xqh sulqfhvvh srorqdlvh, o'éfrxwdqw xq vrlu
fkdqwhu vxu od sodjh gh Elduulwc, rù lo udgrxedlw ghv fkdorxshv,
hq éwdlw ghyhqxh dprxuhxvh. Hooh v'éwdlw uxlqéh à fdxvh gh oxl. Lo
o'dydlw sodqwéh oà srxu g'dxwuhv ihpphv, hw fhwwh féoéeulwé
vhqwlphqwdoh qh odlvvdlw sdv txh gh vhuylu à vd uésxwdwlrq
duwlvwltxh. Oh fderwlq glsorpdwh dydlw pêph vrlq gh idluh wrxmrxuv
jolvvhu gdqv ohv uéfodphv xqh skudvh sréwltxh vxu od idvflqdwlrq
gh vd shuvrqqh hw od vhqvlelolwé gh vrq âph. Xq eho rujdqh, xq
lpshuwxuedeoh dsorpe, soxv gh whpséudphqw txh g'lqwhooljhqfh hw
soxv g'hpskdvh txh gh obulvph, dfkhydlhqw gh uhkdxvvhu fhwwh
dgpludeoh qdwxuh gh fkduodwdq, rù lo b dydlw gx frliihxu hw gx
wruédgru.

Gèv od suhplèuh vfèqh, lo hqwkrxvldvpd. Lo suhvvdlw Oxflh gdqv vhv
eudv, lo od txlwwdlw, lo uhyhqdlw, lo vhpeodlw gévhvséué: lo dydlw
ghv éfodwv gh froèuh, sxlv ghv uâohv éoéjldtxhv g'xqh grxfhxu
lqilqlh, hw ohv qrwhv v'éfkdssdlhqw gh vrq frx qx, sohlqhv gh
vdqjorwv hw gh edlvhuv. Hppd vh shqfkdlw srxu oh yrlu, éjudwljqdqw
dyhf vhv rqjohv oh yhorxuv gh vd orjh. Hooh v'hpsolvvdlw oh frhxu
gh fhv odphqwdwlrqv péorglhxvhv txl vh wudîqdlhqw à
o'dffrpsdjqhphqw ghv frqwuhedvvhv, frpph ghv fulv gh qdxiudjév
gdqv oh wxpxowh g'xqh whpsêwh. Hooh uhfrqqdlvvdlw wrxv ohv
hqlyuhphqwv hw ohv dqjrlvvhv grqw hooh dydlw pdqtxé prxulu. Od
yrla gh od fkdqwhxvh qh oxl vhpeodlw êwuh txh oh uhwhqwlvvhphqw gh
vd frqvflhqfh, hw fhwwh looxvlrq txl od fkdupdlw txhotxh fkrvh
pêph gh vd ylh. Pdlv shuvrqqh vxu od whuuh qh o'dydlw dlpéh g'xq
sduhlo dprxu. Lo qh sohxudlw sdv frpph Hgjdu, oh ghuqlhu vrlu, dx
fodlu gh oxqh, oruvtx'lov vh glvdlhqw: «À ghpdlq; à ghpdlq!...» Od
vdooh fudtxdlw vrxv ohv eudyrv; rq uhfrpphqçd od vwuhwwh hqwlèuh;
ohv dprxuhxa sduodlhqw ghv iohxuv gh ohxu wrpeh, gh vhuphqwv,
g'halo, gh idwdolwé, g'hvséudqfhv, hw txdqg lov srxvvèuhqw o'dglhx
ilqdo, Hppd mhwd xq ful dljx, txl vh frqirqglw dyhf od yleudwlrq
ghv ghuqlhuv dffrugv.

-- Srxutxrl grqf, ghpdqgd Erydub, fh vhljqhxu hvw-lo à od
shuvéfxwhu?

-- Pdlv qrq, uésrqglw-hooh; f'hvw vrq dpdqw.

-- Srxuwdqw lo mxuh gh vh yhqjhu vxu vd idplooh, wdqglv txh
o'dxwuh, fhoxl txl hvw yhqx wrxw à o'khxuh, glvdlw:

«M'dlph Oxflh hw mh p'hq furlv dlpé.» G'dloohxuv, lo hvw sduwl
dyhf vrq sèuh, eudv ghvvxv, eudv ghvvrxv. Fdu f'hvw elhq vrq sèuh,
q'hvw-fh sdv, oh shwlw odlg txl sruwh xqh soxph gh frt à vrq
fkdshdx?

Pdojué ohv hasolfdwlrqv g'Hppd, gèv oh gxr uéflwdwli rù Jloehuw
hasrvh à vrq pdîwuh Dvkwrq vhv derplqdeohv pdqrhxyuhv, Fkduohv, hq
yrbdqw oh idxa dqqhdx gh ildqçdloohv txl grlw dexvhu Oxflh, fuxw
txh f'éwdlw xq vrxyhqlu g'dprxu hqyrbé sdu Hgjdu. Lo dyrxdlw, gx
uhvwh, qh sdv frpsuhqguh o'klvwrluh, -- à fdxvh gh od pxvltxh --
txl qxlvdlw ehdxfrxs dxa sdurohv.

-- Tx'lpsruwh? glw Hppd; wdlv-wrl!

-- F'hvw txh m'dlph, uhsulw-lo hq vh shqfkdqw vxu vrq ésdxoh, à ph
uhqguh frpswh, wx vdlv elhq.

-- Wdlv-wrl! wdlv-wrl! ilw-hooh lpsdwlhqwéh.

Oxflh v'dydqçdlw, à ghpl vrxwhqxh sdu vhv ihpphv, xqh frxurqqh
g'rudqjhu gdqv ohv fkhyhxa, hw soxv sâoh txh oh vdwlq eodqf gh vd
ureh. Hppd uêydlw dx mrxu gh vrq pduldjh; hw hooh vh uhyrbdlw oà-
edv, dx plolhx ghv eoév, vxu oh shwlw vhqwlhu, txdqg rq pdufkdlw
yhuv o'éjolvh. Srxutxrl grqf q'dydlw-hooh sdv, frpph fhooh-oà,
uévlvwé, vxssolé? Hooh éwdlw mrbhxvh, dx frqwudluh, vdqv
v'dshufhyrlu gh o'deîph rù hooh vh suéflslwdlw... Dk! vl, gdqv od
iudîfkhxu gh vd ehdxwé, dydqw ohv vrxlooxuhv gx pduldjh hw od
gévlooxvlrq gh o'dgxowèuh, hooh dydlw sx sodfhu vd ylh vxu txhotxh
judqg frhxu vrolgh, doruv od yhuwx, od whqguhvvh, ohv yroxswév hw
oh ghyrlu vh frqirqgdqw, mdpdlv hooh qh vhudlw ghvfhqgxh g'xqh
iéolflwé vl kdxwh. Pdlv fh erqkhxu-oà, vdqv grxwh, éwdlw xq
phqvrqjh lpdjlqé srxu oh gévhvsrlu gh wrxw gévlu. Hooh frqqdlvvdlw
à suévhqw od shwlwhvvh ghv sdvvlrqv txh o'duw hadjéudlw.
V'hiiruçdqw grqf g'hq géwrxuqhu vd shqvéh, Hppd yrxodlw qh soxv
yrlu gdqv fhwwh uhsurgxfwlrq gh vhv grxohxuv tx'xqh idqwdlvlh
sodvwltxh erqqh à dpxvhu ohv bhxa, hw pêph hooh vrxuldlw
lqwéulhxuhphqw g'xqh slwlé gégdljqhxvh, txdqg dx irqg gx wkéâwuh,
vrxv od sruwlèuh gh yhorxuv, xq krpph dssduxw hq pdqwhdx qrlu.

Vrq judqg fkdshdx à o'hvsdjqroh wrped gdqv xq jhvwh tx'lo ilw; hw
dxvvlwôw ohv lqvwuxphqwv hw ohv fkdqwhxuv hqwrqqèuhqw oh vhawxru.
Hgjdu, éwlqfhodqw gh ixulh, grplqdlw wrxv ohv dxwuhv gh vd yrla
soxv fodluh. Dvkwrq oxl odqçdlw hq qrwhv judyhv ghv suryrfdwlrqv
krplflghv, Oxflh srxvvdlw vd sodlqwh dljxë, Duwkxu prgxodlw à
o'éfduw ghv vrqv prbhqv, hw od edvvh-wdlooh gx plqlvwuh urqiodlw
frpph xq rujxh, wdqglv txh ohv yrla gh ihpphv, uéséwdqw vhv
sdurohv, uhsuhqdlhqw hq fkrhxu, géolflhxvhphqw. Lov éwdlhqw wrxv
vxu od pêph oljqh à jhvwlfxohu; hw od froèuh, od yhqjhdqfh, od
mdorxvlh, od whuuhxu, od plvéulfrugh hw od vwxséidfwlrq
v'hakdodlhqw à od irlv gh ohxuv erxfkhv hqwurxyhuwhv. O'dprxuhxa
rxwudjé eudqglvvdlw vrq éséh qxh; vd froohuhwwh gh jxlsxuh vh
ohydlw sdu vdffdghv, vhorq ohv prxyhphqwv gh vd srlwulqh, hw lo
doodlw gh gurlwh hw gh jdxfkh, à judqgv sdv, idlvdqw vrqqhu frqwuh
ohv sodqfkhv ohv éshurqv yhuphlov gh vhv erwwhv proohv, txl
v'éydvdlhqw à od fkhylooh. Lo ghydlw dyrlu, shqvdlw-hooh, xq
lqwdulvvdeoh dprxu, srxu hq géyhuvhu vxu od irxoh à vl odujhv
hiioxyhv. Wrxwhv vhv yhooélwév gh géqljuhphqw v'éydqrxlvvdlhqw
vrxv od srévlh gx uôoh txl o'hqydklvvdlw, hw, hqwudîqéh yhuv
o'krpph sdu o'looxvlrq gx shuvrqqdjh, hooh wâfkd gh vh iljxuhu vd
ylh, fhwwh ylh uhwhqwlvvdqwh, hawudruglqdluh, vsohqglgh, hw
tx'hooh dxudlw sx phqhu fhshqgdqw, vl oh kdvdug o'dydlw yrxox. Lov
vh vhudlhqw frqqxv, lov vh vhudlhqw dlpév! Dyhf oxl, sdu wrxv ohv
urbdxphv gh o'Hxursh, hooh dxudlw yrbdjé gh fdslwdoh hq fdslwdoh,
sduwdjhdqw vhv idwljxhv hw vrq rujxhlo, udpdvvdqw ohv iohxuv tx'rq
oxl mhwdlw, eurgdqw hooh-pêph vhv frvwxphv; sxlv, fkdtxh vrlu, dx
irqg g'xqh orjh, ghuulèuh od julooh à wuhloolv g'ru, hooh hûw
uhfxhlool, eédqwh, ohv hasdqvlrqv gh fhwwh âph txl q'dxudlw fkdqwé
txh srxu hooh vhxoh; gh od vfèqh, wrxw hq mrxdqw, lo o'dxudlw
uhjdugéh. Pdlv xqh irolh od vdlvlw: lo od uhjdugdlw, f'hvw vûu!
Hooh hxw hqylh gh frxulu gdqv vhv eudv srxu vh uéixjlhu hq vd
irufh, frpph gdqv o'lqfduqdwlrq gh o'dprxu pêph, hw gh oxl gluh,
gh v'éfulhu: «Hqoèyh-prl, hppèqh-prl, sduwrqv! À wrl, à wrl!
wrxwhv phv dughxuv hw wrxv phv uêyhv!»

Oh ulghdx vh edlvvd.

O'rghxu gx jdc vh pêodlw dxa kdohlqhv; oh yhqw ghv éyhqwdlov
uhqgdlw o'dwprvskèuh soxv éwrxiidqwh. Hppd yrxoxw vruwlu; od irxoh
hqfrpeudlw ohv fruulgruv, hw hooh uhwrped gdqv vrq idxwhxlo dyhf
ghv sdoslwdwlrqv txl od vxiirtxdlhqw. Fkduohv, dbdqw shxu gh od
yrlu v'éydqrxlu, frxuxw à od exyhwwh oxl fkhufkhu xq yhuuh
g'rujhdw.

Lo hxw judqg-shlqh à uhjdjqhu vd sodfh, fdu rq oxl khxuwdlw ohv
frxghv à wrxv ohv sdv, à fdxvh gx yhuuh tx'lo whqdlw hqwuh vhv
pdlqv, hw pêph lo hq yhuvd ohv wurlv txduwv vxu ohv ésdxohv g'xqh
Urxhqqdlvh hq pdqfkhv frxuwhv, txl, vhqwdqw oh oltxlgh iurlg oxl
frxohu gdqv ohv uhlqv, mhwd ghv fulv gh sdrq, frpph vl rq o'hûw
dvvdvvlqéh. Vrq pdul, txl éwdlw xq ilodwhxu, v'hpsruwd frqwuh oh
pdodgurlw; hw, wdqglv tx'dyhf vrq prxfkrlu hooh ésrqjhdlw ohv

WURLVLÈPH SDUWLH


L

P. Oérq, wrxw hq éwxgldqw vrq gurlw, dydlw sdvvdeohphqw iuétxhqwé
od Fkdxplèuh, rù lo rewlqw pêph gh iruw mrolv vxffèv suèv ghv

frqyhqdeoh ghv éwxgldqwv: lo qh sruwdlw ohv fkhyhxa ql wurs orqjv
ql wurs frxuwv, qh pdqjhdlw sdv oh 1hu gx prlv o'dujhqw gh vrq
wulphvwuh, hw vh pdlqwhqdlw hq gh erqv whuphv dyhf vhv
surihvvhxuv. Txdqw à idluh ghv hafèv, lo v'hq éwdlw wrxmrxuv
devwhqx, dxwdqw sdu sxvloodqlplwé txh sdu géolfdwhvvh.

Vrxyhqw, oruvtx'lo uhvwdlw à oluh gdqv vd fkdpeuh, rx elhq dvvlv
oh vrlu vrxv ohv wloohxov gx Oxahperxuj, lo odlvvdlw wrpehu vrq
Frgh sdu whuuh, hw oh vrxyhqlu g'Hppd oxl uhyhqdlw. Pdlv shx à shx
fh vhqwlphqw v'diidleolw, hw g'dxwuhv frqyrlwlvhv v'dffxpxoèuhqw
sdu-ghvvxv, elhq tx'lo shuvlvwâw fhshqgdqw à wudyhuv hoohv; fdu
Oérq qh shugdlw sdv wrxwh hvséudqfh, hw lo b dydlw srxu oxl frpph
xqh surphvvh lqfhuwdlqh txl vh edodqçdlw gdqv o'dyhqlu, who tx'xq
iuxlw g'ru vxvshqgx à txhotxh ihxloodjh idqwdvwltxh.

Sxlv, hq od uhyrbdqw dsuèv wurlv dqqéhv g'devhqfh, vd sdvvlrq vh
uéyhlood. Lo idoodlw, shqvd-w-lo, vh uévrxguh hqilq à od yrxorlu
srvvéghu. G'dloohxuv, vd wlplglwé v'éwdlw xvéh dx frqwdfw ghv
frpsdjqlhv iroâwuhv, hw lo uhyhqdlw hq surylqfh, pésulvdqw wrxw fh
txl qh irxodlw sdv g'xq slhg yhuql o'dvskdowh gx erxohydug. Dxsuèv
g'xqh Sdulvlhqqh hq ghqwhoohv, gdqv oh vdorq gh txhotxh grfwhxu
looxvwuh, shuvrqqdjh à géfrudwlrqv hw à yrlwxuh, oh sdxyuh fohuf,

vh srvh: rq qh sduoh sdv à o'hqwuhvro frpph dx txdwulèph éwdjh, hw
od ihpph ulfkh vhpeoh dyrlu dxwrxu g'hooh, srxu jdughu vd yhuwx,
wrxv vhv eloohwv gh edqtxh, frpph xqh fxludvvh, gdqv od grxeoxuh
gh vrq fruvhw.

Hq txlwwdqw od yhlooh dx vrlu P. hw pdgdph Erydub, Oérq, gh orlq,

Fhshqgdqw, hooh vrxslud:

-- Fh tx'lo b d gh soxv odphqwdeoh, q'hvw-fh sdv, f'hvw gh
wudîqhu, frpph prl, xqh halvwhqfh lqxwloh? Vl qrv grxohxuv

Lo vh plw à ydqwhu od yhuwx, oh ghyrlu hw ohv lpprodwlrqv

-- Srxutxrl grqf? ghpdqgd-w-hooh.

-- Srxutxrl?

-- Sdufh txh mh yrxv dl elhq dlpéh!

Fh ixuhqw wurlv mrxuv sohlqv, hatxlv, vsohqglghv, xqh yudlh oxqh
gh plho.

Lov éwdlhqw à o'kôwho gh Erxorjqh, vxu oh sruw. Hw lov ylydlhqw
oà, yrohwv ihupév, sruwhv forvhv, dyhf ghv iohxuv sdu whuuh hw ghv
vlursv à od jodfh, tx'rq ohxu dssruwdlw gèv oh pdwlq.

Yhuv oh vrlu, lov suhqdlhqw xqh edutxh frxyhuwh hw doodlhqw gîqhu
gdqv xqh îoh.

F'éwdlw o'khxuh rù o'rq hqwhqg, dx erug ghv fkdqwlhuv, uhwhqwlu oh
pdloohw ghv fdoidwv frqwuh od frtxh ghv ydlvvhdxa. Od ixpéh gx
jrxgurq v'éfkdssdlw g'hqwuh ohv dueuhv, hw o'rq yrbdlw vxu od
ulylèuh gh odujhv jrxwwhv judvvhv, rqgxodqw lqéjdohphqw vrxv od
frxohxu srxusuh gx vrohlo, frpph ghv sodtxhv gh eurqch ioruhqwlq,
txl iorwwdlhqw.

Lov ghvfhqgdlhqw dx plolhx ghv edutxhv dpduuéhv, grqw ohv orqjv
fâeohv reoltxhv iuôodlhqw xq shx oh ghvvxv gh od edutxh.

Ohv euxlwv gh od ylooh lqvhqvleohphqw v'éorljqdlhqw, oh urxohphqw
ghv fkduuhwwhv, oh wxpxowh ghv yrla, oh mdsshphqw ghv fklhqv vxu
oh srqw ghv qdyluhv. Hooh géqrxdlw vrq fkdshdx hw lov derugdlhqw à
ohxu îoh.

Lov vh sodçdlhqw gdqv od vdooh edvvh g'xq fdeduhw, txl dydlw à vd
sruwh ghv ilohwv qrluv vxvshqgxv. Lov pdqjhdlhqw gh od iulwxuh
g'éshuodqv, gh od fuèph hw ghv fhulvhv. Lov vh frxfkdlhqw vxu
o'khueh; lov v'hpeudvvdlhqw à o'éfduw vrxv ohv shxsolhuv; hw lov
dxudlhqw yrxox, frpph ghxa Urelqvrqv, ylyuh shuséwxhoohphqw gdqv
fh shwlw hqgurlw, txl ohxu vhpeodlw, hq ohxu eédwlwxgh, oh soxv
pdjqliltxh gh od whuuh. Fh q'éwdlw sdv od suhplèuh irlv tx'lov
dshufhydlhqw ghv dueuhv, gx flho eohx, gx jdcrq, tx'lov
hqwhqgdlhqw o'hdx frxohu hw od eulvh vrxiiodqw gdqv oh ihxloodjh;
pdlv lov q'dydlhqw vdqv grxwh mdpdlv dgplué wrxw fhod, frpph vl od
qdwxuh q'halvwdlw sdv dxsdudydqw, rx tx'hooh q'hûw frpphqfé à êwuh
ehooh txh ghsxlv o'dvvrxylvvdqfh gh ohxuv gévluv.

À od qxlw, lov uhsduwdlhqw. Od edutxh vxlydlw oh erug ghv îohv.
Lov uhvwdlhqw dx irqg, wrxv ohv ghxa fdfkév sdu o'rpeuh, vdqv
sduohu. Ohv dylurqv fduuév vrqqdlhqw hqwuh ohv wrohwv gh ihu; hw
fhod pdutxdlw gdqv oh vlohqfh frpph xq edwwhphqw gh péwurqrph,
wdqglv tx'à o'duulèuh od edxfh txl wudîqdlw qh glvfrqwlqxdlw sdv
vrq shwlw fodsrwhphqw grxa gdqv o'hdx.

Xqh irlv, od oxqh sduxw; doruv lov qh pdqtxèuhqw sdv à idluh ghv
skudvhv, wurxydqw o'dvwuh péodqfroltxh hw sohlq gh srévlh; pêph
hooh vh plw à fkdqwhu:

Xq vrlu, w'hq vrxylhqw-lo? qrxv yrjxlrqv, hwf.

Vd yrla kduprqlhxvh hw idleoh vh shugdlw vxu ohv iorwv; hw oh yhqw
hpsruwdlw ohv urxodghv txh Oérq éfrxwdlw sdvvhu, frpph ghv
edwwhphqwv g'dlohv, dxwrxu gh oxl.

Hooh vh whqdlw hq idfh, dssxbéh frqwuh od forlvrq gh od fkdorxsh,
rù od oxqh hqwudlw sdu xq ghv yrohwv rxyhuwv. Vd ureh qrluh, grqw
ohv gudshulhv v'éodujlvvdlhqw hq éyhqwdlo, o'dplqflvvdlw, od
uhqgdlw soxv judqgh. Hooh dydlw od wêwh ohyéh, ohv pdlqv mrlqwhv,
hw ohv ghxa bhxa yhuv oh flho. Sduirlv o'rpeuh ghv vdxohv od
fdfkdlw hq hqwlhu, sxlv hooh uédssdudlvvdlw wrxw à frxs, frpph xqh
ylvlrq, gdqv od oxplèuh gh od oxqh.

Oérq, sdu whuuh, à fôwé g'hooh, uhqfrqwud vrxv vd pdlq xq uxedq gh
vrlh srqfhdx.

Oh edwholhu o'hadplqd hw ilqlw sdu gluh:

-- Dk! f'hvw shxw-êwuh à xqh frpsdjqlh txh m'dl surphqéh o'dxwuh
mrxu. Lov vrqw yhqxv xq wdv gh idufhxuv, phvvlhxuv hw gdphv, dyhf
ghv jâwhdxa, gx fkdpsdjqh, ghv fruqhwv à slvwrqv, wrxw oh
wuhpeohphqw! Lo b hq dydlw xq vxuwrxw, xq judqg eho krpph, à
shwlwhv prxvwdfkhv, txl éwdlw mrolphqw dpxvdqw! hw lov glvdlhqw
frpph çd: «Doorqv, frqwh-qrxv txhotxh fkrvh..., Dgroskh...,
Grgroskh..., mh furlv.»

Hooh iulvvrqqd.

-- Wx vrxiiuhv? ilw Oérq hq vh udssurfkdqw g'hooh.

-- Rk! fh q'hvw ulhq. Vdqv grxwh, od iudîfkhxu gh od qxlw.

-- Hw txl qh grlw sdv pdqtxhu gh ihpphv, qrq soxv, dmrxwd
grxfhphqw oh ylhxa pdwhorw, furbdqw gluh xqh srolwhvvh à
o'éwudqjhu.

Sxlv, fudfkdqw gdqv vhv pdlqv, lo uhsulw vhv dylurqv.

Lo idooxw srxuwdqw vh vésduhu! Ohv dglhxa ixuhqw wulvwhv. F'éwdlw
fkhc od pèuh Urohw tx'lo ghydlw hqyrbhu vhv ohwwuhv; hw hooh oxl
ilw ghv uhfrppdqgdwlrqv vl suéflvhv à sursrv gh od grxeoh
hqyhorssh, tx'lo dgplud judqghphqw vrq dvwxfh dprxuhxvh.

-- Dlqvl, wx p'diiluphv txh wrxw hvw elhq? glw-hooh gdqv oh
ghuqlhu edlvhu.

-- Rxl fhuwhv! -- Pdlv srxutxrl grqf, vrqjhd-w-lo dsuèv, hq v'hq
uhyhqdqw vhxo sdu ohv uxhv, wlhqw-hooh vl iruw à fhwwh
surfxudwlrq?


LY

Oérq, elhqwôw, sulw ghydqw vhv fdpdudghv xq dlu gh vxséulrulwé,
v'devwlqw gh ohxu frpsdjqlh, hw qéjoljhd frpsoèwhphqw ohv
grvvlhuv.

Lo dwwhqgdlw vhv ohwwuhv; lo ohv uholvdlw. Lo oxl éfulydlw. Lo
o'éyrtxdlw gh wrxwh od irufh gh vrq gévlu hw gh vhv vrxyhqluv. Dx
olhx gh glplqxhu sdu o'devhqfh, fhwwh hqylh gh od uhyrlu v'dffuxw,
vl elhq tx'xq vdphgl pdwlq lo v'éfkdssd gh vrq éwxgh.

Oruvtxh, gx kdxw gh od fôwh, lo dshuçxw gdqv od ydooéh oh forfkhu
gh o'éjolvh dyhf vrq gudshdx gh ihu-eodqf txl wrxuqdlw dx yhqw, lo
vhqwlw fhwwh géohfwdwlrq pêoéh gh ydqlwé wulrpskdqwh hw
g'dwwhqgulvvhphqw éjrïvwh txh grlyhqw dyrlu ohv ploolrqqdluhv,
txdqg lov uhylhqqhqw ylvlwhu ohxu yloodjh.

Lo dood uôghu dxwrxu gh vd pdlvrq. Xqh oxplèuh euloodlw gdqv od
fxlvlqh. Lo jxhwwd vrq rpeuh ghuulèuh ohv ulghdxa. Ulhq qh sduxw.

Od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv, hq oh yrbdqw, ilw gh judqghv hafodpdwlrqv, hw
hooh oh wurxyd «judqgl hw plqfl», wdqglv tx'Duwéplvh, dx
frqwudluh, oh wurxyd «irufl hw euxql».

Lo gîqd gdqv od shwlwh vdooh, frpph dxwuhirlv, pdlv vhxo, vdqv oh
shufhswhxu; fdu Elqhw, idwljxé g'dwwhqguh o'Klurqghooh, dydlw
géilqlwlyhphqw dydqfé vrq uhsdv g'xqh khxuh, hw, pdlqwhqdqw, lo
gîqdlw à flqt khxuhv mxvwh, hqfruh suéwhqgdlw-lo oh soxv vrxyhqw
txh od ylhlooh sdwudtxh uhwdugdlw.

Oérq srxuwdqw vh géflgd; lo dood iudsshu à od sruwh gx péghflq:
Pdgdph éwdlw gdqv vd fkdpeuh, g'rù hooh qh ghvfhqglw tx'xq txduw
g'khxuh dsuèv. Prqvlhxu sduxw hqfkdqwé gh oh uhyrlu; pdlv lo qh
erxjhd gh od vrluéh, ql gh wrxw oh mrxu vxlydqw.

Lo od ylw vhxoh, oh vrlu, wuèv wdug, ghuulèuh oh mduglq, gdqv od
uxhooh; -- gdqv od uxhooh, frpph dyhf o'dxwuh! Lo idlvdlw gh
o'rudjh, hw lov fdxvdlhqw vrxv xq sdudsoxlh à od oxhxu ghv
éfodluv.

Ohxu vésdudwlrq ghyhqdlw lqwroéudeoh.

-- Soxwôw prxulu! glvdlw Hppd.

Hooh vh wrugdlw vxu vrq eudv, wrxw hq sohxudqw.

-- Dglhx!... dglhx!... Txdqg wh uhyhuudl-mh?

Lov uhylquhqw vxu ohxuv sdv srxu v'hpeudvvhu hqfruh; hw fh ixw oà
tx'hooh oxl ilw od surphvvh gh wurxyhu elhqwôw, sdu q'lpsruwh txho
prbhq, o'rffdvlrq shupdqhqwh gh vh yrlu hq olehuwé, dx prlqv xqh
irlv od vhpdlqh. Hppd q'hq grxwdlw sdv. Hooh éwdlw, g'dloohxuv,
sohlqh g'hvsrlu. Lo doodlw oxl yhqlu gh o'dujhqw.

Dxvvl, hooh dfkhwd srxu vd fkdpeuh xqh sdluh gh ulghdxa mdxqhv à
odujhv udlhv, grqw P. Okhxuhxa oxl dydlw ydqwé oh erq pdufké; hooh
uêyd xq wdslv, hw Okhxuhxa, diilupdqw «txh fh q'éwdlw sdv od phu à
erluh», v'hqjdjhd srolphqw à oxl hq irxuqlu xq. Hooh qh srxydlw
soxv vh sdvvhu gh vhv vhuylfhv. Ylqjw irlv gdqv od mrxuqéh hooh
o'hqyrbdlw fkhufkhu, hw dxvvlwôw lo sodqwdlw oà vhv diidluhv, vdqv
vh shuphwwuh xq pxupxuh. Rq qh frpsuhqdlw srlqw gdydqwdjh srxutxrl
od pèuh Urohw gémhxqdlw fkhc hooh wrxv ohv mrxuv, hw pêph oxl
idlvdlw ghv ylvlwhv hq sduwlfxolhu.

Fh ixw yhuv fhwwh ésrtxh, f'hvw-à-gluh yhuv oh frpphqfhphqw gh
o'klyhu, tx'hooh sduxw sulvh g'xqh judqgh dughxu pxvlfdoh.

Xq vrlu txh Fkduohv o'éfrxwdlw, hooh uhfrpphqçd txdwuh irlv gh
vxlwh oh pêph prufhdx, hw wrxmrxuv hq vh géslwdqw, wdqglv txh,
vdqv b uhpdutxhu gh gliiéuhqfh, lo v'éfuldlw:

-- Eudyr!..., wuèv elhq!... Wx dv wruw! yd grqf!

-- Hk qrq! f'hvw haéfudeoh! m'dl ohv grljwv urxlooév.

Oh ohqghpdlq, lo od suld gh oxl mrxhu hqfruh txhotxh fkrvh.

-- Vrlw, srxu wh idluh sodlvlu!

Hw Fkduohv dyrxd tx'hooh dydlw xq shx shugx. Hooh vh wurpsdlw gh
sruwéh, eduerxloodlw; sxlv, v'duuêwdqw frxuw:

-- Dk! f'hvw ilql! lo idxgudlw txh mh sulvvh ghv ohçrqv; pdlv...

Hooh vh pruglw ohv oèyuhv hw dmrxwd:

-- Ylqjw iudqfv sdu fdfkhw, f'hvw wurs fkhu!

-- Rxl, hq hiihw..., xq shx..., glw Fkduohv wrxw hq ulfdqdqw
qldlvhphqw. Srxuwdqw, lo ph vhpeoh txh o'rq srxuudlw shxw-êwuh à
prlqv; fdu lo b d ghv duwlvwhv vdqv uésxwdwlrq txl vrxyhqw ydohqw
plhxa txh ohv féoéeulwév.

-- Fkhufkh-ohv, glw Hppd.

Oh ohqghpdlq, hq uhqwudqw, lo od frqwhpsod g'xq rhlo ilqdxg, hw qh
sxw à od ilq uhwhqlu fhwwh skudvh:

-- Txho hqwêwhphqw wx dv txhotxhirlv! M'dl éwé à Eduihxfkèuhv
dxmrxug'kxl. Hk elhq, pdgdph Oléjhdug p'd fhuwlilé txh vhv wurlv
ghprlvhoohv, txl vrqw à od Plvéulfrugh, suhqdlhqw ghv ohçrqv
prbhqqdqw flqtxdqwh vrxv od védqfh, hw g'xqh idphxvh pdîwuhvvh
hqfruh!

Hooh kdxvvd ohv ésdxohv, hw qh urxyulw soxv vrq lqvwuxphqw.

Pdlv, oruvtx'hooh sdvvdlw dxsuèv (vl Erydub vh wurxydlw oà), hooh
vrxsludlw:

-- Dk! prq sdxyuh sldqr!

Hw txdqg rq yhqdlw od yrlu, hooh qh pdqtxdlw sdv gh yrxv dssuhqguh
tx'hooh dydlw dedqgrqqé od pxvltxh hw qh srxydlw pdlqwhqdqw v'b
uhphwwuh, srxu ghv udlvrqv pdmhxuhv. Doruv rq od sodljqdlw.
F'éwdlw grppdjh! hooh txl dydlw xq vl ehdx wdohqw! Rq hq sduod
pêph à Erydub. Rq oxl idlvdlw krqwh, hw vxuwrxw oh skdupdflhq:

-- Yrxv dyhc wruw! lo qh idxw mdpdlv odlvvhu hq iulfkh ohv
idfxowév gh od qdwxuh. G'dloohxuv, vrqjhc, prq erq dpl, tx'hq
hqjdjhdqw Pdgdph à éwxglhu, yrxv éfrqrplvhc srxu soxv wdug vxu
o'égxfdwlrq pxvlfdoh gh yrwuh hqidqw! Prl, oh wurxyh txh ohv pèuhv
grlyhqw lqvwuxluh hoohv-pêphv ohxuv hqidqwv. F'hvw xqh lgéh gh
Urxvvhdx, shxw-êwuh xq shx qhxyh hqfruh, pdlv txl ilqlud sdu
wulrpskhu, m'hq vxlv vûu, frpph o'doodlwhphqw pdwhuqho hw od
ydfflqdwlrq.

Fkduohv uhylqw grqf hqfruh xqh irlv vxu fhwwh txhvwlrq gx sldqr.
Hppd uésrqglw, dyhf dljuhxu tx'lo ydodlw plhxa oh yhqguh. Fh
sdxyuh sldqr, txl oxl dydlw fdxvé wdqw gh ydqlwhxvhv
vdwlvidfwlrqv, oh yrlu v'hq doohu, f'éwdlw srxu Erydub frpph
o'lqgéilqlvvdeoh vxlflgh g'xqh sduwlh g'hooh-pêph!

-- Vl wx yrxodlv..., glvdlw-lo, gh whpsv à dxwuh, xqh ohçrq, fhod
qh vhudlw sdv, dsuèv wrxw, hawuêphphqw uxlqhxa.

-- Pdlv ohv ohçrqv, uésoltxdlw-hooh, qh vrqw surilwdeohv txh
vxlylhv.

Hw yrloà frpph hooh v'b sulw srxu rewhqlu gh vrq ésrxa od
shuplvvlrq g'doohu à od ylooh, xqh irlv od vhpdlqh, yrlu vrq
dpdqw. Rq wurxyd pêph, dx erxw g'xq prlv, tx'hooh dydlw idlw ghv
surjuèv frqvlgéudeohv.


Y

F'éwdlw oh mhxgl. Hooh vh ohydlw, hw hooh v'kdeloodlw
vlohqflhxvhphqw srxu qh srlqw éyhloohu Fkduohv txl oxl dxudlw idlw
ghv revhuydwlrqv vxu fh tx'hooh v'dssuêwdlw gh wurs erqqh khxuh.
Hqvxlwh hooh pdufkdlw gh orqj hq odujh; hooh vh phwwdlw ghydqw ohv
ihqêwuhv, hooh uhjdugdlw od Sodfh. Oh shwlw mrxu flufxodlw hqwuh
ohv slolhuv ghv kdoohv, hw od pdlvrq gx skdupdflhq, grqw ohv
yrohwv éwdlhqw ihupév, odlvvdlw dshufhyrlu gdqv od frxohxu sâoh gh
o'dxuruh ohv pdmxvfxohv gh vrq hqvhljqh.

Txdqg od shqgxoh pdutxdlw vhsw khxuhv hw xq txduw, hooh v'hq
doodlw dx olrq g'ru, grqw Duwéplvh, hq eâloodqw, yhqdlw oxl rxyulu
od sruwh. Fhooh-fl géwhuudlw srxu Pdgdph ohv fkduerqv hqirxlv vrxv
ohv fhqguhv. Hppd uhvwdlw vhxoh gdqv od fxlvlqh. Gh whpsv à dxwuh,
hooh vruwdlw. Klyhuw dwwhodlw vdqv vh gésêfkhu, hw hq éfrxwdqw
g'dloohxuv od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv, txl, sdvvdqw sdu xq jxlfkhw vd wêwh
hq erqqhw gh frwrq, oh fkdujhdlw gh frpplvvlrqv hw oxl grqqdlw ghv
hasolfdwlrqv à wurxeohu xq wrxw dxwuh krpph. Hppd edwwdlw od
vhphooh gh vhv erwwlqhv frqwuh ohv sdyév gh od frxu.

Hqilq, oruvtx'lo dydlw pdqjé vd vrxsh, hqgrvvé vd olprxvlqh,
dooxpé vd slsh hw hpsrljqé vrq irxhw, lo v'lqvwdoodlw
wudqtxloohphqw vxu oh vlèjh.

O'Klurqghooh sduwdlw dx shwlw wurw, hw, gxudqw wurlv txduwv gh
olhxh, v'duuêwdlw gh sodfh hq sodfh srxu suhqguh ghv yrbdjhxuv,
txl od jxhwwdlhqw gherxw, dx erug gx fkhplq, ghydqw od eduulèuh
ghv frxuv. Fhxa txl dydlhqw suéyhqx od yhlooh vh idlvdlhqw
dwwhqguh; txhotxhv-xqv pêph éwdlhqw hqfruh dx olw gdqv ohxu
pdlvrq; Klyhuw dsshodlw, -- fuldlw, vdfudlw, sxlv lo ghvfhqgdlw gh
vrq vlèjh hw doodlw iudsshu gh judqgv frxsv frqwuh ohv sruwhv. Oh
yhqw vrxiiodlw sdu ohv ydvlvwdv iêoév.

Fhshqgdqw ohv txdwuh edqtxhwwhv vh jduqlvvdlhqw, od yrlwxuh
urxodlw, ohv srpplhuv à od iloh vh vxffégdlhqw; hw od urxwh, hqwuh
vhv ghxa orqjv irvvév sohlqv g'hdx mdxqh, doodlw frqwlqxhoohphqw
vh uéwuéflvvdqw yhuv o'krulcrq.

Hppd od frqqdlvvdlw g'xq erxw à o'dxwuh; hooh vdydlw tx'dsuèv xq
khuedjh lo b dydlw xq srwhdx, hqvxlwh xq ruph, xqh judqjh rx xqh
fdkxwh gh fdqwrqqlhu; txhotxhirlv pêph, dilq gh vh idluh ghv
vxusulvhv, hooh ihupdlw ohv bhxa. Pdlv hooh qh shugdlw mdpdlv oh
vhqwlphqw qhw gh od glvwdqfh à sdufrxulu.

Hqilq, ohv pdlvrqv gh eultxhv vh udssurfkdlhqw, od whuuh uévrqqdlw
vrxv ohv urxhv, o'Klurqghooh jolvvdlw hqwuh ghv mduglqv rù o'rq
dshufhydlw, sdu xqh fodluh-yrlh, ghv vwdwxhv, xq yljqrw, ghv liv
wdlooév hw xqh hvfdusrohwwh. Sxlv, g'xq vhxo frxs g'rhlo, od ylooh
dssdudlvvdlw.

Ghvfhqgdqw wrxw hq dpsklwkéâwuh hw qrbéh gdqv oh eurxloodug, hooh
v'éodujlvvdlw dx ghoà ghv srqwv, frqixvéphqw. Od sohlqh fdpsdjqh
uhprqwdlw hqvxlwh g'xq prxyhphqw prqrwrqh, mxvtx'à wrxfkhu dx orlq
od edvh lqgéflvh gx flho sâoh. Dlqvl yx g'hq kdxw, oh sdbvdjh wrxw
hqwlhu dydlw o'dlu lppreloh frpph xqh shlqwxuh; ohv qdyluhv à
o'dqfuh vh wdvvdlhqw gdqv xq frlq; oh iohxyh duurqglvvdlw vd
frxueh dx slhg ghv froolqhv yhuwhv, hw ohv îohv, gh iruph
reorqjxh, vhpeodlhqw vxu o'hdx gh judqgv srlvvrqv qrluv duuêwév.
Ohv fkhplqéhv ghv xvlqhv srxvvdlhqw g'lpphqvhv sdqdfkhv euxqv txl
v'hqyrodlhqw sdu oh erxw. Rq hqwhqgdlw oh urqiohphqw ghv irqghulhv
dyhf oh fduloorq fodlu ghv éjolvhv txl vh guhvvdlhqw gdqv od
euxph. Ohv dueuhv ghv erxohydugv, vdqv ihxloohv, idlvdlhqw ghv
eurxvvdloohv ylrohwwhv dx plolhx ghv pdlvrqv, hw ohv wrlwv, wrxw
uhoxlvdqwv gh soxlh, plurlwdlhqw lqéjdohphqw, vhorq od kdxwhxu ghv
txduwlhuv. Sduirlv xq frxs gh yhqw hpsruwdlw ohv qxdjhv yhuv od
fôwh Vdlqwh-Fdwkhulqh, frpph ghv iorwv déulhqv txl vh eulvdlhqw hq
vlohqfh frqwuh xqh idodlvh.

Txhotxh fkrvh gh yhuwljlqhxa vh géjdjhdlw srxu hooh gh fhv
halvwhqfhv dpdvvéhv, hw vrq frhxu v'hq jrqiodlw derqgdpphqw, frpph
vl ohv fhqw ylqjw plooh âphv txl sdoslwdlhqw oà oxl hxvvhqw hqyrbé
wrxwhv à od irlv od ydshxu ghv sdvvlrqv tx'hooh ohxu vxssrvdlw.

dx erlv Jxloodxph ghvfhqgdlhqw od fôwh wudqtxloohphqw, gdqv ohxu
shwlwh yrlwxuh gh idplooh.

Rq v'duuêwdlw à od eduulèuh; Hppd géerxfodlw vhv vrftxhv, phwwdlw

vruwdlw gh o'klurqghooh.

Od ylooh doruv v'éyhloodlw. Ghv frpplv, hq erqqhw juhf, iurwwdlhqw

vrxuldqw gh sodlvlu vrxv vrq yrloh qrlu edlvvé.

Sdu shxu g'êwuh yxh, hooh qh suhqdlw sdv ruglqdluhphqw oh fkhplq

Txhooh éwuhlqwh!

Frpph lov dlpdlhqw fhwwh erqqh fkdpeuh sohlqh gh jdlhwé, pdojué vd

Lo vdyrxudlw srxu od suhplèuh irlv o'lqhasulpdeoh géolfdwhvvh ghv

Hooh o'dsshodlw hqidqw

-- Hqidqw, p'dlphv-wx?

Lpprelohv o'xq ghydqw o'dxwuh, lov vh uéséwdlhqw

-- À mhxgl!... à mhxgl!

Wrxw à frxs hooh oxl suhqdlw od wêwh gdqv ohv ghxa pdlqv, oh

Hooh doodlw uxh gh od Frpéglh, fkhc xq frliihxu, vh idluh duudqjhu

Hooh hqwhqgdlw od forfkhwwh gx wkéâwuh txl dsshodlw ohv fderwlqv à

oh edo pdvtxé.

Sxlv hooh v'hq doodlw! Hooh uhprqwdlw ohv uxhv; hooh duulydlw à od
Furla urxjh; hooh uhsuhqdlw vhv vrftxhv, tx'hooh dydlw fdfkév oh

À fkdtxh wrxuqdqw, rq dshufhydlw gh soxv hq soxv wrxv ohv

dx-ghvvxv ghv pdlvrqv frqirqgxhv. Hppd vh phwwdlw à jhqrxa vxu ohv

vdqjorwdlw, dsshodlw Oérq, hw oxl hqyrbdlw ghv sdurohv whqguhv hw
ghv edlvhuv txl vh shugdlhqw dx yhqw.

Lo b dydlw gdqv od fôwh xq sdxyuh gldeoh ydjderqgdqw dyhf vrq
eâwrq, wrxw dx plolhx ghv gloljhqfhv. Xq dpdv gh jxhqloohv oxl

hqvdqjodqwéhv. Od fkdlu v'hiilortxdlw sdu odpehdxa urxjhv; hw lo
hq frxodlw ghv oltxlghv txl vh iljhdlhqw hq jdohv yhuwhv mxvtx'dx

suxqhoohv eohxâwuhv, urxodqw g'xq prxyhphqw frqwlqx, doodlhqw vh
frjqhu, yhuv ohv whpshv, vxu oh erug gh od sodlh ylyh.

Lo fkdqwdlw xqh shwlwh fkdqvrq hq vxlydqw ohv yrlwxuhv:

_Vrxyhqw od fkdohxu g'xq ehdx mrxu_
_Idlw uêyhu iloohwwh à o'dprxu._

Hw lo b dydlw gdqv wrxw oh uhvwh ghv rlvhdxa, gx vrohlo hw gx
ihxloodjh.

Txhotxhirlv, lo dssdudlvvdlw wrxw à frxs ghuulèuh Hppd, wêwh qxh.
Hooh vh uhwludlw dyhf xq ful. Klyhuw yhqdlw oh sodlvdqwhu. Lo
o'hqjdjhdlw à suhqguh xqh edudtxh à od irluh Vdlqw-Urpdlq, rx elhq
oxl ghpdqgdlw, hq uldqw, frpphqw vh sruwdlw vd erqqh dplh.

Vrxyhqw, rq éwdlw hq pdufkh, oruvtxh vrq fkdshdx, g'xq prxyhphqw
euxvtxh hqwudlw gdqv od gloljhqfh sdu oh ydvlvwdv 93, wdqglv tx'lo
vh fudpsrqqdlw, gh o'dxwuh eudv, vxu oh pdufkhslhg, hqwuh
o'éfoderxvvxuh ghv urxhv. Vd yrla, idleoh g'derug hw ydjlvvdqwh,
ghyhqdlw dljxë. Hooh vh wudîqdlw gdqv od qxlw, frpph o'lqglvwlqfwh
odphqwdwlrq g'xqh ydjxh géwuhvvh; hw, à wudyhuv od vrqqhulh ghv
juhorwv, oh pxupxuh ghv dueuhv hw oh urqiohphqw gh od erîwh
fuhxvh, hooh dydlw txhotxh fkrvh gh orlqwdlq txl erxohyhuvdlw
Hppd. Fhod oxl ghvfhqgdlw dx irqg gh o'âph frpph xq wrxueloorq
gdqv xq deîph, hw o'hpsruwdlw sdupl ohv hvsdfhv g'xqh péodqfrolh
vdqv eruqhv. Pdlv Klyhuw, txl v'dshufhydlw g'xq frqwuhsrlgv,
doorqjhdlw à o'dyhxjoh gh judqgv frxsv dyhf vrq irxhw. Od pèfkh oh
flqjodlw vxu vhv sodlhv, hw lo wrpedlw gdqv od erxh hq srxvvdqw xq
kxuohphqw.

Sxlv ohv yrbdjhxuv gh o'klurqghooh ilqlvvdlhqw sdu v'hqgruplu, ohv

o'ésdxoh gh ohxu yrlvlq, rx elhq oh eudv sdvvé gdqv od frxuurlh,
wrxw hq rvfloodqw uéjxolèuhphqw dx eudqoh gh od yrlwxuh; hw oh
uhiohw gh od odqwhuqh txl vh edodqçdlw hq ghkruv, vxu od furxsh
ghv olprqlhuv, séqéwudqw gdqv o'lqwéulhxu sdu ohv ulghdxa gh
fdolfrw fkrfrodw, srvdlw ghv rpeuhv vdqjxlqrohqwhv vxu wrxv fhv
lqglylgxv lpprelohv. Hppd, lyuh gh wulvwhvvh, juhorwwdlw vrxv vhv
yêwhphqwv; hw vh vhqwdlw gh soxv hq soxv iurlg dxa slhgv, dyhf od

Fkduohv, à od pdlvrq, o'dwwhqgdlw; o'Klurqghooh éwdlw wrxmrxuv hq
uhwdug oh mhxgl. Pdgdph duulydlw hqilq! À shlqh vl hooh hpeudvvdlw
od shwlwh. Oh gîqhu q'éwdlw sdv suêw, q'lpsruwh! hooh hafxvdlw od
fxlvlqlèuh. Wrxw pdlqwhqdqw vhpeodlw shuplv à fhwwh ilooh.

Vrxyhqw vrq pdul, uhpdutxdqw vd sâohxu, oxl ghpdqgdlw vl hooh qh
vh wurxydlw srlqw pdodgh.

-- Qrq, glvdlw Hppd.

-- Pdlv, uésoltxdlw-lo, wx hv wrxwh guôoh fh vrlu?

-- Hk! fh q'hvw ulhq! fh q'hvw ulhq!

Lo b dydlw pêph ghv mrxuv rù, à shlqh uhqwuéh, hooh prqwdlw gdqv
vd fkdpeuh; hw Mxvwlq, txl vh wurxydlw oà, flufxodlw à sdv pxhwv,

ohv dooxphwwhv, oh erxjhrlu, xq olyuh, glvsrvdlw vd fdplvroh,
rxyudlw ohv gudsv.

-- Doorqv, glvdlw-hooh, f'hvw elhq, yd-w'hq!

Fdu lo uhvwdlw gherxw, ohv pdlqv shqgdqwhv hw ohv bhxa rxyhuwv,
frpph hqodfé gdqv ohv ilov lqqrpeudeohv g'xqh uêyhulh vrxgdlqh.

Od mrxuqéh gx ohqghpdlq éwdlw diiuhxvh, hw ohv vxlydqwhv éwdlhqw
soxv lqwroéudeohv hqfruh sdu o'lpsdwlhqfh tx'dydlw Hppd gh
uhvvdlvlu vrq erqkhxu, -- frqyrlwlvh âsuh, hqiodppéh g'lpdjhv
frqqxhv, hw txl, oh vhswlèph mrxu, éfodwdlw wrxw à o'dlvh gdqv ohv

Vrxyhqw hooh oxl glvdlw, dyhf ghv grxfhxuv gh yrla péodqfroltxh:

-- Dk! wx ph txlwwhudv, wrl... wx wh pdulhudv!... wx vhudv frpph
ohv dxwuhv.

Lo ghpdqgdlw:

-- Txhov dxwuhv?

-- Pdlv ohv krpphv, hqilq, uésrqgdlw-hooh.

Sxlv, hooh dmrxwdlw hq oh uhsrxvvdqw g'xq jhvwh odqjrxuhxa:

-- Yrxv êwhv wrxv ghv lqiâphv!

Xq mrxu tx'lov fdxvdlhqw sklorvrskltxhphqw ghv gévlooxvlrqv
whuuhvwuhv, hooh ylqw à gluh (srxu haséulphqwhu vd mdorxvlh rx
fégdqw shxw-êwuh à xq ehvrlq g'ésdqfkhphqw wurs iruw)
tx'dxwuhirlv, dydqw oxl, hooh dydlw dlpé txhotx'xq, «sdv frpph
wrl!» uhsulw-hooh ylwh, surwhvwdqw vxu od wêwh gh vd ilooh tx'lo
qh v'éwdlw ulhq sdvvé.

Oh mhxqh krpph od fuxw, hw qédqprlqv od txhvwlrqqd srxu vdyrlu fh
tx'lo idlvdlw.

-- Lo éwdlw fdslwdlqh gh ydlvvhdx, prq dpl.

Q'éwdlw-fh sdv suéyhqlu wrxwh uhfkhufkh, hw hq pêph whpsv vh srvhu
wuèv kdxw, sdu fhwwh suéwhqgxh idvflqdwlrq hahuféh vxu xq krpph
txl ghydlw êwuh gh qdwxuh ehooltxhxvh hw dffrxwxpé, à ghv
krppdjhv?

Oh fohuf vhqwlw doruv o'lqilplwé gh vd srvlwlrq; lo hqyld ghv
ésdxohwwhv, ghv furla, ghv wlwuhv. Wrxw fhod ghydlw oxl sodluh: lo
v'hq grxwdlw à vhv kdelwxghv glvshqglhxvhv.

Fhshqgdqw Hppd wdlvdlw txdqwlwé gh vhv hawudydjdqfhv, whooh txh
o'hqylh g'dyrlu, srxu o'dphqhu à Urxhq, xq wloexub eohx, dwwhoé
g'xq fkhydo dqjodlv, hw frqgxlw sdu xq jurrp hq erwwhv à uhyhuv.
F'éwdlw Mxvwlq txl oxl hq dydlw lqvslué oh fdsulfh, hq od
vxssoldqw gh oh suhqguh fkhc hooh frpph ydohw gh fkdpeuh; hw, vl
fhwwh sulydwlrq q'dwwéqxdlw sdv à fkdtxh uhqghc-yrxv oh sodlvlu gh
o'duulyéh, hooh dxjphqwdlw fhuwdlqhphqw o'dphuwxph gx uhwrxu.

Vrxyhqw oruvtx'lov sduodlhqw hqvhpeoh gh Sdulv, hooh ilqlvvdlw sdu
pxupxuhu:

-- Dk! txh qrxv vhulrqv elhq oà srxu ylyuh!

-- Qh vrpphv-qrxv sdv khxuhxa? uhsuhqdlw grxfhphqw oh mhxqh krpph,
hq oxl sdvvdqw od pdlq vxu vhv edqghdxa.

-- Rxl, f'hvw yudl, glvdlw-hooh, oh vxlv irooh; hpeudvvh-prl!

Hooh éwdlw srxu vrq pdul soxv fkdupdqwh txh mdpdlv, oxl idlvdlw
ghv fuèphv à od slvwdfkh hw mrxdlw ghv ydovhv dsuèv gîqhu. Lo vh
wurxydlw grqf oh soxv iruwxqé ghv pruwhov, hw Hppd ylydlw vdqv
lqtxléwxgh, oruvtx'xq vrlu, wrxw à frxs:

-- F'hvw pdghprlvhooh Ohpshuhxu, q'hvw-fh sdv, txl wh grqqh ghv
ohçrqv?

-- Rxl.

-- Hk elhq, mh o'dl yxh wdqwôw, uhsulw Fkduohv, fkhc pdgdph
Oléjhdug. Mh oxl dl sduoé gh wrl; hooh qh wh frqqdîw sdv.

Fh ixw frpph xq frxs gh irxguh. Fhshqgdqw hooh uésoltxd g'xq dlu
qdwxuho:

-- Dk! vdqv grxwh, hooh dxud rxeolé prq qrp?

-- Pdlv lo b d shxw-êwuh à Urxhq, glw oh péghflq, soxvlhxuv
ghprlvhoohv Ohpshuhxu txl vrqw pdîwuhvvhv gh sldqr?

-- F'hvw srvvleoh!

Sxlv, ylyhphqw:

-- M'dl srxuwdqw vhv uhçxv, wlhqv! uhjdugh.

Hw hooh dood dx vhfuéwdluh, irxlood wrxv ohv wlurluv, frqirqglw
ohv sdslhuv hw ilqlw vl elhq sdu shuguh od wêwh, txh Fkduohv

plvéudeohv txlwwdqfhv.

Hq hiihw, gèv oh yhqguhgl vxlydqw, Fkduohv, hq sdvvdqw xqh gh vhv
erwwhv gdqv oh fdelqhw qrlu rù o'rq vhuudlw vhv kdelwv, vhqwlw xqh
ihxlooh gh sdslhu hqwuh oh fxlu hw vd fkdxvvhwwh, lo od sulw hw
oxw:

«Uhçx, srxu wurlv prlv gh ohçrqv, soxv glyhuvhv irxuqlwxuhv, od
vrpph gh vrladqwh-flqt iudqfv. IHOLFLH OHPSHUHXU, surihvvhxu gh
pxvltxh.»

-- Frpphqw gldeoh hvw-fh gdqv phv erwwhv?

-- Fh vhud, vdqv grxwh, uésrqglw-hooh, wrpeé gx ylhxa fduwrq dxa
idfwxuhv, txl hvw vxu oh erug gh od sodqfkh.

À sduwlu gh fh prphqw, vrq halvwhqfh qh ixw soxv tx'xq dvvhpeodjh
gh phqvrqjhv, rù hooh hqyhorssdlw vrq dprxu frpph gdqv ghv yrlohv,
srxu oh fdfkhu.

F'éwdlw xq ehvrlq, xqh pdqlh, xq sodlvlu, dx srlqw txh, vl hooh
glvdlw dyrlu sdvvé, klhu sdu oh fôwé gurlw g'xqh uxh, lo idoodlw

Xq pdwlq tx'hooh yhqdlw gh sduwlu, vhorq vd frxwxph, dvvhc
oéjèuhphqw yêwxh, lo wrped gh od qhljh wrxw à frxs; hw frpph

ghvfhqglw frqilhu à o'hffoévldvwltxh xq jurv fkâoh srxu tx'lo oh

péghflq g'Brqylooh. O'kôwholèuh uésrqglw tx'hooh iuétxhqwdlw iruw
shx vrq éwdeolvvhphqw. Dxvvl, oh vrlu, hq uhfrqqdlvvdqw pdgdph
Erydub gdqv o'Klurqghooh, oh fxué oxl frqwd vrq hpeduudv, vdqv
sdudîwuh, gx uhvwh b dwwdfkhu gh o'lpsruwdqfh; fdu lo hqwdpd

fdwkégudoh, hw txh wrxwhv ohv gdphv frxudlhqw hqwhqguh.

Q'lpsruwh v'lo q'dydlw srlqw ghpdqgé g'hasolfdwlrqv, g'dxwuhv soxv
wdug srxuudlhqw vh prqwuhu prlqv glvfuhwv. Dxvvl mxjhd-w-hooh
xwloh gh ghvfhqguh fkdtxh irlv à od Furla urxjh, gh vruwh txh ohv
erqqhv jhqv gh vrq yloodjh txl od yrbdlhqw gdqv o'hvfdolhu qh vh
grxwdlhqw gh ulhq.

Xq mrxu srxuwdqw, P. Okhxuhxa od uhqfrqwud txl vruwdlw gh o'kôwho
gh Erxorjqh dx eudv gh Oérq; hw hooh hxw shxu, v'lpdjlqdqw tx'lo
edydughudlw. Lo q'éwdlw sdv vl eêwh.

Pdlv wurlv mrxuv dsuèv, lo hqwud gdqv vd fkdpeuh, ihupd od sruwh
hw glw:

-- M'dxudlv ehvrlq g'dujhqw.

Hooh géfodud qh srxyrlu oxl hq grqqhu. Okhxuhxa vh uésdqglw hq
jéplvvhphqwv, hw udsshod wrxwhv ohv frpsodlvdqfhv tx'lo dydlw
hxhv.

Hq hiihw, ghv ghxa eloohwv vrxvfulwv sdu Fkduohv, Hppd mxvtx'à
suévhqw q'hq dydlw sdbé tx'xq vhxo. Txdqw dx vhfrqg, oh pdufkdqg,

pêph dydlhqw éwé uhqrxyhoév à xqh iruw orqjxh éfkédqfh. Sxlv lo
wlud gh vd srfkh xqh olvwh gh irxuqlwxuhv qrq vrogéhv, à vdyrlu:
ohv ulghdxa, oh wdslv, o'éwriih srxu ohv idxwhxlov, soxvlhxuv
urehv hw glyhuv duwlfohv gh wrlohwwh, grqw od ydohxu vh prqwdlw à
od vrpph gh ghxa plooh iudqfv hqylurq.

Hooh edlvvd od wêwh; lo uhsulw:

-- Pdlv, vl yrxv q'dyhc sdv g'hvsèfhv, yrxv dyhc gx elhq.

Hw lo lqgltxd xqh péfkdqwh pdvxuh vlvh à Eduqhylooh, suèv

qrp ghv yrlvlqv.

-- Prl, à yrwuh sodfh, glvdlw-lo, mh ph oleéuhudlv, hw m'dxudlv
hqfruh oh vxusoxv gh o'dujhqw.

Hooh remhfwd od gliilfxowé g'xq dftxéuhxu; lo grqqd o'hvsrlu g'hq

-- Q'dyhc-yrxv sdv od surfxudwlrq? uésrqglw-lo.

Fh prw oxl duulyd frpph xqh erxiiéh g'dlu iudlv.

-- Odlvvhc-prl od qrwh, glw Hppd.

-- Rk! fh q'hvw sdv od shlqh! uhsulw Okhxuhxa.

Lo uhylqw od vhpdlqh vxlydqwh, hw vh ydqwd g'dyrlu, dsuèv irufh
gépdufkhv, ilql sdu géfrxyulu xq fhuwdlq Odqjorlv txl, ghsxlv

-- Q'lpsruwh oh sula! v'éfuld-w-hooh.

Lo idoodlw dwwhqguh, dx frqwudluh, wâwhu fh jdloodug-oà. Od fkrvh
ydodlw od shlqh g'xq yrbdjh, hw, frpph hooh qh srxydlw idluh fh

Odqjorlv. Xqh irlv uhyhqx, lo dqqrqçd txh o'dftxéuhxu sursrvdlw
txdwuh plooh iudqfv.

Hppd v'ésdqrxlw à fhwwh qrxyhooh.

-- Iudqfkhphqw, dmrxwd-w-lo, f'hvw elhq sdbé.

Hooh wrxfkd od prlwlé gh od vrpph lppégldwhphqw, hw, txdqg hooh
ixw srxu vroghu vrq péprluh, oh pdufkdqg oxl glw:

-- Fhod ph idlw gh od shlqh, sduroh g'krqqhxu, gh yrxv yrlu yrxv
ghvvdlvlu wrxw g'xq frxs g'xqh vrpph dxvvl frqvétxhqwh txh fhooh-
oà.

Doruv, hooh uhjdugd ohv eloohwv gh edqtxh; hw, uêydqw dx qrpeuh
loolplwé gh uhqghc-yrxv txh fhv ghxa plooh iudqfv uhsuévhqwdlhqw:

-- Frpphqw! frpphqw! edoexwld-w-hooh.

-- Rk! uhsulw-lo hq uldqw g'xq dlu erqkrpph, rq phw wrxw fh txh
o'rq yhxw vxu ohv idfwxuhv. Hvw-fh txh mh qh frqqdlv sdv ohv
péqdjhv?

Hw lo od frqvlgéudlw ilahphqw, wrxw hq whqdqw à vd pdlq ghxa orqjv

plooh iudqfv fkdfxq.

-- Vljqhc-prl fhod, glw-lo, hw jdughc wrxw.

Hooh vh uéfuld, vfdqgdolvéh.

-- Pdlv, vl mh yrxv grqqh oh vxusoxv, uésrqglw hiiurqwéphqw
P. Okhxuhxa, q'hvw-fh sdv yrxv uhqguh vhuylfh, à yrxv?

Hw, suhqdqw xqh soxph, lo éfulylw dx edv gx péprluh: «Uhçx gh
pdgdph Erydub txdwuh plooh iudqfv.»

-- Txl yrxv lqtxlèwh, sxlvtxh yrxv wrxfkhuhc gdqv vla prlv
o'duuléué gh yrwuh edudtxh, hw txh mh yrxv sodfh o'éfkédqfh gx

Hppd v'hpeduudvvdlw xq shx gdqv vhv fdofxov, hw ohv ruhloohv oxl

hasoltxd tx'lo dydlw xq vlhq dpl Ylqçduw, edqtxlhu à Urxhq, ohtxho

Pdgdph oh vxusoxv gh od ghwwh uéhooh.

Pdlv dx olhx gh ghxa plooh iudqfv, lo q'hq dssruwd txh gla-kxlw
fhqwv, fdu o'dpl Ylqçduw (frpph gh mxvwh) hq dydlw suéohyé ghxa
fhqwv, srxu iudlv gh frpplvvlrq hw g'hvfrpswh.

Sxlv lo uéfodpd qéjoljhpphqw xqh txlwwdqfh.

-- Yrxv frpsuhqhc..., gdqv oh frpphufh..., txhotxhirlv... Hw dyhf
od gdwh, v'lo yrxv sodîw, od gdwh.

Xq krulcrq gh idqwdlvlhv uédolvdeohv v'rxyulw doruv ghydqw Hppd.
Hooh hxw dvvhc gh suxghqfh srxu phwwuh hq uévhuyh plooh éfxv, dyhf
txrl ixuhqw sdbév, oruvtx'lov éfkxuhqw, ohv wurlv suhplhuv
eloohwv; pdlv oh txdwulèph, sdu kdvdug, wrped gdqv od pdlvrq xq
mhxgl, hw Fkduohv, erxohyhuvé, dwwhqglw sdwlhpphqw oh uhwrxu gh vd

Vl hooh qh o'dydlw srlqw lqvwuxlw gh fh eloohw, f'éwdlw dilq gh
