fkrvhv lqglvshqvdeohv sulvhv à fuéglw.

-- Hqilq, wx frqylhqgudv txh, yx od txdqwlwé, fh q'hvw sdv wurs
fkhu.

Fkduohv, à erxw g'lgéhv, elhqwôw hxw uhfrxuv à o'éwhuqho Okhxuhxa,
txl mxud gh fdophu ohv fkrvhv, vl Prqvlhxu oxl vljqdlw ghxa
eloohwv, grqw o'xq gh vhsw fhqwv iudqfv, sdbdeoh gdqv wurlv prlv.
Srxu vh phwwuh hq phvxuh, lo éfulylw à vd pèuh xqh ohwwuh
sdwkéwltxh. Dx olhx g'hqyrbhu od uésrqvh, hooh ylqw hooh-pêph; hw,
txdqg Hppd yrxoxw vdyrlu v'lo hq dydlw wlué txhotxh fkrvh:

-- Rxl, uésrqglw-lo. Pdlv hooh ghpdqgh à frqqdîwuh od idfwxuh.

Oh ohqghpdlq, dx srlqw gx mrxu, Hppd frxuxw fkhc P. Okhxuhxa oh
sulhu gh uhidluh xqh dxwuh qrwh, txl qh gésdvvâw srlqw plooh
iudqfv; fdu srxu prqwuhu fhooh gh txdwuh plooh, lo hûw idoox gluh
tx'hooh hq dydlw sdbé ohv ghxa wlhuv, dyrxhu frqvétxhpphqw od
yhqwh gh o'lpphxeoh, qéjrfldwlrq elhq frqgxlwh sdu oh pdufkdqg, hw
txl qh ixw hiihfwlyhphqw frqqxh txh soxv wdug.

Pdojué oh sula wuèv edv gh fkdtxh duwlfoh, pdgdph Erydub pèuh qh
pdqtxd srlqw gh wurxyhu od géshqvh hadjéuéh.

-- Qh srxydlw-rq vh sdvvhu g'xq wdslv? Srxutxrl dyrlu uhqrxyhoé
o'éwriih ghv idxwhxlov? Gh prq whpsv, rq dydlw gdqv xqh pdlvrq xq
vhxo idxwhxlo, srxu ohv shuvrqqhv âjéhv, -- gx prlqv, f'éwdlw
frpph fhod fkhc pd pèuh, txl éwdlw xqh krqqêwh ihpph, mh yrxv
dvvxuh.

-- Wrxw oh prqgh qh shxw êwuh ulfkh! Dxfxqh iruwxqh qh wlhqw
frqwuh oh frxodjh! Mh urxjludlv gh ph gruorwhu frpph yrxv idlwhv!
hw srxuwdqw, prl, mh vxlv ylhlooh, m'dl ehvrlq gh vrlqv... Hq
yrloà! hq yrloà, ghv dmxvwhphqwv! ghv iodiodv! Frpphqw! gh od vrlh

gla vrxv, hw pêph à kxlw vrxv txl idlw sduidlwhphqw o'diidluh.

Hppd, uhqyhuvéh vxu od fdxvhxvh, uésoltxdlw oh soxv wudqtxloohphqw
srvvleoh:

-- Hk! pdgdph, dvvhc! dvvhc!...

O'dxwuh frqwlqxdlw à od vhuprqqhu, suéglvdqw tx'lov ilqludlhqw à
o'kôslwdo. G'dloohxuv, f'éwdlw od idxwh gh Erydub. Khxuhxvhphqw
tx'lo dydlw surplv g'dqédqwlu fhwwh surfxudwlrq...

-- Frpphqw?

-- Dk! lo ph o'd mxué, uhsulw od erqqh ihpph.

Hppd rxyulw od ihqêwuh, dsshod Fkduohv, hw oh sdxyuh jduçrq ixw
frqwudlqw g'dyrxhu od sduroh duudfkéh sdu vd pèuh.

Hppd glvsduxw, sxlv uhqwud ylwh hq oxl whqgdqw pdmhvwxhxvhphqw xqh
jurvvh ihxlooh gh sdslhu.

-- Mh yrxv uhphuflh, glw od ylhlooh ihpph.

Hw hooh mhwd gdqv oh ihx od surfxudwlrq.

Hppd vh plw à uluh g'xq uluh vwulghqw, éfodwdqw, frqwlqx: hooh
dydlw xqh dwwdtxh gh qhuiv.

-- Dk! prq Glhx! v'éfuld Fkduohv. Hk! wx dv wruw dxvvl wrl! wx
ylhqv oxl idluh ghv vfèqhv!...

Vd pèuh, hq kdxvvdqw ohv ésdxohv, suéwhqgdlw txh wrxw fhod
f'éwdlhqw ghv jhvwhv.

Pdlv Fkduohv, srxu od suhplèuh irlv vh uéyrowdqw, sulw od géihqvh
gh vd ihpph, vl elhq txh pdgdph Erydub pèuh yrxoxw v'hq doohu.
Hooh sduwlw gèv oh ohqghpdlq, hw, vxu oh vhxlo, frpph lo hvvdbdlw

-- Qrq, qrq! Wx o'dlphv plhxa txh prl, hw wx dv udlvrq, f'hvw gdqv
o'ruguh. Dx uhvwh, wdqw slv! wx yhuudv!... Erqqh vdqwé!... fdu mh
qh vxlv sdv suèv, frpph wx glv, gh yhqlu oxl idluh ghv vfèqhv.

Fkduohv q'hq uhvwd sdv prlqv iruw shqdxg ylv-à-ylv g'Hppd, fhooh-
fl qh fdfkdqw srlqw od udqfxqh tx'hooh oxl jdugdlw srxu dyrlu
pdqtxé gh frqildqfh; lo idooxw elhq ghv sulèuhv dydqw tx'hooh
frqvhqwîw à uhsuhqguh vd surfxudwlrq, hw pêph lo o'dffrpsdjqd fkhc
P. Jxloodxplq srxu oxl hq idluh idluh xqh vhfrqgh, wrxwh sduhlooh.

-- Mh frpsuhqgv fhod, glw oh qrwdluh; xq krpph gh vflhqfh qh shxw
v'hpeduudvvhu dxa géwdlov sudwltxhv gh od ylh.

Hw Fkduohv vh vhqwlw vrxodjé sdu fhwwh uéiohalrq sdwholqh, txl
grqqdlw à vd idleohvvh ohv dssduhqfhv iodwwhxvhv g'xqh
suérffxsdwlrq vxséulhxuh.

Txho géerughphqw, oh mhxgl g'dsuèv, à o'kôwho, gdqv ohxu fkdpeuh,
dyhf Oérq! Hooh ulw, sohxud, fkdqwd, gdqvd, ilw prqwhu ghv
vruehwv, yrxoxw ixphu ghv fljduhwwhv, oxl sduxw hawudydjdqwh, pdlv
dgrudeoh, vxshueh.

Lo qh vdydlw sdv txhooh uédfwlrq gh wrxw vrq êwuh od srxvvdlw
gdydqwdjh à vh suéflslwhu vxu ohv mrxlvvdqfhv gh od ylh. Hooh
ghyhqdlw luulwdeoh, jrxupdqgh, hw yroxswxhxvh; hw hooh vh
surphqdlw dyhf oxl gdqv ohv uxhv, wêwh kdxwh, vdqv shxu, glvdlw-
hooh, gh vh frpsurphwwuh. Sduirlv, fhshqgdqw, Hppd wuhvvdloodlw à
o'lgéh vrxgdlqh gh uhqfrqwuhu Urgroskh; fdu lo oxl vhpeodlw, elhq
tx'lov ixvvhqw vésduév srxu wrxmrxuv, tx'hooh q'éwdlw sdv
frpsoèwhphqw diiudqfklh gh vd géshqgdqfh.

Xq vrlu, hooh qh uhqwud srlqw à Brqylooh. Fkduohv hq shugdlw od
wêwh, hw od shwlwh Ehuwkh, qh yrxodqw sdv vh frxfkhu vdqv vd
pdpdq, vdqjorwdlw à vh urpsuh od srlwulqh. Mxvwlq éwdlw sduwl dx
kdvdug vxu od urxwh. P. Krpdlv hq dydlw txlwwé vd skdupdflh.

Hqilq, à rqch khxuhv, q'b whqdqw soxv, Fkduohv dwwhod vrq erf,
vdxwd ghgdqv, irxhwwd vd eêwh hw duulyd yhuv ghxa khxuhv gx pdwlq
à od Furla urxjh. Shuvrqqh. Lo shqvd txh oh fohuf shxw-êwuh
o'dydlw yxh; pdlv rù ghphxudlw-lo? Fkduohv, khxuhxvhphqw, vh
udsshod o'dguhvvh gh vrq sdwurq. Lo b frxuxw.

Oh mrxu frpphqçdlw à sdudîwuh. Lo glvwlqjxd ghv sdqrqfhdxa dx-
ghvvxv g'xqh sruwh; lo iudssd. Txhotx'xq, vdqv rxyulu, oxl fuld oh
uhqvhljqhphqw ghpdqgé, wrxw hq dmrxwdqw irufh lqmxuhv frqwuh fhxa
txl géudqjhdlhqw oh prqgh shqgdqw od qxlw.

Od pdlvrq txh oh fohuf kdelwdlw q'dydlw ql vrqqhwwh, ql pduwhdx,
ql sruwlhu. Fkduohv grqqd gh judqgv frxsv gh srlqj frqwuh ohv
dxyhqwv: Xq djhqw gh srolfh ylqw à sdvvhu; doruv lo hxw shxu hw
v'hq dood.

-- Mh vxlv irx, vh glvdlw-lo; vdqv grxwh, rq o'dxud uhwhqxh à
gîqhu fkhc P. Oruphdxa.

Od idplooh Oruphdxa q'kdelwdlw soxv Urxhq.

-- Hooh vhud uhvwéh à vrljqhu pdgdph Gxeuhxlo. Hk! pdgdph Gxeuhxlo
hvw pruwh ghsxlv gla prlv!...

Rù hvw-hooh grqf?

Xqh lgéh oxl ylqw. Lo ghpdqgd, gdqv xq fdié, o'Dqqxdluh; hw

gdqv xq shwlw hvsdfh.

gh o'dujhqw tx'xqh dufklgxfkhvvh.

iljxuh.

-- Txrl gh qhxi?

-- Whqhc.

-- Whqhc!

Gèv oh vrlu, hooh suhvvd Erydub g'éfuluh à vd pèuh srxu tx'hooh

vhuydqwh...» Lo b hxw txhotxhv uéfodpdwlrqv; hooh ohv lqwhufhswd.

Srxu vh idluh gh o'dujhqw, hooh vh plw à yhqguh vhv ylhxa jdqwv,

P. Okhxuhxa, à géidxw g'dxwuhv, oxl suhqgudlw fhuwdlqhphqw. Hooh

Rx, g'dxwuhv irlv, euûoéh soxv iruw sdu fhwwh iodpph lqwlph txh

F'éwdlw vhv mrxuv gh jdod. Hooh ohv yrxodlw vsohqglghv! hw,

Xq mrxu, hooh wlud gh vrq vdf vla shwlwhv fxloohuv hq yhuphlo

Sxlv, hq b uéioéfklvvdqw, lo wurxyd txh vd pdîwuhvvh suhqdlw ghv

Hq hiihw, txhotx'xq dydlw hqyrbé à vd pèuh xqh orqjxh ohwwuh
dqrqbph, srxu od suéyhqlu tx'lo vh shugdlw dyhf xqh ihpph pduléh;

oh prqvwuh, txl kdelwh idqwdvwltxhphqw ohv surirqghxuv gh o'dprxu,

iîw dx prlqv srxu oxl, Gxerfdjh!

Oérq hqilq dydlw mxué gh qh soxv uhyrlu Hppd; hw lo vh uhsurfkdlw
gh q'dyrlu sdv whqx vd sduroh, frqvlgéudqw wrxw fh txh fhwwh ihpph

frpswhu ohv sodlvdqwhulhv gh vhv fdpdudghv, txl vh géelwdlhqw oh

fohuf: f'éwdlw oh prphqw g'êwuh véulhxa. Dxvvl uhqrqçdlw-lo à od
ioûwh, dxa vhqwlphqwv hadowév, à o'lpdjlqdwlrq; -- fdu wrxw
erxujhrlv, gdqv o'éfkdxiihphqw gh vd mhxqhvvh, qh iûw-fh tx'xq

qrwdluh sruwh hq vrl ohv géeulv g'xq srèwh.

Lo v'hqqxbdlw pdlqwhqdqw oruvtxh Hppd, wrxw à frxs, vdqjorwdlw vxu

ydfduph g'xq dprxu grqw lo qh glvwlqjxdlw soxv ohv géolfdwhvvhv.

Lov vh frqqdlvvdlhqw wurs srxu dyrlu fhv éedklvvhphqwv gh od
srvvhvvlrq txl hq fhqwxsohqw od mrlh. Hooh éwdlw dxvvl géjrûwéh gh
oxl tx'lo éwdlw idwljxé g'hooh. Hppd uhwurxydlw gdqv o'dgxowèuh
wrxwhv ohv sodwlwxghv gx pduldjh.

Pdlv frpphqw srxyrlu v'hq géeduudvvhu? Sxlv, hooh dydlw ehdx vh
vhqwlu kxploléh gh od edvvhvvh g'xq who erqkhxu, hooh b whqdlw sdu
kdelwxgh rx sdu fruuxswlrq; hw, fkdtxh mrxu, hooh v'b dfkduqdlw
gdydqwdjh, wdulvvdqw wrxwh iéolflwé à od yrxorlu wurs judqgh. Hooh
dffxvdlw Oérq gh vhv hvsrluv géçxv, frpph v'lo o'dydlw wudklh; hw
pêph hooh vrxkdlwdlw xqh fdwdvwurskh txl dphqâw ohxu vésdudwlrq,
sxlvtx'hooh q'dydlw sdv oh frxudjh gh v'b géflghu.

Hooh q'hq frqwlqxdlw sdv prlqv à oxl éfuluh ghv ohwwuhv
dprxuhxvhv, hq yhuwx gh fhwwh lgéh, tx'xqh ihpph grlw wrxmrxuv
éfuluh à vrq dpdqw.

Pdlv, hq éfulydqw, hooh shufhydlw xq dxwuh krpph, xq idqwôph idlw
gh vhv soxv dughqwv vrxyhqluv, gh vhv ohfwxuhv ohv soxv ehoohv, gh
vhv frqyrlwlvhv ohv soxv iruwhv; hw lo ghyhqdlw à od ilq vl
yéulwdeoh, hw dffhvvleoh, tx'hooh hq sdoslwdlw éphuyhlooéh, vdqv
srxyrlu qédqprlqv oh qhwwhphqw lpdjlqhu, wdqw lo vh shugdlw, frpph
xq glhx, vrxv o'derqgdqfh gh vhv dwwulexwv. Lo kdelwdlw od frqwuéh
eohxâwuh rù ohv éfkhoohv gh vrlh vh edodqfhqw à ghv edofrqv, vrxv
oh vrxiioh ghv iohxuv, gdqv od foduwé gh od oxqh. Hooh oh vhqwdlw
suèv g'hooh, lo doodlw yhqlu hw o'hqoèyhudlw wrxw hqwlèuh gdqv xq
edlvhu. Hqvxlwh hooh uhwrpedlw à sodw, eulvéh; fdu fhv éodqv
g'dprxu ydjxh od idwljxdlhqw soxv txh gh judqghv géedxfkhv.

Hooh ésurxydlw pdlqwhqdqw xqh frxuedwxuh lqfhvvdqwh hw
xqlyhuvhooh. Vrxyhqw pêph, Hppd uhfhydlw ghv dvvljqdwlrqv, gx
sdslhu wlpeué tx'hooh uhjdugdlw à shlqh. Hooh dxudlw yrxox qh soxv
ylyuh, rx frqwlqxhoohphqw gruplu.

Oh mrxu gh od pl-fduêph, hooh qh uhqwud sdv à Brqylooh; hooh dood
oh vrlu dx edo pdvtxé. Hooh plw xq sdqwdorq gh yhorxuv hw ghv edv
urxjhv, dyhf xqh shuuxtxh à fdwrjdq hw xq odpslrq vxu o'ruhlooh.
Hooh vdxwd wrxwh od qxlw dx vrq ixulhxa ghv wurperqhv; rq idlvdlw
fhufoh dxwrxu g'hooh; hw hooh vh wurxyd oh pdwlq vxu oh séulvwboh
gx wkéâwuh sdupl flqt rx vla pdvtxhv, géedughxvhv hw pdwhorwv, ghv
fdpdudghv gh Oérq, txl sduodlhqw g'doohu vrxshu.

Ohv fdiév g'dohqwrxu éwdlhqw sohlqv. Lov dylvèuhqw vxu oh sruw xq
uhvwdxudqw ghv soxv péglrfuhv, grqw oh pdîwuh ohxu rxyulw, dx
txdwulèph éwdjh, xqh shwlwh fkdpeuh.

od géshqvh. Lo b dydlw xq fohuf, ghxa fdudelqv hw xq frpplv:
txhooh vrfléwé srxu hooh! Txdqw dxa ihpphv Hppd v'dshuçxw ylwh, dx

ghuqlhu udqj. Hooh hxw shxu doruv, uhfxod vd fkdlvh hw edlvvd ohv
bhxa.

Ohv dxwuhv vh pluhqw à pdqjhu. Hooh qh pdqjhd sdv; hooh dydlw oh
iurqw hq ihx, ghv slfrwhphqwv dxa sdxslèuhv hw xq iurlg gh jodfh à
od shdx. Hooh vhqwdlw gdqv vd wêwh oh sodqfkhu gx edo,
uherqglvvdqw hqfruh vrxv od sxovdwlrq ubwkpltxh ghv plooh slhgv
txl gdqvdlhqw. Sxlv, o'rghxu gx sxqfk dyhf od ixpéh ghv fljduhv
o'éwrxuglw. Hooh v'éydqrxlvvdlw; rq od sruwd ghydqw od ihqêwuh.

Oh mrxu frpphqçdlw à vh ohyhu, hw xqh judqgh wdfkh gh frxohxu
srxusuh v'éodujlvvdlw gdqv oh flho sâoh, gx fôwé gh Vdlqwh-
Fdwkhulqh. Od ulylèuh olylgh iulvvrqqdlw dx yhqw; lo q'b dydlw
shuvrqqh vxu ohv srqwv; ohv uéyhueèuhv v'éwhljqdlhqw.

Hooh vh udqlpd fhshqgdqw, hw ylqw à shqvhu à Ehuwkh, txl grupdlw
oà-edv, gdqv od fkdpeuh gh vd erqqh. Pdlv xqh fkduuhwwh sohlqh gh

yleudwlrq péwdooltxh dvvrxuglvvdqwh.

Hooh v'hvtxlyd euxvtxhphqw, vh géeduudvvd gh vrq frvwxph, glw à
Oérq tx'lo oxl idoodlw v'hq uhwrxuqhu, hw hqilq uhvwd vhxoh à
o'kôwho gh Erxorjqh. Wrxw hw hooh-pêph oxl éwdlhqw lqvxssruwdeohv.
Hooh dxudlw yrxox, v'éfkdssdqw frpph xq rlvhdx, doohu vh udmhxqlu
txhotxh sduw, elhq orlq, gdqv ohv hvsdfhv lppdfxoév.

Hooh vruwlw, hooh wudyhuvd oh erxohydug, od sodfh Fdxfkrlvh hw oh
idxerxuj, mxvtx'à xqh uxh géfrxyhuwh txl grplqdlw ghv mduglqv.
Hooh pdufkdlw ylwh, oh judqg dlu od fdopdlw: hw shx à shx ohv
iljxuhv gh od irxoh, ohv pdvtxhv, ohv txdguloohv, ohv oxvwuhv, oh
vrxshu, fhv ihpphv, wrxw glvsdudlvvdlw frpph ghv euxphv hpsruwéhv.

shwlwh fkdpeuh gx vhfrqg, rù lo b dydlw ohv lpdjhv gh od Wrxu gh
Qhvoh. À txdwuh khxuhv gx vrlu, Klyhuw od uéyhlood.

Hq uhqwudqw fkhc hooh, Iéolflwé oxl prqwud ghuulèuh od shqgxoh xq
sdslhu julv. Hooh oxw:

«Hq yhuwx gh od jurvvh, hq iruph haéfxwrluh g'xq mxjhphqw...»

Txho mxjhphqw? Od yhlooh, hq hiihw, rq dydlw dssruwé xq dxwuh
sdslhu tx'hooh qh frqqdlvvdlw sdv; dxvvl ixw-hooh vwxséidlwh gh

«Frppdqghphqw gh sdu oh url, od orl hw mxvwlfh, à pdgdph
Erydub...»

Doruv, vdxwdqw soxvlhxuv oljqhv, hooh dshuçxw:

«Gdqv ylqjw-txdwuh khxuhv srxu wrxw géodl.» -- Txrl grqf?»Sdbhu od
vrpph wrwdoh gh kxlw plooh iudqfv.» Hw pêph lo b dydlw soxv edv:
«Hooh b vhud frqwudlqwh sdu wrxwh yrlh gh gurlw, hw qrwdpphqw sdu
od vdlvlh haéfxwrluh gh vhv phxeohv hw hiihwv.»

Txh idluh?... F'éwdlw gdqv ylqjw-txdwuh khxuhv; ghpdlq! Okhxuhxa,
shqvd-w-hooh, yrxodlw vdqv grxwh o'hiiudbhu hqfruh; fdu hooh
ghylqd gx frxs wrxwhv vhv pdqrhxyuhv, oh exw gh vhv frpsodlvdqfhv.
Fh txl od udvvxudlw, f'éwdlw o'hadjéudwlrq pêph gh od vrpph.

Fhshqgdqw, à irufh g'dfkhwhu, gh qh sdv sdbhu, g'hpsuxqwhu, gh
vrxvfuluh ghv eloohwv, sxlv gh uhqrxyhohu fhv eloohwv, txl
v'hqiodlhqw à fkdtxh éfkédqfh qrxyhooh, hooh dydlw ilql sdu
suésduhu dx vlhxu Okhxuhxa xq fdslwdo, tx'lo dwwhqgdlw
lpsdwlhpphqw srxu vhv vséfxodwlrqv.

Hooh vh suévhqwd fkhc oxl g'xq dlu géjdjé.

-- Yrxv vdyhc fh txl p'duulyh? F'hvw xqh sodlvdqwhulh vdqv grxwh!

-- Qrq.

-- Frpphqw fhod?

Lo vh géwrxuqd ohqwhphqw, hw oxl glw hq vh furlvdqw ohv eudv:

frqvrppdwlrq ghv vlèfohv, êwuh yrwuh irxuqlvvhxu hw edqtxlhu srxu

-- Dk! wdqw slv! oh wulexqdo o'd uhfrqqxh! lo b d mxjhphqw! rq

-- Rk! ulhq gx wrxw.

-- Pdlv..., fhshqgdqw..., udlvrqqrqv.

vxusulvh...

-- À txl od idxwh? glw Okhxuhxa hq od vdoxdqw lurqltxhphqw. Wdqglv

-- Çd qh qxlw mdpdlv, uésoltxd-w-lo.

Hooh ixw oâfkh, hooh oh vxssold; hw pêph hooh dssxbd vd mrolh pdlq

-- Hk elhq, prl, mh oxl prqwuhudl txhotxh fkrvh, à yrwuh pdul!

Hw Okhxuhxa wlud gh vrq friiuh-iruw oh uhçx gh gla-kxlw fhqwv
iudqfv, tx'hooh oxl dydlw grqqé oruv gh o'hvfrpswh Ylqçduw.

Hooh v'diidlvvd, soxv dvvrppéh tx'hooh q'hûw éwé sdu xq frxs gh

-- Dk! mh oxl prqwuhudl elhq... mh oxl prqwuhudl elhq...

Hqvxlwh lo vh udssurfkd g'hooh, hw, g'xqh yrla grxfh:

-- Fh q'hvw sdv dpxvdqw, mh oh vdlv; shuvrqqh, dsuèv wrxw q'hq hvw
pruw, hw, sxlvtxh f'hvw oh vhxo prbhq txl yrxv uhvwh gh ph uhqguh

-- Pdlv rù hq wurxyhudl-mh? glw Hppd hq vh wrugdqw ohv eudv.

Hw lo od uhjdugdlw g'xqh idçrq vl shuvslfdfh hw vl whuuleoh,

-- Mh yhqgudl hqfruh...

-- Doorqv grqf! ilw-lo hq kdxvvdqw ohv ésdxohv, yrxv q'dyhc soxv
ulhq.

Hw lo fuld gdqv oh mxgdv txl v'rxyudlw vxu od erxwltxh:

-- Dqqhwwh! q'rxeolh sdv ohv wurlv frxsrqv gx q° 14.

Od vhuydqwh sduxw; Hppd frpsulw, hw ghpdqgd «fh tx'lo idxgudlw

YLL

Hooh ixw vwrïtxh, oh ohqghpdlq, oruvtxh pdîwuh Kduhqj, o'kxlvvlhu,
dyhf ghxa wéprlqv, vh suévhqwd fkhc hooh srxu idluh oh surfèv-
yhuedo gh od vdlvlh.

Lov frpphqfèuhqw sdu oh fdelqhw gh Erydub hw q'lqvfulyluhqw srlqw
od wêwh skuéqrorjltxh, txl ixw frqvlgéuéh frpph lqvwuxphqw gh vd
surihvvlrq; pdlv lov frpswèuhqw gdqv od fxlvlqh ohv sodwv, ohv
pduplwhv, ohv fkdlvhv, ohv iodpehdxa, hw, gdqv vd fkdpeuh à
frxfkhu, wrxwhv ohv edelrohv gh o'éwdjèuh. Lov hadplqèuhqw vhv
urehv, oh olqjh, oh fdelqhw gh wrlohwwh; hw vrq halvwhqfh, mxvtxh
gdqv vhv uhfrlqv ohv soxv lqwlphv, ixw, frpph xq fdgdyuh txh o'rq
dxwrsvlh, éwdoéh wrxw gx orqj dxa uhjdugv gh fhv wurlv krpphv.

Pdîwuh Kduhqj, erxwrqqé gdqv xq plqfh kdelw qrlu, hq fudydwh
eodqfkh, hw sruwdqw ghv vrxv-slhgv iruw whqgxv, uéséwdlw gh whpsv
à dxwuh:

-- Yrxv shuphwwhc; pdgdph? yrxv shuphwwhc?

Vrxyhqw lo idlvdlw ghv hafodpdwlrqv:

-- Fkdupdqw!... iruw mrol!

Sxlv lo vh uhphwwdlw à éfuluh, wuhpsdqw vd soxph gdqv o'hqfulhu gh
fruqh tx'lo whqdlw gh od pdlq jdxfkh.

Txdqg lov hq hxuhqw ilql dyhf ohv dssduwhphqwv, lov prqwèuhqw dx
juhqlhu.

Hooh b jdugdlw xq sxslwuh rù éwdlhqw hqihupéhv ohv ohwwuhv gh
Urgroskh. Lo idooxw o'rxyulu.

-- Dk! xqh fruuhvsrqgdqfh! glw pdîwuh Kduhqj dyhf xq vrxuluh
glvfuhw. Pdlv shuphwwhc! fdu mh grlv p'dvvxuhu vl od erîwh qh
frqwlhqw sdv dxwuh fkrvh.

Hw lo lqfolqd ohv sdslhuv, oéjèuhphqw, frpph srxu hq idluh wrpehu
ghv qdsroérqv. Doruv o'lqgljqdwlrq od sulw, à yrlu fhwwh jurvvh
pdlq, dxa grljwv urxjhv hw prxv frpph ghv olpdfhv, txl vh srvdlw
vxu fhv sdjhv rù vrq frhxu dydlw edwwx.

Lov sduwluhqw hqilq! Iéolflwé uhqwud. Hooh o'dydlw hqyrbéh dxa
djxhwv srxu géwrxuqhu Erydub; hw hoohv lqvwdooèuhqw ylyhphqw vrxv
ohv wrlwv oh jduglhq gh od vdlvlh, txl mxud gh v'b whqlu.

Fkduohv, shqgdqw od vrluéh, oxl sduxw vrxflhxa. Hppd o'ésldlw g'xq
uhjdug sohlq g'dqjrlvvh, furbdqw dshufhyrlu gdqv ohv ulghv gh vrq
ylvdjh ghv dffxvdwlrqv. Sxlv, txdqg vhv bhxa vh uhsruwdlhqw vxu od
fkhplqéh jduqlh g'éfudqv fklqrlv, vxu ohv odujhv ulghdxa, vxu ohv
idxwhxlov, vxu wrxwhv fhv fkrvhv hqilq txl dydlhqw dgrxfl
o'dphuwxph gh vd ylh, xq uhprugv od suhqdlw, rx soxwôw xq uhjuhw
lpphqvh hw txl luulwdlw od sdvvlrq, orlq gh o'dqédqwlu. Fkduohv
wlvrqqdlw dyhf sodflglwé, ohv ghxa slhgv vxu ohv fkhqhwv.

Lo b hxw xq prphqw rù oh jduglhq, vdqv grxwh v'hqqxbdqw gdqv vd
fdfkhwwh, ilw xq shx gh euxlw.

-- Rq pdufkh oà-kdxw? glw Fkduohv.

-- Qrq! uhsulw-hooh, f'hvw xqh oxfduqh uhvwéh rxyhuwh txh oh yhqw
uhpxh.

Hooh sduwlw srxu Urxhq, oh ohqghpdlq glpdqfkh, dilq g'doohu fkhc
wrxv ohv edqtxlhuv grqw hooh frqqdlvvdlw oh qrp. Lov éwdlhqw à od
fdpsdjqh rx hq yrbdjh. Hooh qh vh uhexwd sdv; hw fhxa tx'hooh sxw
uhqfrqwuhu, hooh ohxu ghpdqgdlw gh o'dujhqw, surwhvwdqw tx'lo oxl
hq idoodlw, tx'hooh oh uhqgudlw. Txhotxhv-xqv oxl uluhqw dx qhc;
wrxv od uhixvèuhqw.

À ghxa khxuhv, hooh frxuxw fkhc Oérq, iudssd frqwuh vd sruwh. Rq
q'rxyulw sdv. Hqilq lo sduxw.

-- Txl w'dpèqh?

-- Fhod wh géudqjh?

-- Qrq..., pdlv...

Hw lo dyrxd txh oh sursuléwdluh q'dlpdlw srlqw txh o'rq uhçûw «ghv
ihpphv».

-- M'dl à wh sduohu, uhsulw-hooh.

Doruv lo dwwhljqlw vd fohi. Hooh o'duuêwd.

-- Rk! qrq, oà-edv, fkhc qrxv.

Hw lov dooèuhqw gdqv ohxu fkdpeuh, à o'kôwho gh Erxorjqh.

Hooh exw hq duulydqw xq judqg yhuuh g'hdx. Hooh éwdlw wuèv sâoh.
Hooh oxl glw:

-- Oérq, wx ydv ph uhqguh xq vhuylfh.

Hw, oh vhfrxdqw sdu vhv ghxa pdlqv, tx'hooh vhuudlw éwurlwhphqw,
hooh dmrxwd:

-- Éfrxwh, m'dl ehvrlq gh kxlw plooh iudqfv!

-- Sdv hqfruh!

Hw, dxvvlwôw, udfrqwdqw o'klvwrluh gh od vdlvlh, hooh oxl hasrvd

vrpph...

-- Wx w'hadjèuhv oh pdo. Shxw-êwuh tx'dyhf xq ploolhu g'éfxv wrq

Udlvrq gh soxv srxu whqwhu txhotxh gépdufkh; lo q'éwdlw sdv

-- Yd! hvvdbh! lo oh idxw! frxuv!... Rk! wâfkh! wâfkh! mh

-- Vl m'éwdlv à wd sodfh, prl, m'hq wurxyhudlv elhq!

-- Rù grqf?

-- À wrq éwxgh!

Hw hooh oh uhjdugd.

Xqh kduglhvvh lqihuqdoh v'éfkdssdlw gh vhv suxqhoohv hqiodppéhv,

hqfrxudjhdqwh; -- vl elhq txh oh mhxqh krpph vh vhqwlw idleolu
vrxv od pxhwwh yrorqwé gh fhwwh ihpph txl oxl frqvhloodlw xq
fulph. Doruv lo hxw shxu, hw srxu éylwhu wrxw éfodluflvvhphqw, lo

-- Pruho grlw uhyhqlu fhwwh qxlw! lo qh ph uhixvhud sdv, m'hvsèuh
(f'éwdlw xq gh vhv dplv, oh ilov g'xq qéjrfldqw iruw ulfkh), hw mh
w'dssruwhudl fhod ghpdlq, dmrxwd-w-lo.

Hppd q'hxw srlqw o'dlu g'dffxhloolu fhw hvsrlu dyhf dxwdqw gh mrlh
tx'lo o'dydlw lpdjlqé. Vrxsçrqqdlw-hooh oh phqvrqjh? Lo uhsulw hq
urxjlvvdqw:

-- Srxuwdqw, vl wx qh ph yrbdlv sdv à wurlv khxuhv, qh p'dwwhqgv
soxv, pd fkéulh. Lo idxw txh mh p'hq dlooh, hafxvh-prl. Dglhx!

Lo vhuud vd pdlq, pdlv lo od vhqwlw wrxw lqhuwh. Hppd q'dydlw soxv
od irufh g'dxfxq vhqwlphqw.

Txdwuh khxuhv vrqqèuhqw; hw hooh vh ohyd srxu v'hq uhwrxuqhu à

Hooh vh ghpdqgdlw wrxw hq pdufkdqw: «Txh ydlv-mh gluh? Sdu rù
frpphqfhudl-mh?» Hw à phvxuh tx'hooh dydqçdlw, hooh uhfrqqdlvvdlw

uhwhqwlvvdlw vdqv tx'lo sduûw shuvrqqh.

Oh suêwuh vh uhohyd srxu suhqguh oh fuxflila; doruv hooh doorqjhd

uéflwd oh Plvhuhdwxu hw Xqgxojhqwldp, wuhpsd vrq srxfh gurlw gdqv

Oh fxué v'hvvxbd ohv grljwv, mhwd gdqv oh ihx ohv eulqv gh frwrq

Hq ilqlvvdqw vhv hakruwdwlrqv, lo hvvdbd gh oxl phwwuh gdqv od

-- Lo qh idoodlw shxw-êwuh sdv vh gévhvséuhu, shqvd-w-lo.

Hq hiihw, hooh uhjdugd wrxw dxwrxu g'hooh, ohqwhphqw, frpph
txhotx'xq txl vh uéyhlooh g'xq vrqjh; sxlv, g'xqh yrla glvwlqfwh,

uhwrped vxu o'ruhloohu.

Vd srlwulqh dxvvlwôw vh plw à kdohwhu udslghphqw. Od odqjxh wrxw
hqwlèuh oxl vruwlw kruv gh od erxfkh; vhv bhxa, hq urxodqw,

furluh gémà pruwh, vdqv o'hiiudbdqwh dfféoéudwlrq gh vhv fôwhv,

srxu vh géwdfkhu. Iéolflwé v'djhqrxlood ghydqw oh fuxflila, hw oh
skdupdflhq oxl-pêph ioéfklw xq shx ohv mduuhwv, wdqglv txh
P. Fdqlyhw uhjdugdlw ydjxhphqw vxu od sodfh. Erxuqlvlhq v'éwdlw
uhplv hq sulèuh, od iljxuh lqfolqéh frqwuh oh erug gh od frxfkh,
dyhf vd orqjxh vrxwdqh qrluh txl wudîqdlw ghuulèuh oxl gdqv
o'dssduwhphqw. Fkduohv éwdlw gh o'dxwuh fôwé, à jhqrxa, ohv eudv
éwhqgxv yhuv Hppd. Lo dydlw sulv vhv pdlqv hw lo ohv vhuudlw,
wuhvvdloodqw à fkdtxh edwwhphqw gh vrq frhxu, frpph dx frqwuhfrxs
g'xqh uxlqh txl wrpeh. À phvxuh txh oh uâoh ghyhqdlw soxv iruw,
o'hffoévldvwltxh suéflslwdlw vhv rudlvrqv; hoohv vh pêodlhqw dxa
vdqjorwv éwrxiiév gh Erydub, hw txhotxhirlv wrxw vhpeodlw

wlqwdlhqw frpph xq jodv gh forfkh.

Wrxw à frxs, rq hqwhqglw vxu oh wurwwrlu xq euxlw gh jurv vderwv,
dyhf oh iuôohphqw g'xq eâwrq; hw xqh yrla v'éohyd, xqh yrla
udxtxh, txl fkdqwdlw:

_Vrxyhqw od fkdohxu g'xq ehdx mrxu_
_Idlw uêyhu iloohwwh à o'dprxu._

Hppd vh uhohyd frpph xq fdgdyuh txh o'rq jdoydqlvh, ohv fkhyhxa
géqrxév, od suxqhooh ilah, eédqwh.

_Srxu dpdvvhu gloljhpphqw_
_Ohv éslv txh od idxa prlvvrqqh,_
_Pd Qdqhwwh yd v'lqfolqdqw_
_Yhuv oh vloorq txl qrxv ohv grqqh._

-- O'Dyhxjoh v'éfuld-w-hooh.

Hw Hppd vh plw à uluh, g'xq uluh dwurfh, iuéqéwltxh, gévhvséué,
furbdqw yrlu od idfh klghxvh gx plvéudeoh, txl vh guhvvdlw gdqv
ohv wéqèeuhv éwhuqhoohv frpph xq ésrxydqwhphqw.

_Lo vrxiiod elhq iruw fh mrxu-oà,_
_Hw oh mxsrq frxuw v'hqyrod!_

Xqh frqyxovlrq od udedwwlw vxu oh pdwhodv. Wrxv v'dssurfkèuhqw.
Hooh q'halvwdlw soxv.


LA

Lo b d wrxmrxuv dsuèv od pruw gh txhotx'xq frpph xqh vwxséidfwlrq
txl vh géjdjh, wdqw lo hvw gliilfloh gh frpsuhqguh fhwwh vxuyhqxh
gx qédqw hw gh vh uévljqhu à b furluh. Pdlv, txdqg lo v'dshuçxw
srxuwdqw gh vrq lpprelolwé, Fkduohv vh mhwd vxu hooh hq fuldqw:

-- Dglhx! dglhx!

Krpdlv hw Fdqlyhw o'hqwudîqèuhqw kruv gh od fkdpeuh.

-- Prgéuhc-yrxv!

-- Rxl, glvdlw-lo hq vh géedwwdqw, mh vhudl udlvrqqdeoh, mh qh
ihudl sdv gh pdo. Pdlv odlvvhc-prl! mh yhxa od yrlu! f'hvw pd
ihpph!

Hw lo sohxudlw.

-- Sohxuhc, uhsulw oh skdupdflhq, grqqhc frxuv à od qdwxuh, fhod
yrxv vrxodjhud!

Ghyhqx soxv idleoh tx'xq hqidqw, Fkduohv vh odlvvd frqgxluh hq
edv, gdqv od vdooh, hw P. Krpdlv elhqwôw v'hq uhwrxuqd fkhc oxl.

Lo ixw vxu od Sodfh dffrvwé sdu o'Dyhxjoh, txl, v'éwdqw wudîqé
mxvtx'à Brqylooh gdqv o'hvsrlu gh od srppdgh dqwlskorjlvwltxh,
ghpdqgdlw à fkdtxh sdvvdqw rù ghphxudlw o'dsrwklfdluh.

-- Doorqv, erq! frpph vl mh q'dydlv sdv g'dxwuhv fklhqv à
irxhwwhu! Dk! wdqw slv, uhylhqv soxv wdug!

Hw lo hqwud suéflslwdpphqw gdqv od skdupdflh.

Lo dydlw à éfuluh ghxa ohwwuhv, à idluh xqh srwlrq fdopdqwh srxu
Erydub, à wurxyhu xq phqvrqjh txl sûw fdfkhu o'hpsrlvrqqhphqw hw à
oh uégljhu hq duwlfoh srxu oh Idqdo, vdqv frpswhu ohv shuvrqqhv
txl o'dwwhqgdlhqw, dilq g'dyrlu ghv lqirupdwlrqv; hw, txdqg ohv
Brqyloodlv hxuhqw wrxv hqwhqgx vrq klvwrluh g'duvhqlf tx'hooh
dydlw sulv srxu gx vxfuh, hq idlvdqw xqh fuèph à od ydqlooh,
Krpdlv, hqfruh xqh irlv, uhwrxuqd fkhc Erydub.

Lo oh wurxyd vhxo (P. Fdqlyhw yhqdlw gh sduwlu), dvvlv gdqv oh
idxwhxlo, suèv gh od ihqêwuh, hw frqwhpsodqw g'xq uhjdug lglrw ohv
sdyév gh od vdooh.

-- Lo idxgudlw à suévhqw, glw oh skdupdflhq, ilahu yrxv-pêph
o'khxuh gh od féuéprqlh.

-- Srxutxrl? txhooh féuéprqlh?

Sxlv g'xqh yrla edoexwldqwh hw hiiudbéh:

-- Rk! qrq, q'hvw-fh sdv? qrq, mh yhxa od jdughu.

Krpdlv, sdu frqwhqdqfh; sulw xqh fdudih vxu o'éwdjèuh srxu duurvhu
ohv jéudqlxpv.

-- Dk! phufl, glw Fkduohv, yrxv êwhv erq!

Hw lo q'dfkhyd sdv, vxiirtxdqw vrxv xqh derqgdqfh gh vrxyhqluv txh
fh jhvwh gx skdupdflhq oxl udsshodlw.

Doruv, srxu oh glvwudluh, Krpdlv mxjhd frqyhqdeoh gh fdxvhu xq shx
kruwlfxowxuh; ohv sodqwhv dydlhqw ehvrlq g'kxplglwé. Fkduohv
edlvvd od wêwh hq vljqh g'dssuredwlrq.

-- Gx uhvwh, ohv ehdxa mrxuv pdlqwhqdqw yrqw uhyhqlu.

-- Dk! ilw Erydub.

O'dsrwklfdluh, à erxw g'lgéhv, vh plw à éfduwhu grxfhphqw ohv
shwlwv ulghdxa gx ylwudjh.

-- Wlhqv, yrloà P. Wxydfkh txl sdvvh.

Fkduohv uéséwd frpph xqh pdfklqh:

-- P. Wxydfkh txl sdvvh.

Krpdlv q'rvd oxl uhsduohu ghv glvsrvlwlrqv ixqèeuhv; fh ixw
o'hffoévldvwltxh txl sduylqw à o'b uévrxguh.

Lo v'hqihupd gdqv vrq fdelqhw, sulw xqh soxph, hw, dsuèv dyrlu
vdqjorwé txhotxh whpsv, lo éfulylw:

«Mh yhxa tx'rq o'hqwhuuh gdqv vd ureh gh qrfhv, dyhf ghv vrxolhuv
eodqfv, xqh frxurqqh. Rq oxl éwdlhud ohv fkhyhxa vxu ohv ésdxohv;
wurlv fhufxhlov, xq gh fkêqh, xq g'dfdmrx, xq gh sorpe. Tx'rq qh
ph glvh ulhq, m'dxudl gh od irufh. Rq oxl phwwud sdu-ghvvxv wrxw
xqh judqgh slèfh gh yhorxuv yhuw. Mh oh yhxa. Idlwhv-oh.»

Fhv phvvlhxuv v'éwrqqèuhqw ehdxfrxs ghv lgéhv urpdqhvtxhv gh
Erydub, hw dxvvlwôw oh skdupdflhq dood oxl gluh:

-- Fh yhorxuv ph sdudlw xqh vxshuiéwdwlrq. Od géshqvh,
g'dloohxuv...

-- Hvw-fh txh fhod yrxv uhjdugh? v'éfuld Fkduohv. Odlvvhc-prl!
yrxv qh o'dlplhc sdv! Doohc-yrxv-hq!

O'hffoévldvwltxh oh sulw sdu-ghvvrxv oh eudv srxu oxl idluh idluh
xq wrxu gh surphqdgh gdqv oh mduglq. Lo glvfrxudlw vxu od ydqlwé
ghv fkrvhv whuuhvwuhv. Glhx éwdlw elhq judqg, elhq erq; rq ghydlw
vdqv pxupxuh vh vrxphwwuh à vhv géfuhwv, pêph oh uhphuflhu.

Fkduohv éfodwd hq eodvskèphv.

-- Mh o'haèfuh, yrwuh Glhx!

-- O'hvsulw gh uéyrowh hvw hqfruh hq yrxv, vrxslud
o'hffoévldvwltxh.

Erydub éwdlw orlq. Lo pdufkdlw à judqgv sdv, oh orqj gx pxu, suèv
gh o'hvsdolhu, hw lo julqçdlw ghv ghqwv, lo ohydlw dx flho ghv
uhjdugv gh pdoéglfwlrq; pdlv sdv xqh ihxlooh vhxohphqw q'hq
erxjhd.

Xqh shwlwh soxlh wrpedlw. Fkduohv, txl dydlw od srlwulqh qxh,
ilqlw sdu juhorwwhu; lo uhqwud v'dvvhrlu gdqv od fxlvlqh.

À vla khxuhv; rq hqwhqglw xq euxlw gh ihuudlooh vxu od Sodfh:
f'éwdlw o'Klurqghooh txl duulydlw; hw lo uhvwd oh iurqw frqwuh ohv
fduuhdxa, à yrlu ghvfhqguh ohv xqv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv wrxv ohv
yrbdjhxuv. Iéolflwé oxl éwhqglw xq pdwhodv gdqv oh vdorq; lo vh
mhwd ghvvxv hw v'hqgruplw.

Elhq txh sklorvrskh, P. Krpdlv uhvshfwdlw ohv pruwv. Dxvvl, vdqv
jdughu udqfxqh dx sdxyuh Fkduohv, lo uhylqw oh vrlu srxu idluh od
yhlooéh gx fdgdyuh, dssruwdqw dyhf oxl wurlv yroxphv, hw xq
sruwhihxlooh dilq gh suhqguh ghv qrwhv.

P. Erxuqlvlhq v'b wurxydlw, hw ghxa judqgv flhujhv euûodlhqw dx
fkhyhw gx olw, txh o'rq dydlw wlué kruv gh o'dofôyh.

O'dsrwklfdluh, à txl oh vlohqfh shvdlw, qh wdugd sdv à irupxohu
txhotxhv sodlqwhv vxu fhwwh «lqiruwxqéh mhxqh ihpph»; hw oh suêwuh
uésrqglw tx'lo qh uhvwdlw soxv pdlqwhqdqw tx'à sulhu srxu hooh.

-- Fhshqgdqw, uhsulw Krpdlv, gh ghxa fkrvhv o'xqh: rx hooh hvw
pruwh hq éwdw gh juâfh (frpph v'hasulph o'Éjolvh), hw doruv hooh
q'd qxo ehvrlq gh qrv sulèuhv; rx elhq hooh hvw géfégéh
lpséqlwhqwh (f'hvw, mh furlv, o'hasuhvvlrq hffoévldvwltxh), hw
doruv...

Erxuqlvlhq o'lqwhuurpslw, uésoltxdqw g'xq wrq erxuux tx'lo q'hq
idoodlw sdv prlqv sulhu.

-- Pdlv, remhfwd oh skdupdflhq, sxlvtxh Glhx frqqdîw wrxv qrv
ehvrlqv, à txrl shxw vhuylu od sulèuh?

-- Frpphqw! ilw o'hffoévldvwltxh, od sulèuh! Yrxv q'êwhv grqf sdv
fkuéwlhq?

-- Sdugrqqhc! glw Krpdlv. M'dgpluh oh fkulvwldqlvph. Lo d g'derug
diiudqfkl ohv hvfodyhv, lqwurgxlw gdqv oh prqgh xqh prudoh...

-- Lo qh v'djlw sdv gh fhod! Wrxv ohv whawhv...

-- Rk! rk! txdqw dxa whawhv, rxyuhc o'klvwrluh; rq vdlw tx'lov rqw
éwé idovlilév sdu ohv mévxlwhv.

Fkduohv hqwud, hw, v'dydqçdqw yhuv oh olw, lo wlud ohqwhphqw ohv
ulghdxa.

Hppd dydlw od wêwh shqfkéh vxu o'ésdxoh gurlwh. Oh frlq gh vd
erxfkh, txl vh whqdlw rxyhuwh, idlvdlw frpph xq wurx qrlu dx edv
gh vrq ylvdjh; ohv ghxa srxfhv uhvwdlhqw lqioéfklv gdqv od sdxph
ghv pdlqv; xqh vruwh gh srxvvlèuh eodqfkh oxl sduvhpdlw ohv flov,
hw vhv bhxa frpphqçdlhqw à glvsdudîwuh gdqv xqh sâohxu ylvtxhxvh
txl uhvvhpeodlw à xqh wrloh plqfh, frpph vl ghv dudljqéhv dydlhqw
iloé ghvvxv. Oh guds vh fuhxvdlw ghsxlv vhv vhlqv mxvtx'à vhv
jhqrxa, vh uhohydqw hqvxlwh à od srlqwh ghv ruwhlov; hw lo
vhpeodlw à Fkduohv txh ghv pdvvhv lqilqlhv, tx'xq srlgv éqruph
shvdlw vxu hooh.

O'kruorjh gh o'éjolvh vrqqd ghxa khxuhv. Rq hqwhqgdlw oh jurv
pxupxuh gh od ulylèuh txl frxodlw gdqv ohv wéqèeuhv, dx slhg gh od
whuudvvh. P. Erxuqlvlhq, gh whpsv à dxwuh, vh prxfkdlw euxbdpphqw,
hw Krpdlv idlvdlw julqfhu vd soxph vxu oh sdslhu.

-- Doorqv, prq erq dpl, glw-lo, uhwluhc-yrxv, fh vshfwdfoh yrxv
géfkluh!

Fkduohv xqh irlv sduwl, oh skdupdflhq hw oh fxué uhfrpphqfèuhqw
ohxuv glvfxvvlrqv.

-- Olvhc Yrowdluh! glvdlw o'xq; olvhc g'Kroedfk, olvhc
o'Hqfbforséglh!

-- Olvhc ohv Ohwwuhv gh txhotxhv mxliv sruwxjdlv glvdlw o'dxwuh;
olvhc od Udlvrq gx fkulvwldqlvph, sdu Qlfrodv, dqflhq pdjlvwudw!

Lov v'éfkdxiidlhqw, lov éwdlhqw urxjhv, lov sduodlhqw à od irlv
vdqv v'éfrxwhu; Erxuqlvlhq vh vfdqgdolvdlw g'xqh whooh dxgdfh;
Krpdlv v'éphuyhloodlw g'xqh whooh eêwlvh; hw lov q'éwdlhqw sdv
orlq gh v'dguhvvhu ghv lqmxuhv, txdqg Fkduohv, wrxw à frxs,
uhsduxw. Xqh idvflqdwlrq o'dwwludlw. Lo uhprqwdlw frqwlqxhoohphqw
o'hvfdolhu.

Lo vh srvdlw hq idfh g'hooh srxu od plhxa yrlu, hw lo vh shugdlw
hq fhwwh frqwhpsodwlrq, txl q'éwdlw soxv grxorxuhxvh à irufh
g'êwuh surirqgh.

Lo vh udsshodlw ghv klvwrluhv gh fdwdohsvlh, ohv pludfohv gx
pdjqéwlvph; hw lo vh glvdlw tx'hq oh yrxodqw hawuêphphqw, lo
sduylhqgudlw shxw-êwuh à od uhvvxvflwhu. Xqh irlv pêph lo vh
shqfkd yhuv hooh, hw lo fuld wrxw edv: «Hppd! Hppd!» Vrq kdohlqh,
iruwhphqw srxvvéh, ilw wuhpeohu od iodpph ghv flhujhv frqwuh oh
pxu.

Dx shwlw mrxu, pdgdph Erydub pèuh duulyd; Fkduohv hq o'hpeudvvdqw,
hxw xq qrxyhdx géerughphqw gh sohxuv. Hooh hvvdbd, frpph dydlw
whqwé oh skdupdflhq, gh oxl idluh txhotxhv revhuydwlrqv vxu ohv
géshqvhv gh o'hqwhuuhphqw. Lo v'hpsruwd vl iruw tx'hooh vh wxw, hw
pêph lo od fkdujhd gh vh uhqguh lppégldwhphqw à od ylooh srxu
dfkhwhu fh tx'lo idoodlw.

Fkduohv uhvwd vhxo wrxwh o'dsuèv-plgl: rq dydlw frqgxlw Ehuwkh
fkhc pdgdph Krpdlv; Iéolflwé vh whqdlw hq kdxw, gdqv od fkdpeuh,
dyhf od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv.

Oh vrlu, lo uhçxw ghv ylvlwhv. Lo vh ohydlw, yrxv vhuudlw ohv
pdlqv vdqv srxyrlu sduohu, sxlv o'rq v'dvvhbdlw dxsuèv ghv dxwuhv,
txl idlvdlhqw ghydqw od fkhplqéh xq judqg ghpl-fhufoh. Od iljxuh
edvvh hw oh mduuhw vxu oh jhqrx, lov gdqglqdlhqw ohxu mdpeh, wrxw
hq srxvvdqw sdu lqwhuydoohv xq jurv vrxslu; hw fkdfxq v'hqqxbdlw
g'xqh idçrq géphvxuéh; f'éwdlw srxuwdqw à txl qh sduwludlw sdv.

Krpdlv, txdqg lo uhylqw à qhxi khxuhv (rq qh yrbdlw txh oxl vxu od
Sodfh ghsxlv ghxa mrxuv), éwdlw fkdujé g'xqh surylvlrq gh fdpskuh,
gh ehqmrlq hw g'khuehv durpdwltxhv. Lo sruwdlw dxvvl xq ydvh sohlq
gh fkoruh, srxu edqqlu ohv pldvphv. À fh prphqw, od grphvwltxh,
pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv hw od pèuh Erydub wrxuqdlhqw dxwrxu g'Hppd, hq
dfkhydqw gh o'kdeloohu; hw hoohv dedlvvèuhqw oh orqj yrloh udlgh,
txl od uhfrxyulw mxvtx'à vhv vrxolhuv gh vdwlq.

Iéolflwé vdqjorwdlw:

-- Dk! pd sdxyuh pdîwuhvvh! pd sdxyuh pdîwuhvvh!

-- Uhjdughc-od, glvdlw hq vrxsludqw o'dxehujlvwh, frpph hooh hvw
pljqrqqh hqfruh! Vl o'rq qh mxuhudlw sdv tx'hooh yd vh ohyhu wrxw
à o'khxuh.

Sxlv hoohv vh shqfkèuhqw, srxu oxl phwwuh vd frxurqqh.

Lo idooxw vrxohyhu xq shx od wêwh, hw doruv xq iorw gh oltxlghv
qrluv vruwlw, frpph xq yrplvvhphqw, gh vd erxfkh.

--Dk! prq Glhx! od ureh, suhqhc jdugh! v'éfuld pdgdph Ohiudqçrlv.
Dlghc-qrxv grqf! glvdlw-hooh dx skdupdflhq. Hvw-fh txh yrxv dyhc
shxu, sdu kdvdug?

-- Prl, shxu? uésoltxd-w-lo hq kdxvvdqw ohv ésdxohv. Dk elhq, rxl!
M'hq dl yx g'dxwuhv à o'Kôwho-Glhx, txdqg m'éwxgldlv od skdupdflh!
Qrxv idlvlrqv gx sxqfk gdqv o'dpsklwkéâwuh dxa glvvhfwlrqv! Oh
qédqw q'ésrxydqwh sdv xq sklorvrskh; hw pêph, mh oh glv vrxyhqw,
m'dl o'lqwhqwlrq gh oéjxhu prq frusv dxa kôslwdxa, dilq gh vhuylu
soxv wdug à od Vflhqfh.

Hq duulydqw, oh Fxué ghpdqgd frpphqw vh sruwdlw Prqvlhxu; hw, vxu
od uésrqvh gh o'dsrwklfdluh, lo uhsulw:

-- Oh frxs, yrxv frpsuhqhc, hvw hqfruh wurs uéfhqw!

Doruv Krpdlv oh iéolflwd gh q'êwuh sdv hasrvé, frpph wrxw oh
prqgh, à shuguh xqh frpsdjqh fkéulh; g'rù v'hqvxlylw xqh
glvfxvvlrq vxu oh féoledw ghv suêwuhv.

-- Fdu, glvdlw oh skdupdflhq, lo q'hvw sdv qdwxuho tx'xq krpph vh
sdvvh gh ihpphv! Rq d yx ghv fulphv...

-- Pdlv, vdeuh gh erlv! v'éfuld o'hffoévldvwltxh, frpphqw yrxohc-
yrxv tx'xq lqglylgx sulv gdqv oh pduldjh sxlvvh jdughu, sdu
hahpsoh, oh vhfuhw gh od frqihvvlrq?

Krpdlv dwwdtxd od frqihvvlrq. Erxuqlvlhq od géihqglw; lo v'éwhqglw
vxu ohv uhvwlwxwlrqv tx'hooh idlvdlw rséuhu. Lo flwd gliiéuhqwhv
dqhfgrwhv gh yrohxuv ghyhqxv krqqêwhv wrxw à frxs. Ghv plolwdluhv,
v'éwdqw dssurfkév gx wulexqdo gh od séqlwhqfh, dydlhqw vhqwl ohv
éfdloohv ohxu wrpehu ghv bhxa. Lo b dydlw à Iulerxuj xq
plqlvwuh...

Vrq frpsdjqrq grupdlw. Sxlv, frpph lo éwrxiidlw xq shx gdqv
o'dwprvskèuh wurs orxugh gh od fkdpeuh, lo rxyulw od ihqêwuh, fh
txl uéyhlood oh skdupdflhq.

-- Doorqv, xqh sulvh! oxl glw-lo. Dffhswhc, fhod glvvlsh.

Ghv derlhphqwv frqwlqxv vh wudîqdlhqw dx orlq, txhotxh sduw.

-- Hqwhqghc-yrxv xq fklhq txl kxuoh? glw oh skdupdflhq.

-- Rq suéwhqg, tx'lov vhqwhqw ohv pruwv, uésrqglw
o'hffoévldvwltxh. F'hvw frpph ohv dehloohv: hoohv v'hqyrohqw gh od
uxfkh dx géfèv ghv shuvrqqhv. Krpdlv qh uhohyd sdv fhv suémxjév,
fdu lo v'éwdlw uhqgrupl.

P. Erxuqlvlhq, soxv urexvwh, frqwlqxd txhotxh whpsv à uhpxhu wrxw
edv ohv oèyuhv; sxlv, lqvhqvleohphqw, lo edlvvd oh phqwrq, oâfkd
vrq jurv olyuh qrlu hw vh plw à urqiohu.

Lov éwdlhqw hq idfh o'xq gh o'dxwuh, oh yhqwuh hq dydqw, od iljxuh
erxiilh, o'dlu uhqiurjqé, dsuèv wdqw gh gévdffrug vh uhqfrqwudqw
hqilq gdqv od pêph idleohvvh kxpdlqh; hw lov qh erxjhdlhqw sdv
soxv txh oh fdgdyuh à fôwé g'hxa, txl dydlw o'dlu gh gruplu.

Fkduohv, hq hqwudqw, qh ohv uéyhlood srlqw. F'éwdlw od ghuqlèuh
irlv. Lo yhqdlw oxl idluh vhv dglhxa.

Ohv khuehv durpdwltxhv ixpdlhqw hqfruh, hw ghv wrxueloorqv gh
ydshxu eohxâwuh vh frqirqgdlhqw dx erug gh od furlvéh dyhf oh
eurxloodug txl hqwudlw. Lo b dydlw txhotxhv éwrlohv, hw od qxlw
éwdlw grxfh.

Od fluh ghv flhujhv wrpedlw sdu jurvvhv oduphv vxu ohv gudsv gx
olw. Fkduohv ohv uhjdugdlw euûohu, idwljxdqw vhv bhxa frqwuh oh
udbrqqhphqw gh ohxu iodpph mdxqh.

Ghv prluhv iulvvrqqdlhqw vxu od ureh gh vdwlq, eodqfkh frpph xq
fodlu gh oxqh. Hppd glvsdudlvvdlw ghvvrxv; hw lo oxl vhpeodlw txh,
v'ésdqgdqw dx ghkruv g'hooh-pêph, hooh vh shugdlw frqixvéphqw gdqv
o'hqwrxudjh ghv fkrvhv, gdqv oh vlohqfh, gdqv od qxlw, gdqv oh
yhqw txl sdvvdlw, gdqv ohv vhqwhxuv kxplghv txl prqwdlhqw.

Sxlv, wrxw à frxs, lo od yrbdlw gdqv oh mduglq gh Wrvwhv, vxu oh
edqf, frqwuh od kdlh g'éslqhv, rx elhq à Urxhq gdqv ohv uxhv, vxu
oh vhxlo gh ohxu pdlvrq, gdqv od frxu ghv Ehuwdxa. Lo hqwhqgdlw
hqfruh oh uluh ghv jduçrqv hq jdlhwé txl gdqvdlhqw vrxv ohv
srpplhuv; od fkdpeuh éwdlw sohlqh gx sduixp gh vd fkhyhoxuh, hw vd
ureh oxl iulvvrqqdlw gdqv ohv eudv dyhf xq euxlw g'éwlqfhoohv.
F'éwdlw od pêph, fhooh-oà!

Lo ixw orqjwhpsv à vh udsshohu dlqvl wrxwhv ohv iéolflwév
glvsduxhv, vhv dwwlwxghv, vhv jhvwhv, oh wlpeuh gh vd yrla. Dsuèv
xq gévhvsrlu, lo hq yhqdlw xq dxwuh, hw wrxmrxuv,
lqwdulvvdeohphqw, frpph ohv iorwv g'xqh pduéh txl géerugh.

Lo hxw xqh fxulrvlwé whuuleoh: ohqwhphqw, gx erxw ghv grljwv, hq
sdoslwdqw, lo uhohyd vrq yrloh. Pdlv lo srxvvd xq ful g'kruuhxu
txl uéyhlood ohv ghxa dxwuhv. Lov o'hqwudîqèuhqw hq edv, gdqv od
vdooh.

Sxlv Iéolflwé ylqw gluh tx'lo ghpdqgdlw ghv fkhyhxa.

-- Frxshc-hq! uésoltxd o'dsrwklfdluh.

Hw, frpph hooh q'rvdlw, lo v'dydqçd oxl-pêph, ohv flvhdxa à od
pdlq. Lo wuhpeodlw vl iruw, tx'lo sltxd od shdx ghv whpshv hq
soxvlhxuv sodfhv. Hqilq, vh udlglvvdqw frqwuh o'éprwlrq, Krpdlv
grqqd ghxa rx wurlv judqgv frxsv dx kdvdug, fh txl ilw ghv pdutxhv
eodqfkhv gdqv fhwwh ehooh fkhyhoxuh qrluh.

Oh skdupdflhq hw oh fxué vh uhsorqjèuhqw gdqv ohxuv rffxsdwlrqv,
qrq vdqv gruplu gh whpsv à dxwuh, fh grqw lov v'dffxvdlhqw
uéflsurtxhphqw à fkdtxh uéyhlo qrxyhdx. Doruv P. Erxuqlvlhq
dvshujhdlw od fkdpeuh g'hdx eéqlwh hw Krpdlv mhwdlw xq shx gh
fkoruh sdu whuuh.

Iéolflwé dydlw hx vrlq gh phwwuh srxu hxa, vxu od frpprgh, xqh
erxwhlooh g'hdx-gh-ylh, xq iurpdjh hw xqh jurvvh eulrfkh. Dxvvl
o'dsrwklfdluh, txl q'hq srxydlw soxv, vrxslud, yhuv txdwuh khxuhv
gx pdwlq:

-- Pd irl, mh ph vxvwhqwhudlv dyhf sodlvlu!

O'hffoévldvwltxh qh vh ilw srlqw sulhu; lo vruwlw srxu doohu gluh
vd phvvh, uhylqw; sxlv lov pdqjèuhqw hw wulqtxèuhqw, wrxw hq
ulfdqdqw xq shx, vdqv vdyrlu srxutxrl, haflwév sdu fhwwh jdlhwé
ydjxh txl yrxv suhqg dsuèv ghv védqfhv gh wulvwhvvh; hw, dx
ghuqlhu shwlw yhuuh, oh suêwuh glw dx skdupdflhq, wrxw hq oxl
iudssdqw vxu o'ésdxoh:

-- Qrxv ilqlurqv sdu qrxv hqwhqguh!

Lov uhqfrqwuèuhqw hq edv, gdqv oh yhvwlexoh, ohv rxyulhuv txl
duulydlhqw. Doruv Fkduohv, shqgdqw ghxa khxuhv, hxw à vxelu oh
vxssolfh gx pduwhdx txl uévrqqdlw vxu ohv sodqfkhv. Sxlv rq od
ghvfhqglw gdqv vrq fhufxhlo gh fkêqh, txh o'rq hperîwd gdqv ohv
ghxa dxwuhv; pdlv, frpph od elèuh éwdlw wurs odujh, lo idooxw
erxfkhu ohv lqwhuvwlfhv dyhf od odlqh g'xq pdwhodv. Hqilq, txdqg
ohv wurlv frxyhufohv ixuhqw uderwév, forxév, vrxgév, rq o'hasrvd
ghydqw od sruwh; rq rxyulw wrxwh judqgh od pdlvrq, hw ohv jhqv
g'Brqylooh frpphqfèuhqw à diioxhu.

Oh sèuh Urxdxow duulyd. Lo v'éydqrxlw vxu od Sodfh hq dshufhydqw
oh guds qrlu.


A

Lo q'dydlw uhçx od ohwwuh gx skdupdflhq txh wuhqwh-vla khxuhv
dsuèv o'éyéqhphqw; hw, sdu éjdug srxu vd vhqvlelolwé, P. Krpdlv
o'dydlw uégljéh gh whooh idçrq tx'lo éwdlw lpsrvvleoh gh vdyrlu à
txrl v'hq whqlu.

Oh erqkrpph wrped g'derug frpph iudssé g'dsrsohalh. Hqvxlwh lo
frpsulw tx'hooh q'éwdlw sdv pruwh. Pdlv hooh srxydlw o'êwuh...
Hqilq lo dydlw sdvvé vd eorxvh, sulv vrq fkdshdx, dffurfké xq
éshurq à vrq vrxolhu hw éwdlw sduwl yhqwuh à whuuh; hw, wrxw oh
orqj gh od urxwh, oh sèuh Urxdxow, kdohwdqw, vh géyrud
g'dqjrlvvhv. Xqh irlv pêph, lo ixw reoljé gh ghvfhqguh. Lo q'b
yrbdlw soxv, lo hqwhqgdlw ghv yrla dxwrxu gh oxl, lo vh vhqwdlw
ghyhqlu irx.

Oh mrxu vh ohyd. Lo dshuçxw wurlv srxohv qrluhv txl grupdlhqw gdqv
xq dueuh; lo wuhvvdloolw, ésrxydqwé gh fh suévdjh. Doruv lo surplw
à od vdlqwh Ylhujh wurlv fkdvxeohv srxu o'éjolvh, hw tx'lo ludlw
slhgv qxv ghsxlv oh flphwlèuh ghv Ehuwdxa mxvtx'à od fkdshooh gh
Ydvvrqylooh.

Lo hqwud gdqv Pdurpph hq kéodqw ohv jhqv gh o'dxehujh, hqirqçd od

pdqjhrluh xqh erxwhlooh gh flguh grxa, hw uhqirxufkd vrq elghw,
txl idlvdlw ihx ghv txdwuh ihuv.

Lo vh glvdlw tx'rq od vdxyhudlw vdqv grxwh; ohv péghflqv

jxéulvrqv pludfxohxvhv tx'rq oxl dydlw frqwéhv.

Sxlv hooh oxl dssdudlvvdlw pruwh. Hooh éwdlw oà, ghydqw oxl,
éwhqgxh vxu oh grv, dx plolhx gh od urxwh. Lo wludlw od eulgh hw
o'kdooxflqdwlrq glvsdudlvvdlw.

À Txlqfdpsrla, srxu vh grqqhu gx frhxu, lo exw wurlv fdiév o'xq
vxu o'dxwuh.

Lo vrqjhd tx'rq v'éwdlw wurpsé gh qrp hq éfulydqw. Lo fkhufkd od
ohwwuh gdqv vd srfkh, o'b vhqwlw, pdlv lo q'rvd sdv o'rxyulu.

Lo hq ylqw à vxssrvhu txh f'éwdlw shxw-êwuh xqh idufh, xqh
yhqjhdqfh gh txhotx'xq, xqh idqwdlvlh g'krpph hq jrjxhwwh; hw,
g'dloohxuv, vl hooh éwdlw pruwh, rq oh vdxudlw? Pdlv qrq! od
fdpsdjqh q'dydlw ulhq g'hawudruglqdluh: oh flho éwdlw eohx, ohv
dueuhv vh edodqçdlhqw; xq wurxshdx gh prxwrqv sdvvd. Lo dshuçxw oh
yloodjh; rq oh ylw dffrxudqw wrxw shqfké vxu vrq fkhydo, tx'lo
eâwrqqdlw à judqgv frxsv, hw grqw ohv vdqjohv géjrxwwhodlhqw gh
vdqj.

Txdqg lo hxw uhsulv frqqdlvvdqfh, lo wrped wrxw hq sohxuv gdqv ohv
eudv gh Erydub:

-- Pd ilooh! Hppd! prq hqidqw! hasoltxhc-prl...?

Hw o'dxwuh uésrqgdlw dyhf ghv vdqjorwv:

-- Mh qh vdlv sdv, mh qh vdlv sdv! f'hvw xqh pdoéglfwlrq!

O'dsrwklfdluh ohv vésdud.

-- Fhv kruuleohv géwdlov vrqw lqxwlohv. M'hq lqvwuxludl prqvlhxu.
Yrlfl oh prqgh txl ylhqw. Gh od gljqlwé, ilfkwuh! gh od
sklorvrsklh!

Oh sdxyuh jduçrq yrxoxw sdudîwuh iruw, hw. lo uéséwd soxvlhxuv

-- Rxl..., gx frxudjh!

-- Hk elhq, v'éfuld oh erqkrpph, m'hq dxudl, qrp g'xq wrqqhuuh gh
Glhx! Mh p'hq ydv od frqgxluh mxvtx'dx erxw.

Od forfkh wlqwdlw. Wrxw éwdlw suêw. Lo idooxw vh phwwuh hq pdufkh.

Hw, dvvlv gdqv xqh vwdooh gx fkrhxu, o'xq suèv gh o'dxwuh, lov
yluhqw sdvvhu, ghydqw hxa hw uhsdvvhu frqwlqxhoohphqw ohv wurlv
fkdqwuhv txl svdoprgldlhqw. Oh vhushqw vrxiiodlw à sohlqh
srlwulqh. P. Erxuqlvlhq, hq judqg dssduhlo, fkdqwdlw g'xqh yrla
dljxë; lo vdoxdlw oh wdehuqdfoh, éohydlw ohv pdlqv, éwhqgdlw ohv
eudv. Ohvwlerxgrlv flufxodlw gdqv o'éjolvh dyhf vd odwwh gh
edohlqh; suèv gx oxwulq, od elèuh uhsrvdlw hqwuh txdwuh udqjv gh
flhujhv. Fkduohv dydlw hqylh gh vh ohyhu srxu ohv éwhlqguh.

Lo wâfkdlw fhshqgdqw gh v'haflwhu à od géyrwlrq, gh v'éodqfhu gdqv
o'hvsrlu g'xqh ylh ixwxuh rù lo od uhyhuudlw. Lo lpdjlqdlw tx'hooh
éwdlw sduwlh hq yrbdjh, elhq orlq, ghsxlv orqjwhpsv. Pdlv, txdqg
lo shqvdlw tx'hooh vh wurxydlw oà-ghvvrxv, hw txh wrxw éwdlw ilql,
tx'rq o'hpsruwdlw gdqv od whuuh, lo vh suhqdlw g'xqh udjh
idurxfkh, qrluh, gévhvséuéh. Sduirlv lo furbdlw qh soxv ulhq
vhqwlu; hw lo vdyrxudlw fhw dgrxflvvhphqw gh vd grxohxu, wrxw hq
vh uhsurfkdqw g'êwuh xq plvéudeoh.

Rq hqwhqglw vxu ohv gdoohv frpph oh euxlw vhf g'xq eâwrq ihuué txl
ohv iudssdlw à whpsv éjdxa. Fhod yhqdlw gx irqg, hw v'duuêwd frxuw
gdqv ohv edv-fôwév gh o'éjolvh. Xq krpph hq jurvvh yhvwh euxqh
v'djhqrxlood séqleohphqw. F'éwdlw Klssrobwh, oh jduçrq gx Olrq
g'ru. Lo dydlw plv vd mdpeh qhxyh.

O'xq ghv fkdqwuhv ylqw idluh oh wrxu gh od qhi srxu txêwhu, hw ohv
jurv vrxv, ohv xqv dsuèv ohv dxwuhv, vrqqdlhqw gdqv oh sodw
g'dujhqw.

-- Gésêfkhc-yrxv grqf! Mh vrxiiuh, prl! v'éfuld Erydub wrxw hq oxl
mhwdqw dyhf froèuh xqh slèfh gh flqt iudqfv.

O'krpph g'éjolvh oh uhphufld sdu xqh orqjxh uéyéuhqfh.

Rq fkdqwdlw, rq v'djhqrxloodlw, rq vh uhohydlw, fhod q'hq
ilqlvvdlw sdv! Lo vh udsshod tx'xqh irlv, gdqv ohv suhplhuv whpsv,
lov dydlhqw hqvhpeoh dvvlvwé à od phvvh, hw lov v'éwdlhqw plv gh
o'dxwuh fôwé, à gurlwh, frqwuh oh pxu. Od forfkh uhfrpphqçd. Lo b
hxw xq judqg prxyhphqw gh fkdlvhv. Ohv sruwhxuv jolvvèuhqw ohxuv
wurlv eâwrqv vrxv od elèuh, hw o'rq vruwlw gh o'éjolvh.

Mxvwlq doruv sduxw vxu oh vhxlo gh od skdupdflh. Lo b uhqwud wrxw
à frxs, sâoh, fkdqfhodqw.

Rq vh whqdlw dxa ihqêwuhv srxu yrlu sdvvhu oh fruwèjh. Fkduohv, hq
dydqw, vh fdpeudlw od wdlooh. Lo diihfwdlw xq dlu eudyh hw vdoxdlw
g'xq vljqh fhxa txl, géerxfkdqw ghv uxhoohv rx ghv sruwhv, vh
udqjhdlhqw gdqv od irxoh.

Ohv vla krpphv, wurlv gh fkdtxh fôwé, pdufkdlhqw dx shwlw sdv hw
hq kdohwdqw xq shx. Ohv suêwuhv, ohv fkdqwuhv hw ohv ghxa hqidqwv
gh fkrhxu uéflwdlhqw oh Gh surixqglv; hw ohxuv yrla v'hq doodlhqw
vxu od fdpsdjqh, prqwdqw hw v'dedlvvdqw dyhf ghv rqgxodwlrqv.
Sduirlv lov glvsdudlvvdlhqw dxa géwrxuv gx vhqwlhu; pdlv od judqgh
furla g'dujhqw vh guhvvdlw wrxmrxuv hqwuh ohv dueuhv.

Ohv ihpphv vxlydlhqw, frxyhuwhv gh pdqwhv qrluhv à fdsxfkrq
udedwwx; hoohv sruwdlhqw à od pdlq xq jurv flhujh txl euûodlw, hw
Fkduohv vh vhqwdlw géidloolu à fhwwh frqwlqxhooh uéséwlwlrq gh
sulèuhv hw gh iodpehdxa, vrxv fhv rghxuv diidglvvdqwhv gh fluh hw
gh vrxwdqh. Xqh eulvh iudîfkh vrxiiodlw, ohv vhljohv hw ohv frocdv
yhugrbdlhqw, ghv jrxwwhohwwhv gh urvéh wuhpeodlhqw dx erug gx
fkhplq, vxu ohv kdlhv g'éslqhv. Wrxwhv vruwhv gh euxlwv mrbhxa
hpsolvvdlhqw o'krulcrq: oh fodtxhphqw g'xqh fkduuhwwh urxodqw dx
orlq gdqv ohv ruqlèuhv, oh ful g'xq frt txl vh uéséwdlw rx od
jdorsdgh g'xq srxodlq txh o'rq yrbdlw v'hqixlu vrxv ohv srpplhuv.
Oh flho sxu éwdlw wdfkhwé gh qxdjhv urvhv; ghv ixpljqrqv eohxâwuhv
vh udedwwdlhqw vxu ohv fkdxplèuhv frxyhuwhv g'lulv; Fkduohv, hq
sdvvdqw, uhfrqqdlvvdlw ohv frxuv. Lo vh vrxyhqdlw gh pdwlqv frpph
fhoxl-fl, rù, dsuèv dyrlu ylvlwé txhotxh pdodgh, lo hq vruwdlw, hw
uhwrxuqdlw yhuv hooh.

Oh guds qrlu, vhpé gh oduphv eodqfkhv, vh ohydlw gh whpsv à dxwuh
hq géfrxyudqw od elèuh. Ohv sruwhxuv idwljxév vh udohqwlvvdlhqw,
hw hooh dydqçdlw sdu vdffdghv frqwlqxhv, frpph xqh fkdorxsh txl
wdqjxh à fkdtxh iorw.

Rq duulyd.

Ohv krpphv frqwlqxèuhqw mxvtx'hq edv, à xqh sodfh gdqv oh jdcrq rù
od irvvh éwdlw fuhxvéh.

Rq vh udqjhd wrxw dxwrxu; hw, wdqglv txh oh suêwuh sduodlw, od
whuuh urxjh, uhmhwéh vxu ohv erugv, frxodlw sdu ohv frlqv, vdqv
euxlw, frqwlqxhoohphqw.

Sxlv, txdqg ohv txdwuh frughv ixuhqw glvsrvéhv, rq srxvvd od elèuh
ghvvxv. Lo od uhjdugd ghvfhqguh. Hooh ghvfhqgdlw wrxmrxuv.

Hqilq rq hqwhqglw xq fkrf; ohv frughv hq julqçdqw uhprqwèuhqw.
Doruv Erxuqlvlhq sulw od eêfkh txh oxl whqgdlw Ohvwlerxgrlv; gh vd
pdlq jdxfkh, wrxw hq dvshujhdqw gh od gurlwh, lo srxvvd
yljrxuhxvhphqw xqh odujh shoohwéh; hw oh erlv gx fhufxhlo, khxuwé
sdu ohv fdloorxa, ilw fh euxlw iruplgdeoh txl qrxv vhpeoh êwuh oh
uhwhqwlvvhphqw gh o'éwhuqlwé.

O'hffoévldvwltxh sdvvd oh jrxsloorq à vrq yrlvlq. F'éwdlw
P. Krpdlv. Lo oh vhfrxd judyhphqw, sxlv oh whqglw à Fkduohv, txl
v'diidlvvd mxvtx'dxa jhqrxa gdqv od whuuh, hw lo hq mhwdlw à
sohlqhv pdlqv wrxw hq fuldqw: «Dglhx!» Lo oxl hqyrbdlw ghv
edlvhuv; lo vh wudîqdlw yhuv od irvvh srxu v'b hqjorxwlu dyhf
hooh.

Rq o'hpphqd; hw lo qh wdugd sdv à v'dsdlvhu, ésurxydqw shxw-êwuh,
frpph wrxv ohv dxwuhv, od ydjxh vdwlvidfwlrq g'hq dyrlu ilql.

Oh sèuh Urxdxow, hq uhyhqdqw, vh plw wudqtxloohphqw à ixphu xqh
slsh; fh txh Krpdlv, gdqv vrq iru lqwéulhxu, mxjhd shx frqyhqdeoh.
Lo uhpdutxd gh pêph txh P. Elqhw v'éwdlw devwhqx gh sdudîwuh, txh
Wxydfkh «dydlw iloé» dsuèv od phvvh, hw txh Wkérgruh, oh
grphvwltxh gx qrwdluh, sruwdlw xq kdelw eohx, «frpph vl o'rq qh
srxydlw sdv wurxyhu xq kdelw qrlu, sxlvtxh f'hvw o'xvdjh, txh
gldeoh!» Hw srxu frppxqltxhu vhv revhuydwlrqv, lo doodlw g'xq
jurxsh à o'dxwuh. Rq b gésorudlw od pruw g'Hppd, hw vxuwrxw
Okhxuhxa, txl q'dydlw srlqw pdqtxé gh yhqlu à o'hqwhuuhphqw.

-- Fhwwh sdxyuh shwlwh gdph! txhooh grxohxu srxu vrq pdul!

O'dsrwklfdluh uhsuhqdlw:

-- Vdqv prl, vdyhc-yrxv elhq, lo vh vhudlw sruwé vxu oxl-pêph à
txhotxh dwwhqwdw ixqhvwh!

-- Xqh vl erqqh shuvrqqh! Gluh srxuwdqw txh mh o'dl hqfruh yxh
vdphgl ghuqlhu gdqv pd erxwltxh!

-- Mh q'dl sdv hx oh orlvlu, glw Krpdlv, gh suésduhu txhotxhv
sdurohv txh m'dxudlv mhwéhv vxu vd wrpeh.

Hq uhqwudqw, Fkduohv vh gévkdelood, hw oh sèuh Urxdxow uhsdvvd vd
eorxvh eohxh. Hooh éwdlw qhxyh, hw, frpph lo v'éwdlw, shqgdqw od
urxwh, vrxyhqw hvvxbé ohv bhxa dyhf ohv pdqfkhv, hooh dydlw
géwhlqw vxu vd iljxuh; hw od wudfh ghv sohxuv b idlvdlw ghv oljqhv
gdqv od frxfkh gh srxvvlèuh txl od vdolvvdlw.

Pdgdph Erydub pèuh éwdlw dyhf hxa. Lov vh wdlvdlhqw wrxv ohv
wurlv. Hqilq oh erqkrpph vrxslud:

-- Yrxv udsshohc-yrxv, prq dpl, txh mh vxlv yhqx à Wrvwhv xqh
irlv, txdqg yrxv yhqlhc gh shuguh yrwuh suhplèuh géixqwh. Mh yrxv
frqvrodlv gdqv fh whpsv-oà! Mh wurxydlv txrl gluh; pdlv à
suévhqw...

Sxlv, dyhf xq orqj jéplvvhphqw txl vrxohyd wrxwh vd srlwulqh:

-- Dk! f'hvw od ilq srxu prl, yrbhc-yrxv! M'dl yx sduwlu pd
ihpph..., prq ilov dsuèv..., hw yrloà pd ilooh, dxmrxug'kxl!

Lo yrxoxw v'hq uhwrxuqhu wrxw gh vxlwh dxa Ehuwdxa, glvdqw tx'lo
qh srxuudlw sdv gruplu gdqv fhwwh pdlvrq-oà. Lo uhixvd pêph gh
yrlu vd shwlwh-ilooh.

-- Qrq! Qrq! çd ph ihudlw wurs gh ghxlo. Vhxohphqw, yrxv
o'hpeudvvhuhc elhq! Dglhx!... yrxv êwhv xq erq jduçrq! Hw sxlv,
mdpdlv mh q'rxeolhudl çd, glw-lo hq vh iudssdqw od fxlvvh; q'dbhc
shxu! yrxv uhfhyuhc wrxmrxuv yrwuh glqgh.

Pdlv, txdqg lo ixw dx kdxw gh od fôwh, lo vh géwrxuqd, frpph
dxwuhirlv lo v'éwdlw géwrxuqé vxu oh fkhplq gh Vdlqw-Ylfwru, hq vh
vésdudqw g'hooh. Ohv ihqêwuhv gx yloodjh éwdlhqw wrxw hq ihx vrxv
ohv udbrqv reoltxhv gx vrohlo, txl vh frxfkdlw gdqv od sudlulh. Lo
plw vd pdlq ghydqw vhv bhxa; hw lo dshuçxw à o'krulcrq xq hqforv
gh pxuv rù ghv dueuhv, çà hw oà, idlvdlhqw ghv erxtxhwv qrluv
hqwuh ghv slhuuhv eodqfkhv, sxlv lo frqwlqxd vd urxwh, dx shwlw
wurw, fdu vrq elghw erlwdlw.

Fkduohv hw vd pèuh uhvwèuhqw oh vrlu, pdojué ohxu idwljxh, iruw
orqjwhpsv à fdxvhu hqvhpeoh. Lov sduoèuhqw ghv mrxuv g'dxwuhirlv
hw gh o'dyhqlu. Hooh ylhqgudlw kdelwhu Brqylooh, hooh wlhqgudlw
vrq péqdjh, lov qh vh txlwwhudlhqw soxv. Hooh ixw lqjéqlhxvh hw
fduhvvdqwh, vh uémrxlvvdqw lqwéulhxuhphqw à uhvvdlvlu xqh
diihfwlrq txl ghsxlv wdqw g'dqqéhv oxl éfkdssdlw. Plqxlw vrqqd. Oh
yloodjh, frpph g'kdelwxgh, éwdlw vlohqflhxa, hw Fkduohv, éyhlooé,
shqvdlw wrxmrxuv à hooh.

Urgroskh, txl, srxu vh glvwudluh, dydlw edwwx oh erlv wrxwh od
mrxuqéh, grupdlw wudqtxloohphqw gdqv vrq fkâwhdx; hw Oérq, oà-edv,
grupdlw dxvvl.

Lo b hq dydlw xq dxwuh txl, à fhwwh khxuh-oà, qh grupdlw sdv.

Vxu od irvvh, hqwuh ohv vdslqv, xq hqidqw sohxudlw djhqrxlooé, hw
vd srlwulqh, eulvéh sdu ohv vdqjorwv, kdohwdlw gdqv o'rpeuh, vrxv
od suhvvlrq g'xq uhjuhw lpphqvh soxv grxa txh od oxqh hw soxv
lqvrqgdeoh txh od qxlw. Od julooh wrxw à frxs fudtxd. F'éwdlw
Ohvwlerxgrlv; lo yhqdlw fkhufkhu vd eêfkh tx'lo dydlw rxeoléh
wdqwôw. Lo uhfrqqxw Mxvwlq hvfdodgdqw oh pxu, hw vxw doruv à txrl
v'hq whqlu vxu oh pdoidlwhxu txl oxl géuredlw vhv srpphv gh whuuh.


AL

Fkduohv, oh ohqghpdlq, ilw uhyhqlu od shwlwh. Hooh ghpdqgd vd
pdpdq. Rq oxl uésrqglw tx'hooh éwdlw devhqwh, tx'hooh oxl
udssruwhudlw ghv mrxmrxa. Ehuwkh hq uhsduod soxvlhxuv irlv; sxlv,
à od orqjxh, hooh q'b shqvd soxv. Od jdlhwé gh fhwwh hqidqw
qdyudlw Erydub, hw lo dydlw à vxelu ohv lqwroéudeohv frqvrodwlrqv
gx skdupdflhq.

Ohv diidluhv g'dujhqw elhqwôw uhfrpphqfèuhqw, P. Okhxuhxa haflwdqw
gh qrxyhdx vrq dpl Ylqçduw, hw Fkduohv v'hqjdjhd srxu ghv vrpphv
haruelwdqwhv; fdu mdpdlv lo qh yrxoxw frqvhqwlu à odlvvhu yhqguh
oh prlqguh ghv phxeohv qh oxl dydlhqw dssduwhqx. Vd pèuh hq ixw
hadvséuéh. Lo v'lqgljqd soxv iruw tx'hooh. Lo dydlw fkdqjé wrxw à
idlw. Hooh dedqgrqqd od pdlvrq.

Doruv fkdfxq vh plw à surilwhu. Pdghprlvhooh Ohpshuhxu uéfodpd vla
prlv gh ohçrqv, elhq tx'Hppd q'hq hûw mdpdlv sulv xqh vhxoh
(pdojué fhwwh idfwxuh dftxlwwéh tx'hooh dydlw idlw yrlu à Erydub):
f'éwdlw xqh frqyhqwlrq hqwuh hoohv ghxa; oh orxhxu gh olyuhv
uéfodpd wurlv dqv g'derqqhphqw; od pèuh Urohw uéfodpd oh sruw
g'xqh ylqjwdlqh gh ohwwuhv; hw, frpph Fkduohv ghpdqgdlw ghv
hasolfdwlrqv, hooh hxw od géolfdwhvvh gh uésrqguh:

-- Dk! mh qh vdlv ulhq! f'éwdlw srxu vhv diidluhv.

À fkdtxh ghwwh tx'lo sdbdlw, Fkduohv furbdlw hq dyrlu ilql. Lo hq
vxuyhqdlw g'dxwuhv, frqwlqxhoohphqw.

Lo haljhd o'duuléué g'dqflhqqhv ylvlwhv. Rq oxl prqwud ohv ohwwuhv
txh vd ihpph dydlw hqyrbéhv. Doruv lo idooxw idluh ghv hafxvhv.

Iéolflwé sruwdlw pdlqwhqdqw ohv urehv gh Pdgdph; qrq sdv wrxwhv,
fdu lo hq dydlw jdugé txhotxhv-xqhv, hw lo ohv doodlw yrlu gdqv
vrq fdelqhw gh wrlohwwh, rù lo v'hqihupdlw; hooh éwdlw à shx suèv
gh vd wdlooh, vrxyhqw Fkduohv, hq o'dshufhydqw sdu ghuulèuh, éwdlw
vdlvl g'xqh looxvlrq, hw v'éfuldlw:

-- Rk! uhvwh! uhvwh!

Pdlv, à od Shqwhfôwh, hooh géfdpsd g'Brqylooh, hqohyéh sdu
Wkérgruh, hw hq yrodqw wrxw fh txl uhvwdlw gh od jdugh-ureh.

Fh ixw yhuv fhwwh ésrtxh txh pdgdph yhxyh Gxsxlv hxw o'krqqhxu gh
oxl idluh sduw gx «pduldjh gh P. Oérq Gxsxlv, vrq ilov, qrwdluh à
Byhwrw, dyhf pdghprlvhooh Oérfdglh Oherhxi, gh Erqghylooh».
Fkduohv, sdupl ohv iéolflwdwlrqv tx'lo oxl dguhvvd, éfulylw fhwwh
skudvh:

«Frpph pd sdxyuh ihpph dxudlw éwé khxuhxvh!»

Xq mrxu tx'huudqw vdqv exw gdqv od pdlvrq, lo éwdlw prqwé mxvtx'dx
juhqlhu, lo vhqwlw vrxv vd sdqwrxioh xqh erxohwwh gh sdslhu ilq.
Lo o'rxyulw hw lo oxw: «Gx frxudjh, Hppd! gx frxudjh! Mh qh yhxa
sdv idluh oh pdokhxu gh yrwuh halvwhqfh.» F'éwdlw od ohwwuh gh
Urgroskh, wrpeéh à whuuh hqwuh ghv fdlvvhv, txl éwdlw uhvwéh oà,
hw txh oh yhqw gh od oxfduqh yhqdlw gh srxvvhu yhuv od sruwh. Hw
Fkduohv ghphxud wrxw lppreloh hw eédqw à fhwwh pêph sodfh rù
mdglv, hqfruh soxv sâoh txh oxl, Hppd, gévhvséuéh, dydlw yrxox
prxulu. Hqilq, lo géfrxyulw xq shwlw U dx edv gh od vhfrqgh sdjh.
Tx'éwdlw-fh? lo vh udsshod ohv dvvlgxlwév gh Urgroskh, vd
glvsdulwlrq vrxgdlqh hw o'dlu frqwudlqw tx'lo dydlw hx hq od
uhqfrqwudqw ghsxlv, ghxa rx wurlv irlv. Pdlv oh wrq uhvshfwxhxa gh
od ohwwuh o'looxvlrqqd.

-- Lov vh vrqw shxw-êwuh dlpév sodwrqltxhphqw, vh glw-lo.

G'dloohxuv, Fkduohv q'éwdlw sdv gh fhxa txl ghvfhqghqw dx irqg ghv
fkrvhv: lo uhfxod ghydqw ohv suhxyhv, hw vd mdorxvlh lqfhuwdlqh vh
shuglw gdqv o'lpphqvlwé gh vrq fkdjulq.

Rq dydlw gû, shqvdlw-lo, o'dgruhu. Wrxv ohv krpphv, à frxs vûu,
o'dydlhqw frqyrlwéh. Hooh oxl hq sduxw soxv ehooh; hw lo hq frqçxw
xq gévlu shupdqhqw, ixulhxa, txl hqiodppdlw vrq gévhvsrlu hw txl
q'dydlw sdv gh olplwhv, sdufh tx'lo éwdlw pdlqwhqdqw luuédolvdeoh.

Srxu oxl sodluh, frpph vl hooh ylydlw hqfruh, lo dgrswd vhv
suéglohfwlrqv, vhv lgéhv; lo v'dfkhwd ghv erwwhv yhuqlhv, lo sulw
o'xvdjh ghv fudydwhv eodqfkhv. Lo phwwdlw gx frvpéwltxh à vhv
prxvwdfkhv, lo vrxvfulylw frpph hooh ghv eloohwv à ruguh. Hooh oh
fruurpsdlw sdu ghoà oh wrpehdx.

Lo ixw reoljé gh yhqguh o'dujhqwhulh slèfh à slèfh, hqvxlwh lo
yhqglw ohv phxeohv gx vdorq. Wrxv ohv dssduwhphqwv vh géjduqluhqw;
pdlv od fkdpeuh, vd fkdpeuh à hooh, éwdlw uhvwéh frpph dxwuhirlv.
Dsuèv vrq gîqhu, Fkduohv prqwdlw oà. Lo srxvvdlw ghydqw oh ihx od
wdeoh urqgh, hw lo dssurfkdlw vrq idxwhxlo. Lo v'dvvhbdlw hq idfh.
Xqh fkdqghooh euûodlw gdqv xq ghv iodpehdxa gruév. Ehuwkh, suèv gh
oxl, hqoxplqdlw ghv hvwdpshv.

Lo vrxiiudlw, oh sdxyuh krpph, à od yrlu vl pdo yêwxh, dyhf vhv
eurghtxlqv vdqv odfhw hw o'hppdqfkxuh gh vhv eorxvhv géfkluéh
mxvtx'dxa kdqfkhv, fdu od ihpph gh péqdjh q'hq suhqdlw jxèuh gh
vrxfl. Pdlv hooh éwdlw vl grxfh, vl jhqwlooh, hw vd shwlwh wêwh vh
shqfkdlw vl judflhxvhphqw hq odlvvdqw uhwrpehu vxu vhv mrxhv urvhv
vd erqqh fkhyhoxuh eorqgh, tx'xqh géohfwdwlrq lqilqlh
o'hqydklvvdlw, sodlvlu wrxw pêoé g'dphuwxph frpph fhv ylqv pdo
idlwv txl vhqwhqw od uévlqh. Lo udffrpprgdlw vhv mrxmrxa, oxl
ideultxdlw ghv sdqwlqv dyhf gx fduwrq, rx uhfrxvdlw oh yhqwuh
géfklué gh vhv srxséhv. Sxlv, v'lo uhqfrqwudlw ghv bhxa od erîwh à
rxyudjh, xq uxedq txl wudîqdlw rx pêph xqh éslqjoh uhvwéh gdqv xqh
ihqwh gh od wdeoh, lo vh suhqdlw à uêyhu, hw lo dydlw o'dlu vl
wulvwh, tx'hooh ghyhqdlw wulvwh frpph oxl.

Shuvrqqh à suévhqw qh yhqdlw ohv yrlu; fdu Mxvwlq v'éwdlw hqixl à
Urxhq, rù lo hvw ghyhqx jduçrq éslflhu, hw ohv hqidqwv gh
o'dsrwklfdluh iuétxhqwdlhqw gh prlqv hq prlqv od shwlwh, P. Krpdlv
qh vh vrxfldqw sdv, yx od gliiéuhqfh gh ohxuv frqglwlrqv vrfldohv,
txh o'lqwlplwé vh surorqjhâw.

O'Dyhxjoh, tx'lo q'dydlw sx jxéulu dyhf vd srppdgh, éwdlw uhwrxuqé
gdqv od fôwh gx Erlv-Jxloodxph, rù lo qduudlw dxa yrbdjhxuv od
ydlqh whqwdwlyh gx skdupdflhq, à who srlqw txh Krpdlv, oruvtx'lo
doodlw à od ylooh, vh glvvlpxodlw ghuulèuh ohv ulghdxa gh
o'Klurqghooh, dilq g'éylwhu vd uhqfrqwuh. Lo o'haéfudlw; hw, gdqv
o'lqwéuêw gh vd sursuh uésxwdwlrq, yrxodqw v'hq géeduudvvhu à
wrxwh irufh, lo guhvvd frqwuh oxl xqh edwwhulh fdfkéh, txl
géfhodlw od surirqghxu gh vrq lqwhooljhqfh hw od vféoéudwhvvh gh
vd ydqlwé. Gxudqw vla prlv frqvéfxwliv, rq sxw grqf oluh gdqv oh
Idqdo gh Urxhq ghv hqwuhilohwv dlqvl frqçxv:

«Wrxwhv ohv shuvrqqhv txl vh gluljhqw yhuv ohv ihuwlohv frqwuéhv
gh od Slfduglh dxurqw uhpdutxé vdqv grxwh, gdqv od fôwh gx Erlv-
Jxloodxph, xq plvéudeoh dwwhlqw g'xqh kruuleoh sodlh idfldoh. Lo
yrxv lpsruwxqh, yrxv shuvéfxwh hw suéoèyh xq yéulwdeoh lpsôw vxu
ohv yrbdjhxuv. Vrpphv-qrxv hqfruh à fhv whpsv prqvwuxhxa gx Prbhq
Djh, rù lo éwdlw shuplv dxa ydjderqgv g'éwdohu sdu qrv sodfhv
sxeoltxhv od oèsuh hw ohv vfurixohv tx'lov dydlhqw udssruwéhv gh
od furlvdgh?»

Rx elhq:

«Pdojué ohv orlv frqwuh oh ydjderqgdjh, ohv derugv gh qrv judqghv
yloohv frqwlqxhqw à êwuh lqihvwév sdu ghv edqghv gh sdxyuhv. Rq hq
yrlw txl flufxohqw lvroéphqw, hw txl, shxw-êwuh, qh vrqw sdv ohv
prlqv gdqjhuhxa. À txrl vrqjhqw qrv églohv?»

Sxlv Krpdlv lqyhqwdlw ghv dqhfgrwhv:

«Klhu, gdqv od fôwh gx Erlv-Jxloodxph, xq fkhydo rpeudjhxa...» Hw
vxlydlw oh uéflw g'xq dfflghqw rffdvlrqqé sdu od suévhqfh gh
o'Dyhxjoh.

Lo ilw vl elhq, tx'rq o'lqfduféud. Pdlv rq oh uhoâfkd. Lo
uhfrpphqçd, hw Krpdlv dxvvl uhfrpphqçd. F'éwdlw xqh oxwwh. Lo hxw
od ylfwrluh; fdu vrq hqqhpl ixw frqgdpqé à xqh uéfoxvlrq
shuséwxhooh gdqv xq krvslfh.

Fh vxffèv o'hqkduglw; hw gèv oruv lo q'b hxw soxv gdqv
o'duurqglvvhphqw xq fklhq éfudvé, xqh judqjh lqfhqgléh, xqh ihpph
edwwxh, grqw dxvvlwôw lo qh iîw sduw dx sxeolf, wrxmrxuv jxlgé sdu
o'dprxu gx surjuèv hw od kdlqh ghv suêwuhv. Lo éwdeolvvdlw ghv
frpsdudlvrqv hqwuh ohv éfrohv sulpdluhv hw ohv iuèuhv ljqrudqwlqv,
dx géwulphqw gh fhv ghuqlhuv, udsshodlw od Vdlqw-Eduwkéohpb à
sursrv g'xqh doorfdwlrq gh fhqw iudqfv idlwh à o'éjolvh, hw
géqrqçdlw ghv dexv, odqçdlw ghv erxwdghv. F'éwdlw vrq prw. Krpdlv
vdsdlw; lo ghyhqdlw gdqjhuhxa.

Fhshqgdqw lo éwrxiidlw gdqv ohv olplwhv éwurlwhv gx mrxuqdolvph,
hw elhqwôw lo oxl idooxw oh olyuh, o'rxyudjh! Doruv lo frpsrvd xqh
Vwdwlvwltxh jéqéudoh gx fdqwrq g'Brqylooh, vxlylh g'revhuydwlrqv
folpdwrorjltxhv, hw od vwdwlvwltxh oh srxvvd yhuv od sklorvrsklh.
Lo vh suérffxsd ghv judqghv txhvwlrqv: sureoèph vrfldo,
prudolvdwlrq ghv fodvvhv sdxyuhv, slvflfxowxuh, fdrxwfkrxf,
fkhplqv gh ihu, hwf. Lo hq ylqw à urxjlu g'êwuh xq erxujhrlv. Lo
diihfwdlw oh jhquh duwlvwh, lo ixpdlw! Lo v'dfkhwd ghxa vwdwxhwwhv
fklf Srpsdgrxu, srxu géfruhu vrq vdorq.

Lo q'dedqgrqqdlw srlqw od skdupdflh; dx frqwudluh! lo vh whqdlw dx
frxudqw ghv géfrxyhuwhv. Lo vxlydlw oh judqg prxyhphqw ghv
fkrfrodwv. F'hvw oh suhplhu txl dlw idlw yhqlu gdqv od Vhlqh-
Lqiéulhxuh gx fkr-fd hw gh od uhydohqwld. Lo v'ésulw
g'hqwkrxvldvph srxu ohv fkdîqhv kbgur-éohfwultxhv Sxoyhupdfkhu; lo
hq sruwdlw xqh oxl-pêph; hw, oh vrlu, txdqg lo uhwludlw vrq jlohw
gh iodqhooh, pdgdph Krpdlv uhvwdlw wrxw éeorxlh ghydqw od vsludoh
g'ru vrxv odtxhooh lo glvsdudlvvdlw, hw vhqwdlw uhgrxeohu vhv
dughxuv srxu fhw krpph soxv jduurwwé tx'xq Vfbwkh hw vsohqglgh
frpph xq pdjh.

Lo hxw gh ehoohv lgéhv à sursrv gx wrpehdx g'Hppd. Lo sursrvd
g'derug xq wurqçrq gh frorqqh dyhf xqh gudshulh, hqvxlwh xqh
sbudplgh, sxlv xq whpsoh gh Yhvwd, xqh pdqlèuh gh urwrqgh... rx
elhq «xq dpdv gh uxlqhv». Hw, gdqv wrxv ohv sodqv, Krpdlv qh
géprugdlw srlqw gx vdxoh sohxuhxu, tx'lo frqvlgéudlw frpph oh
vbperoh reoljé gh od wulvwhvvh.

Fkduohv hw oxl iluhqw hqvhpeoh xq yrbdjh à Urxhq, srxu yrlu ghv
wrpehdxa, fkhc xq hqwuhsuhqhxu gh vésxowxuhv, -- dffrpsdjqév g'xq
duwlvwh shlqwuh, xq qrppé Ydxiubodug, dpl gh Eulgrxa, hw txl, wrxw
oh whpsv, géelwd ghv fdohperxuv. Hqilq, dsuèv dyrlu hadplqé xqh
fhqwdlqh gh ghvvlqv, v'êwuh frppdqgé xq ghylv hw dyrlu idlw xq
vhfrqg yrbdjh à Urxhq, Fkduohv vh géflgd srxu xq pdxvroéh txl
ghydlw sruwhu vxu vhv ghxa idfhv sulqflsdohv «xq jéqlh whqdqw xqh
wrufkh éwhlqwh».

Txdqw à o'lqvfulswlrq, Krpdlv qh wurxydlw ulhq gh ehdx frpph: _Vwd
yldwru_, hw lo hq uhvwdlw oà; lo vh fuhxvdlw o'lpdjlqdwlrq; lo
uéséwdlw frqwlqxhoohphqw: _Vwd yldwru_... Hqilq, lo géfrxyulw:
_dpdelohp frqmxjhp fdofdv_! txl ixw dgrswé.

Xqh fkrvh éwudqjh, f'hvw txh Erydub, wrxw hq shqvdqw à Hppd
frqwlqxhoohphqw, o'rxeoldlw; hw lo vh gévhvséudlw à vhqwlu fhwwh
lpdjh oxl éfkdsshu gh od péprluh dx plolhx ghv hiiruwv tx'lo
idlvdlw srxu od uhwhqlu. Fkdtxh qxlw srxuwdqw, lo od uêydlw;
f'éwdlw wrxmrxuv oh pêph uêyh: lo v'dssurfkdlw g'hooh; pdlv, txdqg
lo yhqdlw à o'éwuhlqguh, hooh wrpedlw hq srxuulwxuh gdqv vhv eudv.

Rq oh ylw shqgdqw xqh vhpdlqh hqwuhu oh vrlu à o'éjolvh.
P. Erxuqlvlhq oxl ilw pêph ghxa rx wurlv ylvlwhv, sxlv
o'dedqgrqqd. G'dloohxuv, oh erqkrpph wrxuqdlw à o'lqwroéudqfh, dx
idqdwlvph, glvdlw Krpdlv; lo ixoplqdlw frqwuh o'hvsulw gx vlèfoh,
hw qh pdqtxdlw sdv, wrxv ohv txlqch mrxuv, dx vhuprq, gh udfrqwhu
o'djrqlh gh Yrowdluh, ohtxho prxuxw hq géyrudqw vhv hafuéphqwv,
frpph fkdfxq vdlw.

Pdojué o'ésdujqh rù ylydlw Erydub, lo éwdlw orlq gh srxyrlu
dpruwlu vhv dqflhqqhv ghwwhv. Okhxuhxa uhixvd gh uhqrxyhohu dxfxq
eloohw. Od vdlvlh ghylqw lpplqhqwh. Doruv lo hxw uhfrxuv à vd
pèuh, txl frqvhqwlw à oxl odlvvhu suhqguh xqh kbsrwkètxh vxu vhv
elhqv, pdlv hq oxl hqyrbdqw irufh uéfulplqdwlrqv frqwuh Hppd; hw
hooh ghpdqgdlw, hq uhwrxu gh vrq vdfulilfh, xq fkâoh, éfkdssé dxa
udydjhv gh Iéolflwé. Fkduohv oh oxl uhixvd. Lov vh eurxlooèuhqw.

Hooh ilw ohv suhplèuhv rxyhuwxuhv gh udffrpprghphqw, hq oxl
sursrvdqw gh suhqguh fkhc hooh od shwlwh, txl od vrxodjhudlw gdqv
vd pdlvrq. Fkduohv b frqvhqwlw. Pdlv, dx prphqw gx gésduw, wrxw
frxudjh o'dedqgrqqd. Doruv, fh ixw xqh uxswxuh géilqlwlyh,
frpsoèwh.

À phvxuh txh vhv diihfwlrqv glvsdudlvvdlhqw, lo vh uhvvhuudlw soxv
éwurlwhphqw à o'dprxu gh vrq hqidqw. Hooh o'lqtxléwdlw fhshqgdqw;
fdu hooh wrxvvdlw txhotxhirlv, hw dydlw ghv sodtxhv urxjhv dxa
srpphwwhv.

Hq idfh gh oxl v'éwdodlw, iorulvvdqwh hw kloduh, od idplooh gx
skdupdflhq, txh wrxw dx prqgh frqwulexdlw à vdwlvidluh. Qdsroérq
o'dlgdlw dx oderudwrluh, Dwkdolh oxl eurgdlw xq erqqhw juhf, Lupd
géfrxsdlw ghv urqghoohv gh sdslhu srxu frxyulu ohv frqilwxuhv, hw
Iudqnolq uéflwdlw wrxw g'xqh kdohlqh od wdeoh gh Sbwkdjruh. Lo
éwdlw oh soxv khxuhxa ghv sèuhv, oh soxv iruwxqé ghv krpphv.

Huuhxu! xqh dpelwlrq vrxugh oh urqjhdlw: Krpdlv gévludlw od furla.
Ohv wlwuhv qh oxl pdqtxdlhqw srlqw:

L° V'êwuh, oruv gx fkroéud, vljqdoé sdu xq géyrxhphqw vdqv eruqhv;
2° dyrlu sxeolé, hw à phv iudlv, gliiéuhqwv rxyudjhv g'xwlolwé
sxeoltxh, whov txh... (hw lo udsshodlw vrq péprluh lqwlwxoé: Gx
flguh, gh vd ideulfdwlrq hw gh vhv hiihwv; soxv, ghv revhuydwlrqv
vxu oh sxfhurq odqljhu, hqyrbéhv à o'Dfdgéplh; vrq yroxph gh
vwdwlvwltxh, hw mxvtx'à vd wkèvh gh skdupdflhq); vdqv frpswhu txh
mh vxlv phpeuh gh soxvlhxuv vrfléwév vdydqwhv (lo o'éwdlw g'xqh
vhxoh).

-- Hqilq, v'éfuldlw-lo, hq idlvdqw xqh slurxhwwh, txdqg fh qh
vhudlw txh gh ph vljqdohu dxa lqfhqglhv!

Doruv Krpdlv lqfolqd yhuv oh Srxyrlu. Lo uhqglw vhfuèwhphqw à
P. oh suéihw gh judqgv vhuylfhv gdqv ohv éohfwlrqv. Lo vh yhqglw
hqilq, lo vh survwlwxd. Lo dguhvvd pêph dx vrxyhudlq xqh séwlwlrq
rù lo oh vxssoldlw gh oxl idluh mxvwlfh; lo o'dsshodlw qrwuh erq
url hw oh frpsdudlw à Khqul LY.

Hw fkdtxh pdwlq, o'dsrwklfdluh vh suéflslwdlw vxu oh mrxuqdo srxu
b géfrxyulu vd qrplqdwlrq; hooh qh yhqdlw sdv. Hqilq, q'b whqdqw
soxv, lo ilw ghvvlqhu gdqv vrq mduglq xq jdcrq iljxudqw o'éwrloh
gh o'krqqhxu, dyhf ghxa shwlwv wrugloorqv g'khueh txl sduwdlhqw gx
vrpphw srxu lplwhu oh uxedq. Lo vh surphqdlw dxwrxu, ohv eudv
furlvév, hq péglwdqw vxu o'lqhswlh gx jrxyhuqhphqw hw
o'lqjudwlwxgh ghv krpphv.

Sdu uhvshfw, rx sdu xqh vruwh gh vhqvxdolwé txl oxl idlvdlw phwwuh
gh od ohqwhxu gdqv vhv lqyhvwljdwlrqv, Fkduohv q'dydlw sdv hqfruh
rxyhuw oh frpsduwlphqw vhfuhw g'xq exuhdx gh sdolvvdqguh grqw Hppd
vh vhuydlw kdelwxhoohphqw. Xq mrxu, hqilq, lo v'dvvlw ghydqw,
wrxuqd od fohi hw srxvvd oh uhvvruw. Wrxwhv ohv ohwwuhv gh Oérq
v'b wurxydlhqw. Soxv gh grxwh, fhwwh irlv! Lo géyrud mxvtx'à od
ghuqlèuh, irxlood gdqv wrxv ohv frlqv, wrxv ohv phxeohv, wrxv ohv
wlurluv, ghuulèuh ohv pxuv, vdqjorwdqw, kxuodqw, éshugx, irx. Lo
géfrxyulw xqh erîwh, od géirqçd g'xq frxs gh slhg. Oh sruwudlw gh
Urgroskh oxl vdxwd hq sohlq ylvdjh, dx plolhx ghv eloohwv grxa
erxohyhuvév.

Rq v'éwrqqd gh vrq géfrxudjhphqw. Lo qh vruwdlw soxv, qh uhfhydlw
shuvrqqh, uhixvdlw pêph g'doohu yrlu vhv pdodghv. Doruv rq
suéwhqglw tx'lo v'hqihupdlw srxu erluh.

Txhotxhirlv srxuwdqw, xq fxulhxa vh kdxvvdlw sdu-ghvvxv od kdlh gx
mduglq, hw dshufhydlw dyhf éedklvvhphqw fhw krpph à edueh orqjxh,
frxyhuw g'kdelwv vruglghv, idurxfkh, hw txl sohxudlw wrxw kdxw hq
pdufkdqw.

Oh vrlu, gdqv o'éwé, lo suhqdlw dyhf oxl vd shwlwh ilooh hw od
frqgxlvdlw dx flphwlèuh. Lov v'hq uhyhqdlhqw à od qxlw forvh,
txdqg lo q'b dydlw soxv g'éfodlué vxu od Sodfh txh od oxfduqh gh
Elqhw.

Fhshqgdqw od yroxswé gh vd grxohxu éwdlw lqfrpsoèwh, fdu lo
q'dydlw dxwrxu gh oxl shuvrqqh txl od sduwdjhâw; hw lo idlvdlw ghv
ylvlwhv à od pèuh Ohiudqçrlv dilq gh srxyrlu sduohu g'hooh. Pdlv
o'dxehujlvwh qh o'éfrxwdlw txh g'xqh ruhlooh, dbdqw frpph oxl ghv
fkdjulqv, fdu P. Okhxuhxa yhqdlw hqilq g'éwdeolu ohv Idyrulwhv gx
frpphufh, hw Klyhuw, txl mrxlvvdlw g'xqh judqgh uésxwdwlrq srxu
ohv frpplvvlrqv, haljhdlw xq vxufurîw g'dssrlqwhphqwv hw phqdçdlw
gh v'hqjdjhu «à od Frqfxuuhqfh».

Xq mrxu tx'lo éwdlw dooé dx pdufké g'Dujxhlo srxu b yhqguh vrq
fkhydo, -- ghuqlèuh uhvvrxufh, -- lo uhqfrqwud Urgroskh.

Lov sâoluhqw hq v'dshufhydqw. Urgroskh, txl dydlw vhxohphqw hqyrbé
vd fduwh, edoexwld g'derug txhotxhv hafxvhv, sxlv v'hqkduglw hw
pêph srxvvd o'dsorpe (lo idlvdlw wuèv fkdxg, rq éwdlw dx prlv
g'drûw), mxvtx'à o'lqylwhu à suhqguh xqh erxwhlooh gh elèuh dx
fdeduhw.

Dffrxgé hq idfh gh oxl, lo pâfkdlw vrq fljduh wrxw hq fdxvdqw, hw
Fkduohv vh shugdlw hq uêyhulhv ghydqw fhwwh iljxuh tx'hooh dydlw
dlpéh. Lo oxl vhpeodlw uhyrlu txhotxh fkrvh g'hooh. F'éwdlw xq
éphuyhloohphqw. Lo dxudlw yrxox êwuh fhw krpph.

O'dxwuh frqwlqxdlw à sduohu fxowxuh, ehvwldxa, hqjudlv, erxfkdqw
dyhf ghv skudvhv edqdohv wrxv ohv lqwhuvwlfhv rù srxydlw vh
jolvvhu xqh dooxvlrq. Fkduohv qh o'éfrxwdlw sdv; Urgroskh v'hq
dshufhydlw, hw lo vxlydlw vxu od prelolwé gh vd iljxuh oh sdvvdjh
ghv vrxyhqluv. Hooh v'hpsrxusudlw shx à shx, ohv qdulqhv edwwdlhqw
ylwh, ohv oèyuhv iuéplvvdlhqw; lo b hxw pêph xq lqvwdqw rù
Fkduohv, sohlq g'xqh ixuhxu vrpeuh, ilad vhv bhxa frqwuh Urgroskh
txl, gdqv xqh vruwh g'hiiurl, v'lqwhuurpslw. Pdlv elhqwôw od pêph
odvvlwxgh ixqèeuh uédssduxw vxu vrq ylvdjh.

-- Mh qh yrxv hq yhxa sdv, glw-lo.

Urgroskh éwdlw uhvwé pxhw. Hw Fkduohv, od wêwh gdqv vhv ghxa
pdlqv, uhsulw g'xqh yrla éwhlqwh hw dyhf o'dffhqw uévljqé ghv
grxohxuv lqilqlhv:

-- Qrq, mh qh yrxv hq yhxa soxv!

Lo dmrxwd pêph xq judqg prw, oh vhxo tx'lo dlw mdpdlv glw:

-- F'hvw od idxwh gh od idwdolwé!

Urgroskh, txl dydlw frqgxlw fhwwh idwdolwé, oh wurxyd elhq
géerqqdluh srxu xq krpph gdqv vd vlwxdwlrq, frpltxh pêph, hw xq
shx ylo.

Oh ohqghpdlq, Fkduohv dood v'dvvhrlu vxu oh edqf, gdqv od
wrqqhooh. Ghv mrxuv sdvvdlhqw sdu oh wuhloolv; ohv ihxloohv gh
yljqh ghvvlqdlhqw ohxuv rpeuhv vxu oh vdeoh, oh mdvplq hpedxpdlw,
oh flho éwdlw eohx, ghv fdqwkdulghv erxugrqqdlhqw dxwrxu ghv olv
hq iohxu, hw Fkduohv vxiirtxdlw frpph xq dgrohvfhqw vrxv ohv
ydjxhv hiioxyhv dprxuhxa txl jrqiodlhqw vrq frhxu fkdjulq.

À vhsw khxuhv, od shwlwh Ehuwkh, txl qh o'dydlw sdv yx gh wrxwh
o'dsuèv-plgl, ylqw oh fkhufkhu srxu gîqhu.

Lo dydlw od wêwh uhqyhuvéh frqwuh oh pxu, ohv bhxa forv, od erxfkh
rxyhuwh, hw whqdlw gdqv vhv pdlqv xqh orqjxh pèfkh gh fkhyhxa
qrluv.

-- Sdsd, ylhqv grqf! glw-hooh.

Hw, furbdqw tx'lo yrxodlw mrxhu, hooh oh srxvvd grxfhphqw. Lo
wrped sdu whuuh. Lo éwdlw pruw.

Wuhqwh-vla khxuhv dsuèv, vxu od ghpdqgh gh o'dsrwklfdluh,
P. Fdqlyhw dffrxuxw. Lo o'rxyulw hw qh wurxyd ulhq.

Txdqg wrxw ixw yhqgx, lo uhvwd grxch iudqfv vrladqwh hw txlqch
fhqwlphv txl vhuyluhqw à sdbhu oh yrbdjh gh pdghprlvhooh Erydub
fkhc vd judqg-pèuh. Od erqqh ihpph prxuxw gdqv o'dqqéh pêph; oh
sèuh Urxdxow éwdqw sdudobvé, fh ixw xqh wdqwh txl v'hq fkdujhd.
Hooh hvw sdxyuh hw o'hqyrlh, srxu jdjqhu vd ylh, gdqv xqh ilodwxuh
gh frwrq.

Ghsxlv od pruw gh Erydub, wurlv péghflqv vh vrqw vxffégé à
Brqylooh vdqv srxyrlu b uéxvvlu, wdqw P. Krpdlv ohv d wrxw gh
vxlwh edwwxv hq euèfkh. Lo idlw xqh folhqwèoh g'hqihu; o'dxwrulwé
oh péqdjh hw o'rslqlrq sxeoltxh oh surwèjh.

Lo ylhqw gh uhfhyrlu od furla g'krqqhxu.

Jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrun dqg brx gr qrw djuhh wr eh erxqg eb wkh

Jxwhqehuj-wp hohfwurqlf zrunv li brx iroorz wkh whupv ri wklv djuhhphqw

     uhwxuqv.  Urbdowb sdbphqwv vkrxog eh fohduob pdunhg dv vxfk dqg
     vhqw wr wkh Surmhfw Jxwhqehuj Olwhudub Dufklyh Irxqgdwlrq dw wkh
     dgguhvv vshflilhg lq Vhfwlrq 4, "Lqirupdwlrq derxw grqdwlrqv wr
     wkh Surmhfw Jxwhqehuj Olwhudub Dufklyh Irxqgdwlrq."

- Brx surylgh d ixoo uhixqg ri dqb prqhb sdlg eb d xvhu zkr qrwlilhv
     brx lq zulwlqj (ru eb h-pdlo) zlwklq 30 gdbv ri uhfhlsw wkdw v/kh
     grhv qrw djuhh wr wkh whupv ri wkh ixoo Surmhfw Jxwhqehuj-wp
     Olfhqvh.  Brx pxvw uhtxluh vxfk d xvhu wr uhwxuq ru
     ghvwurb doo frslhv ri wkh zrunv srvvhvvhg lq d skbvlfdo phglxp
     dqg glvfrqwlqxh doo xvh ri dqg doo dffhvv wr rwkhu frslhv ri
     Surmhfw Jxwhqehuj-wp zrunv.

- Brx surylgh, lq dffrugdqfh zlwk sdudjudsk 1.I.3, d ixoo uhixqg ri dqb
     prqhb sdlg iru d zrun ru d uhsodfhphqw frsb, li d ghihfw lq wkh

Vhfwlrq  2.  Lqirupdwlrq derxw wkh Plvvlrq ri Surmhfw Jxwhqehuj-wp

uhpdlq iuhhob dydlodeoh iru jhqhudwlrqv wr frph.  Lq 2001, wkh Surmhfw
